dard tumhaara kaisa hai
shohrat talwe chaTegi
pas mein jis ke paisa hai

aisā lamha udhār de koī
jis meñ sadiyāñ guzār de koī
baad muddat ke ḳhat likhe vo mujhe
aur kabūtar ko maar de koī
ye jo sardār ban ke baiThā hai
us kī pagḌī utaar de koī
mast rakkhe jo hosh meñ bhī mujhe
ab to aisā ḳhumār de koī
kyā ḳhabar hādsātī duniyā meñ
kab kahāñ mujh ko maar de koī
ek va.ada ki jis ke saa.e meñ
umr saarī guzār de koī
dasht ko ghar banā ke baiThā huuñ
is ko aa kar sañvār de koī
aisa lamha udhaar de koi
jis mein sadiyan guzar de koi
baad muddat ke KHat likhe wo mujhe
aur kabutar ko mar de koi
ye jo sardar ban ke baiTha hai
us ki pagDi utar de koi
mast rakkhe jo hosh mein bhi mujhe
ab to aisa KHumar de koi
kya KHabar hadsati duniya mein
kab kahan mujh ko mar de koi
ek wada ki jis ke sae mein
umr sari guzar de koi
dasht ko ghar bana ke baiTha hun
is ko aa kar sanwar de koi

Thahrī Thahrī sī zindagī kyoñ hai
merī āñkhoñ meñ ye namī kyoñ hai
jis ko āñkho se duur rakhnā thā
aaj qurbat meñ phir vahī kyoñ hai
jabki sachchā.ī sirf syāhī hai
phir mire ghar meñ raushnī kyoñ hai
buuñd kī bhī to ek duniyā hai
buuñd ke bin nadī nadī kyoñ hai
tum ko 'ādarsh' sab milā hai yahāñ
dil meñ phir bhī ye tishnagī kyoñ hai
Thahri Thahri si zindagi kyon hai
meri aankhon mein ye nami kyon hai
jis ko aankho se dur rakhna tha
aaj qurbat mein phir wahi kyon hai
jabki sachchai sirf syahi hai
phir mere ghar mein raushni kyon hai
bund ki bhi to ek duniya hai
bund ke bin nadi nadi kyon hai
tum ko 'adarsh' sab mila hai yahan
dil mein phir bhi ye tishnagi kyon hai

jab judā hone kā manzar aa gayā thā
ek qatre meñ samundar aa gayā thā
haath meñ jab tere patthar aa gayā thā
ghar se maiñ dīvāna bāhar aa gayā thā
DhūñDhtā rahtā huuñ ā.īne meñ ḳhud ko
kaun mere itne andar aa gayā thā
pī liyā thā ek kaḌvā ghūñT us ne
zā.iqa mere laboñ par aa gayā thā
ishq bas pahlī dafa achchhā lagā thā
dūsre chakkar meñ chakkar aa gayā thā
is liye terī kahānī se huuñ bāhar
mujh se ik kirdār behtar aa gayā thā
jab juda hone ka manzar aa gaya tha
ek qatre mein samundar aa gaya tha
hath mein jab tere patthar aa gaya tha
ghar se main diwana bahar aa gaya tha
DhunDhta rahta hun aaine mein KHud ko
kaun mere itne andar aa gaya tha
pi liya tha ek kaDwa ghunT us ne
zaiqa mere labon par aa gaya tha
ishq bas pahli dafa achchha laga tha
dusre chakkar mein chakkar aa gaya tha
is liye teri kahani se hun bahar
mujh se ek kirdar behtar aa gaya tha

gunāh apne ginātā huuñ Darne lagtā huuñ
ḳhudā ke sāmne jaatā huuñ Darne lagtā huuñ
kuchh itnā ḳhaufzada huuñ maiñ apne kamre meñ
koī charāġh jalātā huuñ Darne lagtā huuñ
ab is maqām pe pahuñchī hai merī tanhā.ī
qarīb ḳhud ke bhī jaatā huuñ Darne lagtā huuñ
qarīb dekh ke mujh ko lipaT na jaa.e kahīñ
maiñ us kī bazm meñ jaatā huuñ Darne lagtā huuñ
kahīñ vo jaan na le mere dil kī hālat ko
kisī ko she'r sunātā huuñ Darne lagtā huuñ
gunah apne ginata hun Darne lagta hun
KHuda ke samne jata hun Darne lagta hun
kuchh itna KHaufzada hun main apne kamre mein
koi charagh jalata hun Darne lagta hun
ab is maqam pe pahunchi hai meri tanhai
qarib KHud ke bhi jata hun Darne lagta hun
qarib dekh ke mujh ko lipaT na jae kahin
main us ki bazm mein jata hun Darne lagta hun
kahin wo jaan na le mere dil ki haalat ko
kisi ko she'r sunata hun Darne lagta hun

dil hai alag mizāj ke do bhā.iyoñ kā ghar
lagtā hai sirf mujh ko ye tanhā.iyoñ kā ghar
beTī ga.ī hai ghar se lagā ham ko bas yahī
jaise chalā gayā koī amrā.iyoñ kā ghar
duurī banā lī un se yahī sochne ke baad
ghar un kā thā mire liye rusvā.iyoñ kā ghar
jab se milī hai un se nazar restaurant meñ
dil lag rahā hai pyaar kī shahnā.iyoñ kā ghar
dil hai alag mizaj ke do bhaiyon ka ghar
lagta hai sirf mujh ko ye tanhaiyon ka ghar
beTi gai hai ghar se laga hum ko bas yahi
jaise chala gaya koi amraiyon ka ghar
duri bana li un se yahi sochne ke baad
ghar un ka tha mere liye ruswaiyon ka ghar
jab se mili hai un se nazar restaurant mein
dil lag raha hai pyar ki shahnaiyon ka ghar

mushkil ko us ne sab kī āsān kar diyā hai
maujūdgī kā apnī e'lān kar diyā hai
baiThe hue haiñ patthar shīshoñ kā jism pahne
mahfil ne terī sab ko hairān kar diyā hai
itnī jagah kahāñ thī rakh paa.eñ saarī duniyā
kuchh is liye bhī dil ko vīrān kar diyā hai
hairān haiñ havā.eñ mausam bhī hai pareshāñ
jhoñke ko us ne kaise tūfān kar diyā hai
maiñ chaah ke bhī us ko shāyad na bhuul paatā
ai vaqt tū ne mujh par ehsān kar diyā hai
mushkil ko us ne sab ki aasan kar diya hai
maujudgi ka apni e'lan kar diya hai
baiThe hue hain patthar shishon ka jism pahne
mahfil ne teri sab ko hairan kar diya hai
itni jagah kahan thi rakh paen sari duniya
kuchh is liye bhi dil ko viran kar diya hai
hairan hain hawaen mausam bhi hai pareshan
jhonke ko us ne kaise tufan kar diya hai
main chah ke bhi us ko shayad na bhul pata
ai waqt tu ne mujh par ehsan kar diya hai

mujhe ye Dar hai ki ab bas yahī na kar baiThūñ
tirī ḳhushī meñ kahīñ ḳhud-kushī na kar baiThūñ
vo sun ke is liye mujh ko javāb detā nahīñ
savāl us se koī āḳhirī na kar baiThūñ
maiñ jis ko DhūñD rahā thā vo mil gayā mujh meñ
tamām shikve gile aaj hī na kar baiThūñ
har ek samt mujhe tū dikhā.ī detā hai
maiñ ek 'ishq ke pīchhe ka.ī na kar baiThūñ
baḌe jatan se banāyā hai us ne jis ko ḳhudā
kahīñ maiñ chhū ke use aadmī na kar baiThūñ
chale bhī aao ke ik roz ye bhī mumkin hai
tumhāre naam maiñ ye zindagī na kar baiThūñ
kuchh is liye bhī tavajjoh-talab ziyāda huuñ
jo kah rahā huuñ kahīñ vāqa'ī na kar baiThūñ
mujhe ye Dar hai ki ab bas yahi na kar baiThun
teri KHushi mein kahin KHud-kushi na kar baiThun
wo sun ke is liye mujh ko jawab deta nahin
sawal us se koi aaKHiri na kar baiThun
main jis ko DhunD raha tha wo mil gaya mujh mein
tamam shikwe gile aaj hi na kar baiThun
har ek samt mujhe tu dikhai deta hai
main ek 'ishq ke pichhe kai na kar baiThun
baDe jatan se banaya hai us ne jis ko KHuda
kahin main chhu ke use aadmi na kar baiThun
chale bhi aao ke ek roz ye bhi mumkin hai
tumhaare nam main ye zindagi na kar baiThun
kuchh is liye bhi tawajjoh-talab ziyaada hun
jo kah raha hun kahin waqa'i na kar baiThun

kamāl dekhiye sab kā yaqīñ jalāyā gayā
maiñ ik charāġh huuñ mujh ko nahīñ jalāyā gayā
ye sāneha bhī kisī buġhz kī alāmat hai
makān chhoḌ diyā aur makīñ jalāyā gayā
ḳhudā kā is se baḌā aur kyā karam hogā
jahāñ bujhāyā thā mujh ko vahīñ jalāyā gayā
use batānā havā se nahīñ jahāñ se bache
koī charāġh agar ab kahīñ jalāyā gayā
kamal dekhiye sab ka yaqin jalaya gaya
main ek charagh hun mujh ko nahin jalaya gaya
ye saneha bhi kisi bughz ki alamat hai
makan chhoD diya aur makin jalaya gaya
KHuda ka is se baDa aur kya karam hoga
jahan bujhaya tha mujh ko wahin jalaya gaya
use batana hawa se nahin jahan se bache
koi charagh agar ab kahin jalaya gaya

ummīd kā charāġh jalā kar chalā gayā
ik shaḳhs mere ḳhvāb meñ aa kar chalā gayā
us ke hī dam se naqsh-o-nigār-e-bahār hai
patthar meñ bhī jo phuul khilā kar chalā gayā
dīvār kī tarah maiñ tire rāste meñ thā
aur ret kī tarah tū girā kar chalā gayā
aaya thā kaun ḳhvāb meñ chingāriyāñ liye
nīñdoñ meñ merī aag lagā kar chalā gayā
yūñhī nahīñ huā huuñ maiñ patthar mire aziiz
ā.īna koī mujh ko dikhā kar chalā gayā
ummid ka charagh jala kar chala gaya
ek shaKHs mere KHwab mein aa kar chala gaya
us ke hi dam se naqsh-o-nigar-e-bahaar hai
patthar mein bhi jo phul khila kar chala gaya
diwar ki tarah main tere raste mein tha
aur ret ki tarah tu gira kar chala gaya
aaya tha kaun KHwab mein chingariyan liye
nindon mein meri aag laga kar chala gaya
yunhi nahin hua hun main patthar mere aziz
aaina koi mujh ko dikha kar chala gaya

tamām nekiyāñ dariyā meñ Dālne ke liye
nikal paḌe haiñ samundar khañgālne ke liye
sitam to ye hai ke tesha nahīñ milā ham ko
pahāḌ kaaT ke rastā nikālne ke liye
na jaane kitnoñ kī qīmat girā.ī jaatī hai
amīr-e-shahr kī qīmat uchhālne ke liye
ham aise logoñ ko laayā gayā hai duniyā meñ
kueñ meñ kuud ke sikka nikālne ke liye
kisī ke hijr kī ham aag piite rahte haiñ
sulagte lafzoñ ko ġhazloñ meñ Dhālne ke liye
zarā sañbhālnā aa jaa.e aadmī ko agar
to ek ġham hī bahut hai sañbhālne ke liye
tamam nekiyan dariya mein Dalne ke liye
nikal paDe hain samundar khangalne ke liye
sitam to ye hai ke tesha nahin mila hum ko
pahaD kaT ke rasta nikalne ke liye
na jaane kitnon ki qimat girai jati hai
amir-e-shahr ki qimat uchhaalne ke liye
hum aise logon ko laya gaya hai duniya mein
kuen mein kud ke sikka nikalne ke liye
kisi ke hijr ki hum aag pite rahte hain
sulagte lafzon ko ghazlon mein Dhaalne ke liye
zara sanbhaalna aa jae aadmi ko agar
to ek gham hi bahut hai sanbhaalne ke liye

suunā paḌā hai dil kā makāñ aap ke binā
rah rah ke uTh rahā hai dhuāñ aap ke binā
yuuñ to khile haiñ phuul ka.ī rañg ke magar
phīke paḌe haiñ donoñ jahāñ aap ke binā
ye soch ke maiñ ghuum rahā huuñ yahāñ vahāñ
rāhat milegī dil ko kahāñ aap ke binā
bas is liye hī gaañv se maiñ shahr aa basā
maiñ kyā karūñgā rah ke vahāñ aap ke binā
'ādarsh' kah rahā hai ki mat aao mere paas
barbād ho gayā huuñ yahāñ aap ke binā
suna paDa hai dil ka makan aap ke bina
rah rah ke uTh raha hai dhuan aap ke bina
yun to khile hain phul kai rang ke magar
phike paDe hain donon jahan aap ke bina
ye soch ke main ghum raha hun yahan wahan
rahat milegi dil ko kahan aap ke bina
bas is liye hi ganw se main shahr aa basa
main kya karunga rah ke wahan aap ke bina
'adarsh' kah raha hai ki mat aao mere pas
barbaad ho gaya hun yahan aap ke bina

ġhazal ke misra.a ko misra.a se joḌā jaatā hai
tamām raat ġhamoñ ko nichoḌā jaatā hai
purāne jaal se bāhar nikalnā mushkil hai
isī liye to rivāyat ko toḌā jaatā hai
utar gayā huuñ to ab jītnā hī manzil hai
yuuñ ham se bhī kahāñ maidān chhoḌā jaatā hai
uThānā paḌtā hai phir haath gar nahīñ sudhre
haañ pahlī baar meñ hāthoñ ko joḌā jaatā hai
yahāñ pe hindū bhī hoñge yahāñ musalmāñ bhī
ye shā.irī hai yahāñ sab ko joḌā jaatā hai
dikhā diyā mire dushman ne dostī kar ke
ġhurūr TuuTā nahīñ hai to toḌā jaatā hai
likhā thā naam jahāñ tū ne ḳhūn-e-dil se mirā
vahīñ se ishq ke kāġhaz ko moḌā jaatā hai
ghazal ke misra ko misra se joDa jata hai
tamam raat ghamon ko nichoDa jata hai
purane jal se bahar nikalna mushkil hai
isi liye to riwayat ko toDa jata hai
utar gaya hun to ab jitna hi manzil hai
yun hum se bhi kahan maidan chhoDa jata hai
uThana paDta hai phir hath gar nahin sudhre
han pahli bar mein hathon ko joDa jata hai
yahan pe hindu bhi honge yahan musalman bhi
ye shairi hai yahan sab ko joDa jata hai
dikha diya mere dushman ne dosti kar ke
ghurur TuTa nahin hai to toDa jata hai
likha tha nam jahan tu ne KHun-e-dil se mera
wahin se ishq ke kaghaz ko moDa jata hai

jaate jaate mujhe ḳhushī de dī
us ne āvāz āḳhirī de dī
jab sitāroñ ne pher lī āñkheñ
ek jugnū ne raushnī de dī
us ne inkār kar diyā merā
aur is ġham ne shā.erī de dī
zaḳhm bharne ko de diye aañsū
dard sahne ko bebasī de dī
us ne āñkhoñ se kah diyā sab kuchh
aur paḌhne ko diary de dī
jate jate mujhe KHushi de di
us ne aawaz aaKHiri de di
jab sitaron ne pher li aankhen
ek jugnu ne raushni de di
us ne inkar kar diya mera
aur is gham ne shaeri de di
zaKHm bharne ko de diye aansu
dard sahne ko bebasi de di
us ne aankhon se kah diya sab kuchh
aur paDhne ko diary de di

ḳhud mazedār tabī.at hai to sāmāñ kaisā
zaḳhm-e-dil aap haiñ shorish pe namak-dāñ kaisā
haath vahshat meñ na poñchhe to garebāñ kaisā
ḳhār-e-sahrā se na uljhe to vo dāmāñ kaisā
kūcha-e-yār ko da.avā hai ki jannat maiñ huuñ
ḳhuld kahte haiñ kise rauza-e-rizvāñ kaisā
usī ma.abūd kā hai dair-o-haram meñ jalva
bahs kis baat kī hai gabr o musalmāñ kaisā
va.ada-e-bāda-e-at.har kā bharosa kab tak
chal ke bhaTTī pe piyeñ jur.a-e-irfāñ kaisā
ham hue 'qais' hue 'vāmiq' o 'farhād' hue
zulf-e-pur-ḳham ne kiyā sab ko pareshāñ kaisā
duur ke Dhol haiñ yūsuf kī kahānī sāhab
kis ko ma.alūm hai hogā mah-e-kan.āñ kaisā
tere qurbān maiñ itnā to batā de qātil
merī gardan pe chalā ḳhanjar-e-burrāñ kaisā
dil ke ā.īne meñ tasvīr-e-sanam rakhtā hai
nahīñ ma.alūm ki 'āġhā' hai musalmāñ kaisā
KHud mazedar tabiat hai to saman kaisa
zaKHm-e-dil aap hain shorish pe namak-dan kaisa
hath wahshat mein na ponchhe to gareban kaisa
KHar-e-sahra se na uljhe to wo daman kaisa
kucha-e-yar ko dawa hai ki jannat main hun
KHuld kahte hain kise rauza-e-rizwan kaisa
usi mabud ka hai dair-o-haram mein jalwa
bahs kis baat ki hai gabr o musalman kaisa
wada-e-baada-e-athar ka bharosa kab tak
chal ke bhaTTi pe piyen jura-e-irfan kaisa
hum hue 'qais' hue 'wamiq' o 'farhad' hue
zulf-e-pur-KHam ne kiya sab ko pareshan kaisa
dur ke Dhol hain yusuf ki kahani sahab
kis ko malum hai hoga mah-e-kanan kaisa
tere qurban main itna to bata de qatil
meri gardan pe chala KHanjar-e-burran kaisa
dil ke aaine mein taswir-e-sanam rakhta hai
nahin malum ki 'agha' hai musalman kaisa

hazār jaan se sāhab nisār ham bhī haiñ
tumhārī tīr-e-nigah ke shikār ham bhī haiñ
azal se dāḳhil-e-fard-e-shumār ham bhī haiñ
tumhāre chāhne vāloñ meñ yaar ham bhī haiñ
hamesha ham se kudūrat rahī hasīnoñ ko
na dil se nikle kabhī vo ġhubār ham bhī haiñ
musāfiroñ kī tavāzo se naam hotā hai
karam karo ki ġharīb-ud-dayār ham bhī haiñ
sharāb piite haiñ to jāgte haiñ saarī raat
mudām ābid-e-shab-zinda-dār ham bhī haiñ
hazār baar hasīnoñ se ham ne nok kī lī
guloñ kī aañkh meñ khaTke vo ḳhaar ham bhī haiñ
ajiib rutba ināyat kiyā hai qambar ko
ġhulām yā shah-e-duldul-savār ham bhī haiñ
junūñ ke haath se hai in dinoñ garebāñ tañg
qabā pukārtī hai taar taar ham bhī haiñ
baḌe hī chāliye haiñ chaal chalte haiñ har dam
vo chūkte nahīñ par hoshiyār ham bhī haiñ
raqīb ko bhī hai baar un kī bazm meñ 'āġhā'
sharīk-e-sohbat-e-bos-o-kanār ham bhī haiñ
hazar jaan se sahab nisar hum bhi hain
tumhaari tir-e-nigah ke shikar hum bhi hain
azal se daKHil-e-fard-e-shumar hum bhi hain
tumhaare chahne walon mein yar hum bhi hain
hamesha hum se kudurat rahi hasinon ko
na dil se nikle kabhi wo ghubar hum bhi hain
musafiron ki tawazo se nam hota hai
karam karo ki gharib-ud-dayar hum bhi hain
sharab pite hain to jagte hain sari raat
mudam aabid-e-shab-zinda-dar hum bhi hain
hazar bar hasinon se hum ne nok ki li
gulon ki aankh mein khaTke wo KHar hum bhi hain
ajib rutba inayat kiya hai qambar ko
ghulam ya shah-e-duldul-sawar hum bhi hain
junun ke hath se hai in dinon gareban tang
qaba pukarti hai tar tar hum bhi hain
baDe hi chaaliye hain chaal chalte hain har dam
wo chukte nahin par hoshiyar hum bhi hain
raqib ko bhi hai bar un ki bazm mein 'agha'
sharik-e-sohbat-e-bos-o-kanar hum bhi hain

āñkhoñ pe vo zulf aa rahī hai
kaalī jaadū jagā rahī hai
zanjīr jo khaḌkhaḌā rahī hai
vahshat kyā ġhul machā rahī hai
lailā ḳhāka uḌā rahī hai
majnūñ ko havā batā rahī hai
zulfeñ vo parī hilā rahī hai
dīvānoñ kī shāmat aa rahī hai
pāmāl-e-ḳhirām ho chuke dafn
pisne ko bas ab hinā rahī hai
haiñ chaal se un kī zinda dargor
murdoñ pe qayāmat aa rahī hai
dil ne ulfat se zak uThā.ī
āñkhoñ dekhā rulā rahī hai
goyā hone de be-zabānī
kyuuñ merā galā dabā rahī hai
'āġhā' sāhab galī meñ un kī
ik huur tumheñ bulā rahī hai
aankhon pe wo zulf aa rahi hai
kali jadu jaga rahi hai
zanjir jo khaDkhaDa rahi hai
wahshat kya ghul macha rahi hai
laila KHaka uDa rahi hai
majnun ko hawa bata rahi hai
zulfen wo pari hila rahi hai
diwanon ki shamat aa rahi hai
pamal-e-KHiram ho chuke dafn
pisne ko bas ab hina rahi hai
hain chaal se un ki zinda dargor
murdon pe qayamat aa rahi hai
dil ne ulfat se zak uThai
aankhon dekha rula rahi hai
goya hone de be-zabani
kyun mera gala daba rahi hai
'agha' sahab gali mein un ki
ek hur tumhein bula rahi hai

but-e-ġhuncha-dahan pe nisār huuñ maiñ nahīñ jhuuT kuchh is meñ ḳhudā kī qasam
mirā tā.ir-e-dil isī qaid meñ hai mujhe zulf ke dām-e-balā kī qasam
nahīñ bhātā mujhe koī rashk-e-parī koī laakh hasīñ ho balā se mirī
mirā dil tirā āshiq-e-shefta hai mujhe tere hī nāz-o-adā kī qasam
mire dil ko zarā nahīñ tāb-o-ta.ab ki uThā.ūñ tumhārā ye qahr-o-ġhazab
mire qatl meñ der na chāhiye ab tumheñ apne hī jaur-o-jafā kī qasam
na to huur hī ko ye milā hai namak na parī hī ke ruḳh meñ hai aisī chamak
tire sāmne phīke haiñ shams-o-qamar mujhe tire hī ruḳh kī ziyā kī qasam
mujhe itr-e-hinā kī nahīñ hai havā mujhe phūloñ se hotā hai dāġh-e-sivā
kabhī nik.hat-e-zulf suñghā de sabā tujhe nāfa-e-mushk-e-ḳhatā kī qasam
mire ba.ad sahegā na koī bhī ġham na uThegā kisī se ye rañj-o-alam
karo tark tum aaj se zulm-o-sitam tumheñ apnī hī mehr-o-vafā kī qasam
kabhī dard se rotā ho 'āġhā' agar to hañsī se ye kahtā hai vo gul-e-tar
mirā maan kahā are naala na kar tujhe bulbul-e-naġhma-sarā kī qasam
but-e-ghuncha-dahan pe nisar hun main nahin jhuT kuchh is mein KHuda ki qasam
mera tair-e-dil isi qaid mein hai mujhe zulf ke dam-e-bala ki qasam
nahin bhata mujhe koi rashk-e-pari koi lakh hasin ho bala se meri
mera dil tera aashiq-e-shefta hai mujhe tere hi naz-o-ada ki qasam
mere dil ko zara nahin tab-o-tab ki uThaun tumhaara ye qahr-o-ghazab
mere qatl mein der na chahiye ab tumhein apne hi jaur-o-jafa ki qasam
na to hur hi ko ye mila hai namak na pari hi ke ruKH mein hai aisi chamak
tere samne phike hain shams-o-qamar mujhe tere hi ruKH ki ziya ki qasam
mujhe itr-e-hina ki nahin hai hawa mujhe phulon se hota hai dagh-e-siwa
kabhi nikhat-e-zulf sungha de saba tujhe nafa-e-mushk-e-KHata ki qasam
mere baad sahega na koi bhi gham na uThega kisi se ye ranj-o-alam
karo tark tum aaj se zulm-o-sitam tumhein apni hi mehr-o-wafa ki qasam
kabhi dard se rota ho 'agha' agar to hansi se ye kahta hai wo gul-e-tar
mera man kaha are nala na kar tujhe bulbul-e-naghma-sara ki qasam

tire jalāl se ḳhurshīd ko zavāl huā
tire jamāl se mahtāb ko kamāl huā
ḳhirām-e-nāz meñ un ko ye kab ḳhayāl huā
ki dil kisī kā pisā koī pā.emāl huā
shabāb se tirī rañgat kā turfa haal huā
sapīd joḌā jo pahnā badan meñ laal huā
jo vasl-e-yār kī tadbīr kī visāl huā
ḳhayāl aish kā aayā to ik malāl huā
hilāl badar huā badar se hilāl huā
yahāñ kamāl kisī kā na be-zavāl huā
hazāroñ saikḌoñ paidā hue hue nāpaid
na ek dam bhī zamāne ko e'tidāl huā
raqīb qatl huā us kī teġh-e-abrū se
harām-zāda thā achchhā huā halāl huā
butoñ kā zulm kisī ne sunā na mahshar meñ
ḳhudā se bhī mirā jhagḌā na infisāl huā
kiye haiñ ḳhuuñ se kisī ke ye dast-o-pā rañgīn
shikār taaza koī aaj kyā halāl huā
jalāyā mujh ko to tujh ko bhī lag gayā dhabba
jigar pe daaġh mire ruḳh pe tere ḳhaal huā
jo maiñ junūñ meñ gayā sū-e-dasht ai 'āġhā'
to mujh ko dekh ke dīvāna har ġhazāl huā
tere jalal se KHurshid ko zawal hua
tere jamal se mahtab ko kamal hua
KHiram-e-naz mein un ko ye kab KHayal hua
ki dil kisi ka pisa koi paemal hua
shabab se teri rangat ka turfa haal hua
sapid joDa jo pahna badan mein lal hua
jo wasl-e-yar ki tadbir ki visal hua
KHayal aish ka aaya to ek malal hua
hilal badar hua badar se hilal hua
yahan kamal kisi ka na be-zawal hua
hazaron saikDon paida hue hue napaid
na ek dam bhi zamane ko e'tidal hua
raqib qatl hua us ki tegh-e-abru se
haram-zada tha achchha hua halal hua
buton ka zulm kisi ne suna na mahshar mein
KHuda se bhi mera jhagDa na infisal hua
kiye hain KHun se kisi ke ye dast-o-pa rangin
shikar taza koi aaj kya halal hua
jalaya mujh ko to tujh ko bhi lag gaya dhabba
jigar pe dagh mere ruKH pe tere KHal hua
jo main junun mein gaya su-e-dasht ai 'agha'
to mujh ko dekh ke diwana har ghazal hua

dil meñ tire ai nigār kyā hai
hotā nahīñ ham-kanār kyā hai
aayā jo dam vo hai ġhanīmat
is ziist kā e'tibār kyā hai
haiñ seb se bhī vo chhātiyāñ saḳht
aage un ke anaar kyā hai
duniyā ke ye sab Dhakosle haiñ
turbat kaisī mazār kyā hai
tā.ūs se chheḌ-chhāḌ kaisī
haañ ai dil-e-dāġh-dār kyā hai
jo jo vo rañj deñ uThāo
jab dil hī diyā to aar kyā hai
maiñ chāhtā huuñ use na chāhūñ
dil par mirā iḳhtiyār kyā hai
mizhgāñ kā hai mere dil meñ khaTkā
ai ḳhushbū-e-nok-e-ḳhār kyā hai
miTTī mirī ḳhaak meñ milā.ī
mujh se un ko ġhubār kyā hai
dauḌūñ to mujhe sabā na paa.e
paidal kaisā savār kyā hai
bose kī talab ki vasl kā zikr
farmā.iye nāgavār kyā hai
hai kyā 'āġhā' taḌap rahā hai
kyuuñ kahte ho baar baar kyā hai
dil mein tere ai nigar kya hai
hota nahin ham-kanar kya hai
aaya jo dam wo hai ghanimat
is zist ka e'tibar kya hai
hain seb se bhi wo chhatiyan saKHt
aage un ke anar kya hai
duniya ke ye sab Dhakosle hain
turbat kaisi mazar kya hai
taus se chheD-chhaD kaisi
han ai dil-e-dagh-dar kya hai
jo jo wo ranj den uThao
jab dil hi diya to aar kya hai
main chahta hun use na chahun
dil par mera iKHtiyar kya hai
mizhgan ka hai mere dil mein khaTka
ai KHushbu-e-nok-e-KHar kya hai
miTTi meri KHak mein milai
mujh se un ko ghubar kya hai
dauDun to mujhe saba na pae
paidal kaisa sawar kya hai
bose ki talab ki wasl ka zikr
farmaiye nagawar kya hai
hai kya 'agha' taDap raha hai
kyun kahte ho bar bar kya hai

jā laḌī yaar se hamārī aañkh
dekho kar baiThī faujdārī aañkh
shoḳhiyāñ bhuul jaa.e āhū-e-chīñ
dekh paa.e agar tumhārī aañkh
laakh inkār mai-kashī se karo
kahīñ chhuptī bhī hai ḳhumārī aañkh
hovegā rañj yā ḳhushī hogī
kyuuñ phaḌakne lagī hamārī aañkh
jānib-e-dar nigāh-e-hasrat hai
kis kī kartī hai intizārī aañkh
kar ke iqrār ho gayā munkir
sāmne aa ke kis ne maarī aañkh
murġh-e-dil par nigāh hai un kī
aisī dekhī nahīñ shikārī aañkh
hai sitam nok-jhoñk chitvan meñ
laḌ rahī hai chhurī kaTārī aañkh
dil jigar donoñ ho ga.e majrūh
ban ga.ī hai chhurī kaTārī aañkh
koī dam meñ ubhārte haiñ use
us ne dekhā ki ham ne maarī aañkh
'āġhā' sāhab tumhāre dilbar kī
kyā rasīlī hai kyā hai pyārī aañkh
ja laDi yar se hamari aankh
dekho kar baiThi faujdari aankh
shoKHiyan bhul jae aahu-e-chin
dekh pae agar tumhaari aankh
lakh inkar mai-kashi se karo
kahin chhupti bhi hai KHumari aankh
howega ranj ya KHushi hogi
kyun phaDakne lagi hamari aankh
jaanib-e-dar nigah-e-hasrat hai
kis ki karti hai intizari aankh
kar ke iqrar ho gaya munkir
samne aa ke kis ne mari aankh
murgh-e-dil par nigah hai un ki
aisi dekhi nahin shikari aankh
hai sitam nok-jhonk chitwan mein
laD rahi hai chhuri kaTari aankh
dil jigar donon ho gae majruh
ban gai hai chhuri kaTari aankh
koi dam mein ubhaarte hain use
us ne dekha ki hum ne mari aankh
'agha' sahab tumhaare dilbar ki
kya rasili hai kya hai pyari aankh

sarv-qad lāla-ruḳh o ġhuncha-dahan yaad aayā
phir bahār aa.ī mujhe lutf-e-chaman yaad aayā
go ki thī saltanat-e-misr magar āḳhir-e-kār
is hukūmat pe bhī yūsuf ko vatan yaad aayā
rag-e-gul par hai kabhī aur kabhī ġhunche pe nigāh
baaġh meñ kis kī kamar kis kā dahan yaad aayā
safar-e-mulk-e-adam kī huī aisī ujlat
zād-e-rah kuchh na ba-juz gor-o-kafan yaad aayā
sohbat-e-lāla-ruḳhāñ ahd-e-shabāb-o-shab-e-vasl
mai-e-kohna jo milī dāġh-e-kuhan yaad aayā
jab se aayā hai nazar ye tirā husn-e-be-dāġh
kabk ko maah na bulbul ko chaman yaad aayā
tere saudā.ī ko phir josh huā vahshat kā
qaidī-e-zulf ko phir tauq-o-rasan yaad aayā
paan khā kar jo ugaal aap ne thūkā sāhab
jauharī mahv hue la.al-e-yaman yaad aayā
ba.ad muddat ke talab aap ne bande ko kiyā
shukr-sad-shukr maiñ ai mushfiq-e-man yaad aayā
fasl-e-gul aate hī 'āġhā' ne bhī vahshat kī lī
kaisī ye chaal chalā kis kā chalan yaad aayā
sarw-qad lala-ruKH o ghuncha-dahan yaad aaya
phir bahaar aai mujhe lutf-e-chaman yaad aaya
go ki thi saltanat-e-misr magar aaKHir-e-kar
is hukumat pe bhi yusuf ko watan yaad aaya
rag-e-gul par hai kabhi aur kabhi ghunche pe nigah
bagh mein kis ki kamar kis ka dahan yaad aaya
safar-e-mulk-e-adam ki hui aisi ujlat
zad-e-rah kuchh na ba-juz gor-o-kafan yaad aaya
sohbat-e-lala-ruKHan ahd-e-shabab-o-shab-e-wasl
mai-e-kohna jo mili dagh-e-kuhan yaad aaya
jab se aaya hai nazar ye tera husn-e-be-dagh
kabk ko mah na bulbul ko chaman yaad aaya
tere saudai ko phir josh hua wahshat ka
qaidi-e-zulf ko phir tauq-o-rasan yaad aaya
pan kha kar jo ugal aap ne thuka sahab
jauhari mahw hue lal-e-yaman yaad aaya
baad muddat ke talab aap ne bande ko kiya
shukr-sad-shukr main ai mushfiq-e-man yaad aaya
fasl-e-gul aate hi 'agha' ne bhi wahshat ki li
kaisi ye chaal chala kis ka chalan yaad aaya

namāz kaisī kahāñ kā roza abhī maiñ shaġhl-e-sharāb meñ huuñ
ḳhudā kī yaad aa.e kis tarah se butoñ ke qahr-o-itāb meñ huuñ
sharāb kā shaġhl ho rahā hai baġhal meñ paatā huuñ maiñ kisī ko
maiñ jāgtā huuñ ki so rahā huuñ ḳhayāl meñ huuñ ki ḳhvāb meñ huuñ
na chheḌ is vaqt mujh ko zāhid nahīñ ye mauqa.a hai guftugū kā
savār jaatā hai vo sharābī maiñ hāzir us kī rikāb meñ huuñ
kabhī sharābī kabhī namāzī kabhī huuñ maiñ rind-gāh zāhid
ḳhudā kā Dar hai butoñ kā khaTkā ajab tarah ke azaab meñ huuñ
qayāmat aane kā ḳhauf kaisā taraddud-o-fikr kyuuñ hai 'āġhā'
hisāb kyā koī mujh se legā batā to maiñ kis hisāb meñ huuñ
namaz kaisi kahan ka roza abhi main shaghl-e-sharab mein hun
KHuda ki yaad aae kis tarah se buton ke qahr-o-itab mein hun
sharab ka shaghl ho raha hai baghal mein pata hun main kisi ko
main jagta hun ki so raha hun KHayal mein hun ki KHwab mein hun
na chheD is waqt mujh ko zahid nahin ye mauqa hai guftugu ka
sawar jata hai wo sharabi main hazir us ki rikab mein hun
kabhi sharabi kabhi namazi kabhi hun main rind-gah zahid
KHuda ka Dar hai buton ka khaTka ajab tarah ke azab mein hun
qayamat aane ka KHauf kaisa taraddud-o-fikr kyun hai 'agha'
hisab kya koi mujh se lega bata to main kis hisab mein hun

nahīñ mumkin ki tire hukm se bāhar maiñ huuñ
ai sanam tābe-e-farmān-e-muqaddar maiñ huuñ
dil to hairān hai kyuuñ shashdar-o-muztar maiñ huuñ
ishq kahtā hai ki us parde ke andar maiñ huuñ
pairav-e-silsila-e-zulf-e-muambar maiñ huuñ
tauq se uzr na zanjīr se bāhar maiñ huuñ
āb-rū-e-sadaf o zīnat-e-gosh-e-mahbūb
durr-e-nāyāb jo sunte ho vo gauhar maiñ huuñ
ab subuk-dosh maiñ huuñ bojh gale kā Tal jaa.e
teġh-e-qātil se ilāhī kaheñ be-sar maiñ huuñ
tā.er-e-qibla-numā kā hai ishāra mujh se
naama pahuñchāne ko pardār kabūtar maiñ huuñ
aa.ī phir fasl-e-bahārī madad ai josh-e-junūñ
do qadam chal nahīñ saktā huuñ vo lāġhar maiñ huuñ
nutq kahtā hai ki iisā mirā dam bhartā hai
dahan-e-yār ko da.avā hai ki kausar maiñ huuñ
jaadū bar-haq hai to kāfir hai ayaañ rā-che-bayāñ
terā maarā huā ai chashm-e-fusūñ-gar maiñ huuñ
mohtasib ko bhī hidāyat karūñ mai-noshī kī
vā.izā terī jagah gar sar-e-mimbar maiñ huuñ
na unheñ merī shikāyat na mujhe un kā gila
na kudūrat unheñ mujh se na mukaddar maiñ huuñ
hairat-e-husn se ik sakta kā aalam dekhā
ā.īna muñh ko tire taktā hai shashdar maiñ huuñ
daur-e-farhād gayā ye hai zamāna merā
be-sutūñ ab to uThā.e hue sar par maiñ huuñ
āj-kal husn-e-javānī pe jo hai un ko ġhurūr
naaz kahtā hai ki andāz se bāhar maiñ huuñ
barq o sīmāb kā 'āġhā' na rahe nām-o-nishāñ
dil kī betābī se ik baar jo muztar maiñ huuñ
nahin mumkin ki tere hukm se bahar main hun
ai sanam tabe-e-farman-e-muqaddar main hun
dil to hairan hai kyun shashdar-o-muztar main hun
ishq kahta hai ki us parde ke andar main hun
pairaw-e-silsila-e-zulf-e-muambar main hun
tauq se uzr na zanjir se bahar main hun
aab-ru-e-sadaf o zinat-e-gosh-e-mahbub
durr-e-nayab jo sunte ho wo gauhar main hun
ab subuk-dosh main hun bojh gale ka Tal jae
tegh-e-qatil se ilahi kahen be-sar main hun
taer-e-qibla-numa ka hai ishaara mujh se
nama pahunchane ko pardar kabutar main hun
aai phir fasl-e-bahaari madad ai josh-e-junun
do qadam chal nahin sakta hun wo laghar main hun
nutq kahta hai ki isa mera dam bharta hai
dahan-e-yar ko dawa hai ki kausar main hun
jadu bar-haq hai to kafir hai ayan ra-che-bayan
tera mara hua ai chashm-e-fusun-gar main hun
mohtasib ko bhi hidayat karun mai-noshi ki
waiza teri jagah gar sar-e-mimbar main hun
na unhen meri shikayat na mujhe un ka gila
na kudurat unhen mujh se na mukaddar main hun
hairat-e-husn se ek sakta ka aalam dekha
aaina munh ko tere takta hai shashdar main hun
daur-e-farhad gaya ye hai zamana mera
be-sutun ab to uThae hue sar par main hun
aaj-kal husn-e-jawani pe jo hai un ko ghurur
naz kahta hai ki andaz se bahar main hun
barq o simab ka 'agha' na rahe nam-o-nishan
dil ki betabi se ek bar jo muztar main hun

jīte-jī ke āshnā haiñ phir kisī kā kaun hai
naam ke apne huā karte haiñ apnā kaun hai
jān-e-jāñ tere sivā rashk-e-masīhā kaun hai
maar kar Thokar jilā de mujh ko aisā kaun hai
ye siyah ḳhema hai kis kā is meñ lailā kaun hai
chamber-e-aflāk ke parde meñ baiThā kaun hai
ham na kahte the ki saudā zulf kā achchhā nahīñ
dekhiye to ab sar-e-bāzār rusvā kaun hai
vo to hai be-nūr aur ye nuur se mā'mūr hai
chashm ko nargis kahegā aisā andhā kaun hai
dam-ba-dam har baat meñ karte ho ThanDī garmiyāñ
aap kī ukhḌī huī bātoñ pe jamtā kaun hai
vādī-e-vahshat meñ bhī ham-rāh haiñ āh-o-fuġhāñ
apne hamdam saath haiñ ai jaan tanhā kaun hai
ḳhair hai ai mehrbāñ kis ne unheñ sīdhā kyā
aap kyuuñ bal karte haiñ zulfoñ se uljhā kaun hai
duḳhtar-e-raz sach batā terī nazar kis par paḌī
TaTTiyoñ kī aaḌ meñ se kis ko taakā kaun hai
aaj maqtal meñ khaḌe kahte haiñ vo ḳhanjar-ba-kaf
bol uTThe chāhne vaalā hamārā kaun hai
chaar din jo kuchh tamāshā dekhnā hai dekh le
sair ko phir gulshan-e-duniyā meñ aatā kaun hai
bāñdh kar teġh o kafan jaate haiñ us qātil ke paas
ham bhī dekheñ rokne vaalā hamārā kaun hai
kyā tajāhul hai ki vo farmāte haiñ aġhyār se
maiñ nahīñ pahchāntā mutlaq ki 'āġhā' kaun hai
jite-ji ke aashna hain phir kisi ka kaun hai
nam ke apne hua karte hain apna kaun hai
jaan-e-jaan tere siwa rashk-e-masiha kaun hai
mar kar Thokar jila de mujh ko aisa kaun hai
ye siyah KHema hai kis ka is mein laila kaun hai
chamber-e-aflak ke parde mein baiTha kaun hai
hum na kahte the ki sauda zulf ka achchha nahin
dekhiye to ab sar-e-bazar ruswa kaun hai
wo to hai be-nur aur ye nur se ma'mur hai
chashm ko nargis kahega aisa andha kaun hai
dam-ba-dam har baat mein karte ho ThanDi garmiyan
aap ki ukhDi hui baaton pe jamta kaun hai
wadi-e-wahshat mein bhi ham-rah hain aah-o-fughan
apne hamdam sath hain ai jaan tanha kaun hai
KHair hai ai mehrban kis ne unhen sidha kya
aap kyun bal karte hain zulfon se uljha kaun hai
duKHtar-e-raz sach bata teri nazar kis par paDi
TaTTiyon ki aaD mein se kis ko taka kaun hai
aaj maqtal mein khaDe kahte hain wo KHanjar-ba-kaf
bol uTThe chahne wala hamara kaun hai
chaar din jo kuchh tamasha dekhna hai dekh le
sair ko phir gulshan-e-duniya mein aata kaun hai
bandh kar tegh o kafan jate hain us qatil ke pas
hum bhi dekhen rokne wala hamara kaun hai
kya tajahul hai ki wo farmate hain aghyar se
main nahin pahchanta mutlaq ki 'agha' kaun hai

nigāhoñ meñ iqrār saare hue haiñ
ham un ke hue vo hamāre hue haiñ
jin āñkhoñ meñ aañsū chakāre hue haiñ
ham un kī nigāhoñ ke maare hue haiñ
na ḳhaTkeñ kaho kis tarah tīr-e-mizhgāñ
jigar par hamāre utāre hue haiñ
jhaḌe jo tirī kafsh-e-zarrīñ ke zarre
falak par vo jā kar sayyāre hue haiñ
'abas jaan detī hai bulbul guloñ par
ye us ruḳh ke sadqe utāre hue haiñ
kis andāz se band-e-mahram kase haiñ
ki joban ko un ke ubhāre hue haiñ
yaqīñ hai balā ho koī aaj nāzil
vo bāloñ ko apne sañvāre hue haiñ
ḳhabar-dār hāthoñ se jaane na paa.eñ
ye duzd-e-hinā maal maare hue haiñ
kahe detī haiñ saaf āñkheñ tumhārī
kisī ġhair se kuchh ishāre hue haiñ
maiñ mañjdhār meñ Dūbtā huuñ ilāhī
vo dil le ke merā kināre hue haiñ
hamesha jo bharte the dam dostī kā
vahī dushman-e-jāñ hamāre hue haiñ
nazar kar du'ā par ḳhudāvand-e-ālam
ki ham haath apne pasāre hue haiñ
bhalā ġhair kī is meñ hai kyā shikāyat
vahī dushman-e-jāñ hamāre hue haiñ
unheñ ham ne nahlā diyā de ke chhīñTeñ
'ajab lutf dariyā kināre hue haiñ
ḳhabar āmad-e-gul kī shāyad hai 'āġhā'
chaman saare jhāḌe bahāre hue haiñ
nigahon mein iqrar sare hue hain
hum un ke hue wo hamare hue hain
jin aankhon mein aansu chakare hue hain
hum un ki nigahon ke mare hue hain
na KHaTken kaho kis tarah tir-e-mizhgan
jigar par hamare utare hue hain
jhaDe jo teri kafsh-e-zarrin ke zarre
falak par wo ja kar sayyare hue hain
'abas jaan deti hai bulbul gulon par
ye us ruKH ke sadqe utare hue hain
kis andaz se band-e-mahram kase hain
ki joban ko un ke ubhaare hue hain
yaqin hai bala ho koi aaj nazil
wo baalon ko apne sanware hue hain
KHabar-dar hathon se jaane na paen
ye duzd-e-hina mal mare hue hain
kahe deti hain saf aankhen tumhaari
kisi ghair se kuchh ishaare hue hain
main manjdhaar mein Dubta hun ilahi
wo dil le ke mera kinare hue hain
hamesha jo bharte the dam dosti ka
wahi dushman-e-jaan hamare hue hain
nazar kar du'a par KHudawand-e-alam
ki hum hath apne pasare hue hain
bhala ghair ki is mein hai kya shikayat
wahi dushman-e-jaan hamare hue hain
unhen hum ne nahla diya de ke chhinTen
'ajab lutf dariya kinare hue hain
KHabar aamad-e-gul ki shayad hai 'agha'
chaman sare jhaDe bahaare hue hain

hamāre sāmne kuchh zikr ġhairoñ kā agar hogā
bashar haiñ ham bhī sāhab dekhiye nāhaq kā shar hogā
na muḌ kar tū ne dekhā aur na maiñ taḌpā na ḳhanjar
na dil hovegā terā sā na merā sā jigar hogā
maiñ kuchh majnūñ nahīñ huuñ jo ki sahrā ko chalā jā.ūñ
tumhāre dar se sar phoḌūñgā saudā bhī agar hogā
chaman meñ laa.ī hogī to sabā-mashshātgī kar ke
jo gul se aage lipTā hai kisī bulbul kā par hogā
tarī kā bhī vahī mālik hai jo mālik hai ḳhushkī kā
madad-gār apnā har mushkil meñ shāh-e-bahr-o-bar hogā
tasavvur zulf kā gar chhoḌ duuñ mizhgāñ kā khaTkā hai
jo sar ke dard se fursat milī dard-e-jigar hogā
tabībo tum abas aa.e maiñ kushta huuñ firañgan kā
mirī tadbīr karne ko muqarrar doctor hogā
kisī ko koste kyuuñ ho duā apne liye māñgo
tumhārā fā.eda kyā hai jo dushman kā zarar hogā
mazā aa.egā dīvānoñ kī bātoñ meñ parī-zādo
jo 'āġhā' kā kisī din dasht-e-majnūñ meñ guzar hogā
hamare samne kuchh zikr ghairon ka agar hoga
bashar hain hum bhi sahab dekhiye nahaq ka shar hoga
na muD kar tu ne dekha aur na main taDpa na KHanjar
na dil howega tera sa na mera sa jigar hoga
main kuchh majnun nahin hun jo ki sahra ko chala jaun
tumhaare dar se sar phoDunga sauda bhi agar hoga
chaman mein lai hogi to saba-mashshatgi kar ke
jo gul se aage lipTa hai kisi bulbul ka par hoga
tari ka bhi wahi malik hai jo malik hai KHushki ka
madad-gar apna har mushkil mein shah-e-bahr-o-bar hoga
tasawwur zulf ka gar chhoD dun mizhgan ka khaTka hai
jo sar ke dard se fursat mili dard-e-jigar hoga
tabibo tum abas aae main kushta hun firangan ka
meri tadbir karne ko muqarrar doctor hoga
kisi ko koste kyun ho dua apne liye mango
tumhaara faeda kya hai jo dushman ka zarar hoga
maza aaega diwanon ki baaton mein pari-zado
jo 'agha' ka kisi din dasht-e-majnun mein guzar hoga

malte haiñ hāth, haath lageñge anaar kab
joban kā un ke dekhiye hogā ubhār kab
ushshāq muntazir haiñ qayāmat kab aa.egī
be-parda muñh dikhā.egā vo parda-dār kab
ik roz apnī jaan pe ham khel jā.eñge
tum pūchhte rahoge yūñhī baar baar kab
bekas ko kaun ro.e ġharīboñ kā kaun hai
merī lahad pe sham.a huī ashk-bār kab
kaun aayā paḌhte fātiha kis ne chaḌhā.e phuul
marne ke ba.ad pūchhtā hai koī yaar kab
ummīd nā-umīd ko un se nahīñ rahī
dushman ke dost haiñ vo hue mere yaar kab
jo ūñche ūñche haiñ vahī jaate haiñ baam par
mahfil meñ ham ġharīboñ ko miltā hai yaar kab
jab naqd maal tū ne diyā ham ne naqd-e-dil
saaqī hameñ batā de ki pī thī udhār kab
milnā chhuḌāyā tum se mirā rashk-e-ġhair ne
kartā hai koī aap se jabr iḳhtiyār kab
'āġhā' ko zab.h karte ho apnī galī meñ kyuuñ
jaa.ez hai merī jaan haram meñ shikār kab
malte hain hath, hath lagenge anar kab
joban ka un ke dekhiye hoga ubhaar kab
ushshaq muntazir hain qayamat kab aaegi
be-parda munh dikhaega wo parda-dar kab
ek roz apni jaan pe hum khel jaenge
tum puchhte rahoge yunhi bar bar kab
bekas ko kaun roe gharibon ka kaun hai
meri lahad pe shama hui ashk-bar kab
kaun aaya paDhte fatiha kis ne chaDhae phul
marne ke baad puchhta hai koi yar kab
ummid na-umid ko un se nahin rahi
dushman ke dost hain wo hue mere yar kab
jo unche unche hain wahi jate hain baam par
mahfil mein hum gharibon ko milta hai yar kab
jab naqd mal tu ne diya hum ne naqd-e-dil
saqi hamein bata de ki pi thi udhaar kab
milna chhuDaya tum se mera rashk-e-ghair ne
karta hai koi aap se jabr iKHtiyar kab
'agha' ko zabh karte ho apni gali mein kyun
jaez hai meri jaan haram mein shikar kab

kyā banā.e sāne-e-qudrat ne pyāre haath paañv
nuur ke sāñche meñ Dhāle haiñ tumhāre haath paañv
zo.af-e-pīrī chhā gayā zor-e-javānī chal basā
ab chaleñ batlā.īye kis ke sahāre haath paañv
machhliyāñ baazū pe ubhrīñ sāq-e-pā sham.eñ banīñ
ḳhuub sāhab ne nikāle ab to baare haath paañv
fauq hiire se nahīñ hai merī jaañ yāqūt ko
kyuuñ rañge haiñ aap ne mehñdī se saare haath paañv
mānī-o-bahzād ne mulk-e-adam kī raah lī
vo kamar mutlaq na paa.ī laakh maare haath paañv
ham na kahte the ki har dam shoḳhiyāñ achchhī nahīñ
āḳhirash mehñdī ne bāñdhe lo tumhāre haath paañv
hāthā-pā.ī meñ bhī ham chūke na apne kaam se
vasl kī shab yaar ne kyā kyā na maare haath paañv
hai za.īfī meñ bhī ham ko naujavānī kā ḳhayāl
dil nahīñ haarā hai ab tak go ki haare haath paañv
ġhair kī dhamkī se ham Dar jaa.eñ ye mumkin nahīñ
aise buude bhī nahīñ haiñ kuchh hamāre haath paañv
ma.adan-e-yāqūt ko dariyā banāyā aap ne
mehñdī mal kar dho.e jab dariyā kināre haath paañv
is buḌhāpe meñ bhī 'āġhā' so javāñ meñ ek hai
go za.īfī aa ga.ī par haiñ karāre haath paañv
kya banae sane-e-qudrat ne pyare hath panw
nur ke sanche mein Dhaale hain tumhaare hath panw
zoaf-e-piri chha gaya zor-e-jawani chal basa
ab chalen batlaiye kis ke sahaare hath panw
machhliyan bazu pe ubhrin saq-e-pa shamen banin
KHub sahab ne nikale ab to bare hath panw
fauq hire se nahin hai meri jaan yaqut ko
kyun range hain aap ne mehndi se sare hath panw
mani-o-bahzad ne mulk-e-adam ki rah li
wo kamar mutlaq na pai lakh mare hath panw
hum na kahte the ki har dam shoKHiyan achchhi nahin
aaKHirash mehndi ne bandhe lo tumhaare hath panw
hatha-pai mein bhi hum chuke na apne kaam se
wasl ki shab yar ne kya kya na mare hath panw
hai zaifi mein bhi hum ko naujawani ka KHayal
dil nahin haara hai ab tak go ki haare hath panw
ghair ki dhamki se hum Dar jaen ye mumkin nahin
aise bude bhi nahin hain kuchh hamare hath panw
madan-e-yaqut ko dariya banaya aap ne
mehndi mal kar dhoe jab dariya kinare hath panw
is buDhape mein bhi 'agha' so jawan mein ek hai
go zaifi aa gai par hain karare hath panw

shiddat-e-zāt ne ye haal banāyā apnā
jism-e-majnūñ meñ huā tañg shalokā apnā
yaar bantā nahīñ vo nuur kā putlā apnā
ḳhaak meñ mil gayā tasḳhīr kā da.avā apnā
mai-kashoñ meñ na koī mujh sā namāzī hogā
dar-e-mai-ḳhāna pe bichhtā hai musallā apnā
vasl kī raat bahut tuul huā āḳhir-kār
muḳhtasar ye hai ki faisal huā qissa apnā
gul khilā kar abhī bulbul ko jalā.ūñ kyā kyā
vo ināyat kareñ gar por kā chhallā apnā
rabbī-arenī kī sadā ho bhī to but bol uTheñ
aap dikhlā.eñ agar dair meñ jalva apnā
ā.īna-ḳhāna meñ chal baiThiye do-chār ghaḌī
dekhnā hove jo manzūr tamāshā apnā
jīte-jī ḳhvesh-o-aqārib the pas-e-marg afsos
ḳhaak meñ daab diyā koī na samjhā apnā
kisī sayyād kī paḌ jaa.e na chiḌiyā pe nazar
aap sarkā.eñ na mahram se dupaTTā apnā
aap sau baar ukhaḌ jaa.eñ nahīñ kuchh parvā
jam gayā ek parī-zād se naqsha apnā
dām-e-mahram meñ phañsāyā hai ḳhudā ḳhair kare
āshiyāna na banā baiThe ye chiḌiyā apnā
garm-ḳhvābī ne tirī zab.h kiyā ai qātil
ek dam bhī na kalejā huā ThanDā apnā
riñd-mashrab haiñ kisī se hameñ kuchh kaam nahīñ
dair apnā hai na ka.aba na kalīsā apnā
hai vahī sar vahī saudā vahī josh-e-vahshat
vasl tabdīl huī rañg na badlā apnā
un kī zulfoñ ko ye da.avā hai ki ham kaale haiñ
ham ne bachte nahīñ dekhā kabhī maarā apnā
ġhair se rakhiye na imdād kī ummīd 'āġhā'
kaam aatā hai mirī jaan bharosā apnā
shiddat-e-zat ne ye haal banaya apna
jism-e-majnun mein hua tang shaloka apna
yar banta nahin wo nur ka putla apna
KHak mein mil gaya tasKHir ka dawa apna
mai-kashon mein na koi mujh sa namazi hoga
dar-e-mai-KHana pe bichhta hai musalla apna
wasl ki raat bahut tul hua aaKHir-kar
muKHtasar ye hai ki faisal hua qissa apna
gul khila kar abhi bulbul ko jalaun kya kya
wo inayat karen gar por ka chhalla apna
rabbi-areni ki sada ho bhi to but bol uThen
aap dikhlaen agar dair mein jalwa apna
aaina-KHana mein chal baiThiye do-chaar ghaDi
dekhna howe jo manzur tamasha apna
jite-ji KHwesh-o-aqarib the pas-e-marg afsos
KHak mein dab diya koi na samjha apna
kisi sayyaad ki paD jae na chiDiya pe nazar
aap sarkaen na mahram se dupaTTa apna
aap sau bar ukhaD jaen nahin kuchh parwa
jam gaya ek pari-zad se naqsha apna
dam-e-mahram mein phansaya hai KHuda KHair kare
aashiyana na bana baiThe ye chiDiya apna
garm-KHwabi ne teri zabh kiya ai qatil
ek dam bhi na kaleja hua ThanDa apna
rind-mashrab hain kisi se hamein kuchh kaam nahin
dair apna hai na kaba na kalisa apna
hai wahi sar wahi sauda wahi josh-e-wahshat
wasl tabdil hui rang na badla apna
un ki zulfon ko ye dawa hai ki hum kale hain
hum ne bachte nahin dekha kabhi mara apna
ghair se rakhiye na imdad ki ummid 'agha'
kaam aata hai meri jaan bharosa apna

daur sāġhar kā chale saaqī dobārā ek aur
abr kā'ba se uThā hai maan kahnā ek aur
jhūmtā aatā hai vo bādal kā TukḌā ek aur
sāqiyā bhar kar pilā de jām-e-sahbā ek aur
din ko jo kuchh tum ne dekhā ye to thī sab dil-lagī
shab ko rah jaao to dikhlā.eñ tamāshā ek aur
maiñ unheñ kahtā huuñ tum bedard ho nā-āshnā
vo lagāte haiñ mujhe ilzām ulTā ek aur
dil ko nafrat ho ga.ī nazroñ se āḳhir gir ga.e
tum se behtar apnī āñkhoñ meñ samāyā ek aur
kyuuñ sisaktā chhoḌe jaate ho mujhe maqtal meñ tum
faisla kar duuñ maiñ qurbāñ de ke charkā ek aur
tere aane meñ tavaqquf jab huā ai nāma-bar
ḳhat unheñ bechain ho kar ham ne likkhā ek aur
band mahram ke khule kuchh be-hijābī ho chukī
vo bhī ab uTh jaa.e jo baaqī hai pardā ek aur
dost dushman ho ga.e yāroñ ne āñkheñ pher liiñ
rah gayā hai aap kā mujh ko bharosā ek aur
vasl kī shab meñ kiyā murġh-e-sahar kā band-o-bast
na.ara-e-allāhu-akbar kā hai dhaḌkā ek aur
ho chukā zikr-e-dahan vasf-e-kamar likhte haiñ ham
daam meñ sayyād ke phañstā hai anqā ek aur
said kī kasrat se 'āġhā' ban paḌī sayyād kī
do ne gar paa.ī rihā.ī aa ke uljhā ek aur
daur saghar ka chale saqi dobara ek aur
abr ka'ba se uTha hai man kahna ek aur
jhumta aata hai wo baadal ka TukDa ek aur
saqiya bhar kar pila de jam-e-sahba ek aur
din ko jo kuchh tum ne dekha ye to thi sab dil-lagi
shab ko rah jao to dikhlaen tamasha ek aur
main unhen kahta hun tum bedard ho na-ashna
wo lagate hain mujhe ilzam ulTa ek aur
dil ko nafrat ho gai nazron se aaKHir gir gae
tum se behtar apni aankhon mein samaya ek aur
kyun sisakta chhoDe jate ho mujhe maqtal mein tum
faisla kar dun main qurban de ke charka ek aur
tere aane mein tawaqquf jab hua ai nama-bar
KHat unhen bechain ho kar hum ne likkha ek aur
band mahram ke khule kuchh be-hijabi ho chuki
wo bhi ab uTh jae jo baqi hai parda ek aur
dost dushman ho gae yaron ne aankhen pher lin
rah gaya hai aap ka mujh ko bharosa ek aur
wasl ki shab mein kiya murgh-e-sahar ka band-o-bast
nara-e-allahu-akbar ka hai dhaDka ek aur
ho chuka zikr-e-dahan wasf-e-kamar likhte hain hum
dam mein sayyaad ke phansta hai anqa ek aur
said ki kasrat se 'agha' ban paDi sayyaad ki
do ne gar pai rihai aa ke uljha ek aur

sikka-e-dāġh-e-junūñ milte jo daulat māñgtā
tañg kartī muflisī gar maiñ farāġhat māñgtā
rañj se fursat na miltī maiñ jo rāhat māñgtā
bojh hotā sar pe gar qārūñ kī daulat māñgtā
gar mujhe hotī ḳhabar merā masīhā aa.egā
ai ajal ik dam kī maiñ bhī tujh se mohlat māñgtā
ḳhizr kī sī zindagī hotī jo mujh nākām kī
maiñ duā-e-vasl-e-jānāñ tā-qayāmat māñgtā
ashk ke dariyā ne rakh lī aabrū ai chashm-e-tar
marte dam do gaz zamīn kyā bahr-e-turbat māñgtā
kis kī aamad aamad apne kalba-e-ahzāñ meñ hai
peshvā.ī ko hai dil pahlū se ruḳhsat māñgtā
dar-guzartā jaan tak kartā zamīñ us se aziiz
mujh se darbān-e-dar-e-jānāñ jo rishvat māñgtā
naza.a tak dīdār kī hasrat rahī mushtāq ko
ai masīhā mar gayā bīmār sharbat māñgtā
dar-ba-dar phirne ne merī qadr khoī ai falak
un ke dil meñ hai jagah miltī jo ḳhalvat māñgtā
minnateñ kar ke chhuḌātā bulbuloñ ko daam se
maiñ zar-e-gul detā agar sayyād qīmat māñgtā
ādamiyyat se haiñ duur in zāhidoñ ke qaul-o-fe.al
haqq-e-maurūsī thā merā kyuuñ maiñ jannat māñgtā
jaan dī nāhaq ko makkāra ke dam meñ aan kar
kohkan shīrīñ se mehnat kī jo ujrat māñgtā
qasd kartā gar bulandī kā to pastī dekhtā
kund ho jaatī tabī.at gar maiñ jaudat māñgtā
zulf ke janjāl meñ phañsne kī ḳhud kartā duā
maiñ siḌī thā jo ḳhudā se apnī shāmat māñgtā
qaa.el apnī guftugū se ḳhaas kā hotā kalīm
'sa.adī'-e-shīrāz bhī mujh se fasāhat māñgtā
yaar hotā baaġh hotā aise gar hote nasīb
mai-kashī kī mohtasib se maiñ ijāzat māñgtā
dasht-e-vahshat-ḳhez meñ uryāñ hai 'āġhā' aap hī
qāsid-e-jānāñ ko kyā detā jo ḳhil.at māñgtā
sikka-e-dagh-e-junun milte jo daulat mangta
tang karti muflisi gar main faraghat mangta
ranj se fursat na milti main jo rahat mangta
bojh hota sar pe gar qarun ki daulat mangta
gar mujhe hoti KHabar mera masiha aaega
ai ajal ek dam ki main bhi tujh se mohlat mangta
KHizr ki si zindagi hoti jo mujh nakaam ki
main dua-e-wasl-e-jaanan ta-qayamat mangta
ashk ke dariya ne rakh li aabru ai chashm-e-tar
marte dam do gaz zamin kya bahr-e-turbat mangta
kis ki aamad aamad apne kalba-e-ahzan mein hai
peshwai ko hai dil pahlu se ruKHsat mangta
dar-guzarta jaan tak karta zamin us se aziz
mujh se darban-e-dar-e-jaanan jo rishwat mangta
naza tak didar ki hasrat rahi mushtaq ko
ai masiha mar gaya bimar sharbat mangta
dar-ba-dar phirne ne meri qadr khoi ai falak
un ke dil mein hai jagah milti jo KHalwat mangta
minnaten kar ke chhuData bulbulon ko dam se
main zar-e-gul deta agar sayyaad qimat mangta
aadamiyyat se hain dur in zahidon ke qaul-o-feal
haqq-e-maurusi tha mera kyun main jannat mangta
jaan di nahaq ko makkara ke dam mein aan kar
kohkan shirin se mehnat ki jo ujrat mangta
qasd karta gar bulandi ka to pasti dekhta
kund ho jati tabiat gar main jaudat mangta
zulf ke janjal mein phansne ki KHud karta dua
main siDi tha jo KHuda se apni shamat mangta
qael apni guftugu se KHas ka hota kalim
'sadi'-e-shiraaz bhi mujh se fasahat mangta
yar hota bagh hota aise gar hote nasib
mai-kashi ki mohtasib se main ijazat mangta
dasht-e-wahshat-KHez mein uryan hai 'agha' aap hi
qasid-e-jaanan ko kya deta jo KHilat mangta

mazā hai imtihāñ kā aazmā le jis kā jī chāhe
namak zaḳhm-e-jigar par aur Daale jis kā jī chāhe
jigar maujūd hai to vo banā le jis kā jī chāhe
galā hāzir hai ḳhanjar aazmā le jis kā jī chāhe
agar hai husn kā da.avā mah o ḳhurshīd donoñ meñ
kaf-e-pā se tumhāre muñh milā le jis kā jī chāhe
ye musht-e-ustuḳhvāñ apne kisī ke kaam meñ aa.eñ
humā ho yā sag-e-dildār khā le jis kā jī chāhe
agar hai zindagī baaqī to ham hasrat nikāleñge
dil-e-pur-ārzū par ḳhaak Daale jis kā jī chāhe
faqīroñ ko nahīñ kuchh zīnat-e-duniyā se matlab hai
maiñ ḳhush kambal meñ huuñ oḌhe doshāle jis kā jī chāhe
jo raushan dil meñ un kī raushnī chhuptī nahīñ hargiz
mah-e-tābāñ pe sāhab ḳhaak Daale jis kā jī chāhe
shikāyat mujh ko donoñ se hai nāseh ho ki vaa.iz ho
na samjhā huuñ na samjhūñ sar phirā le jis kā jī chāhe
maiñ huuñ barg-e-ḳhizāñ-uftāda maiñ mardūd dahqāñ huuñ
girā huuñ un kī nazroñ se uThā le jis kā jī chāhe
nahīñ hotā kabhī āb-e-ravāñ par shak najāsat kā
mire ashkoñ ke dariyā meñ nahā le jis kā jī chāhe
chaman meñ gul ke murjhāne se 'āġhā' ho gayā sābit
bisān-e-ġhuncha dam bhar muskurā le jis kā jī chāhe
maza hai imtihan ka aazma le jis ka ji chahe
namak zaKHm-e-jigar par aur Dale jis ka ji chahe
jigar maujud hai to wo bana le jis ka ji chahe
gala hazir hai KHanjar aazma le jis ka ji chahe
agar hai husn ka dawa mah o KHurshid donon mein
kaf-e-pa se tumhaare munh mila le jis ka ji chahe
ye musht-e-ustuKHwan apne kisi ke kaam mein aaen
huma ho ya sag-e-dildar kha le jis ka ji chahe
agar hai zindagi baqi to hum hasrat nikalenge
dil-e-pur-arzu par KHak Dale jis ka ji chahe
faqiron ko nahin kuchh zinat-e-duniya se matlab hai
main KHush kambal mein hun oDhe doshaale jis ka ji chahe
jo raushan dil mein un ki raushni chhupti nahin hargiz
mah-e-taban pe sahab KHak Dale jis ka ji chahe
shikayat mujh ko donon se hai naseh ho ki waiz ho
na samjha hun na samjhun sar phira le jis ka ji chahe
main hun barg-e-KHizan-uftada main mardud dahqan hun
gira hun un ki nazron se uTha le jis ka ji chahe
nahin hota kabhi aab-e-rawan par shak najasat ka
mere ashkon ke dariya mein naha le jis ka ji chahe
chaman mein gul ke murjhane se 'agha' ho gaya sabit
bisan-e-ghuncha dam bhar muskura le jis ka ji chahe

vo kahte haiñ uTTho sahar ho ga.ī
azaañ ho ga.ī top-sar ho ga.ī
gale se milo ab to bahr-e-ḳhudā
taḌapte mujhe raat bhar ho ga.ī
ilāhī huā jazb-e-ulfat ko kyā
mirī aah kyuuñ be-asar ho ga.ī
zamāna to ai jaan bargashta thā
tumhārī bhī tirchhī nazar ho ga.ī
hue sar kaTāne ko tayyār ham
jo vaañ teġh zeb-e-kamar ho ga.ī
dikhā.ī mujhe kis liye shām-e-hijr
shab-e-vasl kī kyuuñ sahar ho ga.ī
milā vasl meñ bhī na 'āġhā' ko chain
shikāyat meñ shab bhar basar ho ga.ī
wo kahte hain uTTho sahar ho gai
azan ho gai top-sar ho gai
gale se milo ab to bahr-e-KHuda
taDapte mujhe raat bhar ho gai
ilahi hua jazb-e-ulfat ko kya
meri aah kyun be-asar ho gai
zamana to ai jaan bargashta tha
tumhaari bhi tirchhi nazar ho gai
hue sar kaTane ko tayyar hum
jo wan tegh zeb-e-kamar ho gai
dikhai mujhe kis liye sham-e-hijr
shab-e-wasl ki kyun sahar ho gai
mila wasl mein bhi na 'agha' ko chain
shikayat mein shab bhar basar ho gai

paañv phir hoveñge aur dasht-e-muġhīlāñ hogā
haath phir hoveñge aur apnā garebāñ hogā
dil-e-vahshī tū na kar ishq pareshāñ hogā
misl ā.īna ke phir shashdar-o-hairāñ hogā
gar yahī ishq kā āġhāz hai to sun lenā
laash hovegī mirī kūcha-e-jānāñ hogā
Duub kar marne kā shauq us se hī pūchh ai qātil
jis ne dekhā ye tirā chāh-e-zanaḳhdāñ hogā
kahtī thī daam meñ sayyād ke ro kar bulbul
ab kabhī ham ko mayassar na gulistāñ hogā
jitne duniyā meñ sitam chāhe tū kar le mujh par
hashr meñ haath mirā terā garebāñ hogā
jaan de baiThegā ik roz tū us par 'āġhā'
vo nahīñ haal kā tere kabhī pursāñ hogā
panw phir howenge aur dasht-e-mughilan hoga
hath phir howenge aur apna gareban hoga
dil-e-wahshi tu na kar ishq pareshan hoga
misl aaina ke phir shashdar-o-hairan hoga
gar yahi ishq ka aaghaz hai to sun lena
lash howegi meri kucha-e-jaanan hoga
Dub kar marne ka shauq us se hi puchh ai qatil
jis ne dekha ye tera chah-e-zanaKHdan hoga
kahti thi dam mein sayyaad ke ro kar bulbul
ab kabhi hum ko mayassar na gulistan hoga
jitne duniya mein sitam chahe tu kar le mujh par
hashr mein hath mera tera gareban hoga
jaan de baiThega ek roz tu us par 'agha'
wo nahin haal ka tere kabhi pursan hoga

maddāh huuñ maiñ dil se mohammad kī aal kā
mushtāq huuñ vasī-e-nabī ke jamāl kā
ḳhvāhāñ guhar kā huuñ na maiñ tālib huuñ laal kā
mushtāq huuñ tumhāre dahan ke ugaal kā
dekho to ek jā pe Thahartī nahīñ nazar
lapkā paḌā hai aañkh ko kyā dekh-bhāl kā
kyā un se faiz pahuñche jo ḳhud tīra-baḳht haiñ
khilte na dekhā ham ne kabhī phuul Dhaal kā
ham haiñ faqīr daulat-e-duniyā se kaam kyā
behtar hai jām-e-jam se piyāla sifāl kā
daana dikhā ke daam meñ anqā ko lā.ūñgā
mazmūn likh rahā huuñ tire ḳhat-o-ḳhāl kā
sau jaan se fidā huuñ mohammad ke naam par
jis ne batāyā farq harām o halāl kā
vo aañkh bhī uThā ke hameñ dekhte nahīñ
rutba pahuñch gayā hai ye ranj-o-malāl kā
kis zindagī ke vāste daulat kī aarzū
dekho natīja ġhaur se qārūñ ke maal kā
iqbāl gar nahīñ hai tū inkār kījiye
kuchh dījiye javāb hamāre savāl kā
muTThī ko khol kar yad-e-baizā dikhāte haiñ
nāḳhun pe un ke hotā hai dhokā hilāl kā
shā'ir ġhazab ke hote haiñ hargiz na chūkte
mauqa' nahīñ dahan meñ tire qīl-o-qāl kā
ai rashk-e-mehr vasl meñ ġhussa hai kis liye
ye vaqt merī jaan nahīñ hai jalāl kā
tārīkī-e-lahad se kuchh 'āġhā' na ḳhauf kar
dāman hai tere haath meñ zahrā ke laal kā
maddah hun main dil se mohammad ki aal ka
mushtaq hun wasi-e-nabi ke jamal ka
KHwahan guhar ka hun na main talib hun lal ka
mushtaq hun tumhaare dahan ke ugal ka
dekho to ek ja pe Thaharti nahin nazar
lapka paDa hai aankh ko kya dekh-bhaal ka
kya un se faiz pahunche jo KHud tira-baKHt hain
khilte na dekha hum ne kabhi phul Dhaal ka
hum hain faqir daulat-e-duniya se kaam kya
behtar hai jam-e-jam se piyala sifal ka
dana dikha ke dam mein anqa ko launga
mazmun likh raha hun tere KHat-o-KHal ka
sau jaan se fida hun mohammad ke nam par
jis ne bataya farq haram o halal ka
wo aankh bhi uTha ke hamein dekhte nahin
rutba pahunch gaya hai ye ranj-o-malal ka
kis zindagi ke waste daulat ki aarzu
dekho natija ghaur se qarun ke mal ka
iqbaal gar nahin hai tu inkar kijiye
kuchh dijiye jawab hamare sawal ka
muTThi ko khol kar yad-e-baiza dikhate hain
naKHun pe un ke hota hai dhoka hilal ka
sha'ir ghazab ke hote hain hargiz na chukte
mauqa' nahin dahan mein tere qil-o-qal ka
ai rashk-e-mehr wasl mein ghussa hai kis liye
ye waqt meri jaan nahin hai jalal ka
tariki-e-lahad se kuchh 'agha' na KHauf kar
daman hai tere hath mein zahra ke lal ka

chāhat ġhamze jatā rahī hai
vahshat sahrā dikhā rahī hai
ġhunchoñ kā jigar hilā rahī hai
bulbul kyā gul khilā rahī hai
yūsuf kā patā lagā rahī hai
ḳhushbū kan.āñ meñ aa rahī hai
shīrīñ kyā rañg lā rahī hai
'āshiq kā lahū bahā rahī hai
kis shoḳh ko dījiye dil-e-zār
kis meñ sāhab vafā rahī hai
āvāza-e-faiz hai jahāñ meñ
jis kī shohrat sadā rahī hai
Daa.in hai parī-vashoñ kī furqat
dil khā ke kaleja khā rahī hai
jaañ nazr huī parī-ruḳhoñ kī
miTTī ko havā uḌā rahī hai
chāhat kī kashish ne lo Dubo dī
yūsuf ko kuñ.eñ jhukā rahī hai
dil meñ jo base hue haiñ gul-rū
surḳhī āñkhoñ meñ chhā rahī hai
gahtā huuñ jabīñ ko pā-e-but se
taqdīr likhā miTā rahī hai
hañste hue dekh kar guloñ ko
shabnam aañsū bahā rahī hai
andher kā aaj sāmnā hai
surma vo parī lagā rahī hai
kyuuñ jaan nahīñ nikaltī 'āġhā'
kaise sadme uThā rahī hai
chahat ghamze jata rahi hai
wahshat sahra dikha rahi hai
ghunchon ka jigar hila rahi hai
bulbul kya gul khila rahi hai
yusuf ka pata laga rahi hai
KHushbu kanan mein aa rahi hai
shirin kya rang la rahi hai
'ashiq ka lahu baha rahi hai
kis shoKH ko dijiye dil-e-zar
kis mein sahab wafa rahi hai
aawaza-e-faiz hai jahan mein
jis ki shohrat sada rahi hai
Dain hai pari-washon ki furqat
dil kha ke kaleja kha rahi hai
jaan nazr hui pari-ruKHon ki
miTTi ko hawa uDa rahi hai
chahat ki kashish ne lo Dubo di
yusuf ko kunen jhuka rahi hai
dil mein jo base hue hain gul-ru
surKHi aankhon mein chha rahi hai
gahta hun jabin ko pa-e-but se
taqdir likha miTa rahi hai
hanste hue dekh kar gulon ko
shabnam aansu baha rahi hai
andher ka aaj samna hai
surma wo pari laga rahi hai
kyun jaan nahin nikalti 'agha'
kaise sadme uTha rahi hai

muddat ke ba.ad is ne likhā mere naam ḳhat
merī shikāyatoñ se bharā hai tamām ḳhat
ghabrā na is qadar dil-e-betāb sabr kar
aatā hai koī roz meñ ab sub.h-o-shām ḳhat
likkhā huā hai ḳhaas tumhāre hī haath kā
pahchāntā hai ḳhuub tumhārā ġhulām ḳhat
tahrīr un kī siina pe rakh dījiyo mire
badle javāb-e-nāma ke aa.egā kaam ḳhat
likkhā hai ab na likkheñge ham koī ḳhat tujhe
ḳhat aayā merī maut kā laayā payām ḳhat
zaa.e' na jā.egī tirī mehnat kisī tarah
qāsid ajūra detā huuñ chuTkī meñ thaam ḳhat
āshiq-navāziyāñ haiñ tabī.at meñ yaar kī
likkhā hai har mahīne meñ bhejo mudām ḳhat
tahrīr kar ke saikaḌoñ va.ade mukar ga.e
dikhlā.ūñgā huzūr ko roz-e-qayām ḳhat
ḳhat likh ke aaj Daak pe pahuñcheñge yaar ko
pahuñchā.egā hamārā payām-o-salām ḳhat
'āġhā' nisār hojiye in.aam dījiye
laayā hai un kā qāsid-e-sarsar-ḳhirām ḳhat
muddat ke baad is ne likha mere nam KHat
meri shikayaton se bhara hai tamam KHat
ghabra na is qadar dil-e-betab sabr kar
aata hai koi roz mein ab subh-o-sham KHat
likkha hua hai KHas tumhaare hi hath ka
pahchanta hai KHub tumhaara ghulam KHat
tahrir un ki sina pe rakh dijiyo mere
badle jawab-e-nama ke aaega kaam KHat
likkha hai ab na likkhenge hum koi KHat tujhe
KHat aaya meri maut ka laya payam KHat
zae' na jaegi teri mehnat kisi tarah
qasid ajura deta hun chuTki mein tham KHat
aashiq-nawaziyan hain tabiat mein yar ki
likkha hai har mahine mein bhejo mudam KHat
tahrir kar ke saikaDon wade mukar gae
dikhlaunga huzur ko roz-e-qayam KHat
KHat likh ke aaj Dak pe pahunchenge yar ko
pahunchaega hamara payam-o-salam KHat
'agha' nisar hojiye inam dijiye
laya hai un ka qasid-e-sarsar-KHiram KHat

diye us ne auroñ ko sāġhar pe sāġhar
chubho.e mire dil meñ nashtar pe nashtar
marīz-e-mohabbat kī hai ab ye hālat
ki aate haiñ har vaqt chakkar pe chakkar
mirī saḳht-jānī ġhazab rang laa.ī
hue kund qātil ke ḳhanjar pe ḳhanjar
karam hai ye saaqī kī dariyā-dilī kā
mile mujh ko bhar-bhar ke sāġhar pe sāġhar
chaḌhāte haiñ tyorī dikhāte haiñ āñkheñ
chubhote haiñ dil meñ vo nashtar pe nashtar
tirī justujū meñ mah-o-mehr donoñ
lagāte haiñ din raat chakkar pe chakkar
muqābil huā un kī chitvan se jab dil
paḌe tiir par tiir ḳhanjar pe ḳhanjar
nigāhoñ ne dil meñ chubhoī haiñ chhuriyāñ
adāoñ ne maare haiñ ḳhanjar pe ḳhanjar
na sarkā sar us dar se 'āfāq' hargiz
lagā kar ise laakh Thokar pe Thokar
diye us ne auron ko saghar pe saghar
chubhoe mere dil mein nashtar pe nashtar
mariz-e-mohabbat ki hai ab ye haalat
ki aate hain har waqt chakkar pe chakkar
meri saKHt-jaani ghazab rang lai
hue kund qatil ke KHanjar pe KHanjar
karam hai ye saqi ki dariya-dili ka
mile mujh ko bhar-bhar ke saghar pe saghar
chaDhate hain tyori dikhate hain aankhen
chubhote hain dil mein wo nashtar pe nashtar
teri justuju mein mah-o-mehr donon
lagate hain din raat chakkar pe chakkar
muqabil hua un ki chitwan se jab dil
paDe tir par tir KHanjar pe KHanjar
nigahon ne dil mein chubhoi hain chhuriyan
adaon ne mare hain KHanjar pe KHanjar
na sarka sar us dar se 'afaq' hargiz
laga kar ise lakh Thokar pe Thokar

dikhā kar mujh ko chashm-e-mast mastāna banā Daalā
pilā kar aaj saaqī tū ne dīvāna banā Daalā
qiyām-e-yād-e-ḳhūbāñ ko taraqqī de ḳhudā is ne
mire ujḌe hue dil ko parī-ḳhāna banā Daalā
dil-e-sad-chāk merā thā bhalā kis kaam ke qābil
magar ik shoḳh ne le kar ise shānā banā Daalā
zarar pahuñchā na mai-ḳhāne ko kuchh sang-e-havādis se
agar TuuTī koī botal to paimāna banā Daalā
ġhazab jaadū bharī hotī haiñ āñkheñ husn vāloñ kī
nazar jis se milā.ī us ko dīvāna banā Daalā
tamannā vasl kī dil se jo niklī ye ḳhayāl aayā
ki ik ābād ghar ko haa.e vīrāna banā Daalā
vo mai-kash huuñ ki har dam shīsha-o-sāġhar hai saath apne
jahāñ baiThā vahīñ par ek mai-ḳhāna banā Daalā
kHayāl-e-bada-noshī furqat-e-sāqī meñ jab aayā
banāyā dil ko ḳhum āñkhoñ ko paimāna banā Daalā
ḳhudā ke fazl se 'āfāq' thā farzāna-o-‘āqil
navāzish kī butoñ ne us ko dīvāna banā Daalā
dikha kar mujh ko chashm-e-mast mastana bana Dala
pila kar aaj saqi tu ne diwana bana Dala
qiyam-e-yaad-e-KHuban ko taraqqi de KHuda is ne
mere ujDe hue dil ko pari-KHana bana Dala
dil-e-sad-chaak mera tha bhala kis kaam ke qabil
magar ek shoKH ne le kar ise shana bana Dala
zarar pahuncha na mai-KHane ko kuchh sang-e-hawadis se
agar TuTi koi botal to paimana bana Dala
ghazab jadu bhari hoti hain aankhen husn walon ki
nazar jis se milai us ko diwana bana Dala
tamanna wasl ki dil se jo nikli ye KHayal aaya
ki ek aabaad ghar ko hae virana bana Dala
wo mai-kash hun ki har dam shisha-o-saghar hai sath apne
jahan baiTha wahin par ek mai-KHana bana Dala
kHayal-e-bada-noshi furqat-e-saqi mein jab aaya
banaya dil ko KHum aankhon ko paimana bana Dala
KHuda ke fazl se 'afaq' tha farzana-o-‘aqil
nawazish ki buton ne us ko diwana bana Dala

chubhe jab dil meñ ḳhār-e-‘ishq phir kamtar nikalte haiñ
nikalte haiñ agar to jaan hī le kar nikalte haiñ
tire nāvak jo siine meñ kabhī chubh kar nikalte haiñ
to ban kar ḳhuun armān-e-dil-e-muztar nikalte haiñ
kidhar kā qasd hai kis kā muqaddar aaj jaagā hai
talab hotā hai shāna aa.ina zevar nikalte haiñ
tumhārā tiir rasta rok kar siine meñ baiThā hai
jo naale bhī nikalte haiñ to ruk-ruk kar nikalte haiñ
vo kahte haiñ ajal hotī hai jis kī ham pe martā hai
qazā aatī hai jab chyūñTī kī us ke par nikalte haiñ
hasīnoñ ko jo dekho shakl kaisī bholī hotī hai
TaTolo dil agar un ke to vo patthar nikalte haiñ
lagā dī garmī-e-ulfat ne kaisī aag siine meñ
ki āñkhoñ se jo aañsū kī jagah aḳhgar nikalte haiñ
koī dekhe zarā 'āfāq' kī us vaqt kaifiyyat
kabhī hazrat jo sahbā-e-suḳhan pī kar nikalte haiñ
chubhe jab dil mein KHar-e-‘ishq phir kamtar nikalte hain
nikalte hain agar to jaan hi le kar nikalte hain
tere nawak jo sine mein kabhi chubh kar nikalte hain
to ban kar KHun arman-e-dil-e-muztar nikalte hain
kidhar ka qasd hai kis ka muqaddar aaj jaga hai
talab hota hai shana aaina zewar nikalte hain
tumhaara tir rasta rok kar sine mein baiTha hai
jo nale bhi nikalte hain to ruk-ruk kar nikalte hain
wo kahte hain ajal hoti hai jis ki hum pe marta hai
qaza aati hai jab chyunTi ki us ke par nikalte hain
hasinon ko jo dekho shakl kaisi bholi hoti hai
TaTolo dil agar un ke to wo patthar nikalte hain
laga di garmi-e-ulfat ne kaisi aag sine mein
ki aankhon se jo aansu ki jagah aKHgar nikalte hain
koi dekhe zara 'afaq' ki us waqt kaifiyyat
kabhi hazrat jo sahba-e-suKHan pi kar nikalte hain

paḌh legā koī raat kī roī huī āñkheñ
har samt haiñ ārām se soī huī āñkheñ
jin logoñ kī manzil pe nazar hotī hai har dam
un kā hī tamāshā haiñ ye khoī huī āñkheñ
din bhar to jame rahte haiñ palkoñ pe vahī ḳhvāb
kyoñ hosh meñ laatī nahīñ dhoī huī āñkheñ
āñkhoñ kā jamāl aap ko ma.alūm hī kyā hai
dekhīñ haiñ kabhī raat vo soī huī āñkheñ
dil hai ki tujhe paa.eñ bikhar jaa.eñ ai maulā
bīnā.ī ke dhāge meñ piroī huī āñkheñ
kuchh bhī na dikhā mo.ajiza thā hī yahī 'āmir'
kholī ga.iiñ zamzam se bhigoī huī āñkheñ
paDh lega koi raat ki roi hui aankhen
har samt hain aaram se soi hui aankhen
jin logon ki manzil pe nazar hoti hai har dam
un ka hi tamasha hain ye khoi hui aankhen
din bhar to jame rahte hain palkon pe wahi KHwab
kyon hosh mein lati nahin dhoi hui aankhen
aankhon ka jamal aap ko malum hi kya hai
dekhin hain kabhi raat wo soi hui aankhen
dil hai ki tujhe paen bikhar jaen ai maula
binai ke dhage mein piroi hui aankhen
kuchh bhi na dikha moajiza tha hi yahi 'amir'
kholi gain zamzam se bhigoi hui aankhen

baḌe din se hare haiñ paat yahāñ
koī Tiktī nahīñ hai baat yahāñ
kahāñ sīkhe the naam aadam ne
kahāñ tahqīq se najāt yahāñ
vahī likhte haiñ jo nisāb meñ hai
vahī taqdīr sī hai baat yahāñ
ye takalluf kā koī baab nahīñ
lagī rahtī hai ehtiyāt yahāñ
jī mirā naam vaise 'āmir' hai
khaḌā miltā huuñ roz raat yahāñ
baDe din se hare hain pat yahan
koi Tikti nahin hai baat yahan
kahan sikhe the nam aadam ne
kahan tahqiq se najat yahan
wahi likhte hain jo nisab mein hai
wahi taqdir si hai baat yahan
ye takalluf ka koi bab nahin
lagi rahti hai ehtiyat yahan
ji mera nam waise 'amir' hai
khaDa milta hun roz raat yahan

dar darīche ke binā aur kisī chhat ke baġhair
ham tire shahr meñ sākin haiñ sukūnat ke baġhair
jang aisī hai abad tak bhī rahegī jaarī
mas.ala hal nahīñ honā hai qayāmat ke baġhair
ḳhāmushī jism pe chaḌhtī hai harārat kī tarah
roz ik shor utartā hai 'alāmat ke baġhair
saath meñ yaar bhī ho aur phir itvār bhī ho
baat bantī nahīñ cigarette kī ri'āyat ke baġhair
yaar kaise na ho merā ki mirā yaar mujhe
har tarah se hai qubūl aur vazāhat ke baġhair
dhyān rakhnā ki ye lahja hai hamārā lahja
pur-asar ho nahīñ saktā hai mohabbat ke baġhair
kaam aisā hai ki karnā hī paḌegā 'āmir'
chāhe teshe ke binā ho yā riyāzat ke baġhair
dar dariche ke bina aur kisi chhat ke baghair
hum tere shahr mein sakin hain sukunat ke baghair
jang aisi hai abad tak bhi rahegi jari
masala hal nahin hona hai qayamat ke baghair
KHamushi jism pe chaDhti hai hararat ki tarah
roz ek shor utarta hai 'alamat ke baghair
sath mein yar bhi ho aur phir itwar bhi ho
baat banti nahin cigarette ki ri'ayat ke baghair
yar kaise na ho mera ki mera yar mujhe
har tarah se hai qubul aur wazahat ke baghair
dhyan rakhna ki ye lahja hai hamara lahja
pur-asar ho nahin sakta hai mohabbat ke baghair
kaam aisa hai ki karna hi paDega 'amir'
chahe teshe ke bina ho ya riyazat ke baghair

is masāfat meñ kitne dar guzre
terī manzil se ham kidhar guzre
the musāfir safar jachā na jinheñ
qāfile un pe raat bhar guzre
merī āñkhoñ ko chhoḌne vaale
merā darvāza band kar guzre
raat pāband hai to din baḳhsho
aa bhī jaao ki dopahar guzre
bad-gumānī se kyā bacheñge ham
bad-gumānī jo aap par guzre
kyā guzartī rahī guzarne tak
aur guzre to be-asar guzre
bazm-e-hastī meñ yaar 'āmir'-ḳhāñ
marne aa.e the aur kar guzre
is masafat mein kitne dar guzre
teri manzil se hum kidhar guzre
the musafir safar jacha na jinhen
qafile un pe raat bhar guzre
meri aankhon ko chhoDne wale
mera darwaza band kar guzre
raat paband hai to din baKHsho
aa bhi jao ki dopahar guzre
bad-gumani se kya bachenge hum
bad-gumani jo aap par guzre
kya guzarti rahi guzarne tak
aur guzre to be-asar guzre
bazm-e-hasti mein yar 'amir'-KHan
marne aae the aur kar guzre

guzre hue vaqtoñ kā nishāñ thā to kahāñ thā
ham se jo nihāñ hai vo ayaañ thā to kahāñ thā
is tarah lipaTtī hai udāsī ki ye socheñ
do pal kī ḳhushī kā jo gumāñ thā to kahāñ thā
bastī kā taqāza hai kahīñ haiñ to kahāñ haiñ
majnūñ kā bayābāñ meñ makāñ thā to kahāñ thā
baiThā hai mire paas ki chalnā nahīñ mumkin
sohbat kī hadoñ kā jo nishāñ thā to kahāñ thā
ab sochte haiñ baiTh ke gulshan kī fazā meñ
sahrā meñ hamārā jo makāñ thā to kahāñ thā
piirī hai buzurgī hai buḌhāpā hai ki kyā hai
is karb meñ rahnā ki javāñ thā to kahāñ thā
nashsha hī nahīñ sab kā bharam TuuT rahā thā
sunte the koī pīr-e-muġhāñ thā to kahāñ thā
'āmir' ko hamīñ DhūñD ke laa.eñ haiñ ba-mushkil
kahte haiñ vo pahle se yahāñ thā to kahāñ thā
guzre hue waqton ka nishan tha to kahan tha
hum se jo nihan hai wo ayan tha to kahan tha
is tarah lipaTti hai udasi ki ye sochen
do pal ki KHushi ka jo guman tha to kahan tha
basti ka taqaza hai kahin hain to kahan hain
majnun ka bayaban mein makan tha to kahan tha
baiTha hai mere pas ki chalna nahin mumkin
sohbat ki hadon ka jo nishan tha to kahan tha
ab sochte hain baiTh ke gulshan ki faza mein
sahra mein hamara jo makan tha to kahan tha
piri hai buzurgi hai buDhapa hai ki kya hai
is karb mein rahna ki jawan tha to kahan tha
nashsha hi nahin sab ka bharam TuT raha tha
sunte the koi pir-e-mughan tha to kahan tha
'amir' ko hamin DhunD ke laen hain ba-mushkil
kahte hain wo pahle se yahan tha to kahan tha

kab tak vahī sarāb vahī iztirāb ho
maiñ hī karūñ bhī yaad mujhī par 'azāb ho
paḌhte to hoñ ka.ī pe samajhtā na ho koī
aisā na ho ki dil bhī ḳhudā kī kitāb ho
māñgī jo jā rahī hai du'ā kāmyābī kī
apnī to ye du'ā hai du'ā kāmyāb ho
kab tak wahi sarab wahi iztirab ho
main hi karun bhi yaad mujhi par 'azab ho
paDhte to hon kai pe samajhta na ho koi
aisa na ho ki dil bhi KHuda ki kitab ho
mangi jo ja rahi hai du'a kaamyabi ki
apni to ye du'a hai du'a kaamyab ho

dard-e-dil hai na falsafa mire paas
daal roTī kā mas.ala mire paas
paas mere bhī hai tirī hī du'ā
kaash hotā tirā ḳhudā mire paas
āgahī aa ga.ī to aa hī ga.ī
ab nahīñ koī rāsta mire paas
ek pal ek pal na rok sakā
vaqt merā thā kab mirā mire paas
sust rātoñ meñ jis ne chhoḌā thā
tez bārish meñ aa gayā mire paas
tum parī-zād ho maiñ aadam huuñ
aise be-sudh na baiThnā mire paas
vāqi'a ye hai tū jo aa na sakā
tab se maiñ bhī na aa sakā mire paas
merā ġham bhī hai tere ġham jaisā
hai par is ġham kī intihā mire paas
dard jaalī haiñ ashk naqlī haiñ
ek hai niiñd kī davā mire paas
vaqt kā kyā qusūr vaqt thā vo
tū bhī 'āmir' kahāñ rahā mire paas
dard-e-dil hai na falsafa mere pas
dal roTi ka masala mere pas
pas mere bhi hai teri hi du'a
kash hota tera KHuda mere pas
aagahi aa gai to aa hi gai
ab nahin koi rasta mere pas
ek pal ek pal na rok saka
waqt mera tha kab mera mere pas
sust raaton mein jis ne chhoDa tha
tez barish mein aa gaya mere pas
tum pari-zad ho main aadam hun
aise be-sudh na baiThna mere pas
waqi'a ye hai tu jo aa na saka
tab se main bhi na aa saka mere pas
mera gham bhi hai tere gham jaisa
hai par is gham ki intiha mere pas
dard jali hain ashk naqli hain
ek hai nind ki dawa mere pas
waqt ka kya qusur waqt tha wo
tu bhi 'amir' kahan raha mere pas

na sabāt hai na davām hai
ḳhum-e-zindagī hai so ḳhaam hai
hameñ mausamoñ se umiid kyā
hameñ roz roz kā kaam hai
tujhe rāstoñ kā pata na thā
tire hausloñ ko salām hai
na ye sard ho na ye ḳhatm ho
mirī tishnagī mirā jaam hai
maiñ ye pūchhtā huā chal diyā
koī kaam hai koī kaam hai
mujhe 'āmir' aap se kyā ġharaz
ye kalām sab kā kalām hai
na sabaat hai na dawam hai
KHum-e-zindagi hai so KHam hai
hamein mausamon se umid kya
hamein roz roz ka kaam hai
tujhe raston ka pata na tha
tere hauslon ko salam hai
na ye sard ho na ye KHatm ho
meri tishnagi mera jam hai
main ye puchhta hua chal diya
koi kaam hai koi kaam hai
mujhe 'amir' aap se kya gharaz
ye kalam sab ka kalam hai

badan utaar ke kapḌe badal rahā hai koī
na.ī sarisht pahan kar nikal rahā hai koī
qadam qadam pe añdherā bhī baḌhtā jaatā hai
gumān hotā hai pīchhe bhī chal rahā hai koī
yaqīn hī nahīñ aatā vo kaise bol paḌā
mirā ḳhayāl thā bas vahm pal rahā hai koī
baḌā gumān hai vā'doñ pe Taal rakkhā hai
huzūr aap ke Taale se Tal rahā hai koī
maiñ apnī zaat meñ utrā to maiñ ne ye dekhā
bahut ḳhamoshī se bāhar nikal rahā hai koī
tamāsha ādhā-adhūrā hai dekhiye 'āmir'
tasavvurāt ko āñkhoñ pe mal rahā hai koī
badan utar ke kapDe badal raha hai koi
nai sarisht pahan kar nikal raha hai koi
qadam qadam pe andhera bhi baDhta jata hai
guman hota hai pichhe bhi chal raha hai koi
yaqin hi nahin aata wo kaise bol paDa
mera KHayal tha bas wahm pal raha hai koi
baDa guman hai wa'don pe Tal rakkha hai
huzur aap ke Tale se Tal raha hai koi
main apni zat mein utra to main ne ye dekha
bahut KHamoshi se bahar nikal raha hai koi
tamasha aadha-adhura hai dekhiye 'amir'
tasawwuraat ko aankhon pe mal raha hai koi

ġham utārā gayā sabhī ke liye
ashk utre haiñ aadmī ke liye
ik tajallī mujhe 'ināyat ho
merī āñkhoñ kī raushnī ke liye
jī ke lagtā nahīñ munāsib hai
zindagī lafz zindagī ke liye
baar hotā rahā kisī ke sipurd
shukr kartā rahā kisī ke liye
maiñ ne had-darja koshisheñ kar liiñ
dil banā hī nahīñ ḳhushī ke liye
kuchh darinde bhī jaane jaate haiñ
apnī insān-dostī ke liye
sab nahīñ jānte ye vo dar hai
yuuñ to darvāza hai sabhī ke liye
us ne bādal haTā liye 'āmir'
chand lamhoñ kī chāñdnī ke liye
gham utara gaya sabhi ke liye
ashk utre hain aadmi ke liye
ek tajalli mujhe 'inayat ho
meri aankhon ki raushni ke liye
ji ke lagta nahin munasib hai
zindagi lafz zindagi ke liye
bar hota raha kisi ke sipurd
shukr karta raha kisi ke liye
main ne had-darja koshishen kar lin
dil bana hi nahin KHushi ke liye
kuchh darinde bhi jaane jate hain
apni insan-dosti ke liye
sab nahin jaante ye wo dar hai
yun to darwaza hai sabhi ke liye
us ne baadal haTa liye 'amir'
chand lamhon ki chandni ke liye

chalte jaate haiñ par nahīñ aatī
āḳhirī rah-guzar nahīñ aatī
ham ko bechain kar ke rakhtī hai
ek shai jo nazar nahīñ aatī
aañkh meñ kuchh chalā gayā shāyad
aañkh yūñhī to bhar nahīñ aatī
baiThe baiThe ḳhayāl aatā hai
un kī koī ḳhabar nahīñ aatī
is qadar kam dikhā.ī detā hai
ek sūrat nazar nahīñ aatī
vo balā mere sar meñ rahtī hai
jo balā mere sar nahīñ aatī
roz pursish ko log aate haiñ
maut jab vaqt par nahīñ aatī
chalte jate hain par nahin aati
aaKHiri rah-guzar nahin aati
hum ko bechain kar ke rakhti hai
ek shai jo nazar nahin aati
aankh mein kuchh chala gaya shayad
aankh yunhi to bhar nahin aati
baiThe baiThe KHayal aata hai
un ki koi KHabar nahin aati
is qadar kam dikhai deta hai
ek surat nazar nahin aati
wo bala mere sar mein rahti hai
jo bala mere sar nahin aati
roz pursish ko log aate hain
maut jab waqt par nahin aati

lag rahā thā yahīñ kahīñ ho tum
kaash hote magar nahīñ ho tum
sirf bārish meñ vasl mumkin hai
āsmāñ maiñ huuñ aur zamīñ ho tum
duur se bhī ho dil-nashīñ lekin
sāmne kis qadar hasīñ ho tum
kab se mujh ko nahīñ mile dekho
yaar kyā zer-e-āstīñ ho tum
jis jagah thā maiñ phir vahīñ huuñ maiñ
jis jagah thā maiñ kyā vahīñ ho tum
lag raha tha yahin kahin ho tum
kash hote magar nahin ho tum
sirf barish mein wasl mumkin hai
aasman main hun aur zamin ho tum
dur se bhi ho dil-nashin lekin
samne kis qadar hasin ho tum
kab se mujh ko nahin mile dekho
yar kya zer-e-astin ho tum
jis jagah tha main phir wahin hun main
jis jagah tha main kya wahin ho tum

maiñ rahā umr bhar yahīñ kā rahā
maiñ kināroñ pe bhī zamīñ kā rahā
le gayā vaqt terā naqsh kahāñ
jo kahīñ thā na phir kahīñ kā rahā
mere āñgan meñ ik kalī na milī
koī qissa na nāznīñ kā rahā
thā ye tohfa agarche mere liye
terā ḳhanjar to āstīñ kā rahā
terā inkār ḳhāmoshī se huā
bahut isrār phir nahīñ kā rahā
vo jo Thahre kahīñ vahīñ na rahe
merā 'āmir' kahāñ kahīñ kā rahā
main raha umr bhar yahin ka raha
main kinaron pe bhi zamin ka raha
le gaya waqt tera naqsh kahan
jo kahin tha na phir kahin ka raha
mere aangan mein ek kali na mili
koi qissa na naznin ka raha
tha ye tohfa agarche mere liye
tera KHanjar to aastin ka raha
tera inkar KHamoshi se hua
bahut israr phir nahin ka raha
wo jo Thahre kahin wahin na rahe
mera 'amir' kahan kahin ka raha

dastaras chhin jā.egī aur naqsh-e-pā kho jā.eñge
ham vahāñ par baiThe baiThe ret ke ho jā.eñge
kab se marnā chāhte haiñ tujh pe ham terī qasam
jaan se to jā rahe haiñ jaan mar to jā.eñge
vo nahīñ samjheñge lailā kaun hai maiñ kaun huuñ
bas zarā sahrā taraf jaanā hai pūchho jā.eñge
ik kahānī sunte sunte itnā 'arsa ho gayā
ab agar vo dikh gayā to andhe hī ho jā.eñge
ye jo tāroñ kā fusūñ hai TūTnā hai sub.h ko
jab tirī āñkhoñ se ham bhī Tuut kar kho jā.eñge
aap agar ḳhud se muḳhātib haiñ to 'āmir' Thiik hai
aap kī bātoñ ko sun kar log to so jā.eñge
dastaras chhin jaegi aur naqsh-e-pa kho jaenge
hum wahan par baiThe baiThe ret ke ho jaenge
kab se marna chahte hain tujh pe hum teri qasam
jaan se to ja rahe hain jaan mar to jaenge
wo nahin samjhenge laila kaun hai main kaun hun
bas zara sahra taraf jaana hai puchho jaenge
ek kahani sunte sunte itna 'arsa ho gaya
ab agar wo dikh gaya to andhe hi ho jaenge
ye jo taron ka fusun hai TuTna hai subh ko
jab teri aankhon se hum bhi Tut kar kho jaenge
aap agar KHud se muKHatib hain to 'amir' Thik hai
aap ki baaton ko sun kar log to so jaenge

kyā kisī rābte meñ rakkhā hai
ham ne dil rāste meñ rakkhā hai
ab ḳhudāoñ kī kyā zarūrat hai
aa.ina but-kade meñ rakkhā hai
nā tumhārī ḳhatā hai nā merī
mas.ala mas.ale meñ rakkhā hai
raat rakkhī hai us ne din ke baad
aap ko fā.ede meñ rakkhā hai
us ko andāz hai tasalsul kā
zulf ko silsile meñ rakkhā hai
kyā rakhā hai purānī chīzoñ meñ
jo nayā hai na.e meñ rakkhā hai
agle vaqtoñ pe soch kar 'āmir'
vaqt ko qā.ede meñ rakkhā hai
kya kisi rabte mein rakkha hai
hum ne dil raste mein rakkha hai
ab KHudaon ki kya zarurat hai
aaina but-kade mein rakkha hai
na tumhaari KHata hai na meri

aap ko faede mein rakkha hai
us ko andaz hai tasalsul ka

jo naya hai nae mein rakkha hai
agle waqton pe soch kar 'amir'
