us ki surat dekh kar bola sitaron se qamar
yar lagta hai ki apni naukri KHatre mein hai
us ke hathon mein chhuri ko dekh kar hairan hun
ungliyan KHatre mein hain ya phir chhuri KHatre mein hai
kya kaha tum ne use dekha hai apne shahr mein
yani ab to shahr ka har aadmi KHatre mein hai
kaun hira hai yahan aur kaun hai hira-numa
farq itna sa bata kar jauhari KHatre mein hai
jhil si aankhon mein us ki Dub sakti hai kabhi
rok lo us ko koi ja kar nadi KHatre mein hai
be-sar-o-pa sher kah kar KHush tha main aamir-'ata'
'mir' ji sapne mein bole shaeri KHatre mein hai

puure majme’ ko lā-javāb kiyā
husn par us ne jab ḳhitāb kiyā
'umr bhar phir nahīñ hue nākām
tū ne jis jis ko kāmyāb kiyā
tere jaate hī khul ga.iiñ āñkheñ
niiñd aadhī kī puurā ḳhvāb kiyā
haal achchhā thā ab talak merā
pūchh kar tū ne sab ḳharāb kiyā
ehtirāman sabhī ḳhutūt tire
jā ke sāhil pe ġharq-e-āb kiyā
sifr bachtā hai dil ke ḳhāne meñ
maiñ ne ḳhushiyoñ kā jab hisāb kiyā
shukr sad-shukr aisī ġhurbat kā
jis ne apnoñ ko be-naqāb kiyā
lag ga.ī us kī naukrī jis ne
jī-huzūr aur jī janāb kiyā
pure majme’ ko la-jawab kiya
husn par us ne jab KHitab kiya
'umr bhar phir nahin hue nakaam
tu ne jis jis ko kaamyab kiya
tere jate hi khul gain aankhen
nind aadhi ki pura KHwab kiya
haal achchha tha ab talak mera
puchh kar tu ne sab KHarab kiya
ehtiraman sabhi KHutut tere
ja ke sahil pe gharq-e-ab kiya
sifr bachta hai dil ke KHane mein
main ne KHushiyon ka jab hisab kiya
shukr sad-shukr aisi ghurbat ka
jis ne apnon ko be-naqab kiya
lag gai us ki naukri jis ne
ji-huzur aur ji janab kiya

ḳhvāb meñ kar ke rihā.ī ke nazāre qaidī
jaag kar rote rahe aaj bechāre qaidī
aap kī duniyā meñ jhūle kī suhūlat hogī
jhūlte haiñ yahāñ suulī ke sahāre qaidī
jānte the ki rihā.ī kī koī raah nahīñ
roz karte the par andhoñ ko ishāre qaidī
raat kī aaḌ meñ miltī haiñ sazā.eñ kyā kyā
shāhzādī ko lubhāte haiñ kuñvāre qaidī
us ne zindān ke sūrāḳh talak band kiye
kaaT leñ raat na ginte hue taare qaidī
hai giraftār-e-anā har koī tā-hadd-e-nigāh
zulmat-ābād meñ ab kis ko pukāre qaidī
tum to yādoñ ko bhī hamrāh liye jaate ho
chhoḌ kar jaao inheñ ye haiñ hamāre qaidī
KHwab mein kar ke rihai ke nazare qaidi
jag kar rote rahe aaj bechaare qaidi
aap ki duniya mein jhule ki suhulat hogi
jhulte hain yahan suli ke sahaare qaidi
jaante the ki rihai ki koi rah nahin
roz karte the par andhon ko ishaare qaidi
raat ki aaD mein milti hain sazaen kya kya
shahzadi ko lubhate hain kunware qaidi
us ne zindan ke suraKH talak band kiye
kaT len raat na ginte hue tare qaidi
hai giraftar-e-ana har koi ta-hadd-e-nigah
zulmat-abaad mein ab kis ko pukare qaidi
tum to yaadon ko bhi hamrah liye jate ho
chhoD kar jao inhen ye hain hamare qaidi

pahle apnāyā ḳhaar phūloñ kā
tab kahīñ paayā pyaar phūloñ kā
maiñ bhī gulshan sameT laayā huuñ
us ne māñgā thā haar phūloñ kā
yaad aatī hai us kī mat chheḌo
zikr yuuñ baar baar phūloñ kā
tujh se milne ke ba.ad ye jaanā
kaun hai dastkār phūloñ kā
phail jā ban ke ḳhushbū gulshan meñ
chhīn le iḳhtiyār phūloñ kā
tere chhūne se hī to chaltā hai
aaj kal rozgār phūloñ kā
de ke iz.hār-e-ishq karte haiñ
is se samjho vaqār phūloñ kā
jab se āmir-'atā' huā āshiq
chaḌh gayā hai udhār phūloñ kā
pahle apnaya KHar phulon ka
tab kahin paya pyar phulon ka
main bhi gulshan sameT laya hun
us ne manga tha haar phulon ka
yaad aati hai us ki mat chheDo
zikr yun bar bar phulon ka
tujh se milne ke baad ye jaana
kaun hai dastkar phulon ka
phail ja ban ke KHushbu gulshan mein
chhin le iKHtiyar phulon ka
tere chhune se hi to chalta hai
aaj kal rozgar phulon ka
de ke izhaar-e-ishq karte hain
is se samjho waqar phulon ka
jab se aamir-'ata' hua aashiq
chaDh gaya hai udhaar phulon ka

kisī tarah to use maar duuñ jo bāhar hai
vo shaḳhs kaise maregā jo mere andar hai
sikhā diyā mujhe ādāb-e-guftugū tū ne
mire liye to tirā husn hī grammar hai
ab us ke sāmne sach bolne na lag jaanā
vo mere baare meñ pūchhe to kahnā behtar hai
lo ab to baiThe-biThā.e hī diid hotī hai
vabā kā daur hai so āj-kal vo ghar par hai
ab aise meñ mire dil se duā hī niklegī
vo surḳh joḌe meñ jo aaj ban-sañvar kar hai
phir ashk ho ga.e be-mol jab ye us ne kahā
nikāl duuñ maiñ tirī aañkh meñ jo kankar hai
har ek raah se guzrā huuñ be-niyāzāna
'atā' ġharaz kā pujārī nahīñ qalandar hai
kisi tarah to use mar dun jo bahar hai
wo shaKHs kaise marega jo mere andar hai
sikha diya mujhe aadab-e-guftugu tu ne
mere liye to tera husn hi grammar hai
ab us ke samne sach bolne na lag jaana
wo mere bare mein puchhe to kahna behtar hai
lo ab to baiThe-biThae hi did hoti hai
waba ka daur hai so aaj-kal wo ghar par hai
ab aise mein mere dil se dua hi niklegi
wo surKH joDe mein jo aaj ban-sanwar kar hai
phir ashk ho gae be-mol jab ye us ne kaha
nikal dun main teri aankh mein jo kankar hai
har ek rah se guzra hun be-niyazana
'ata' gharaz ka pujari nahin qalandar hai

aañkh to an-paḌh hai aur nādān hai
dil kī ḳhvāhish ek hī insān hai
is liye sab aage pīchhe haiñ mire
tujh se jo thoḌī bahut pahchān hai
ham khaḌe haiñ dil hathelī par liye
husn vāloñ par hī us kā dhyān hai
tere qadmoñ kī ziyāfat ke liye
maiñ ne chaukhaT par rakhā guldān hai
paas ik gaz bhī ḳhushī kā hai nahīñ
aur ġham kā puurā puurā thaan hai
hukm rab kā jab talak hotā nahīñ
zindagī kī maut ḳhud nigrān hai
kyā milī shohrat ki sab milne lage
vo bhī jin se duur kī pahchān hai
dil meñ hai hirs-o-havas kī bū bharī
aur phūloñ se sajā dālān hai
ġham bhī itrā kar ḳhushī se kah uThā
ye 'atā' to roz kā mehmān hai
aankh to an-paDh hai aur nadan hai
dil ki KHwahish ek hi insan hai
is liye sab aage pichhe hain mere
tujh se jo thoDi bahut pahchan hai
hum khaDe hain dil hatheli par liye
husn walon par hi us ka dhyan hai
tere qadmon ki ziyafat ke liye
main ne chaukhaT par rakha guldan hai
pas ek gaz bhi KHushi ka hai nahin
aur gham ka pura pura than hai
hukm rab ka jab talak hota nahin
zindagi ki maut KHud nigran hai
kya mili shohrat ki sab milne lage
wo bhi jin se dur ki pahchan hai
dil mein hai hirs-o-hawas ki bu bhari
aur phulon se saja dalan hai
gham bhi itra kar KHushi se kah uTha
ye 'ata' to roz ka mehman hai

sab ko apnī tarah samajhtī hai
yaar tū bhī na kitnī bholī hai
surḳh dekhe haiñ maiñ ne lab us ke
aisā lagtā hai ḳhuun piitī hai
laḌ rahī hai vo be-sabab mujh se
shukr hai 'ishq ab bhī baaqī hai
us ko suljhāne meñ lage haiñ sab
shā'irī zulf yā pahelī hai
kal talak maiñ hī jis kā sab kuchh thā
aaj vo naam se bhī chiḌhtī hai
jaate jaate vo kah rahī thī mujhe
kyā karūñ ye ḳhudā kī marzī hai
maut to sar pe hai khaḌī kab se
baiThiye aap kursī ḳhālī hai
sab ko apni tarah samajhti hai
yar tu bhi na kitni bholi hai
surKH dekhe hain main ne lab us ke
aisa lagta hai KHun piti hai
laD rahi hai wo be-sabab mujh se
shukr hai 'ishq ab bhi baqi hai
us ko suljhane mein lage hain sab
sha'iri zulf ya paheli hai
kal talak main hi jis ka sab kuchh tha
aaj wo nam se bhi chiDhti hai
jate jate wo kah rahi thi mujhe
kya karun ye KHuda ki marzi hai
maut to sar pe hai khaDi kab se
baiThiye aap kursi KHali hai

ḳhushī kā ek lamha chāhiye thā
ghaḌī-bhar saath terā chāhiye thā
milā thā maiñ mahīnoñ baad tum se
tumheñ siine se lagnā chāhiye thā
maiñ duniyā ghūmne bekār niklā
tirī āñkhoñ ko taknā chāhiye thā
hamesha ham ne kī terī tamanna
hameñ kab tere jaisā chāhiye thā
tujhe sauñpā thā apnā aap maiñ ne
to phir mahfūz rakhnā chāhiye thā
use ahvāl batlānā hai apnā
koī zaḳhmī parinda chāhiye thā
tumhāre ishq ne maarā hai jis ko
mujhe vo shaḳhs zinda chāhiye thā
daġhā kar ke bhī kitne mutma.in ho
tumheñ to Duub marnā chāhiye thā
use baḳhshā gayā phir hijr jis ko
javānī meñ buḌhāpā chāhiye thā
sabhī achchhe hoñ kab chāhā thā maiñ ne
mujhe ik dost achchhā chāhiye thā
phañse haiñ ab vahī mushkil Dagar meñ
jinheñ āsān rasta chāhiye thā
koī beva ke dukh ko kyā samajhtā
sabhoñ ko ghar meñ hissa chāhiye thā
maiñ samjhā vo mirī ḳhātir khaḌī hai
magar us ko to rickshaw chāhiye thā
KHushi ka ek lamha chahiye tha
ghaDi-bhar sath tera chahiye tha
mila tha main mahinon baad tum se
tumhein sine se lagna chahiye tha
main duniya ghumne bekar nikla
teri aankhon ko takna chahiye tha
hamesha hum ne ki teri tamanna
hamein kab tere jaisa chahiye tha
tujhe saunpa tha apna aap main ne
to phir mahfuz rakhna chahiye tha
use ahwal batlana hai apna
koi zaKHmi parinda chahiye tha
tumhaare ishq ne mara hai jis ko
mujhe wo shaKHs zinda chahiye tha
dagha kar ke bhi kitne mutmain ho
tumhein to Dub marna chahiye tha
use baKHsha gaya phir hijr jis ko
jawani mein buDhapa chahiye tha
sabhi achchhe hon kab chaha tha main ne
mujhe ek dost achchha chahiye tha
phanse hain ab wahi mushkil Dagar mein
jinhen aasan rasta chahiye tha
koi bewa ke dukh ko kya samajhta
sabhon ko ghar mein hissa chahiye tha
main samjha wo meri KHatir khaDi hai
magar us ko to rickshaw chahiye tha

batā tū ai chaman laayā kahāñ se
tirī ḳhushbū to miltī hai fulāñ se
vo ik sūrat jo kal shab ḳhvāb meñ thī
yaqīnan hogī pariyoñ ke jahāñ se
vo kahtā hai ki taj de man kī ḳhvāhish
milan kaisā zamīñ kā āsmāñ se
mire chhe foot kā qad bhī haar baiThā
faqat do inch kī lambī zabāñ se
vahīñ aTkī huī hai saañs merī
kisī se rabt TuuTā thā jahāñ se
vo merī zindagī se yuuñ hī niklī
nikaltā tiir hai jaise kamāñ se
yaqīñ ko raah mil saktī hai sāhib
nikal jaa.e agar shak darmiyāñ se
bata tu ai chaman laya kahan se
teri KHushbu to milti hai fulan se
wo ek surat jo kal shab KHwab mein thi
yaqinan hogi pariyon ke jahan se
wo kahta hai ki taj de man ki KHwahish
milan kaisa zamin ka aasman se
mere chhe foot ka qad bhi haar baiTha
faqat do inch ki lambi zaban se
wahin aTki hui hai sans meri
kisi se rabt TuTa tha jahan se
wo meri zindagi se yun hi nikli
nikalta tir hai jaise kaman se
yaqin ko rah mil sakti hai sahib
nikal jae agar shak darmiyan se

nīchī nazar kushāda jabīñ darmiyāna qad
gesū darāz shīrīñ zabāñ husn mustanad
maanā vafā ke bal pe khaḌā hai to Thiik hai
gir jā.egā par ishq kī dīvār se na lad
tab der ho chukī thī bahut kaise roktā
palTī thī jab vo rote hue chuum kar lahad
hājat to ek tīsrī cigarette kī hai magar
us kā ye hukm hai ki bas ik din meñ do adad
begāna kar de ishq ġham-e-rozgār se
bas ek diid ke liye din-bhar ke kaam radd
nichi nazar kushada jabin darmiyana qad
gesu daraaz shirin zaban husn mustanad
mana wafa ke bal pe khaDa hai to Thik hai
gir jaega par ishq ki diwar se na lad
tab der ho chuki thi bahut kaise rokta
palTi thi jab wo rote hue chum kar lahad
hajat to ek tisri cigarette ki hai magar
us ka ye hukm hai ki bas ek din mein do adad
begana kar de ishq gham-e-rozgar se
bas ek did ke liye din-bhar ke kaam radd

yaad bhī us kī ḳhvāb kī sī hai
ek laḌkī hijāb kī sī hai
chūmtā huuñ savāb jaan ke maiñ
tū muqaddas kitāb kī sī hai
jo milī hai savāb kī ḳhātir
ziist vo bhī 'azāb kī sī hai
us meñ ḳhushbū rahī na rang rahā
ab vo sūkhe gulāb kī sī hai
zikr terā 'atā' ke she'r meñ hai
tū ġhazal par shabāb kī sī hai
yaad bhi us ki KHwab ki si hai
ek laDki hijab ki si hai
chumta hun sawab jaan ke main
tu muqaddas kitab ki si hai
jo mili hai sawab ki KHatir
zist wo bhi 'azab ki si hai
us mein KHushbu rahi na rang raha
ab wo sukhe gulab ki si hai
zikr tera 'ata' ke she'r mein hai
tu ghazal par shabab ki si hai

be-hijābāna vo kal jab bar-sar-e-mahfil ga.e
jitne murjhā.e the chehre ek dam se khil ga.e
yaar vo nāzuk hai itnā maiñ ne us ke aane par
farsh phūloñ kā bichhāyā paañv phir bhī chhil ga.e
jaane us āvāz meñ kaisī shifā maujūd hai
us ne pūchhā Thiik ho aur zaḳhm ḳhud hī sil ga.e
vo jo apnī be-tukī bātoñ se hī mash.hūr hai
us kī bāteñ sunñe ko sab shahr ke 'āqil ga.e
sirf us ke husn kī ḳhairāt lene ke liye
ban ke shāhān-e-zamāna bhī vahāñ saa.il ga.e
baiThe baiThe us ne naddī meñ Dubo.e paañv aur
dekhte hī dekhte donoñ kināre mil ga.e
apnī manzil paane vāloñ meñ vahī kuchh log haiñ
rauñd kar apnī anā jo jānib-e-manzil ga.e
be-hijabana wo kal jab bar-sar-e-mahfil gae
jitne murjhae the chehre ek dam se khil gae
yar wo nazuk hai itna main ne us ke aane par
farsh phulon ka bichhaya panw phir bhi chhil gae
jaane us aawaz mein kaisi shifa maujud hai
us ne puchha Thik ho aur zaKHm KHud hi sil gae
wo jo apni be-tuki baaton se hi mashhur hai
us ki baaten sunne ko sab shahr ke 'aqil gae
sirf us ke husn ki KHairaat lene ke liye
ban ke shahan-e-zamana bhi wahan sail gae
baiThe baiThe us ne naddi mein Duboe panw aur
dekhte hi dekhte donon kinare mil gae
apni manzil pane walon mein wahi kuchh log hain
raund kar apni ana jo jaanib-e-manzil gae

ishq meñ ab ḳhuun paanī kījiye
nazr-e-vahshat ye javānī kījiye
aap ke hāthoñ meñ hai sāñsoñ kī Dor
jitnī chāhe khīñchā-tānī kījiye
iltijā kar ke na sharminda kareñ
hukmrāñ haiñ hukmrānī kījiye
mil rahe haiñ ham purāne moḌ par
aap phir bāteñ purānī kījiye
maiñ bahut mushkil se miltā huuñ huzūr
mil gayā huuñ mezbānī kījiye
merā to hai lab-kushā honā gunāh
aap hī jādū-bayānī kījiye
zikr kiije ab 'atā' ke sher kā
ḳhatm 'āmir' kī kahānī kījiye
ishq mein ab KHun pani kijiye
nazr-e-wahshat ye jawani kijiye
aap ke hathon mein hai sanson ki Dor
jitni chahe khincha-tani kijiye
iltija kar ke na sharminda karen
hukmran hain hukmrani kijiye
mil rahe hain hum purane moD par
aap phir baaten purani kijiye
main bahut mushkil se milta hun huzur
mil gaya hun mezbani kijiye
mera to hai lab-kusha hona gunah
aap hi jadu-bayani kijiye
zikr kije ab 'ata' ke sher ka
KHatm 'amir' ki kahani kijiye

'umr guzrī hai tirī galiyoñ ke chakkar kaaT kar
kyoñ na likhkhūñ ḳhud ko majnūñ maiñ suḳhanvar kaaT kar
jaane ye kaisī sharārat aaj sūjhī hai use
vo mujhe uḌne ko kahtī hai mire par kaaT kar
jab bhī maiñ himmat juTā kar kartā huuñ iz.hār-e-'ishq
bolne lagtī hai paglī baat aksar kaaT kar
kitnī āsānī se karte haiñ vo puurī ḳhvāhisheñ
maa.ī patthar dil pe rakh kar baabā patthar kaaT kar
aaj phir pīchhe paḌā hai qāfila fir.aun kā
ai mire rahbar banā rasta samundar kaaT kar
ai 'atā' zāhir to kar bechainiyoñ ke raaz kuchh
likh rahā hai naam kis kā tū barābar kaaT kar
'umr guzri hai teri galiyon ke chakkar kaT kar
kyon na likhkhun KHud ko majnun main suKHanwar kaT kar
jaane ye kaisi shararat aaj sujhi hai use
wo mujhe uDne ko kahti hai mere par kaT kar
jab bhi main himmat juTa kar karta hun izhaar-e-'ishq
bolne lagti hai pagli baat aksar kaT kar
kitni aasani se karte hain wo puri KHwahishen
mai patthar dil pe rakh kar baba patthar kaT kar
aaj phir pichhe paDa hai qafila firaun ka
ai mere rahbar bana rasta samundar kaT kar
ai 'ata' zahir to kar bechainiyon ke raaz kuchh
likh raha hai nam kis ka tu barabar kaT kar

kisī ke hijr ke saa.e meñ aa khaḌā huuñ maiñ
'ajīb dukh hai mirā chhāñv meñ jalā huuñ maiñ
abhī to saañs hai baaqī zarā bachā huuñ maiñ
vo kab talak nahīñ aa.egā dekhtā huuñ maiñ
maiñ sar pe gaThrī ġhamoñ kī uThā.e phirtā huuñ
ab ahl-e-'ilm kaheñge ki sar-phirā huuñ maiñ
bas is liye ki tirā hausla na maañd paḌe
bas is liye hī to kahtā huuñ ab nayā huuñ maiñ
bas is liye ki mujhe kah ke sochnā na paḌe
hamesha soch-samajh kar hī boltā huuñ maiñ
ab is se qabl ta'āruf maiñ apnā pesh karūñ
harīf pahle batā dete haiñ 'atā' huuñ maiñ
kisi ke hijr ke sae mein aa khaDa hun main
'ajib dukh hai mera chhanw mein jala hun main
abhi to sans hai baqi zara bacha hun main
wo kab talak nahin aaega dekhta hun main
main sar pe gaThri ghamon ki uThae phirta hun
ab ahl-e-'ilm kahenge ki sar-phira hun main
bas is liye ki tera hausla na mand paDe
bas is liye hi to kahta hun ab naya hun main
bas is liye ki mujhe kah ke sochna na paDe
hamesha soch-samajh kar hi bolta hun main
ab is se qabl ta'aruf main apna pesh karun
harif pahle bata dete hain 'ata' hun main

ab vo sab kuchh kar rahe haiñ dostī kī aaḌ meñ
ġhair mumkin thā jo shāyad dushmanī kī aaḌ meñ
is qadar naḳhre na kar ai maut aa jā sāmne
kab talak chhup kar rahegī zindagī kī aaḌ meñ
aaj ik mahfil meñ jab us se nazar Takrā ga.ī
ham ne kah dī dil kī bāteñ shā.erī kī aaḌ meñ
ik salīqe se kiyā hai phuul de kar phuul ko
ishq kā iz.hār chaudah farvarī kī aaḌ meñ
pichhlī shab kā vāqi.a ab kyā batā.ūñ dostoñ
chuum aaya chāñd ko maiñ tīrgī kī aaḌ meñ
ab wo sab kuchh kar rahe hain dosti ki aaD mein
ghair mumkin tha jo shayad dushmani ki aaD mein
is qadar naKHre na kar ai maut aa ja samne
kab talak chhup kar rahegi zindagi ki aaD mein
aaj ek mahfil mein jab us se nazar Takra gai
hum ne kah di dil ki baaten shaeri ki aaD mein
ek saliqe se kiya hai phul de kar phul ko
ishq ka izhaar chaudah farwari ki aaD mein
pichhli shab ka waqia ab kya bataun doston
chum aaya chand ko main tirgi ki aaD mein

har zulm tirā yaad hai bhūlā to nahīñ huuñ
ai va.ada-farāmosh maiñ tujh sā to nahīñ huuñ
ai vaqt miTānā mujhe āsān nahīñ hai
insāñ huuñ koī naqsh-e-kaf-e-pā to nahīñ huuñ
chup-chāp sahī maslahatan vaqt ke hāthoñ
majbūr sahī vaqt se haarā to nahīñ huuñ
ye din to mujhe un ke taġhāful ne dikhā.e
maiñ gardish-e-daurāñ tirā maarā to nahīñ huuñ
un ke liye laḌ jā.ūñgā taqdīr maiñ tujh se
hālāñki kabhī tujh se maiñ uljhā to nahīñ huuñ
sāhil pe khaḌe ho tumheñ kyā ġham chale jaanā
maiñ Duub rahā huuñ abhī Duubā to nahīñ huuñ
kyoñ shor bapā hai zarā dekho to nikal kar
maiñ us kī galī se abhī guzrā to nahīñ huuñ
'muztar' mujhe kyoñ dekhtā rahtā hai zamāna
dīvāna sahī un kā tamāshā to nahīñ huuñ
har zulm tera yaad hai bhula to nahin hun
ai wada-faramosh main tujh sa to nahin hun
ai waqt miTana mujhe aasan nahin hai
insan hun koi naqsh-e-kaf-e-pa to nahin hun
chup-chap sahi maslahatan waqt ke hathon
majbur sahi waqt se haara to nahin hun
ye din to mujhe un ke taghaful ne dikhae
main gardish-e-dauran tera mara to nahin hun
un ke liye laD jaunga taqdir main tujh se
haalanki kabhi tujh se main uljha to nahin hun
sahil pe khaDe ho tumhein kya gham chale jaana
main Dub raha hun abhi Duba to nahin hun
kyon shor bapa hai zara dekho to nikal kar
main us ki gali se abhi guzra to nahin hun
'muztar' mujhe kyon dekhta rahta hai zamana
diwana sahi un ka tamasha to nahin hun

jo bhī hai hasb-e-hāl khīñcheñge
us kā naqsha kamāl khīñcheñge
chuTkī kāTegī vo sharārat se
aur ham us ke baal khīñcheñge
tujh ko mujh se milāne vaale log
donoñ jānib se maal khīñcheñge
yaar lamhoñ meñ sāmne hogā
is tarah māh-o-sāl khīñcheñge
bharne vaalā hai ye mohabbat se
vaqt par apnā jaal khīñcheñge
koī cigarette mazā na degā to phir
capstan paal mall khīñcheñge
dene hoñge javāb āḳhir-kār
tujh ko mere savāl khīñcheñge
zaḳhm ġhurbat ke sab raqam kar ke
karb-e-qaht-ur-rijāl khīñcheñge
āḳhir aanā paḌegā mere liye
tujh ko mere ḳhayāl khīñcheñge
gar ye mumkin huā to apnī taraf
ek do ḳhush-ḳhisāl khīñcheñge
itne bigḌe haiñ Dar nahīñ baaqī
kyā baḌe apne gaal khīñcheñge
merī ġhurbat milegī virse meñ
is ko mere ayaal khīñcheñge
toḌ deñ Dor hijr kī 'ābid'
kab talak ye vabāl khīñcheñge
jo bhi hai hasb-e-haal khinchenge
us ka naqsha kamal khinchenge
chuTki kaTegi wo shararat se
aur hum us ke baal khinchenge
tujh ko mujh se milane wale log
donon jaanib se mal khinchenge
yar lamhon mein samne hoga
is tarah mah-o-sal khinchenge
bharne wala hai ye mohabbat se
waqt par apna jal khinchenge
koi cigarette maza na dega to phir
capstan pal mall khinchenge
dene honge jawab aaKHir-kar
tujh ko mere sawal khinchenge
zaKHm ghurbat ke sab raqam kar ke
karb-e-qaht-ur-rijal khinchenge
aaKHir aana paDega mere liye
tujh ko mere KHayal khinchenge
gar ye mumkin hua to apni taraf
ek do KHush-KHisal khinchenge
itne bigDe hain Dar nahin baqi
kya baDe apne gal khinchenge
meri ghurbat milegi wirse mein
is ko mere ayal khinchenge
toD den Dor hijr ki 'abid'
kab talak ye wabaal khinchenge

baa'd marne ke koī bosa-e-ruḳhsat degā
kyā ḳhudā mujh ko bhī aisī bhalī qismat degā
zindagī hai ye miyāñ ranj-o-alam to hoñge
jo guzāregā vo lāzim hai ki qīmat degā
farzī duniyā se nikal aur haqīqat likh de
she'r parvāz karegā tujhe 'izzat degā
dekh māyūs na ho kufr nahīñ kar pyāre
be-dilī chhoḌ ḳhudā tujh ko bhī rāhat degā
kar ga.ī 'umr akārat mirī haa.e haa.e
ik ġhalat-fahmī ki tū mujh ko mohabbat degā
kul milā ke hai asāsa mirā ye umr-e-ravāñ
rad nahīñ hogī du'ā rab mirā barakat degā
maiñ to samjhā thā mohabbat kā bulāvā hai 'umar'
kyā ḳhabar thī vo mujhe maut kī dāvat degā
ba'd marne ke koi bosa-e-ruKHsat dega
kya KHuda mujh ko bhi aisi bhali qismat dega
zindagi hai ye miyan ranj-o-alam to honge
jo guzarega wo lazim hai ki qimat dega
farzi duniya se nikal aur haqiqat likh de
she'r parwaz karega tujhe 'izzat dega
dekh mayus na ho kufr nahin kar pyare
be-dili chhoD KHuda tujh ko bhi rahat dega
kar gai 'umr akarat meri hae hae
ek ghalat-fahmi ki tu mujh ko mohabbat dega
kul mila ke hai asasa mera ye umr-e-rawan
rad nahin hogi du'a rab mera barakat dega
main to samjha tha mohabbat ka bulawa hai 'umar'
kya KHabar thi wo mujhe maut ki dawat dega

burā hī kyā thā jo aap apnī misāl hote kamāl hote
kisī tarah se jo TuuTe rishte bahāl hote kamāl hote
ye lailā majnūñ ye hiir rāñjhā ye shīrīñ farhād kī mohabbat
thī aisī shiddat kahīñ jo un ke visāl hote kamāl hote
paḌhā nahīñ thā nisāb-e-ulfat amal meñ aage the har kisī se
samajhtī duniyā agar hameñ be-misāl hote kamāl hote
vo mujh se miltā ḳhamosh rahtā ḳhamoshiyoñ par hī daad paatā
magar jo nazroñ se munfarid se savāl hote kamāl hote
ye kyā ki tanhā.iyoñ se rishta banā ke ḳhud ko gañvā liyā hai
samā ke mujh meñ jo aap merā jamāl hote kamāl hote
jise bhī dekhā usī ko da.avā-e-husn karte sunā gayā hai
jahān bhar meñ hasīñ agar ḳhāl-ḳhāl hote kamāl hote
nasīb apnā suḳhanvaroñ meñ hamārī gintī na ho sakegī
'umar' adākār ham agar bā-kamāl hote kamāl hote
bura hi kya tha jo aap apni misal hote kamal hote
kisi tarah se jo TuTe rishte bahaal hote kamal hote
ye laila majnun ye hir ranjha ye shirin farhad ki mohabbat
thi aisi shiddat kahin jo un ke visal hote kamal hote
paDha nahin tha nisab-e-ulfat amal mein aage the har kisi se
samajhti duniya agar hamein be-misal hote kamal hote
wo mujh se milta KHamosh rahta KHamoshiyon par hi dad pata
magar jo nazron se munfarid se sawal hote kamal hote
ye kya ki tanhaiyon se rishta bana ke KHud ko ganwa liya hai
sama ke mujh mein jo aap mera jamal hote kamal hote
jise bhi dekha usi ko dawa-e-husn karte suna gaya hai
jahan bhar mein hasin agar KHal-KHal hote kamal hote
nasib apna suKHanwaron mein hamari ginti na ho sakegi
'umar' adakar hum agar ba-kamal hote kamal hote

ye kyā paḌī hai tujhe dil jaloñ meñ baiThne kī
ye umr to hai miyāñ dostoñ meñ baiThne kī
chhupā.ī jaatī nahīñ zardiyāñ so duur huuñ maiñ
vagarna hotī hai ḳhvāhish guloñ meñ baiThne kī
shumār merā bhī karte haiñ log in meñ magar
mirī majāl kahāñ shā.iroñ meñ baiThne kī
abhī na uñglī uThā mujh pe thoḌī mohlat de
tamīz siikh rahā huuñ baḌoñ meñ baiThne kī
mujhe badal ke koī aur hī banā diyā hai
ki intihā hai ye sūrat-garoñ meñ baiThne kī
dikhā rahe haiñ tavātur se ḳhāmiyāñ merī
bhagat rahā huuñ sazā ā.inoñ meñ baiThne kī
nahīñ majāl kisī kī ki muntashir kar de
banā chuke haiñ jo aadat safoñ meñ baiThne kī
ḳhazāne luTte raheñge ye ḳhālī hone tak
ujaaḌ degī ye aadat gharoñ meñ baiThne kī
ḳhudā atā kare ohda baḌā ġharīb ko aur
badal sake na vo ḳhū naukaroñ meñ baiThne kī
ḳhushāmadī nahīñ rakhtā hai apne kaam se kaam
to kyā paḌī hai tujhe afsaroñ meñ baiThne kī
ye dil scan karānā bahut zarūrī hai
ki ittilā.a hai tire dhaḌkanoñ meñ baiThne kī
hayāt sū-e-adam le ke jā rahī haiñ 'umar'
jo ādateñ haiñ ga.e mausamoñ meñ baiThne kī
ye kya paDi hai tujhe dil jalon mein baiThne ki
ye umr to hai miyan doston mein baiThne ki
chhupai jati nahin zardiyan so dur hun main
wagarna hoti hai KHwahish gulon mein baiThne ki
shumar mera bhi karte hain log in mein magar
meri majal kahan shairon mein baiThne ki
abhi na ungli uTha mujh pe thoDi mohlat de
tamiz sikh raha hun baDon mein baiThne ki
mujhe badal ke koi aur hi bana diya hai
ki intiha hai ye surat-garon mein baiThne ki
dikha rahe hain tawatur se KHamiyan meri
bhagat raha hun saza aainon mein baiThne ki
nahin majal kisi ki ki muntashir kar de
bana chuke hain jo aadat safon mein baiThne ki
KHazane luTte rahenge ye KHali hone tak
ujaD degi ye aadat gharon mein baiThne ki
KHuda ata kare ohda baDa gharib ko aur
badal sake na wo KHu naukaron mein baiThne ki
KHushamadi nahin rakhta hai apne kaam se kaam
to kya paDi hai tujhe afsaron mein baiThne ki
ye dil scan karana bahut zaruri hai
ki ittilaa hai tere dhaDkanon mein baiThne ki
hayat su-e-adam le ke ja rahi hain 'umar'
jo aadaten hain gae mausamon mein baiThne ki

varaq vahī thā magar dūsrī parat chāhī
ki maiñ ne us kī mohabbat se manfa.at chāhī
mazā ajab thā mohabbat bharī laḌā.ī meñ
ki chheḌ kar use faurī muzāhimat chāhī
bichhaḌte vaqt use muḌ ke bhī nahīñ dekhā
tamām umr judā.ī meñ āfiyat chāhī
maiñ aur hī thā judā hī thā is zamāne se
aur us ne qais ke jaisī mutābaqat chāhī
ḳhud apnī ziist ko barbād kar liyā āḳhir
ki jis ne mujh se zarā bhī munāfiqat chāhī
na jaane kyoñ mujhe Thukrā diyā zamāne ne
na sīm-o-zar kī talab kī na saltanat chāhī
bas ek baar mujhe khol kar paḌhā 'ābid'
phir us ne merī mohabbat se ma.azarat chāhī
waraq wahi tha magar dusri parat chahi
ki main ne us ki mohabbat se manfat chahi
maza ajab tha mohabbat bhari laDai mein
ki chheD kar use fauri muzahimat chahi
bichhaDte waqt use muD ke bhi nahin dekha
tamam umr judai mein aafiyat chahi
main aur hi tha juda hi tha is zamane se
aur us ne qais ke jaisi mutabaqat chahi
KHud apni zist ko barbaad kar liya aaKHir
ki jis ne mujh se zara bhi munafiqat chahi
na jaane kyon mujhe Thukra diya zamane ne
na sim-o-zar ki talab ki na saltanat chahi
bas ek bar mujhe khol kar paDha 'abid'
phir us ne meri mohabbat se mazarat chahi

yuuñ tirī raah meñ paḌe hue haiñ
jaise dargāh meñ paḌe hue haiñ
ġham haiñ jitne bhī is zamāne ke
merī ik aah meñ paḌe hue haiñ
mere bachchoñ ke ḳhvāb to filhāl
chhoTī tanḳhvāh meñ paḌe hue haiñ
bach ke nikle jo maut ke muñh se
yād-e-allāh meñ paḌe hue haiñ
kab kisī kī huī hai ye duniyā
ham abas chaah meñ paḌe hue haiñ
ḳhaak honā nasīb hai lekin
hashmat-o-jāh meñ paḌe hue haiñ
ik nazar ham pe mahvish-e-āzam
tere kunjāh meñ paḌe hue haiñ
kuchh ġharaz hī nahīñ jise ham se
us kī parvāh meñ paḌe hue haiñ
jin ko zindāñ meñ honā chāhiye thā
hujra-e-shāh meñ paḌe hue haiñ
aap se ham-kalām hai 'ābid'
log kyoñ vaah meñ paḌe hue haiñ
yun teri rah mein paDe hue hain
jaise dargah mein paDe hue hain
gham hain jitne bhi is zamane ke
meri ek aah mein paDe hue hain
mere bachchon ke KHwab to filhaal
chhoTi tanKHwah mein paDe hue hain
bach ke nikle jo maut ke munh se
yaad-e-allah mein paDe hue hain
kab kisi ki hui hai ye duniya
hum abas chah mein paDe hue hain
KHak hona nasib hai lekin
hashmat-o-jah mein paDe hue hain
ek nazar hum pe mahwish-e-azam
tere kunjah mein paDe hue hain
kuchh gharaz hi nahin jise hum se
us ki parwah mein paDe hue hain
jin ko zindan mein hona chahiye tha
hujra-e-shah mein paDe hue hain
aap se ham-kalam hai 'abid'
log kyon wah mein paDe hue hain

mujh aise shaḳhs kī hājat-ravā.ī karte hue
bhaTak gayā thā vo kār-e-ḳhudā.ī karte hue
ki bātoñ bātoñ meñ manzil se duur le gayā thā
vo nā-ḳhudā-e-suḳhan rahnumā.ī karte hue
abhī hai vaise kā vaisā hī haal andar kā
ki umr Dhal ga.ī dil kī safā.ī karte hue
nisāb-e-ishq abhī tak hai māvarā-e-ḳhirad
ki tiis saal hue haiñ paḌhā.ī karte hue
halāl luqma khilānā hai apne bachchoñ ko
hamesha soch ye rakkhī kamā.ī karte hue
vo khel baiThā mohabbat se phir mohabbat ne
javābī vaar kiyā kāravā.ī karte hue
na koī dukh kā ta.assur na thī pashemānī
malāl tak na huā bevafā.ī karte hue
diyā palaT ke sahārā sisaktī beTī ne
ki baap girne lagā thā vidā.ī karte hue
taḌap ke rakh diye āñkhoñ pe merī haath us ne
maiñ zaḳhm dekh rahā thā silā.ī karte hue
jo mo'atabar gine jaate the vo bhī paa.e ga.e
ġhalat jagah pe ġhalat ham-navā.ī karte hue
ḳhulūs raas na aayā 'umar' ki jo bhī milā
daġhā hī detā gayā bhaa.ī bhaa.ī karte hue
mujh aise shaKHs ki hajat-rawai karte hue
bhaTak gaya tha wo kar-e-KHudai karte hue
ki baaton baaton mein manzil se dur le gaya tha
wo na-KHuda-e-suKHan rahnumai karte hue
abhi hai waise ka waisa hi haal andar ka
ki umr Dhal gai dil ki safai karte hue
nisab-e-ishq abhi tak hai mawara-e-KHirad
ki tis sal hue hain paDhai karte hue
halal luqma khilana hai apne bachchon ko
hamesha soch ye rakkhi kamai karte hue
wo khel baiTha mohabbat se phir mohabbat ne
jawabi war kiya karawai karte hue
na koi dukh ka tassur na thi pashemani
malal tak na hua bewafai karte hue
diya palaT ke sahaara sisakti beTi ne
ki bap girne laga tha widai karte hue
taDap ke rakh diye aankhon pe meri hath us ne
main zaKHm dekh raha tha silai karte hue
jo mo'atabar gine jate the wo bhi pae gae
ghalat jagah pe ghalat ham-nawai karte hue
KHulus ras na aaya 'umar' ki jo bhi mila
dagha hi deta gaya bhai bhai karte hue

vafā kī ḳhū pas-e-jāh-o-jalāl rah ga.ī thī
anā ke ḳhol meñ vo be-misāl rah ga.ī thī
khaTak rahī hai na jaane kyoñ aaj bhī dil meñ
jo ek baat darūn-e-savāl rah ga.ī thī
milā jo mauqa to ham fā.eda uThā.eñge
ki pichhlī baar adhūrī dhamāl rah ga.ī thī
janāb-e-qais bhī marne meñ haq-ba-jānib the
ki shahr bhar meñ vahī ḳhush-ḳhisāl rah ga.ī thī
samay kī gard ne ojhal kiye sabhī qisse
magar jo ek thī chāhat kamāl rah ga.ī thī
ġhalat kahā thā ki rāhat milī mohabbat se
ye zindagī to thakan se niDhāl rah ga.ī thī
ye log aag lagāne meñ itne māhir the
musālahat to pas-e-ishti.āl rah ga.ī thī
maiñ oḌhe phirtā huuñ ab june ke mahīne meñ
nishānī us kī jo ik zard shaal rah ga.ī thī
vo misl-e-dard paḌā rah gayā thā siine meñ
so us kī yaad bhī ban ke malāl rah ga.ī thī
kabhī na sochā 'umar' us ko Thes pahuñchegī
use mirī mujhe fikr-e-ayāl rah ga.ī thī
wafa ki KHu pas-e-jah-o-jalal rah gai thi
ana ke KHol mein wo be-misal rah gai thi
khaTak rahi hai na jaane kyon aaj bhi dil mein
jo ek baat darun-e-sawal rah gai thi
mila jo mauqa to hum faeda uThaenge
ki pichhli bar adhuri dhamal rah gai thi
janab-e-qais bhi marne mein haq-ba-jaanib the
ki shahr bhar mein wahi KHush-KHisal rah gai thi
samay ki gard ne ojhal kiye sabhi qisse
magar jo ek thi chahat kamal rah gai thi
ghalat kaha tha ki rahat mili mohabbat se
ye zindagi to thakan se niDhaal rah gai thi
ye log aag lagane mein itne mahir the
musalahat to pas-e-ishtial rah gai thi
main oDhe phirta hun ab june ke mahine mein
nishani us ki jo ek zard shaal rah gai thi
wo misl-e-dard paDa rah gaya tha sine mein
so us ki yaad bhi ban ke malal rah gai thi
kabhi na socha 'umar' us ko Thes pahunchegi
use meri mujhe fikr-e-ayal rah gai thi

ho gayā jaise tirā dīdār pahlā āḳhirī
ho bhī saktā hai kisī kā pyaar pahlā āḳhirī
umr bhar vo shaḳhs apnī baat par qaa.em rahā
aur yuuñ sābit huā inkār pahlā āḳhirī
jis qadar ghāyal kiyā ḳhud sau gunā ghāyal huā
ishq hī to thā mirā hathiyār pahlā āḳhirī
is liye maiñ ne guzārī ziist ho kar mo.atadil
samjhā jaatā hai yahāñ me.aar pahlā āḳhirī
jin kā da.avā thā ki har tūfān se Takrā.eñge
un ko hī lagne lagā āzār pahlā āḳhirī
har taraf hī pārsāoñ kā milā jamm-e-ġhafīr
puurī bastī meñ thā maiñ bad-kār pahlā āḳhirī
chor thā munsif ke dil meñ tujh pe qābiz ho gayā
varna 'ābid' thā tirā haqdār pahlā āḳhirī
ho gaya jaise tera didar pahla aaKHiri
ho bhi sakta hai kisi ka pyar pahla aaKHiri
umr bhar wo shaKHs apni baat par qaem raha
aur yun sabit hua inkar pahla aaKHiri
jis qadar ghayal kiya KHud sau guna ghayal hua
ishq hi to tha mera hathiyar pahla aaKHiri
is liye main ne guzari zist ho kar moatadil
samjha jata hai yahan mear pahla aaKHiri
jin ka dawa tha ki har tufan se Takraenge
un ko hi lagne laga aazar pahla aaKHiri
har taraf hi parsaon ka mila jamm-e-ghafir
puri basti mein tha main bad-kar pahla aaKHiri
chor tha munsif ke dil mein tujh pe qabiz ho gaya
warna 'abid' tha tera haqdar pahla aaKHiri

jo sāf-go hoñ to ūñchī jagah khaḌā milūñgā
vagarna tujh ko kahīñ ḳhaak meñ paḌā milūñgā
tū sāloñ baad bhī mujh ko manāne aa.e to
maiñ apnī ek hī zid par tujhe aḌā milūñgā
tū ḳhud ko yūñhī girātā rahā to āḳhir-kār
maiñ tere qad se tujhe sau gunā baḌā milūñgā
lakīr khīñch ke rakhnā tasallī kī ḳhātir
ki apnī had se na yaksar tujhe baḌhā milūñgā
huuñ bā-vafā to mirā sar nahīñ jhukegā kabhī
jo bevafā huuñ to phir sharm se gaḌā milūñgā
sadāqateñ mirī shādāb hī rakheñgī mujhe
maiñ zard pattā nahīñ huuñ ki jo jhaḌā milūñgā
sitam se bhaag ke jiinā hai maut se bad-tar
barā-e-haq maiñ tujhe daar par chaḌhā milūñgā
jo saf-go hon to unchi jagah khaDa milunga
wagarna tujh ko kahin KHak mein paDa milunga
tu salon baad bhi mujh ko manane aae to
main apni ek hi zid par tujhe aDa milunga
tu KHud ko yunhi giraata raha to aaKHir-kar
main tere qad se tujhe sau guna baDa milunga
lakir khinch ke rakhna tasalli ki KHatir
ki apni had se na yaksar tujhe baDha milunga
hun ba-wafa to mera sar nahin jhukega kabhi
jo bewafa hun to phir sharm se gaDa milunga
sadaqaten meri shadab hi rakhengi mujhe
main zard patta nahin hun ki jo jhaDa milunga
sitam se bhag ke jina hai maut se bad-tar
bara-e-haq main tujhe dar par chaDha milunga

dikhā rahā hai añgūThā falak se taarā mujhe
dhakel de na bulandī se phir dobārā mujhe
mire sivā bhī koī qaid hai ḳharābe meñ
ajiib taur se vo rāt-bhar pukārā mujhe
mire ḳhilāf khaḌā ho gayā hai kaun āḳhir
jo ruup dhaar ke merā hī tiir maarā mujhe
kiyā jab us ne tah-e-āb merī kashtī ko
samajh meñ baat nahīñ aa.ī kyoñ ubhārā mujhe
abhī sameT rahā huuñ maiñ dhajjiyāñ apnī
na jaao chhoḌ ke aise meñ be-sahārā mujhe
dikha raha hai anguTha falak se tara mujhe
dhakel de na bulandi se phir dobara mujhe
mere siwa bhi koi qaid hai KHarabe mein
ajib taur se wo raat-bhar pukara mujhe
mere KHilaf khaDa ho gaya hai kaun aaKHir
jo rup dhaar ke mera hi tir mara mujhe
kiya jab us ne tah-e-ab meri kashti ko
samajh mein baat nahin aai kyon ubhaara mujhe
abhi sameT raha hun main dhajjiyan apni
na jao chhoD ke aise mein be-sahaara mujhe

āñdhiyāñ ġham kī chalīñ aur karb-bādal chhā ga.e
tujh se kaise ho milan sab rāste dhuñdlā ga.e
kirchī kirchī ḳhvāhisheñ āñkhoñ meñ chubh kar rah ga.iiñ
zard mausam aas kī hariyāliyoñ ko khā ga.e
maiñ ki jis ne har sa.ūbat muskurā kar jhel lī
manzileñ aa.iiñ to kyuuñ āñkhoñ meñ aañsū aa ga.e
tere nā aane ke dukh meñ shiddateñ phūloñ ne kiiñ
vaqt se pahle hī sab gajre mire murjhā ga.e
qaht jazboñ kā paḌā vīrāñ se haiñ dil ke nagar
shahr par aaseb shāyad hijr ke mañDlā ga.e
da.avā chāhat kā nahīñ par jab use sochā 'urūj'
phuul ḳhushbū rang taare aañkh meñ lahrā ga.e
aandhiyan gham ki chalin aur karb-baadal chha gae
tujh se kaise ho milan sab raste dhundla gae
kirchi kirchi KHwahishen aankhon mein chubh kar rah gain
zard mausam aas ki hariyaliyon ko kha gae
main ki jis ne har saubat muskura kar jhel li
manzilen aain to kyun aankhon mein aansu aa gae
tere na aane ke dukh mein shiddaten phulon ne kin
waqt se pahle hi sab gajre mere murjha gae
qaht jazbon ka paDa viran se hain dil ke nagar
shahr par aaseb shayad hijr ke manDla gae
dawa chahat ka nahin par jab use socha 'uruj'
phul KHushbu rang tare aankh mein lahra gae

āzmā.ish meñ kaTī kuchh imtihānoñ meñ rahī
zindagī kin rāstoñ meñ kin Thikānoñ meñ rahī
vo to ik halkī sī dastak de ke ruḳhsat ho gayā
ik sadā ras gholtī din-rāt kānoñ meñ rahī
likh ga.ī apne gharoñ meñ ek karb-e-nā-tamām
zindagī goyā hamāre mehrbānoñ meñ rahī
miT ga.iiñ āñgan meñ saarī kheltī parchhā.iyāñ
ek be-kaifī musalsal āshiyānoñ meñ rahī
vo zamīñ kī sarhadoñ meñ hī rahā 'anjum' muqīm
kyuuñ talāsh insān ko phir āsmānoñ meñ rahī
aazmaish mein kaTi kuchh imtihanon mein rahi
zindagi kin raston mein kin Thikanon mein rahi
wo to ek halki si dastak de ke ruKHsat ho gaya
ek sada ras gholti din-raat kanon mein rahi
likh gai apne gharon mein ek karb-e-na-tamam
zindagi goya hamare mehrbanon mein rahi
miT gain aangan mein sari khelti parchhaiyan
ek be-kaifi musalsal aashiyanon mein rahi
wo zamin ki sarhadon mein hi raha 'anjum' muqim
kyun talash insan ko phir aasmanon mein rahi

lahū lahū aarzū badan kā lihāf hogā
vo kitnā buzdil hai aaj ye inkishāf hogā
mirī har ik baat thī haqā.eq kī raushnī meñ
ye jāntā thā zamāna mere ḳhilāf hogā
haqīqatoñ ke charāġh har-sū jalā ke rakhnā
mujhe yaqīñ hai ki jhuuT kā in.etāf hogā
ye ġham nahīñ hai shanāḳht apnī maiñ kho chukā huuñ
tumhārī hastī se kab mujhe inhirāf hogā
na khoj ḳhud ko purāne kal kī kahāniyoñ meñ
purānā kal to shikast kā e'tirāf hogā
hamārī bātoñ meñ koī pechīdgī nahīñ hai
hamārī bātoñ se kab use iḳhtilāf hogā
rumūz-e-ālam pe dastaras us ko hogī hāsil
vo shaḳhs kirdār jis kā shaffaf-o-sāf hogā
sazā ke Dar se abas tū ghabrā rahā hai 'anjum'
qusūr pahlā to har kisī ko muaaf hogā
lahu lahu aarzu badan ka lihaf hoga
wo kitna buzdil hai aaj ye inkishaf hoga
meri har ek baat thi haqaeq ki raushni mein
ye jaanta tha zamana mere KHilaf hoga
haqiqaton ke charagh har-su jala ke rakhna
mujhe yaqin hai ki jhuT ka inetaf hoga
ye gham nahin hai shanaKHt apni main kho chuka hun
tumhaari hasti se kab mujhe inhiraf hoga
na khoj KHud ko purane kal ki kahaniyon mein
purana kal to shikast ka e'tiraf hoga
hamari baaton mein koi pechidgi nahin hai
hamari baaton se kab use iKHtilaf hoga
rumuz-e-alam pe dastaras us ko hogi hasil
wo shaKHs kirdar jis ka shaffaf-o-saf hoga
saza ke Dar se abas tu ghabra raha hai 'anjum'
qusur pahla to har kisi ko muaf hoga

us ke chehre pe tabassum kī ziyā aa.egī
vo mujhe yaad karegā to hayā aa.egī
oḌh kar jism pe yādoñ kī ridā aa.egī
jab bhī maazī ke jharokoñ se havā aa.egī
kaun mazlūm kī fariyād sunegā nā-haq
lauT kar dasht meñ ḳhud apnī sadā aa.egī
kis qadar bikhrā huā huuñ maiñ bichhaḌ ke tujh se
yaad ab kis kī mujhe tere sivā aa.egī
band kamroñ meñ kisī ko bhī ye ehsās na thā
dar khuleñge to bahut tez havā aa.egī
ġhair-mānūs fazāoñ meñ to ḳhush huuñ lekin
jaane kis moḌ pe mānūs fazā aa.egī
naam to apnā gunahgāroñ kī fihrist meñ likh
tere hisse meñ bhī rañgīn qabā aa.egī
zindagī sab se judā guzregī apnī 'anjum'
maut bhī aa.ī to vo sab se judā aa.egī
us ke chehre pe tabassum ki ziya aaegi
wo mujhe yaad karega to haya aaegi
oDh kar jism pe yaadon ki rida aaegi
jab bhi mazi ke jharokon se hawa aaegi
kaun mazlum ki fariyaad sunega na-haq
lauT kar dasht mein KHud apni sada aaegi
kis qadar bikhra hua hun main bichhaD ke tujh se
yaad ab kis ki mujhe tere siwa aaegi
band kamron mein kisi ko bhi ye ehsas na tha
dar khulenge to bahut tez hawa aaegi
ghair-manus fazaon mein to KHush hun lekin
jaane kis moD pe manus faza aaegi
nam to apna gunahgaron ki fihrist mein likh
tere hisse mein bhi rangin qaba aaegi
zindagi sab se juda guzregi apni 'anjum'
maut bhi aai to wo sab se juda aaegi

har shai ānī-jānī hai
jīvan bahtā paanī hai
hijr kī rāteñ vasl ke din
ik dilchasp kahānī hai
husn hai faanī ishq mirā
an-miT hai lā-fānī hai
jo nā-ahl hai un hāthoñ meñ
phūloñ kī nigarānī hai
rahte ek galī meñ haiñ
donoñ ko hairānī hai
sab chalte haiñ Dagar Dagar
ek Dagar an-jānī hai
apnā hai phir apnā lahū
paanī āḳhir paanī hai
'anjum' terī ġhazloñ meñ
sachche pyaar kī baanī hai
har shai aani-jaani hai
jiwan bahta pani hai
hijr ki raaten wasl ke din
ek dilchasp kahani hai
husn hai fani ishq mera
an-miT hai la-fani hai
jo na-ahl hai un hathon mein
phulon ki nigarani hai
rahte ek gali mein hain
donon ko hairani hai
sab chalte hain Dagar Dagar
ek Dagar an-jaani hai
apna hai phir apna lahu
pani aaKHir pani hai
'anjum' teri ghazlon mein
sachche pyar ki bani hai

maiñ Dar rahā huuñ har ik imtihān se pahle
mire paroñ ko huā kyā uḌaan se pahle
mire nasīb meñ rastoñ kī dhuul likkhī thī
na mil sakī mujhe manzil takān se pahle
ye kaun shaḳhs thā chālāk kis qadar niklā
ki baat chheḌ gayā darmiyān se pahle
maiñ us ke dard kā darmāñ to jāntā thā magar
vo kuchh to boltā apnī zabān se pahle
tum us ke ghar kī taraf chal paḌe to ho lekin
koī paḌāv nahīñ āsmān se pahle
khaḌā huuñ aaj maiñ 'anjum' yaqīñ kī sarhad par
ajiib karb meñ gum thā gumān se pahle
main Dar raha hun har ek imtihan se pahle
mere paron ko hua kya uDan se pahle
mere nasib mein raston ki dhul likkhi thi
na mil saki mujhe manzil takan se pahle
ye kaun shaKHs tha chaalak kis qadar nikla
ki baat chheD gaya darmiyan se pahle
main us ke dard ka darman to jaanta tha magar
wo kuchh to bolta apni zaban se pahle
tum us ke ghar ki taraf chal paDe to ho lekin
koi paDaw nahin aasman se pahle
khaDa hun aaj main 'anjum' yaqin ki sarhad par
ajib karb mein gum tha guman se pahle

ho ga.e āñgan judā aur rāste bhī baT ga.e
kyā huā ye log kyuuñ ik dūsre se kaT ga.e
ġham ne har ik rāste meñ khol rakkhā thā mahāz
ham bhī chehre par hañsī kā ḳhol le kar DaT ga.e
nafratoñ kī dhuup jhulsāne lagī har shaḳhs ko
pyaar ke us shahr meñ sab peḌ kaise kaT ga.e
Dar kī jab saarī haqīqat munkashif ham par huī
ḳhud-baḳhud Dar ke sabhī saa.e achānak haT ga.e
kaun jaane kis nasheman par girī haiñ bijliyāñ
kis taraf TuuTe hue tāroñ ke ye jhurmaT ga.e
mo'atabar hone lagīñ jab bazm meñ tārīkiyāñ
ḳhāmushī kī oT meñ ham log pīchhe haT ga.e
ghar se ai 'anjum' zarā bāhar nikal kar dekhnā
log kahte haiñ ki ab tārīk bādal chhaT ga.e
ho gae aangan juda aur raste bhi baT gae
kya hua ye log kyun ek dusre se kaT gae
gham ne har ek raste mein khol rakkha tha mahaz
hum bhi chehre par hansi ka KHol le kar DaT gae
nafraton ki dhup jhulsane lagi har shaKHs ko
pyar ke us shahr mein sab peD kaise kaT gae
Dar ki jab sari haqiqat munkashif hum par hui
KHud-baKHud Dar ke sabhi sae achanak haT gae
kaun jaane kis nasheman par giri hain bijliyan
kis taraf TuTe hue taron ke ye jhurmaT gae
mo'atabar hone lagin jab bazm mein tarikiyan
KHamushi ki oT mein hum log pichhe haT gae
ghar se ai 'anjum' zara bahar nikal kar dekhna
log kahte hain ki ab tarik baadal chhaT gae

har duā hogī be-asar na samajh
aaj nāhaq hai aañkh tar na samajh
ziist mushkil sahī magar ai dost
maut āsān rahguzar na samajh
hausla rakh tū rahrav-e-manzil
thak ke raste ko apnā ghar na samajh
pūjtā huuñ maiñ pattharoñ ke sanam
mere dil meñ hai koī Dar na samajh
jā-ba-jā sun tū merī sargoshī
maiñ fazā meñ huuñ muntashir na samajh
jin charāġhoñ kī lau bahut kam hai
un charāġhoñ ko mo'atabar na samajh
maiñ tahī-dast muflis-o-nādār
tū mujhe dast-e-be-hunar na samajh
maiñ huuñ qaa.il tirī parastish kā
tujh se māñgūñgā maiñ guhar na samajh
terī dastak kā muntazir 'anjum'
shahr meñ hogā koī dar na samajh
har dua hogi be-asar na samajh
aaj nahaq hai aankh tar na samajh
zist mushkil sahi magar ai dost
maut aasan rahguzar na samajh
hausla rakh tu rahraw-e-manzil
thak ke raste ko apna ghar na samajh
pujta hun main pattharon ke sanam
mere dil mein hai koi Dar na samajh
ja-ba-ja sun tu meri sargoshi
main faza mein hun muntashir na samajh
jin charaghon ki lau bahut kam hai
un charaghon ko mo'atabar na samajh
main tahi-dast muflis-o-nadar
tu mujhe dast-e-be-hunar na samajh
main hun qail teri parastish ka
tujh se mangunga main guhar na samajh
teri dastak ka muntazir 'anjum'
shahr mein hoga koi dar na samajh

na.e zamāne ke nit-na.e hādsāt likhnā
udaas phūloñ kī zard pattoñ kī baat likhnā
falak darīchoñ se jhāñkte ḳhushnumā manāzir
zamīñ pe be-zāriyoñ meñ lipTī hayāt likhnā
thakan kā ehsās ho to kar lenā yaad us ko
adhūre ḳhvāboñ kī sar-phirī kā.enāt likhnā
siyāhī kis ne bikher dī kore kāġhazoñ par
ki ujle alfāz khā ga.e kaise maat likhnā
ye kaun us kī kahāniyāñ phir sunā rahā hai
kahāñ se aa.ī hai ḳhushbuoñ kī barāt likhnā
añdhere raste meñ raushnī kī sadā se pahle
ye kis ne kāñdhe pe rakh diyā apnā haat likhnā
ujāle fardā ke DhūñDhtī haiñ thakī nigāheñ
ye kin hisāroñ meñ qaid hai apnī zaat likhnā
bhaTak ga.ī hai chahār samtoñ meñ soch kyuuñ kar
ki zehn-o-dil par lagā gayā kaun ghaat likhnā
kalām terā fasurda chehroñ kā aa.ina ho
tū apne ash.ār meñ har ik dil kī baat likhnā
use ye zid thī ki din ko likhūñ maiñ raat 'anjum'
mujhe na manzūr thā kabhī din ko raat likhnā
nae zamane ke nit-nae hadsat likhna
udas phulon ki zard patton ki baat likhna
falak darichon se jhankte KHushnuma manazir
zamin pe be-zariyon mein lipTi hayat likhna
thakan ka ehsas ho to kar lena yaad us ko
adhure KHwabon ki sar-phiri kaenat likhna
siyahi kis ne bikher di kore kaghazon par
ki ujle alfaz kha gae kaise mat likhna
ye kaun us ki kahaniyan phir suna raha hai
kahan se aai hai KHushbuon ki baraat likhna
andhere raste mein raushni ki sada se pahle
ye kis ne kandhe pe rakh diya apna hat likhna
ujale farda ke DhunDhti hain thaki nigahen
ye kin hisaron mein qaid hai apni zat likhna
bhaTak gai hai chahaar samton mein soch kyun kar
ki zehn-o-dil par laga gaya kaun ghat likhna
kalam tera fasurda chehron ka aaina ho
tu apne ashaar mein har ek dil ki baat likhna
use ye zid thi ki din ko likhun main raat 'anjum'
mujhe na manzur tha kabhi din ko raat likhna

havā chalī hai na pattā koī hilā ab tak
vahī hai ek ḳhamoshī kā silsila ab tak
vo kaun log haiñ kis kī talāsh meñ gum haiñ
hameñ to apnā pata bhī nahīñ milā ab tak
tū apne chāhne vāloñ se āshnā na huī
yahī to tujh se hai ai ziist ik gilā ab tak
kisī kā dāman-e-sad-chāk kyā rafū karte
ki ham se apnā bhī dāman nahīñ silā ab tak
vahī safar vahī taare vahī thakan baaqī
vahī hai bujhte charāġhoñ kā silsila ab tak
purānī baat maiñ kal kī samajh ke bhuul gayā
magar hai zaḳhm tamannā-e-dil khulā ab tak
jise maiñ DhūñD rahā huuñ galī galī 'anjum'
vo shaḳhs mujh se bichhaḌ kar nahīñ milā ab tak
hawa chali hai na patta koi hila ab tak
wahi hai ek KHamoshi ka silsila ab tak
wo kaun log hain kis ki talash mein gum hain
hamein to apna pata bhi nahin mila ab tak
tu apne chahne walon se aashna na hui
yahi to tujh se hai ai zist ek gila ab tak
kisi ka daman-e-sad-chaak kya rafu karte
ki hum se apna bhi daman nahin sila ab tak
wahi safar wahi tare wahi thakan baqi
wahi hai bujhte charaghon ka silsila ab tak
purani baat main kal ki samajh ke bhul gaya
magar hai zaKHm tamanna-e-dil khula ab tak
jise main DhunD raha hun gali gali 'anjum'
wo shaKHs mujh se bichhaD kar nahin mila ab tak

kuchh bhī nahīñ hai paas tumhārī duā to hai
is shahr-e-be-charāġh meñ ik aasrā to hai
hāthoñ meñ mere chāñd sitāre nahīñ to kyā
dil meñ tire yaqīn kā raushan diyā to hai
raste kī mushkiloñ se hirāsāñ hai kis liye
jis kā nahīñ hai koī bhī us kā ḳhudā to hai
kis se chhupā rahā hai tū dil kī kahāniyāñ
vo hāl-e-roz-o-shab se tire āshnā to hai
'anjum' kisī se laakh bahāne kare magar
lekin bichhaḌ ke tujh se vo bikhrā huā to hai
kuchh bhi nahin hai pas tumhaari dua to hai
is shahr-e-be-charagh mein ek aasra to hai
hathon mein mere chand sitare nahin to kya
dil mein tere yaqin ka raushan diya to hai
raste ki mushkilon se hirasan hai kis liye
jis ka nahin hai koi bhi us ka KHuda to hai
kis se chhupa raha hai tu dil ki kahaniyan
wo haal-e-roz-o-shab se tere aashna to hai
'anjum' kisi se lakh bahane kare magar
lekin bichhaD ke tujh se wo bikhra hua to hai

udāsiyoñ kā musalsal ye daur chalnā hai
na koī hādsa honā na jī bahalnā hai
vo aur hoñge milā jin ko raushnī kā safar
hameñ to bujhte charāġhoñ ke saath chalnā hai
ye Dhaltī umr ke raste bahut thakā deñge
qadam qadam pe nayā rāsta nikalnā hai
vidā.a ho ga.ī kah kar ye ḳhushbuoñ kī sadā
gulāb-jismoñ ko ab pattharoñ meñ Dhalnā hai
kisī kā lahreñ manā.eñgī jashn-e-ġharqābī
phir aaj raat samundar bahut uchhalnā hai
mirī shikast meñ muzmar hai terī kotāhī
tujhe bhī merī tarah kal ko haath malnā hai
udasiyon ka musalsal ye daur chalna hai
na koi hadsa hona na ji bahalna hai
wo aur honge mila jin ko raushni ka safar
hamein to bujhte charaghon ke sath chalna hai
ye Dhalti umr ke raste bahut thaka denge
qadam qadam pe naya rasta nikalna hai
widaa ho gai kah kar ye KHushbuon ki sada
gulab-jismon ko ab pattharon mein Dhalna hai
kisi ka lahren manaengi jashn-e-gharqabi
phir aaj raat samundar bahut uchhalna hai
meri shikast mein muzmar hai teri kotahi
tujhe bhi meri tarah kal ko hath malna hai

yahāñ makīnoñ se ḳhālī makān rahte haiñ
mohabbateñ nahīñ rahtīñ gumān rahte haiñ
ḳhudā kare ki sune tū zabān-e-ḳhāmoshī
tire paḌos meñ kuchh be-zabān rahte haiñ
na kiije takiya buzurgoñ kī Dhaltī chhāñv par
kahāñ saroñ pe sadā sā.ebān rahte haiñ
yahī jahāñ hai hamārā jahān-e-gumshudgī
yahī nishān ki bas be-nishān rahte haiñ
mohabbateñ jis ufuq se tulūa hotī haiñ
vahīñ pe mil ke zamīñ āsmān rahte haiñ
tire sulūk ne dhuñdlā diye sab afsāne
ham apne se bhī bahut bad-gumān rahte haiñ
har ek shaḳhs ko majbūr 'aah' mat jaano
ki shīshe bhī kahīñ ban kar chaTān rahte haiñ
yahan makinon se KHali makan rahte hain
mohabbaten nahin rahtin guman rahte hain
KHuda kare ki sune tu zaban-e-KHamoshi
tere paDos mein kuchh be-zaban rahte hain
na kije takiya buzurgon ki Dhalti chhanw par
kahan saron pe sada saeban rahte hain
yahi jahan hai hamara jahan-e-gumshudgi
yahi nishan ki bas be-nishan rahte hain
mohabbaten jis ufuq se tulua hoti hain
wahin pe mil ke zamin aasman rahte hain
tere suluk ne dhundla diye sab afsane
hum apne se bhi bahut bad-guman rahte hain
har ek shaKHs ko majbur 'ah' mat jaano
ki shishe bhi kahin ban kar chaTan rahte hain

mujhe bhī paḌh lo ki harf-e-savāb ban jā.ūñ
varaq varaq huuñ kisī din kitāb ban jā.ūñ
mire baġhair bhī kuchh din guzār le ai dost
na itnā pī ki maiñ terī sharāb ban jā.ūñ
baḌhā na fāsle har roz ajnabī kī tarah
na yuuñ bulā ki maiñ tujh par azaab ban jā.ūñ
kiyā thā tū ne to raushan charāġh kah ke mujhe
ye merā hausla maiñ āftāb ban jā.ūñ
kahāñ ye sochā thā ghabrā ke jis se niklā huuñ
phir ek din usī jangal kā ḳhvāb ban jā.ūñ
bulā rahī haiñ mujhe duur kī havā.eñ 'aah'
ye lag rahā hai ki ḳhāna-ḳharāb ban jā.ūñ
mujhe bhi paDh lo ki harf-e-sawab ban jaun
waraq waraq hun kisi din kitab ban jaun
mere baghair bhi kuchh din guzar le ai dost
na itna pi ki main teri sharab ban jaun
baDha na fasle har roz ajnabi ki tarah
na yun bula ki main tujh par azab ban jaun
kiya tha tu ne to raushan charagh kah ke mujhe
ye mera hausla main aaftab ban jaun
kahan ye socha tha ghabra ke jis se nikla hun
phir ek din usi jangal ka KHwab ban jaun
bula rahi hain mujhe dur ki hawaen 'ah'
ye lag raha hai ki KHana-KHarab ban jaun

mat fikr-e-mudāvā kar ai dast-e-masīhā.ī
dariyāoñ se gahrī hai is zaḳhm kī gahrā.ī
ik manzil-e-hijrat meñ jab yaad tirī aa.ī
rangoñ ko churā laa.ī ḳhushbū ko uḌā laa.ī
har chehra parāyā hai har aañkh meñ nafrat hai
jā.egī kahāñ le kar ai sharm-e-shanāsā.ī
ye kaisā saverā thā kis dard kā sūraj thā
har raushnī zulmat kī dahlīz pe le aa.ī
jab hijr muqaddar hai milne hī nahīñ degā
sūraj kī to yaktā.ī meñ chāñd kī tanhā.ī
ab tum ko bhī honā hai ojhal mirī nazroñ se
detī hai sadā mujh ko vo manzil-e-rusvā.ī
mat fikr-e-mudawa kar ai dast-e-masihai
dariyaon se gahri hai is zaKHm ki gahrai
ek manzil-e-hijrat mein jab yaad teri aai
rangon ko chura lai KHushbu ko uDa lai
har chehra paraya hai har aankh mein nafrat hai
jaegi kahan le kar ai sharm-e-shanasai
ye kaisa sawera tha kis dard ka suraj tha
har raushni zulmat ki dahliz pe le aai
jab hijr muqaddar hai milne hi nahin dega
suraj ki to yaktai mein chand ki tanhai
ab tum ko bhi hona hai ojhal meri nazron se
deti hai sada mujh ko wo manzil-e-ruswai

jāgnā saa.e meñ aur dhuup meñ sonā us kā
us ke ehsās se sābit thā na honā us kā
dil-shikasta ho vo kyoñ sar-phirī bātoñ se mirī
maiñ ne bachpan meñ bhī toḌā thā khilaunā us kā
ik sitam-pesha tabī.at kā pata detā hai
kāġhazī naav ko bārish meñ Dubonā us kā
phir koī yaad chhuḌā letī hai uñglī mujh se
yaad aatā hai kisī bhiiḌ meñ khonā us kā
ek hī TuuTe hue pul ke the raahī donoñ
maut se baḌh ke thā vo duur se ronā us kā
ḳhud-shanāsī kā koī ilm na thā 'aah' use
log miTTī meñ milāte rahe sonā us kā
jagna sae mein aur dhup mein sona us ka
us ke ehsas se sabit tha na hona us ka
dil-shikasta ho wo kyon sar-phiri baaton se meri
main ne bachpan mein bhi toDa tha khilauna us ka
ek sitam-pesha tabiat ka pata deta hai
kaghazi naw ko barish mein Dubona us ka
phir koi yaad chhuDa leti hai ungli mujh se
yaad aata hai kisi bhiD mein khona us ka
ek hi TuTe hue pul ke the rahi donon
maut se baDh ke tha wo dur se rona us ka
KHud-shanasi ka koi ilm na tha 'ah' use
log miTTi mein milate rahe sona us ka

ḳhizr jis se bane us āb-e-baqā se Dariye
lambī umroñ se buzurgoñ kī duā se Dariye
ham-qadam ban ga.e us ke to Thikāna hī nahīñ
aatī jaatī huī be-samt havā se Dariye
niyyat-e-jurm hī hai jurm kā āġhāz yahāñ
jo na kī ho usī nā-karda ḳhatā se Dariye
sāneha rūnumā ho jā.egā shaq hone par
teshe ko rokiye patthar kī anā se Dariye
pattā pattā yahāñ baiThā hai sameTe ḳhud ko
gungunātī huī is bād-e-sabā se Dariye
aur shai haiñ to koī Darne kī hājat hī nahīñ
aap bande haiñ ḳhudā ke to ḳhudā se Dariye
rahmateñ zahmateñ ban jaatī haiñ aksar ai 'aah'
ho na ye sail-e-balā kaalī ghaTā se Dariye
KHizr jis se bane us aab-e-baqa se Dariye
lambi umron se buzurgon ki dua se Dariye
ham-qadam ban gae us ke to Thikana hi nahin
aati jati hui be-samt hawa se Dariye
niyyat-e-jurm hi hai jurm ka aaghaz yahan
jo na ki ho usi na-karda KHata se Dariye
saneha runuma ho jaega shaq hone par
teshe ko rokiye patthar ki ana se Dariye
patta patta yahan baiTha hai sameTe KHud ko
gungunati hui is baad-e-saba se Dariye
aur shai hain to koi Darne ki hajat hi nahin
aap bande hain KHuda ke to KHuda se Dariye
rahmaten zahmaten ban jati hain aksar ai 'ah'
ho na ye sail-e-bala kali ghaTa se Dariye

vo vāhima hai kahāñ ye usuul jaanā thā
mile the us se to phir us ko bhuul jaanā thā
gañvā dī umr kisī rabt-e-rā.egāñ ke liye
hameñ to TūTte rishtoñ ko bhuul jaanā thā
na kaam aa.ī tab-o-tāb-e-fikr-o-fan merī
vo aa.ina huuñ jise sab ne dhuul jaanā thā
vo ḳhushbuoñ ke musāfir the saath chalte kyā
mujhe to sūrat-e-gard-e-malūl jaanā thā
vo sāda-lauh hamāre sivā koī na thā 'aah'
ki jis ne gul-shuda dāġhoñ ko bhuul jaanā thā
wo wahima hai kahan ye usul jaana tha
mile the us se to phir us ko bhul jaana tha
ganwa di umr kisi rabt-e-raegan ke liye
hamein to TuTte rishton ko bhul jaana tha
na kaam aai tab-o-tab-e-fikr-o-fan meri
wo aaina hun jise sab ne dhul jaana tha
wo KHushbuon ke musafir the sath chalte kya
mujhe to surat-e-gard-e-malul jaana tha
wo sada-lauh hamare siwa koi na tha 'ah'
ki jis ne gul-shuda daghon ko bhul jaana tha

sadā-bahār jo the dard vo purāne ga.e
hamāre saath meñ mausam bhī sab suhāne ga.e
tujhe ḳhabar nahīñ tāmīr-e-nau ke pāgal-pan
chhateñ girīñ to parindoñ ke āshiyāne ga.e
jahāñ sarāboñ kā ik mauj-mauj sūraj thā
vahīñ bhaḌaktī huī pyaas sab bujhāne ga.e
bikharne do kisī āvāra yaad kī ḳhushbū
ki bhuul jaane ke bhī ab use zamāne ga.e
us ek naqsh-e-gurezāñ pe dastaras kaisī
havā jo rūThī to rastoñ meñ ham manāne ga.e
vo ḳhud bhī TuuT gayā lams-e-dīda-var se 'aah'
mizāj phuul kā patthar se āzmāne ga.e
sada-bahaar jo the dard wo purane gae
hamare sath mein mausam bhi sab suhane gae
tujhe KHabar nahin tamir-e-nau ke pagal-pan
chhaten girin to parindon ke aashiyane gae
jahan sarabon ka ek mauj-mauj suraj tha
wahin bhaDakti hui pyas sab bujhane gae
bikharne do kisi aawara yaad ki KHushbu
ki bhul jaane ke bhi ab use zamane gae
us ek naqsh-e-gurezan pe dastaras kaisi
hawa jo ruThi to raston mein hum manane gae
wo KHud bhi TuT gaya lams-e-dida-war se 'ah'
mizaj phul ka patthar se aazmane gae

pas-e-sāhil tamāshā kyā hai baḌh kar dekh lenā thā
ki pahle pheñk kar dariyā meñ patthar dekh lenā thā
mukammal jism ik parchhā.īñ meñ Dhal jaatā hai kaise
tumheñ khiḌkī se apnī ye bhī manzar dekh lenā thā
zamīnoñ par utartā āsmāñ dekhā kabhī tum ne
bulāte vaqt us ko ḳhaak kā ghar dekh lenā thā
khulīñ āñkheñ jo ba.ad-az-vaqt to ab kyā talāfī ho
safīna dekhne vaalo samundar dekh lenā thā
charāġh-e-tāq-e-nisyāñ se na jalte ho na bujhte ho
tumheñ ik din havā se bhī lipaT kar dekh lenā thā
liye ik nāfā-e-āhū phire ho dar-ba-dar tum 'aah'
tumheñ us kā sarāpā apne andar dekh lenā thā
pas-e-sahil tamasha kya hai baDh kar dekh lena tha
ki pahle phenk kar dariya mein patthar dekh lena tha
mukammal jism ek parchhain mein Dhal jata hai kaise
tumhein khiDki se apni ye bhi manzar dekh lena tha
zaminon par utarta aasman dekha kabhi tum ne
bulate waqt us ko KHak ka ghar dekh lena tha
khulin aankhen jo baad-az-waqt to ab kya talafi ho
safina dekhne walo samundar dekh lena tha
charagh-e-taq-e-nisyan se na jalte ho na bujhte ho
tumhein ek din hawa se bhi lipaT kar dekh lena tha
liye ek nafa-e-ahu phire ho dar-ba-dar tum 'ah'
tumhein us ka sarapa apne andar dekh lena tha

vo to hai dushman-e-jāñ dād-e-vafā kyā degā
jo kabhī zahr na dai paayā davā kyā degā
kal kahīñ aaj kahīñ apnā safar nā-mā'lūm
koī be-samt havāoñ kā patā kyā degā
is se sar phoḌ ke mar jaao to kuchh baat bane
zindagī ye tumheñ patthar kā ḳhudā kyā degā
ḳhud tumhīñ jism kī dīvār meñ khiḌkī kholo
ek zindān hai sāñsoñ kā havā kyā degā
zard pattoñ kī tarah girte haiñ pal pal aañsū
terā ġham bhī mujhe ab saaya ghanā kyā degā
zindagī naam huī us ke to Darnā kaisā
'aah' ab maut se baḌh kar vo sazā kyā degā
wo to hai dushman-e-jaan dad-e-wafa kya dega
jo kabhi zahr na dai paya dawa kya dega
kal kahin aaj kahin apna safar na-ma'lum
koi be-samt hawaon ka pata kya dega
is se sar phoD ke mar jao to kuchh baat bane
zindagi ye tumhein patthar ka KHuda kya dega
KHud tumhin jism ki diwar mein khiDki kholo
ek zindan hai sanson ka hawa kya dega
zard patton ki tarah girte hain pal pal aansu
tera gham bhi mujhe ab saya ghana kya dega
zindagi nam hui us ke to Darna kaisa
'ah' ab maut se baDh kar wo saza kya dega

koī rukne kī tire shahr meñ tadbīr na thī
mere hāthoñ meñ tirī zulf bhī zanjīr na thī
dekh kar tum ko sarāboñ kā tamāshā sā rahā
ḳhvāb thā ye bhī kisī ḳhvāb kī ta.abīr na thī
so chukā thā kisī ma.asūm farishte kī tarah
us kī āñkhoñ meñ to qātil kī bhī tasvīr na thī
regzāroñ se lagāo rahā yuuñ hī varna
ret par mere liye koī bhī tahrīr na thī
itnī qurbat pe vo begāna rahā kyoñ mujh se
us ke dil meñ koī dīvār to ta.amīr na thī
sar qalam hote rahe naam pe chāhat ke magar
koī rāñjhā na thā bastī meñ koī hiir na thī
aaj fankār hai ik miTTī ke Dhele kī tarah
thī to pahle bhī par itnī kabhī tahqīr na thī
koi rukne ki tere shahr mein tadbir na thi
mere hathon mein teri zulf bhi zanjir na thi
dekh kar tum ko sarabon ka tamasha sa raha
KHwab tha ye bhi kisi KHwab ki tabir na thi
so chuka tha kisi masum farishte ki tarah
us ki aankhon mein to qatil ki bhi taswir na thi
regzaron se lagao raha yun hi warna
ret par mere liye koi bhi tahrir na thi
itni qurbat pe wo begana raha kyon mujh se
us ke dil mein koi diwar to tamir na thi
sar qalam hote rahe nam pe chahat ke magar
koi ranjha na tha basti mein koi hir na thi
aaj fankar hai ek miTTi ke Dhele ki tarah
thi to pahle bhi par itni kabhi tahqir na thi

ab na vo ishq na kuchh us kī ḳhabar baaqī hai
hai safar ḳhatm ik āshob-e-safar baaqī hai
koī aayā na gayā barsoñ se in rāhoñ meñ
ma.arka kaisā sar-e-rāhguzar baaqī hai
jalne paatā nahīñ koī diyā koī jugnū
tāq-e-dil meñ ga.ī āñdhī kā asar baaqī hai
ab bhī kahlātā hai vo shaḳhs to mahbūb-e-nazar
dil dukhāne kā abhī us meñ hunar baaqī hai
āḳhirī sham.a to lo bujh ga.ī jal kar yaaro
is dhueñ meñ magar imkān-e-sahar baaqī hai
sab marāhil se guzar bhī liye kab ke ham 'aah'
habs-e-tanhā.ī meñ mar jaane kā Dar baaqī hai
ab na wo ishq na kuchh us ki KHabar baqi hai
hai safar KHatm ek aashob-e-safar baqi hai
koi aaya na gaya barson se in rahon mein
marka kaisa sar-e-rahguzar baqi hai
jalne pata nahin koi diya koi jugnu
taq-e-dil mein gai aandhi ka asar baqi hai
ab bhi kahlata hai wo shaKHs to mahbub-e-nazar
dil dukhane ka abhi us mein hunar baqi hai
aaKHiri shama to lo bujh gai jal kar yaro
is dhuen mein magar imkan-e-sahar baqi hai
sab marahil se guzar bhi liye kab ke hum 'ah'
habs-e-tanhai mein mar jaane ka Dar baqi hai

sub.h-e-be-nūr na ho dhyān meñ rakh
ek sūraj ko garebān meñ rakh
din meñ kuchh aur huuñ shab meñ kuchh aur
lamha lamha mujhe pahchān meñ rakh
jal bujhā tāq-e-sahar meñ kab kā
ab mujhe shab ke bayābān meñ rakh
huiiñ yaḳh-basta sabhī pichhlī ruteñ
yaad kī dhuup ko dālān meñ rakh
bach ke is shor-e-samā.at se zarā
apne kuchh raaz mire kaan meñ rakh
maiñ kahāñ aur kahāñ bāzār-e-hunar
dard huuñ 'mīr' ke dīvān meñ rakh
abhī ho jā.egā farq-e-gul-o-sang
maiñ huuñ kyā shai mujhe mīzān meñ rakh
subh-e-be-nur na ho dhyan mein rakh
ek suraj ko gareban mein rakh
din mein kuchh aur hun shab mein kuchh aur
lamha lamha mujhe pahchan mein rakh
jal bujha taq-e-sahar mein kab ka
ab mujhe shab ke bayaban mein rakh
huin yaKH-basta sabhi pichhli ruten
yaad ki dhup ko dalan mein rakh
bach ke is shor-e-samaat se zara
apne kuchh raaz mere kan mein rakh
main kahan aur kahan bazar-e-hunar
dard hun 'mir' ke diwan mein rakh
abhi ho jaega farq-e-gul-o-sang
main hun kya shai mujhe mizan mein rakh

ta.alluqāt-e-musalsal bhī tāziyāne the
vo dhāge TuuT ga.e jo bahut purāne the
tire milan se tirā intizār behtar thā
bane na jism jo saa.e vahī suhāne the
sinā.eñ lafzoñ kī sab sat.h-e-sang par TūTīñ
tumheñ ye vaar to phūloñ pe āzmāne the
hamāre baa'd bhī raunaq na aa.ī us ghar par
charāġh ek havā ko ka.ī bujhāne the
bachā na koī musāfir bhī darmiyān-e-safar
na jaane kaun se tīroñ ke sab nishāne the
ye bām-o-dar pe jo chamkī thī dhuup sī ai 'aah'
mirī talāsh meñ guzre hue zamāne the
talluqat-e-musalsal bhi taziyane the
wo dhage TuT gae jo bahut purane the
tere milan se tera intizar behtar tha
bane na jism jo sae wahi suhane the
sinaen lafzon ki sab sath-e-sang par TuTin
tumhein ye war to phulon pe aazmane the
hamare ba'd bhi raunaq na aai us ghar par
charagh ek hawa ko kai bujhane the
bacha na koi musafir bhi darmiyan-e-safar
na jaane kaun se tiron ke sab nishane the
ye baam-o-dar pe jo chamki thi dhup si ai 'ah'
meri talash mein guzre hue zamane the

vo ḳhvāboñ meñ to aanā chāhtā hai
magar nīñdeñ uḌānā chāhtā hai
jise maiñ ne bachāyā zulmatoñ se
diyā merā bujhānā chāhtā hai
use kahnā tumhārā haal sun kar
koī aañsū bahānā chāhtā hai
laboñ se kuchh bhī kahtā hī nahīñ hai
vo āñkhoñ se jatānā chāhtā hai
vo da.ave achchhe din ke karke 'āqib'
hameñ pāgal banānā chāhtā hai
wo KHwabon mein to aana chahta hai
magar ninden uDana chahta hai
jise main ne bachaya zulmaton se
diya mera bujhana chahta hai
use kahna tumhaara haal sun kar
koi aansu bahana chahta hai
labon se kuchh bhi kahta hi nahin hai
wo aankhon se jatana chahta hai
wo dawe achchhe din ke karke 'aqib'
hamein pagal banana chahta hai

Dubo ke mulk se tere hisāb kā sūraj
nikālnā hai hameñ inqalāb kā sūraj
kisī bhī shaḳhs ko laate nahīñ vo nazroñ meñ
bulandiyoñ pe abhī hai janāb kā sūraj
miTā ke zulm kī rakh degā ye tamāzat ko
nikal rahā hai na.ī āb-o-tāb kā sūraj
hai nuur chhāyā huā har taraf zamāne meñ
chamak rahā hai kisī ke shabāb kā sūraj
agar ġharīb kā bebas kā dil dukhā.egā
jalā ke chhoḌegā tujh ko azaab kā sūraj
jabīñ pe aap kī sajdoñ ke gar nishāñ hoñge
lahad ko rakkhegā raushan savāb kā sūraj
ḳhudā kī zaat se ummīd hai ye 'shād' hameñ
ugegā ek din apne hisāb kā sūraj
Dubo ke mulk se tere hisab ka suraj
nikalna hai hamein inqalab ka suraj
kisi bhi shaKHs ko late nahin wo nazron mein
bulandiyon pe abhi hai janab ka suraj
miTa ke zulm ki rakh dega ye tamazat ko
nikal raha hai nai aab-o-tab ka suraj
hai nur chhaya hua har taraf zamane mein
chamak raha hai kisi ke shabab ka suraj
agar gharib ka bebas ka dil dukhaega
jala ke chhoDega tujh ko azab ka suraj
jabin pe aap ki sajdon ke gar nishan honge
lahad ko rakkhega raushan sawab ka suraj
KHuda ki zat se ummid hai ye 'shad' hamein
ugega ek din apne hisab ka suraj

dhuup thī sā.ebān thā hī nahīñ
merā koī makān thā hī nahīñ
maiñ jahāñ jā ke lauT aayā huuñ
us ke aage jahān thā hī nahīñ
tum mujhe chhoḌ bhī to sakte ho
ye to mujh ko gumān thā hī nahīñ
aap ro.e the kyoñ bichhaḌte hue
kuchh agar darmiyān thā hī nahīñ
kaise mushkil kā sāmnā karte
hausla jab chaTān thā hī nahīñ
vaqt itnā burā bhī aa.egā
ye kisī ko gumān thā hī nahīñ
hāl-e-dil kis ke sāmne rakhte
jab koī mehrbān thā hī nahīñ
is zamāne ne kar diyā patthar
varna maiñ saḳht-jān thā hī nahīñ
us pe sab kuchh luTā diyā 'āqib'
jo mirā qadr-dān thā hī nahīñ
dhup thi saeban tha hi nahin
mera koi makan tha hi nahin
main jahan ja ke lauT aaya hun
us ke aage jahan tha hi nahin
tum mujhe chhoD bhi to sakte ho
ye to mujh ko guman tha hi nahin
aap roe the kyon bichhaDte hue
kuchh agar darmiyan tha hi nahin
kaise mushkil ka samna karte
hausla jab chaTan tha hi nahin
waqt itna bura bhi aaega
ye kisi ko guman tha hi nahin
haal-e-dil kis ke samne rakhte
jab koi mehrban tha hi nahin
is zamane ne kar diya patthar
warna main saKHt-jaan tha hi nahin
us pe sab kuchh luTa diya 'aqib'
jo mera qadr-dan tha hi nahin

ham jo guzre hue lamhoñ kī taraf dekhte haiñ
aisā lagtā hai ki sadiyoñ kī taraf dekhte haiñ
jin ko mālūm hai nīñdoñ ke ujaḌne kā azaab
jāgtī aañkh se ḳhvāboñ kī taraf dekhte haiñ
yaad aatā hai hameñ aap kā chehra aksar
ham agar chāñd-sitāroñ kī taraf dekhte haiñ
muntazir hoñge ka.ī din se kisī ke shāyad
log hasrat se jo rastoñ kī taraf dekhte haiñ
us kī ik baar nazar paḌne pe maġhrūr na ban
log bāzār meñ kitnoñ kī taraf dekhte haiñ
aisī tartīb se zaḳhmoñ ko siyā hai maiñ ne
chārāgar ġhaur se Tāñkoñ kī taraf dekhte haiñ
hum jo guzre hue lamhon ki taraf dekhte hain
aisa lagta hai ki sadiyon ki taraf dekhte hain
jin ko malum hai nindon ke ujaDne ka azab
jagti aankh se KHwabon ki taraf dekhte hain
yaad aata hai hamein aap ka chehra aksar
hum agar chand-sitaron ki taraf dekhte hain
muntazir honge kai din se kisi ke shayad
log hasrat se jo raston ki taraf dekhte hain
us ki ek bar nazar paDne pe maghrur na ban
log bazar mein kitnon ki taraf dekhte hain
aisi tartib se zaKHmon ko siya hai main ne
chaaragar ghaur se Tankon ki taraf dekhte hain

merī ḳhvāhish qubūl kar liije
ishq karne kī bhuul kar liije
baḳhsh diije mujhe sabhī kāñTe
apne dāman meñ phuul kar liije
aa.ine ko na dījiye tohmat
saaf chehre kī dhuul kar liije
aap ko koī kyā harā.egā
apne puḳhta usuul kar liije
dil ko lāzim qarār aa.egā
aap zikr-e-rasūl kar liije
meri KHwahish qubul kar lije
ishq karne ki bhul kar lije
baKHsh dije mujhe sabhi kanTe
apne daman mein phul kar lije
aaine ko na dijiye tohmat
saf chehre ki dhul kar lije
aap ko koi kya haraega
apne puKHta usul kar lije
dil ko lazim qarar aaega
aap zikr-e-rasul kar lije

batā.ūñ kyā kisī se dil meñ kyā kyā TuuT jaatā hai
ki jab muflis ke bachche kā khilaunā TuuT jaatā hai
ye merī bad-nasībī hai batā.ūñ kis tarah tum ko
vo jab sapne meñ aate haiñ to sapnā TuuT jaatā hai
bahut hī muztarib rahtā hai vo har pal zamāne meñ
ki jis insāñ kā ulfat se bharosa TuuT jaatā hai
lagā.e laakh chehre par koī chehra magar sun le
bahut din tak nahīñ rahtā mukhauTā TuuT jaatā hai
zamīñ āvāz detī hai mohabbat se mujhe 'āqib'
to merā chāñd chhūne kā irāda TuuT jaatā hai
bataun kya kisi se dil mein kya kya TuT jata hai
ki jab muflis ke bachche ka khilauna TuT jata hai
ye meri bad-nasibi hai bataun kis tarah tum ko
wo jab sapne mein aate hain to sapna TuT jata hai
bahut hi muztarib rahta hai wo har pal zamane mein
ki jis insan ka ulfat se bharosa TuT jata hai
lagae lakh chehre par koi chehra magar sun le
bahut din tak nahin rahta mukhauTa TuT jata hai
zamin aawaz deti hai mohabbat se mujhe 'aqib'
to mera chand chhune ka irada TuT jata hai

na rakkhā kahīñ kā na apnā banāyā
vo kyā chāhte haiñ samajh meñ na aaya
diyā dil to kaif-e-vafā haath aaya
vo kyā jaane jis ne na khoyā na paayā
yahī farz kar lo ki dard-e-mohabbat
na tum ne sunā aur na maiñ ne sunāyā
kaḌī dhuup meñ hai mohabbat kī manzil
zarā der kā hai sar-e-rāh saayā
nasheman ġharīboñ ke ujḌe paḌe haiñ
havā-e-gulistāñ ko chalnā na aaya
'razā' khelnā thā ġham-e-zindagī se
mohabbat ko ham ne vasīla banāyā
na rakkha kahin ka na apna banaya
wo kya chahte hain samajh mein na aaya
diya dil to kaif-e-wafa hath aaya
wo kya jaane jis ne na khoya na paya
yahi farz kar lo ki dard-e-mohabbat
na tum ne suna aur na main ne sunaya
kaDi dhup mein hai mohabbat ki manzil
zara der ka hai sar-e-rah saya
nasheman gharibon ke ujDe paDe hain
hawa-e-gulistan ko chalna na aaya
'raza' khelna tha gham-e-zindagi se
mohabbat ko hum ne wasila banaya

yahī achchhā hai jo is tarah miTā.e koī
aap bhī phir mujhe DhūñDe to na paa.e koī
kaundtī barq na detī ho jahāñ fursat-e-dīd
taab kyā hai jo vahāñ aañkh uThā.e koī
bandisheñ ishq meñ duniyā se nirālī dekheñ
dil taḌap jaa.e magar lab na hilā.e koī
yahi achchha hai jo is tarah miTae koi
aap bhi phir mujhe DhunDe to na pae koi
kaundti barq na deti ho jahan fursat-e-did
tab kya hai jo wahan aankh uThae koi
bandishen ishq mein duniya se nirali dekhen
dil taDap jae magar lab na hilae koi

junūñ bigḌī huī hālāt ke banñe kā gumāñ kab tak
girebāñ jā chukā kab kā raheñgī dhajjiyāñ kab tak
mohabbat-nā-shanāsoñ meñ mohabbat kī fuġhāñ kab tak
na jaane kaT ke dil se kaam degī ab zabāñ kab tak
tahayya kar chuke jis bevafā ko bhuul jaane kā
usī kī yaad āḳhir dil meñ legī chuTkiyāñ kab tak
idhar tinkā uThāyā aur udhar phir barq ne pūchhā
ki phir tayyār ho jā.egā ban kar āshiyāñ kab tak
khule kuchh paikar-e-ummīd yā ye vahm miT jaa.e
nazar ā.eñgī dhuñdlī dhuñdlī sī parchhā.iyāñ kab tak
tumhārī aas par kis kis tarah dil ko na samjhāyā
magar ye ehtimām-e-ḳhud-farebī mehrbāñ kab tak
'razā' kab se yahī fariyād hai bāġh-e-tamannā kī
mujhe luuTe chalā jā.egā merā bāġhbāñ kab tak
junun bigDi hui haalat ke banne ka guman kab tak
gireban ja chuka kab ka rahengi dhajjiyan kab tak
mohabbat-na-shanason mein mohabbat ki fughan kab tak
na jaane kaT ke dil se kaam degi ab zaban kab tak
tahayya kar chuke jis bewafa ko bhul jaane ka
usi ki yaad aaKHir dil mein legi chuTkiyan kab tak
idhar tinka uThaya aur udhar phir barq ne puchha
ki phir tayyar ho jaega ban kar aashiyan kab tak

magar ye ehtimam-e-KHud-farebi mehrban kab tak
'raza' kab se yahi fariyaad hai bagh-e-tamanna ki
mujhe luTe chala jaega mera baghban kab tak

tum ko to kabhī dil se bulānā nahīñ aatā
ham aa ke jo baiThe haiñ to jaanā nahīñ aatā
kah duuñ to maze par ye fasāna nahīñ aatā
Thahrūñ to palaT kar ye zamāna nahīñ aatā
kaahe ko ye phir hosh meñ laane ke Thahoke
jaao tumheñ dīvāna banānā nahīñ aatā
aatī hai bahār aur luTā detī hai daulat
ik phuul kī muTThī meñ ḳhazāna nahīñ aatā
tum ko to ye aatā hai ki yaad aa.e chale jaao
ham tum ko bhulā.eñ to bhulānā nahīñ aatā
maqdūr thā bas ek hī sajda tire dar par
sar maiñ ne jhukāyā hai uThānā nahīñ aatā
aatī hai hameñ sirf mohabbat kī ġhulāmī
ehsān mohabbat kā jatānā nahīñ aatā
phir laakh mohabbat ko 'razā' koī sañvāre
āġhāz-e-mohabbat kā zamāna nahīñ aatā
tum ko to kabhi dil se bulana nahin aata
hum aa ke jo baiThe hain to jaana nahin aata
kah dun to maze par ye fasana nahin aata
Thahrun to palaT kar ye zamana nahin aata
kahe ko ye phir hosh mein lane ke Thahoke
jao tumhein diwana banana nahin aata
aati hai bahaar aur luTa deti hai daulat
ek phul ki muTThi mein KHazana nahin aata
tum ko to ye aata hai ki yaad aae chale jao
hum tum ko bhulaen to bhulana nahin aata
maqdur tha bas ek hi sajda tere dar par
sar main ne jhukaya hai uThana nahin aata
aati hai hamein sirf mohabbat ki ghulami
ehsan mohabbat ka jatana nahin aata
phir lakh mohabbat ko 'raza' koi sanware
aaghaz-e-mohabbat ka zamana nahin aata

jo ḳhud na apne irāde se bad-gumāñ hotā
qadam uThāte hī manzil pe kārvāñ hotā
ye lutf un ke taġhāful meñ phir kahāñ hotā
jo ik latīf tabassum na darmiyāñ hotā
khile haiñ phuul jo aise meñ tum chale aate
ye ehtimām-e-bahārāñ na rā.egāñ hotā
dimāġh arsh pe hai jis kī dhun meñ vo sajda
mire nasīb meñ hotā to maiñ kahāñ hotā
samajh to ye ki na samjhe ḳhud apnā rang-e-junūñ
mizāj ye ki zamāna mizāj-dāñ hotā
bharī bahār ke din haiñ ḳhayāl aa hī gayā
ujaḌ na jaatā to phūloñ meñ āshiyāñ hotā
hasīn qadmoñ se lipTī huī kashish thī jahāñ
vahīñ thā dil bhī 'razā' aur dil kahāñ hotā
jo KHud na apne irade se bad-guman hota
qadam uThate hi manzil pe karwan hota
ye lutf un ke taghaful mein phir kahan hota
jo ek latif tabassum na darmiyan hota
khile hain phul jo aise mein tum chale aate
ye ehtimam-e-bahaaran na raegan hota
dimagh arsh pe hai jis ki dhun mein wo sajda
mere nasib mein hota to main kahan hota
samajh to ye ki na samjhe KHud apna rang-e-junun
mizaj ye ki zamana mizaj-dan hota
bhari bahaar ke din hain KHayal aa hi gaya
ujaD na jata to phulon mein aashiyan hota
hasin qadmon se lipTi hui kashish thi jahan
wahin tha dil bhi 'raza' aur dil kahan hota

kab phuul khileñ shaġhl chhiḌe jāma-darī kā
dīvānoñ ko chaska hai isī ḳhush-ḳhabarī kā
so.e the sar-e-shām khulī pichhle pahar aañkh
muñh dekh ke uTThe haiñ charāġh-e-saharī kā
kuchh apnī taraf merī nigāhoñ se bhī dekho
is ruḳh se bhī ik baab khule ḳhud-nigarī kā
nā-sāz havā-e-par-e-parvāz na ho jaa.e
mausam to gayā ḳhair se be-bāl-o-parī kā
ye chāñd ye sūraj ye añdherā ye ujālā
muñh dekh rahā hai safarī har safarī kā
qaa.em nahīñ rahtī haiñ kisī shai pe nigāheñ
ab koī Thikānā hai pareshāñ-nazarī kā
fitrat hī se miltī hai 'razā' dād-e-suḳhan bhī

na-saz hawa-e-par-e-parwaz na ho jae

munh dekh raha hai safari har safari ka
qaem nahin rahti hain kisi shai pe nigahen
ab koi Thikana hai pareshan-nazari ka
fitrat hi se milti hai 'raza' dad-e-suKHan bhi
jab farz ada hota hai paighambari ka

husn kī fitrat meñ dil-āzāriyāñ
us pe zālim nit-na.ī tayyāriyāñ
muttasil tiflī se āġhāz-e-shabāb
ḳhvāb ke āġhosh meñ bedāriyāñ
soch kar un kī galī meñ jaa.e kaun
be-irāda hotī haiñ tayyāriyāñ
dard-e-dil aur jān-levā pursisheñ
ek bīmārī kī sau bīmāriyāñ
aur dīvāne ko dīvāna banāo
allāh allāh itnī ḳhātir-dāriyāñ
bañdh rahā hai ai 'razā' raḳht-e-safar
ho rahī haiñ kuuch kī tayyāriyāñ
husn ki fitrat mein dil-azariyan
us pe zalim nit-nai tayyariyan
muttasil tifli se aaghaz-e-shabab
KHwab ke aaghosh mein bedariyan
soch kar un ki gali mein jae kaun
be-irada hoti hain tayyariyan
dard-e-dil aur jaan-lewa pursishen
ek bimari ki sau bimariyan
aur diwane ko diwana banao
allah allah itni KHatir-dariyan
bandh raha hai ai 'raza' raKHt-e-safar
ho rahi hain kuch ki tayyariyan

hamīñ ne un kī taraf se manā liyā dil ko
vo karte uzr to ye aur bhī garāñ hotā

jo chāhte ho so kahte ho chup rahne kī lazzat kyā jaano
ye rāz-e-mohabbat hai pyāre tum rāz-e-mohabbat kyā jaano
alfāz kahāñ se lā.ūñ chhāle kī Tapak ko samjhā.ūñ
iz.hār-e-mohabbat karte ho ehsās-e-mohabbat kyā jaano
kyā husn kī bhiik bhī hotī hai jab chuTkī chuTkī juḌtī hai
ham ahl-e-ġharaz jāneñ is ko tum sāhab-e-daulat kyā jaano
hai farq baḌā ai jān-e-'razā' dil dene meñ dil lene meñ

hai farq baDa ai jaan-e-'raza' dil dene mein dil lene mein

vaqār-e-zabt yahī dil ko dil banā ke rahā
jahāñ se dard uThā thā vahīñ samā ke rahā
mizāj-e-yār tujhe kyoñ vo e.atibār thā shaaq
ye aa.e din kā talavvun jise miTā ke rahā
havā ke ruḳh pe sañbhal kar chalī to thī kashtī
magar vo ruḳh thā ki tūfān hī uThā ke rahā
malāl ko thī ye zid ab tirā ḳhayāl na aa.e
ḳhayāl aa ke rahā aur malāl jā ke rahā
tum apne saath zamāne ko le ke badle ho
'razā' bhī badlā magar paas kyā 'razā' ke rahā
waqar-e-zabt yahi dil ko dil bana ke raha
jahan se dard uTha tha wahin sama ke raha
mizaj-e-yar tujhe kyon wo eatibar tha shaq
ye aae din ka talawwun jise miTa ke raha
hawa ke ruKH pe sanbhal kar chali to thi kashti
magar wo ruKH tha ki tufan hi uTha ke raha
malal ko thi ye zid ab tera KHayal na aae
KHayal aa ke raha aur malal ja ke raha
tum apne sath zamane ko le ke badle ho
'raza' bhi badla magar pas kya 'raza' ke raha

darmāñ milā to dard kā unvāñ badal gayā
aaya samajh meñ dard to darmāñ badal gayā
aisī bhī kyā nigāh-e-mohabbat se dushmanī
phūloñ samet rang-e-gulistāñ badal gayā
sāhil pe lā ke TuuTī huī naav pheñk dī
khā kar taras irāda-e-tūfāñ badal gayā
kāfir banā ke kufr-navāzī bhī chhoḌ dī
īmān le ke dushman-e-īmāñ badal gayā
mahfil meñ vo the aur mohabbat pe guftugū
pahuñchā jo maiñ to baat kā unvāñ badal gayā
āzād kar rahe haiñ ziyārat asiir kī
kis ke qadam se ālam-e-zindāñ badal gayā
tum to badal sake na pareshānī-e-ḳhayāl
ham ko 'razā' ḳhayāl-e-pareshāñ badal gayā
darman mila to dard ka unwan badal gaya
aaya samajh mein dard to darman badal gaya
aisi bhi kya nigah-e-mohabbat se dushmani
phulon samet rang-e-gulistan badal gaya
sahil pe la ke TuTi hui naw phenk di
kha kar taras irada-e-tufan badal gaya
kafir bana ke kufr-nawazi bhi chhoD di
iman le ke dushman-e-iman badal gaya
mahfil mein wo the aur mohabbat pe guftugu
pahuncha jo main to baat ka unwan badal gaya
aazad kar rahe hain ziyarat asir ki
kis ke qadam se aalam-e-zindan badal gaya
tum to badal sake na pareshani-e-KHayal
hum ko 'raza' KHayal-e-pareshan badal gaya

ab ham ko kisī se koī shikva na rahegā
jab tum na rahe koī hamārā na rahegā
duniyā meñ rahe silsila-e-husn mujhe kyā
ai vaqt mirā ahd-e-tamannā na rahegā
shāyad koī had sail-e-tamannā kī ho lekin
dhārā to ye kahtā hai kinārā na rahegā
baiThe the ghanī chhāñv meñ is kī na ḳhabar thī

rāt-bhar fasl-e-bahār aane kā sāmāñ honā
sub.h pau phaTte hī hāthoñ meñ girebāñ honā
tum mirā haal na dekho ki mileñgī nazreñ
mujh se dekhā nahīñ jā.egā pashemāñ honā
hijr aur jī ke bahal jaane kī koshish tauba
mushkileñ aur baġhair aap ke āsāñ honā
merī kashtī ko bahar-hāl hai maujoñ se lagāv
ho jo har mauj ko hai shāmil-e-tūfāñ honā
chheḌ dī zulm kī taujīh salāmat rahiye
sharm aa.ī bhī to aaya na pashemāñ honā
apne hī dil meñ khile phuul se kahtā hai 'razā'
tū jahāñ hai use raas aa.e gulistāñ honā
raat-bhar fasl-e-bahaar aane ka saman hona
subh pau phaTte hi hathon mein gireban hona
tum mera haal na dekho ki milengi nazren
mujh se dekha nahin jaega pasheman hona
hijr aur ji ke bahal jaane ki koshish tauba
mushkilen aur baghair aap ke aasan hona
meri kashti ko bahar-haal hai maujon se lagaw
ho jo har mauj ko hai shamil-e-tufan hona
chheD di zulm ki taujih salamat rahiye
sharm aai bhi to aaya na pasheman hona
apne hi dil mein khile phul se kahta hai 'raza'
tu jahan hai use ras aae gulistan hona

qarīb kuchh na milā duur se dhuāñ dekhā
qafas se chhūT ke kyā ḳhuub āshiyāñ dekhā
yahī hai sair faqīroñ kī aur yahī fariyād
zamīñ pe baiTh ga.e sū-e-āsmāñ dekhā
hue tamām jo sajde the duur ke ādāb
yahāñ se aur hai aalam ki āstāñ dekhā
hisār khīñch ke apne hī dil kā baiTh rahe
zamāne-bhar ko mohabbat se bad-gumāñ dekhā
chaman chaman tirī saireñ nazar bahār bahār
chaTak chaTak paḌe ġhunche jahāñ jahāñ dekhā

hisar khinch ke apne hi dil ka baiTh rahe
zamane-bhar ko mohabbat se bad-guman dekha

chaTak chaTak paDe ghunche jahan jahan dekha
harim-e-naz pe wo rang-o-nur ki barish
harim-e-naz mein kya tha ye phir kahan dekha
'raza' ne dil ko saja kar tere tasawwur se
jahan-e-husn mein ek husn-e-do-jahan dekha

raat guzrī phir añdherā chhā gayā
apnā sūraj din chaḌhe gahnā gayā
ham na jaane kaun aalam meñ rahe
vaqt kaaTā jī na bahlāyā gayā
bas yahī thā un ko patthar dil pe naaz
zulm farmā.eñ taras kyoñ aa gayā

biich meñ dil aa gayā maarā gayā

din hai bhārī ġham-e-furqat ke giraftāroñ par
raat kaTtī hai dahakte hue angāroñ par
husn vāloñ kī ḳhudā.ī hai ḳhudā.ī barham
kis ko rahm aa.e mohabbat ke gunah-gāroñ par
phūñk de barq nasheman ko chamak kar na Darā.e
āñkheñ ab rakkhī nahīñ jaatī haiñ angāroñ par
dil kī qīmat nahīñ koī ki yahī ek hai dil
maiñ ne ḳhud chhoḌ diyā mol ḳharīdāroñ par
āshiqī ko jo gadā.ī se milāyā na 'razā'
to ra.ūnat kā bhī ilzām hai ḳhuddāroñ par
din hai bhaari gham-e-furqat ke giraftaron par
