aashiqi ko jo gadai se milaya na 'raza'
to raunat ka bhi ilzam hai KHuddaron par

māyūs ḳhud-ba-ḳhud dil-e-ummīd-vār hai
is gul meñ bū ḳhizāñ kī hai rañg-e-bahār hai
tai ho chukīñ shikast-e-tamannā kī manzileñ
ab is ke baad girya-e-be-iḳhtiyār hai
us bevafā se kar ke vafā mar-miTā 'razā'
ik qissa-e-tavīl kā ye iḳhtisār hai
mayus KHud-ba-KHud dil-e-ummid-war hai
is gul mein bu KHizan ki hai rang-e-bahaar hai
tai ho chukin shikast-e-tamanna ki manzilen
ab is ke baad girya-e-be-iKHtiyar hai
us bewafa se kar ke wafa mar-miTa 'raza'
ek qissa-e-tawil ka ye iKHtisar hai

niyāz-o-nāz kā ye silsila nahīñ jaatā
jafā ko chheḌ ke shauq-e-vafā nahīñ jaatā
khaTak rahī haiñ jo rag rag meñ pairtī phāñseñ
kisī se ek Thikāne rahā nahīñ jaatā
jo aap vaj.h na pūchheñ to ek baat kahūñ
baġhair aap ke mujh se jiyā nahīñ jaatā
ḳhatā muaaf bahut de diyā tumhārā saath
ab apne haal pe mujh se hañsā nahīñ jaatā
ye aur baat hai jab bhī uThā diye jaa.eñ
tumhārī bazm se lekin uThā nahīñ jaatā
ajiib tiir kaleje pe khaa.e baiThā huuñ
ajiib zaḳhm ki jis kā mazā nahīñ jaatā
jahāñ banāte hoñ qismat miTā ke ḳhuddārī
zamāna jaa.e to jaa.e 'razā' nahīñ jaatā
niyaz-o-naz ka ye silsila nahin jata
jafa ko chheD ke shauq-e-wafa nahin jata
khaTak rahi hain jo rag rag mein pairti phansen
kisi se ek Thikane raha nahin jata
jo aap wajh na puchhen to ek baat kahun
baghair aap ke mujh se jiya nahin jata
KHata muaf bahut de diya tumhaara sath
ab apne haal pe mujh se hansa nahin jata
ye aur baat hai jab bhi uTha diye jaen
tumhaari bazm se lekin uTha nahin jata
ajib tir kaleje pe khae baiTha hun
ajib zaKHm ki jis ka maza nahin jata
jahan banate hon qismat miTa ke KHuddari
zamana jae to jae 'raza' nahin jata

aaj yuuñ dil ne un kā naam liyā
jaise girte hue ko thaam liyā
ham ne be-intihā vafā kar ke
be-vafāoñ se intiqām liyā
mujh ko kahnā thā tum se kyā kyā kuchh
tum ne bhī kis nazar se kaam liyā
baat puurī na kar sake un se
jab liyā ahd-e-nā-tamām liyā
jaise pahle kabhī milī hī na thiiñ
un nigāhoñ ne yuuñ salām liyā
vaah zikr-e-habīb kyā kahnā
aah kis be-vafā kā naam liyā
thā to un se gila 'razā' lekin
apne hī dil se intiqām liyā
aaj yun dil ne un ka nam liya
jaise girte hue ko tham liya
hum ne be-intiha wafa kar ke
be-wafaon se intiqam liya
mujh ko kahna tha tum se kya kya kuchh
tum ne bhi kis nazar se kaam liya
baat puri na kar sake un se
jab liya ahd-e-na-tamam liya
jaise pahle kabhi mili hi na thin
un nigahon ne yun salam liya
wah zikr-e-habib kya kahna
aah kis be-wafa ka nam liya
tha to un se gila 'raza' lekin
apne hi dil se intiqam liya

un ke sitam bhī kah nahīñ sakte kisī se ham
ghuT ghuT ke mar rahe haiñ ajab bebasī se ham
yādash-ba-ḳhair dil kā ḳhayāl aa ke rah gayā
is be-dilī meñ jiite haiñ kis be-hisī se ham
jo dil meñ thā vo miltā hai saath apne ḳhaak meñ
tum duur aur kah na sake kuchh kisī se ham
un ke sitam bhi kah nahin sakte kisi se hum
ghuT ghuT ke mar rahe hain ajab bebasi se hum
yaadash-ba-KHair dil ka KHayal aa ke rah gaya
is be-dili mein jite hain kis be-hisi se hum
jo dil mein tha wo milta hai sath apne KHak mein
tum dur aur kah na sake kuchh kisi se hum

qismat meñ ḳhushī jitnī thī huī aur ġham bhī hai jitnā honā hai
ghar phūñk tamāshā dekh chuke ab jañgal jañgal ronā hai
hastī ke bhayānak nazzāre saath apne chale haiñ duniyā se
ye ḳhvāb-e-pareshāñ aur ham ko tā-sub.h-e-qayāmat sonā hai
dam hai ki hai ukhḌā ukhḌā sā aur vo bhī nahīñ aa chukte haiñ
qismat meñ ho marnā yā jiinā ab ho bhī chuke jo honā hai
dil hī to hai āḳhir bhar aayā tum chīñ-ba-jabīñ kyuuñ hote ho
ham tum ko bhalā kuchh kahte haiñ taqdīr kā apnī ronā hai
ġham kaahe kā yaaro mātam kyā badloge nizām-e-ālam kyā
marnā thā 'razā' ko martā hai ye kaahe kā ronā dhonā hai
qismat mein KHushi jitni thi hui aur gham bhi hai jitna hona hai
ghar phunk tamasha dekh chuke ab jangal jangal rona hai
hasti ke bhayanak nazzare sath apne chale hain duniya se
ye KHwab-e-pareshan aur hum ko ta-subh-e-qayamat sona hai
dam hai ki hai ukhDa ukhDa sa aur wo bhi nahin aa chukte hain
qismat mein ho marna ya jina ab ho bhi chuke jo hona hai
dil hi to hai aaKHir bhar aaya tum chin-ba-jabin kyun hote ho
hum tum ko bhala kuchh kahte hain taqdir ka apni rona hai
gham kahe ka yaro matam kya badloge nizam-e-alam kya
marna tha 'raza' ko marta hai ye kahe ka rona dhona hai

soch kyā is kā milā kyā aur kyā matlūb thā
ḳhvāb hī Thahrā tū jitnī der dekhā ḳhuub thā
aag de de kar ba-hadd-e-āshiyāñ ye intiqām
tinkā tinkā kyoñ kisī ko is qadar mahbūb thā
vo nigāhoñ ke payām aur vo payāmoñ kī bahār
dekhiye merī taraf vo bhī zamāna ḳhuub thā
ab to saudā-e-mohabbat hai faqat dīvāngī
varna saudā-e-mohabbat kā bhī ik uslūb thā
kab khulā uqda 'razā' jab kar chuke iz.hār-e-shauq
mudda.ā jaa.ez thā harf-e-mudda.ā ma.ayūb thā
soch kya is ka mila kya aur kya matlub tha
KHwab hi Thahra tu jitni der dekha KHub tha
aag de de kar ba-hadd-e-ashiyan ye intiqam
tinka tinka kyon kisi ko is qadar mahbub tha
wo nigahon ke payam aur wo payamon ki bahaar
dekhiye meri taraf wo bhi zamana KHub tha
ab to sauda-e-mohabbat hai faqat diwangi
warna sauda-e-mohabbat ka bhi ek uslub tha
kab khula uqda 'raza' jab kar chuke izhaar-e-shauq
muddaa jaez tha harf-e-muddaa mayub tha

allāh nazar koī Thikāna nahīñ aatā
aane ko chale aate haiñ jaanā nahīñ aatā
kah duuñ to maze par ye fasāna nahīñ aatā
Thahrūñ to palaT kar ye zamāna nahīñ aatā
yuuñ roz huā karte the be-sāḳhta chakkar
ab aaj bulāyā hai to jaanā nahīñ aatā
tadbīr sī tadbīr duāoñ sī duā.eñ
sab aatā hai taqdīr banānā nahīñ aatā
allah nazar koi Thikana nahin aata
aane ko chale aate hain jaana nahin aata
kah dun to maze par ye fasana nahin aata
Thahrun to palaT kar ye zamana nahin aata
yun roz hua karte the be-saKHta chakkar
ab aaj bulaya hai to jaana nahin aata
tadbir si tadbir duaon si duaen
sab aata hai taqdir banana nahin aata

pahūñchī na dil kī baat hudūd-e-payām tak
baaqī haiñ un pe kitne javāb-e-salām tak
but-ḳhāna-sāz rang-e-zamāna hai kis qadar
chhoḌā na us ne kā'ba-e-ālī-maqām tak
mānūs ho rahe haiñ tirī jalva-gāh se
pahoñche abhī haiñ manzil-e-māh-e-tamām tak
jab tak rahe vo merī nigāhoñ ke sāmne
Thahrī na ek ruḳh se adā-e-ḳhirām tak
dil de ke un ko aap se aise guzar ga.e
jaise ki ham the sirf isī intizām tak
anjām-e-kār shab ke añdhere meñ luT gayā
rakkhā thā kaif-e-sub.h bachā kar jo shaam tak
is tarah kar rahe haiñ 'razā' kā vo tazkira
ḳhālī nahīñ hai tanz se husn-e-kalām tak
pahunchi na dil ki baat hudud-e-payam tak
baqi hain un pe kitne jawab-e-salam tak
but-KHana-saz rang-e-zamana hai kis qadar
chhoDa na us ne ka'ba-e-ali-maqam tak
manus ho rahe hain teri jalwa-gah se
pahonche abhi hain manzil-e-mah-e-tamam tak
jab tak rahe wo meri nigahon ke samne
Thahri na ek ruKH se ada-e-KHiram tak
dil de ke un ko aap se aise guzar gae
jaise ki hum the sirf isi intizam tak
anjam-e-kar shab ke andhere mein luT gaya
rakkha tha kaif-e-subh bacha kar jo sham tak
is tarah kar rahe hain 'raza' ka wo tazkira
KHali nahin hai tanz se husn-e-kalam tak

tarī sūkhe hue hoñToñ pe aa jaane se kyā hogā
bahut tarse haiñ saaqī ek paimāne se kyā hogā
jo āñkheñ dekhtī rahtī haiñ jhuTlāne se kyā hogā
nazar taḌpā rahī hai dil ko bahlāne se kyā hogā
nasheman kī binā rakkhī hai kuchh to soch kar ham ne
chamā-cham bijliyāñ har-sū chamak jaane se kyā hogā
mohabbat ne kahā tayyār kar ke pahlā dīvāna
abhī lākhoñ baneñge ek dīvāne se kyā hogā
hazāroñ inqalāb-e-dard haiñ karvaT se karvaT tak
taḌapte hī raho pahlū badal jaane se kyā hogā
'razā' dekho jo tum un kī taraf se dil meñ kahte the
tabī.at meñ zarā sā inqalāb aane se kyā hogā
tari sukhe hue honTon pe aa jaane se kya hoga
bahut tarse hain saqi ek paimane se kya hoga
jo aankhen dekhti rahti hain jhuTlane se kya hoga
nazar taDpa rahi hai dil ko bahlane se kya hoga
nasheman ki bina rakkhi hai kuchh to soch kar hum ne
chama-cham bijliyan har-su chamak jaane se kya hoga
mohabbat ne kaha tayyar kar ke pahla diwana
abhi lakhon banenge ek diwane se kya hoga
hazaron inqalab-e-dard hain karwaT se karwaT tak
taDapte hi raho pahlu badal jaane se kya hoga
'raza' dekho jo tum un ki taraf se dil mein kahte the
tabiat mein zara sa inqalab aane se kya hoga

ik chaah kī nigāh kā afsāna ban gayā
vo uñgliyāñ uThīñ ki maiñ dīvāna ban gayā
apne hī dil kī baat hai apne kiye kī laaj
kā'ba banā rahā thā maiñ but-ḳhāna ban gayā
allah-re bazm-e-nāz tirī nā-shanāsiyāñ
jis ko kiyā salām vo begāna ban gayā
chupke se un kā naam liyā dil se baat kī
ye kaun sun rahā thā ki afsāna ban gayā
ḳhallāq-e-husn-o-ishq baḌā dil-navāz hai
taḳhlīq-e-sham.a hote hī parvāna ban gayā
duniyā ke taḳht-o-tāj 'razā' Thokaroñ pe haiñ
kyā chiiz apnā ThāTh faqīrāna ban gayā
ek chah ki nigah ka afsana ban gaya
wo ungliyan uThin ki main diwana ban gaya
apne hi dil ki baat hai apne kiye ki laj
ka'ba bana raha tha main but-KHana ban gaya
allah-re bazm-e-naz teri na-shanasiyan
jis ko kiya salam wo begana ban gaya
chupke se un ka nam liya dil se baat ki
ye kaun sun raha tha ki afsana ban gaya
KHallaq-e-husn-o-ishq baDa dil-nawaz hai
taKHliq-e-shama hote hi parwana ban gaya
duniya ke taKHt-o-taj 'raza' Thokaron pe hain
kya chiz apna ThaTh faqirana ban gaya

ba-qadr-e-shauq jo ab un kā aasrā na rahā
ji.e to jaate haiñ jiine kā hausla na rahā
usī ko ham ne manāyā usī ko chheḌeñge
ḳhafā bhī ho ke jo ham se bahut ḳhafā na rahā
ḳhayāl meñ bhī ye aa.e to saañs ruk jaa.e
ki ham se un se mohabbat kā vāsta na rahā
hameñ kuchh un se the shikve magar isī had tak
ki muskurā ke sunā aur koī gila na rahā
ġham-e-firāq zarā sī to aas rahne de
kahīñ mile to kaheñge 'razā' 'razā' na rahā
ba-qadr-e-shauq jo ab un ka aasra na raha
jie to jate hain jine ka hausla na raha
usi ko hum ne manaya usi ko chheDenge
KHafa bhi ho ke jo hum se bahut KHafa na raha
KHayal mein bhi ye aae to sans ruk jae
ki hum se un se mohabbat ka wasta na raha
hamein kuchh un se the shikwe magar isi had tak
ki muskura ke suna aur koi gila na raha
gham-e-firaq zara si to aas rahne de
kahin mile to kahenge 'raza' 'raza' na raha

hai mazāq-e-zinda-dilī yahī isī maslahat ne mazā diyā
na judā ho dil se kasak kabhī vo mizāj-e-dard banā diyā
maiñ abhī kahāñ thā dil-e-hazīñ jo khulī hai aañkh to kuchh nahīñ
mirā farsh-e-ḳhāk to hai vahīñ mujhe arsh-e-ḳhvāb ne kyā diyā
koī haq thā jis kā gila karūñ koī tum se kahne kī baat hai
ki hañsī ḳhushī ke sulūk kā jo rivāj thā vo uThā diyā
mire dard-e-dil kī kise ḳhabar ki ġharīb-e-dil kā payāmbar
vahī rang-e-ruḳh thā kisī qadar jo hañsī meñ sab ne uḌā diyā
hai muġhālta bhī ajiib shai vo na yaad aa.egā tā-ba-ke
jo chhupā ke apne hī zehn meñ ye samajh liyā ki bhulā diyā
rah-o-rasm-e-ishq kī manzileñ vo nazākateñ vo latāfateñ
kabhī lutf āfat-e-jāñ banā kabhī jhiḌkiyoñ ne mazā diyā
vo talavvun-e-dam-e-hosh thā kabhī kuchh bane kabhī kuchh bane
ye junūn-e-ishq kī shaan hai jo banā diyā so banā diyā
ye charāg merī umiid kā ye ghaḌī ghaḌī tirā mashġhala
kabhī duur hī se jalā diyā kabhī paas aa ke bujhā diyā
jo nazar milī to ye soch thā ki savāl aap se kyā karūñ
jo kiyā savāl to soch hai ki javāb aap ne kyā diyā
hai 'razā' ye hasb-e-maqām-e-dil ki payām-e-dil ho ba-nām-e-dil
koī qadr-dān-e-kalām-e-dil kahīñ mil gayā to sunā diyā
hai mazaq-e-zinda-dili yahi isi maslahat ne maza diya
na juda ho dil se kasak kabhi wo mizaj-e-dard bana diya
main abhi kahan tha dil-e-hazin jo khuli hai aankh to kuchh nahin
mera farsh-e-KHak to hai wahin mujhe arsh-e-KHwab ne kya diya
koi haq tha jis ka gila karun koi tum se kahne ki baat hai
ki hansi KHushi ke suluk ka jo riwaj tha wo uTha diya
mere dard-e-dil ki kise KHabar ki gharib-e-dil ka payambar
wahi rang-e-ruKH tha kisi qadar jo hansi mein sab ne uDa diya
hai mughaalta bhi ajib shai wo na yaad aaega ta-ba-ke
jo chhupa ke apne hi zehn mein ye samajh liya ki bhula diya
rah-o-rasm-e-ishq ki manzilen wo nazakaten wo latafaten
kabhi lutf aafat-e-jaan bana kabhi jhiDkiyon ne maza diya
wo talawwun-e-dam-e-hosh tha kabhi kuchh bane kabhi kuchh bane
ye junun-e-ishq ki shan hai jo bana diya so bana diya
ye charag meri umid ka ye ghaDi ghaDi tera mashghala
kabhi dur hi se jala diya kabhi pas aa ke bujha diya
jo nazar mili to ye soch tha ki sawal aap se kya karun
jo kiya sawal to soch hai ki jawab aap ne kya diya
hai 'raza' ye hasb-e-maqam-e-dil ki payam-e-dil ho ba-nam-e-dil
koi qadr-dan-e-kalam-e-dil kahin mil gaya to suna diya

tumhāre naam kā sikka uchhāl saktā huuñ
tumheñ salīqe se maiñ dekh-bhāl saktā huuñ
abhī to sirf bigāḌā hai terī 'ādat ko
maiñ tujh ko ḳhud meñ abhī aur Dhaal saktā huuñ
jo terī zaat se mujh ko mile haiñ ai jānāñ
maiñ un ġhamoñ ko kaleje meñ paal saktā huuñ
mire ḳhudā kī ḳhudā.ī agar navāz de to
samundaroñ meñ bhī rastā nikāl saktā huuñ
maiñ apne 'ahd kā jugnū huuñ dekhnā ik din
baḌe baḌoñ ko maiñ hairat meñ Daal saktā huuñ
agar mile jo ġham-e-rozgār se fursat
to maiñ bhī zehn kā dariyā khañgāl saktā huuñ
paḌegī dhuup jo tum par to abr ban kar ke
tumhāre sar se maiñ sūraj ko Taal saktā huuñ
tumhaare nam ka sikka uchhaal sakta hun
tumhein saliqe se main dekh-bhaal sakta hun
abhi to sirf bigaDa hai teri 'adat ko
main tujh ko KHud mein abhi aur Dhaal sakta hun
jo teri zat se mujh ko mile hain ai jaanan
main un ghamon ko kaleje mein pal sakta hun
mere KHuda ki KHudai agar nawaz de to
samundaron mein bhi rasta nikal sakta hun
main apne 'ahd ka jugnu hun dekhna ek din
baDe baDon ko main hairat mein Dal sakta hun
agar mile jo gham-e-rozgar se fursat
to main bhi zehn ka dariya khangal sakta hun
paDegi dhup jo tum par to abr ban kar ke
tumhaare sar se main suraj ko Tal sakta hun

pahle pahal to mujh ko hichkī aatī thī
baa'd meñ tere naam kī chiTTī aatī thī
baañT liyā karte the donoñ ghar kā dukh
vo bhī daftar thoḌā jaldī aatī thī
kab milnā hai aur kahāñ par milnā hai
copy meñ rakh kar ye parchī aatī thī
ham milte the us se aise mausam meñ
jab sarsoñ ke phuul pe titlī aatī thī
bāġhoñ kī jānib ham dauḌ lagāte the
aam ke mausam meñ jab āñdhī aatī thī
ham bachche bhī kitnā shor machāte the
shaam ko jab bhī gaañv meñ bijlī aatī thī
pahle pahal to mujh ko hichki aati thi
ba'd mein tere nam ki chiTTi aati thi
banT liya karte the donon ghar ka dukh
wo bhi daftar thoDa jaldi aati thi
kab milna hai aur kahan par milna hai
copy mein rakh kar ye parchi aati thi
hum milte the us se aise mausam mein
jab sarson ke phul pe titli aati thi
baghon ki jaanib hum dauD lagate the
aam ke mausam mein jab aandhi aati thi
hum bachche bhi kitna shor machate the
sham ko jab bhi ganw mein bijli aati thi

bhale hī der se tum se kiyā iz.hār shahzādī
magar bachpan se karte haiñ tumhīñ se pyaar shahzādī
kahānī meñ kahānī-kār ne sau rang Daale haiñ
magar is meñ hai sab se qīmtī kirdār shahzādī
nahīñ aatā tumhārā ab koī message ki kaise ho
kahāñ itnī busy rahne lagī ho yaar shahzādī
mirī tasvīr ko tum chūmtī ho be-ḳhayālī meñ
nazar aane lage haiñ 'ishq ke āsār shahzādī
tirī sāñsoñ kī lai meñ jab talak shāmil mirī lai hai
tumhārā kaun ho saktā hai dā’vedār shahzādī
bhale hi der se tum se kiya izhaar shahzadi
magar bachpan se karte hain tumhin se pyar shahzadi
kahani mein kahani-kar ne sau rang Dale hain
magar is mein hai sab se qimti kirdar shahzadi
nahin aata tumhaara ab koi message ki kaise ho
kahan itni busy rahne lagi ho yar shahzadi
meri taswir ko tum chumti ho be-KHayali mein
nazar aane lage hain 'ishq ke aasar shahzadi
teri sanson ki lai mein jab talak shamil meri lai hai
tumhaara kaun ho sakta hai da’wedar shahzadi

agar vo chāhne kā man banātā
qasam se maiñ use dul.han banātā
jhaTak ke zulf añgḌā.ī vo letī
idhar maiñ jhūmtā sāvan banātā
banātā maiñ agar tasvīr terī
surāhī kī tarah gardan banātā
kisī patthar ko pahle kartā mūrat
phir us ke vāste dhaḌkan banātā
banā letā maiñ ḳhud ko raam lekin
ye duvidhā thī kise laxman banātā
jahāñ par ham mohabbat baañT sakte
ḳhudā aisā koī upvan banātā
agar wo chahne ka man banata
qasam se main use dulhan banata
jhaTak ke zulf angDai wo leti
idhar main jhumta sawan banata
banata main agar taswir teri
surahi ki tarah gardan banata
kisi patthar ko pahle karta murat
phir us ke waste dhaDkan banata
bana leta main KHud ko ram lekin
ye duwidha thi kise laxman banata
jahan par hum mohabbat banT sakte
KHuda aisa koi upwan banata

jin bātoñ ko kahnā mushkil hotā hai
un bātoñ ko sahnā mushkil hotā hai
is duniyā meñ rah kar ham ne ye jaanā
is duniyā meñ rahnā mushkil hotā hai
jis dhārā meñ bahnā sab se āsāñ ho
us dhārā meñ bahnā mushkil hotā hai
us ke saath hameñ āsānī hai kitnī
us se ye bhī kahnā mushkil hotā hai
us ke ta.ane us ke ta.ane hote haiñ
mushkil se bhī sahnā mushkil hotā hai
vo sab bāteñ jo tum aksar kahtī ho
un bātoñ kā sahnā mushkil hotā hai
vo bāteñ jo kahne meñ āsān lageñ
un bātoñ kā kahnā mushkil hotā hai
maazī kī yādeñ bhī aisā sūraj haiñ
jis sūraj kā gahnā mushkil hotā hai
maiñ apnī duniyā kā aisā sūraj huuñ
jis sūraj kā gahnā mushkil hotā hai
lagtī hai ye bahr bahut āsān magar
is meñ ġhazleñ kahnā mushkil hotā hai
jin baaton ko kahna mushkil hota hai
un baaton ko sahna mushkil hota hai
is duniya mein rah kar hum ne ye jaana
is duniya mein rahna mushkil hota hai
jis dhaara mein bahna sab se aasan ho
us dhaara mein bahna mushkil hota hai
us ke sath hamein aasani hai kitni
us se ye bhi kahna mushkil hota hai
us ke tane us ke tane hote hain
mushkil se bhi sahna mushkil hota hai
wo sab baaten jo tum aksar kahti ho
un baaton ka sahna mushkil hota hai
wo baaten jo kahne mein aasan lagen
un baaton ka kahna mushkil hota hai
mazi ki yaaden bhi aisa suraj hain
jis suraj ka gahna mushkil hota hai
main apni duniya ka aisa suraj hun
jis suraj ka gahna mushkil hota hai
lagti hai ye bahr bahut aasan magar
is mein ghazlen kahna mushkil hota hai

dhaḌakte saañs lete rukte chalte maiñ ne dekhā hai
koī to hai jise apne meñ palte maiñ ne dekhā hai
tumhāre ḳhuun se merī ragoñ meñ ḳhvāb raushan hai
tumhārī ādatoñ meñ ḳhud ko Dhalte maiñ ne dekhā hai
na jaane kaun hai jo ḳhvāb meñ āvāz detā hai
ḳhud apne-āp ko nīñdoñ meñ chalte maiñ ne dekhā hai
merī ḳhāmoshiyoñ meñ tairtī haiñ terī āvāzeñ
tire siine meñ apnā dil machalte maiñ ne dekhā hai
badal jā.egā sab kuchh bādaloñ se dhuup chaTḳhegī
bujhī āñkhoñ meñ koī ḳhvāb jalte maiñ ne dekhā hai
mujhe mālūm hai un kī duā.eñ saath chaltī haiñ
safar kī mushkiloñ ko haath malte maiñ ne dekhā hai
dhaDakte sans lete rukte chalte main ne dekha hai
koi to hai jise apne mein palte main ne dekha hai
tumhaare KHun se meri ragon mein KHwab raushan hai
tumhaari aadaton mein KHud ko Dhalte main ne dekha hai
na jaane kaun hai jo KHwab mein aawaz deta hai
KHud apne-ap ko nindon mein chalte main ne dekha hai
meri KHamoshiyon mein tairti hain teri aawazen
tere sine mein apna dil machalte main ne dekha hai
badal jaega sab kuchh baadalon se dhup chaTKHegi
bujhi aankhon mein koi KHwab jalte main ne dekha hai
mujhe malum hai un ki duaen sath chalti hain
safar ki mushkilon ko hath malte main ne dekha hai

Thiik huā jo bik ga.e sainik muTThī bhar dīnāroñ meñ
vaise bhī to zañg lagā thā pushtainī hathiyāroñ meñ
sard nasoñ meñ chalte chalte garm lahū jab barf huā
chaar paḌosī jism uThā kar jhoñk aa.e añgāroñ meñ
khetoñ ko muTThī meñ bharnā ab tak siikh nahīñ paayā
yuuñ to merā jīvan biitā sāmantī ayyāroñ meñ
kaise us ke chāl-chalan meñ añgrezī andāz na ho
āḳhir us ne sāñseñ liiñ haiñ pachchhim ke darbāroñ meñ
nazdīkī aksar duurī kā kāran bhī ban jaatī hai
soch-samajh kar ghulnā-milnā apne rishte-dāroñ meñ
chāñd agar puurā chamke to us ke daaġh khaTakte haiñ
ek na ek burā.ī tai hai saare izzat-dāroñ meñ
Thik hua jo bik gae sainik muTThi bhar dinaron mein
waise bhi to zang laga tha pushtaini hathiyaron mein
sard nason mein chalte chalte garm lahu jab barf hua
chaar paDosi jism uTha kar jhonk aae angaron mein
kheton ko muTThi mein bharna ab tak sikh nahin paya
yun to mera jiwan bita samanti ayyaron mein
kaise us ke chaal-chalan mein angrezi andaz na ho
aaKHir us ne sansen lin hain pachchhim ke darbaron mein
nazdiki aksar duri ka karan bhi ban jati hai
soch-samajh kar ghulna-milna apne rishte-daron mein
chand agar pura chamke to us ke dagh khaTakte hain
ek na ek burai tai hai sare izzat-daron mein

ye sochnā ġhalat hai ki tum par nazar nahīñ
masrūf ham bahut haiñ magar be-ḳhabar nahīñ
ab to ḳhud apne ḳhuun ne bhī saaf kah diyā
maiñ aap kā rahūñgā magar 'umr bhar nahīñ
aa hī ga.e haiñ ḳhvāb to phir jā.eñge kahāñ
āñkhoñ se aage un kī koī rahguzar nahīñ
kitnā ji.eñ kahāñ se ji.eñ aur kis liye
ye iḳhtiyār ham pe hai taqdīr par nahīñ
maazī kī raakh ulTīñ to chingāriyāñ milīñ
be-shak kisī ko chāho magar is qadar nahīñ
ye sochna ghalat hai ki tum par nazar nahin
masruf hum bahut hain magar be-KHabar nahin
ab to KHud apne KHun ne bhi saf kah diya
main aap ka rahunga magar 'umr bhar nahin
aa hi gae hain KHwab to phir jaenge kahan
aankhon se aage un ki koi rahguzar nahin
kitna jien kahan se jien aur kis liye
ye iKHtiyar hum pe hai taqdir par nahin
mazi ki rakh ulTin to chingariyan milin
be-shak kisi ko chaho magar is qadar nahin

tū vafā kar ke bhuul jā mujh ko
ab zarā yuuñ bhī aazmā mujh ko
ye zamāna burā nahīñ hai magar
apnī nazroñ se dekhnā mujh ko
be-sadā kāġhazoñ meñ aag lagā
aaj kī raat gungunā mujh ko
tujh ko kis kis meñ DhūñDhtā āḳhir
tū bhī kis kis se māñgtā mujh ko
ab kisī aur kā pujārī hai
jis ne maanā thā devtā mujh ko
tu wafa kar ke bhul ja mujh ko
ab zara yun bhi aazma mujh ko
ye zamana bura nahin hai magar
apni nazron se dekhna mujh ko
be-sada kaghazon mein aag laga
aaj ki raat gunguna mujh ko
tujh ko kis kis mein DhunDhta aaKHir
tu bhi kis kis se mangta mujh ko
ab kisi aur ka pujari hai
jis ne mana tha dewta mujh ko

ghar kī buniyādeñ dīvāreñ bām-o-dar the baabū jī
sab ko bāñdh ke rakhne vaalā ḳhaas hunar the baabū jī
tiin mohalloñ meñ un jaisī qad kāThī kā koī na thā
achchhe-ḳhāse ūñche puure qad-āvar the baabū jī
ab to us suune māthe par kore-pan kī chādar hai
ammā jī kī saarī saj-dhaj sab zevar the baabū jī
bhītar se ḳhālis jazbātī aur uupar se TheTh pitā
alag anūThā anbūjhā sā ik tevar the baabū jī
kabhī baḌā sā hāth-ḳharch the kabhī hathelī kī sūjan
mere man kā aadhā sāhas aadhā Dar the baabū jī
ghar ki buniyaaden diwaren baam-o-dar the babu ji
sab ko bandh ke rakhne wala KHas hunar the babu ji
tin mohallon mein un jaisi qad kaThi ka koi na tha
achchhe-KHase unche pure qad-awar the babu ji
ab to us sune mathe par kore-pan ki chadar hai
amma ji ki sari saj-dhaj sab zewar the babu ji
bhitar se KHalis jazbaati aur upar se TheTh pita
alag anuTha anbujha sa ek tewar the babu ji
kabhi baDa sa hath-KHarch the kabhi hatheli ki sujan
mere man ka aadha sahas aadha Dar the babu ji

kisī aur ne to bunā nahīñ mirā āsmāñ mirā āsmāñ
tire āsmāñ se judā nahīñ mirā āsmāñ mirā āsmāñ
ye zamīn merī zamīn hai ye jahān merā jahān hai
kisī dūsre se milā nahīñ mirā āsmāñ mirā āsmāñ
kahīñ dhuup hai kahīñ chāñdnī kahīñ rañg hai kahīñ raushnī
kahīñ āñ.suoñ se dhulā nahīñ mirā āsmāñ mirā āsmāñ
use chhū sakūñ ye junūn hai merī ruuh ko ye sukūn hai
yahāñ kab kisī kā huā nahīñ mirā āsmāñ mirā āsmāñ
girīñ bijliyāñ merī raah par ka.ī āñdhiyāñ bhī chalīñ magar
kabhī bādaloñ sā jhukā nahīñ mirā āsmāñ mirā āsmāñ
kisi aur ne to buna nahin mera aasman mera aasman
tere aasman se juda nahin mera aasman mera aasman
ye zamin meri zamin hai ye jahan mera jahan hai
kisi dusre se mila nahin mera aasman mera aasman
kahin dhup hai kahin chandni kahin rang hai kahin raushni
kahin aansuon se dhula nahin mera aasman mera aasman
use chhu sakun ye junun hai meri ruh ko ye sukun hai
yahan kab kisi ka hua nahin mera aasman mera aasman
girin bijliyan meri rah par kai aandhiyan bhi chalin magar
kabhi baadalon sa jhuka nahin mera aasman mera aasman

manzil pe dhyān ham ne zarā bhī agar diyā
ākāsh ne Dagar ko ujāloñ se bhar diyā
rukne kī bhuul haar kā kāran na ban sakī
chalne kī dhun ne raah ko āsān kar diyā
paanī ke bulbuloñ kā safar jānte hue
tohfe meñ dil na denā thā ham ne magar diyā
pīpal kī chhāñv bujh ga.ī tālāb saḌ ga.e
kis ne ye mere gaañv pe ehsān kar diyā
ghar khet gaa.e bail raqam ab kahāñ rahe
jo kuchh thā sab nikāl ke fasloñ meñ bhar diyā
manDī ne luuT liiñ javāñ-fasleñ kisān kī
qarze ne ḳhud-kushī kī taraf dhyān kar diyā
manzil pe dhyan hum ne zara bhi agar diya
aakash ne Dagar ko ujalon se bhar diya
rukne ki bhul haar ka karan na ban saki
chalne ki dhun ne rah ko aasan kar diya
pani ke bulbulon ka safar jaante hue
tohfe mein dil na dena tha hum ne magar diya
pipal ki chhanw bujh gai talab saD gae
kis ne ye mere ganw pe ehsan kar diya
ghar khet gae bail raqam ab kahan rahe
jo kuchh tha sab nikal ke faslon mein bhar diya
manDi ne luT lin jawan-faslen kisan ki
qarze ne KHud-kushi ki taraf dhyan kar diya

vahī āñgan vahī khiḌkī vahī dar yaad aatā hai
akelā jab bhī hotā huuñ mujhe ghar yaad aatā hai
mirī be-sāḳhta hichkī mujhe khul kar batātī hai
tire apnoñ ko gaaoñ meñ to aksar yaad aatā hai
jo apne paas hoñ un kī koī qīmat nahīñ hotī
hamāre bhaa.ī ko hī lo bichhaḌ kar yaad aatā hai
saphaltā ke safar meñ to kahāñ fursat ki kuchh socheñ
magar jab choT lagtī hai muqaddar yaad aatā hai
may aur june kī garmī badan se jab Tapaktī hai
november yaad aatā hai december yaad aatā hai
wahi aangan wahi khiDki wahi dar yaad aata hai
akela jab bhi hota hun mujhe ghar yaad aata hai
meri be-saKHta hichki mujhe khul kar batati hai
tere apnon ko gaon mein to aksar yaad aata hai
jo apne pas hon un ki koi qimat nahin hoti
hamare bhai ko hi lo bichhaD kar yaad aata hai
saphalta ke safar mein to kahan fursat ki kuchh sochen
magar jab choT lagti hai muqaddar yaad aata hai
may aur june ki garmi badan se jab Tapakti hai
nowember yaad aata hai december yaad aata hai

mujhe sire se pakaḌ kar udheḌ detī hai
maiñ ek jhuuT vo sachche subūt jaisī hai
maiñ roz roz tabassum meñ chhuptā phirtā huuñ
udāsī hai ki mujhe roz DhūñDh letī hai
zarūr kuchh to banā.egī zindagī mujh ko
qadam qadam pe mirā imtihān letī hai
jo ek phuul khilā hai sahar kī palkoñ par
tumhāre jism kī ḳhushbū usī ke jaisī hai
vo raushnī jo sitāroñ kā ḳhaas zevar hai
amiiq āñkhoñ meñ aksar dikhā.ī detī hai
mujhe sire se pakaD kar udheD deti hai
main ek jhuT wo sachche subut jaisi hai
main roz roz tabassum mein chhupta phirta hun
udasi hai ki mujhe roz DhunDh leti hai
zarur kuchh to banaegi zindagi mujh ko
qadam qadam pe mera imtihan leti hai
jo ek phul khila hai sahar ki palkon par
tumhaare jism ki KHushbu usi ke jaisi hai
wo raushni jo sitaron ka KHas zewar hai
amiq aankhon mein aksar dikhai deti hai

har baar huā hai jo vahī to nahīñ hogā
Dar jis kā satātā hai abhī to nahīñ hogā
duniyā ko chalo parkheñ na.e dost banā.eñ
har shaḳhs zamāne meñ vahī to nahīñ hogā
vo shaḳhs baḌā hai to ġhalat ho nahīñ saktā
duniyā ko bharosa ye abhī to nahīñ hogā
hai us kā ishāra bhī samajhne kī zarūrat
hogā to kabhī hogā abhī to nahīñ hogā
do-chār gaḌe murde ukhāḌeñge kisī roz
har baar nayā jhagḌā kabhī to nahīñ hogā
kuchh aur bhī ho saktā hai taqrīr kā matlab
jo aap ne samjhā hai vahī to nahīñ hogā
har baar zamāne kā sitam hogā mujhī par
haañ maiñ hī badal jā.ūñ kabhī to nahīñ hogā
har bar hua hai jo wahi to nahin hoga
Dar jis ka satata hai abhi to nahin hoga
duniya ko chalo parkhen nae dost banaen
har shaKHs zamane mein wahi to nahin hoga
wo shaKHs baDa hai to ghalat ho nahin sakta
duniya ko bharosa ye abhi to nahin hoga
hai us ka ishaara bhi samajhne ki zarurat
hoga to kabhi hoga abhi to nahin hoga
do-chaar gaDe murde ukhaDenge kisi roz
har bar naya jhagDa kabhi to nahin hoga
kuchh aur bhi ho sakta hai taqrir ka matlab
jo aap ne samjha hai wahi to nahin hoga
har bar zamane ka sitam hoga mujhi par
han main hi badal jaun kabhi to nahin hoga

ye aur baat duur rahe manziloñ se ham
bach kar chale hamesha magar qāfiloñ se ham
hone ko phir shikār na.ī uljhanoñ se ham
milte haiñ roz apne ka.ī dostoñ se ham
barsoñ fareb khāte rahe dūsroñ se ham
apnī samajh meñ aa.e baḌī mushkiloñ se ham
manzil kī hai talab to hameñ saath le chalo
vāqif haiñ ḳhuub raah kī bārīkiyoñ se ham
jin ke paroñ se sub.h kī ḳhushbū ke rañg haiñ
bachpan udhār laa.e haiñ un titliyoñ se ham
guzre hamāre ghar kī kisī rahguzar se vo
parde haTā.e dekheñ unheñ khiḌkiyoñ se ham
ab to hamāre beach kabhī dūriyāñ bhī hoñ
tañg aa ga.e haiñ roz kī nazdīkiyoñ se ham
jab bhī kahā ki yaad hamārī kahāñ unheñ
pakḌe ga.e haiñ Thiik tabhī hichkiyoñ se ham
ye aur baat dur rahe manzilon se hum
bach kar chale hamesha magar qafilon se hum
hone ko phir shikar nai uljhanon se hum
milte hain roz apne kai doston se hum
barson fareb khate rahe dusron se hum
apni samajh mein aae baDi mushkilon se hum
manzil ki hai talab to hamein sath le chalo
waqif hain KHub rah ki barikiyon se hum
jin ke paron se subh ki KHushbu ke rang hain
bachpan udhaar lae hain un titliyon se hum
guzre hamare ghar ki kisi rahguzar se wo
parde haTae dekhen unhen khiDkiyon se hum
ab to hamare beach kabhi duriyan bhi hon
tang aa gae hain roz ki nazdikiyon se hum
jab bhi kaha ki yaad hamari kahan unhen
pakDe gae hain Thik tabhi hichkiyon se hum

jhilmilāte hue din-rāt hamāre le kar
kaun aayā hai hathelī pe sitāre le kar
ham use āñkhoñ kī dehrī nahīñ chaḌhne dete
niiñd aatī na agar ḳhvāb tumhāre le kar
raat laa.ī hai sitāroñ se sajī qindīleñ
sar-nigūñ din hai dhanak vaale nazāre le kar
ek ummīd baḌī duur talak jaatī hai
terī āvāz ke ḳhāmosh ishāre le kar
raat shabnam se bhigo detī hai chehrā chehrā
din chalā aatā hai āñkhoñ meñ sharāre le kar
ek din us ne mujhe paak nazar se chūmā
umr-bhar chalnā paḌā mujh ko sahāre le kar
jhilmilate hue din-raat hamare le kar
kaun aaya hai hatheli pe sitare le kar
hum use aankhon ki dehri nahin chaDhne dete
nind aati na agar KHwab tumhaare le kar
raat lai hai sitaron se saji qindilen
sar-nigun din hai dhanak wale nazare le kar
ek ummid baDi dur talak jati hai
teri aawaz ke KHamosh ishaare le kar
raat shabnam se bhigo deti hai chehra chehra
din chala aata hai aankhon mein sharare le kar
ek din us ne mujhe pak nazar se chuma
umr-bhar chalna paDa mujh ko sahaare le kar

roz ḳhvāboñ meñ aa ke chal dūñgā
terī nīñdoñ meñ yuuñ ḳhalal dūñgā
maiñ na.ī shaam kī alāmat huuñ
ḳhaak sūraj ke muñh pe mal dūñgā
ab nayā pairahan zarūrī hai
ye badan shaam tak badal dūñgā
apnā ehsās chhoḌ jā.ūñgā
terī tanhā.ī le ke chal dūñgā
tum mujhe roz chiTThiyāñ likhnā
maiñ tumheñ roz ik ġhazal dūñgā
roz KHwabon mein aa ke chal dunga
teri nindon mein yun KHalal dunga
main nai sham ki alamat hun
KHak suraj ke munh pe mal dunga
ab naya pairahan zaruri hai
ye badan sham tak badal dunga
apna ehsas chhoD jaunga
teri tanhai le ke chal dunga
tum mujhe roz chiTThiyan likhna
main tumhein roz ek ghazal dunga

jab bhī taqdīr kā halkā sā ishāra hogā
āsmāñ par kahīñ merā bhī sitāra hogā
dushmanī niiñd se kar ke huuñ pashemānī meñ
kis tarah ab mire ḳhvāboñ kā guzāra hogā
muntazir jis ke liye ham haiñ ka.ī sadiyoñ se
jaane kis daur meñ vo shaḳhs hamārā hogā
maiñ ne palkoñ ko chamakte hue dekhā hai abhī
aaj āñkhoñ meñ koī ḳhvāb tumhārā hogā
dil parastār nahīñ apnā pujārī bhī nahīñ
devtā koī bhalā kaise hamārā hogā
tez-rau apne qadam ho ga.e patthar kaise
kaun hai kis ne mujhe aise pukārā hogā
jab bhi taqdir ka halka sa ishaara hoga
aasman par kahin mera bhi sitara hoga
dushmani nind se kar ke hun pashemani mein
kis tarah ab mere KHwabon ka guzara hoga
muntazir jis ke liye hum hain kai sadiyon se
jaane kis daur mein wo shaKHs hamara hoga
main ne palkon ko chamakte hue dekha hai abhi
aaj aankhon mein koi KHwab tumhaara hoga
dil parastar nahin apna pujari bhi nahin
dewta koi bhala kaise hamara hoga
tez-rau apne qadam ho gae patthar kaise
kaun hai kis ne mujhe aise pukara hoga

tumhāre paas aate haiñ to sāñseñ bhiig jaatī haiñ
mohabbat itnī miltī hai ki āñkheñ bhiig jaatī haiñ
tabassum itr jaisā hai hañsī barsāt jaisī hai
vo jab bhī baat kartī hai to bāteñ bhiig jaatī haiñ
tumhārī yaad se dil meñ ujālā hone lagtā hai
tumheñ jab gungunātā huuñ to rāteñ bhiig jaatī haiñ
zamīñ kī god bhartī hai to qudrat bhī chahaktī hai
na.e pattoñ kī aahaT se bhī shāḳheñ bhiig jaatī haiñ
tire ehsās kī ḳhushbū hamesha taaza rahtī hai
tirī rahmat kī bārish se murādeñ bhiig jaatī haiñ
tumhaare pas aate hain to sansen bhig jati hain
mohabbat itni milti hai ki aankhen bhig jati hain
tabassum itr jaisa hai hansi barsat jaisi hai
wo jab bhi baat karti hai to baaten bhig jati hain
tumhaari yaad se dil mein ujala hone lagta hai
tumhein jab gungunata hun to raaten bhig jati hain
zamin ki god bharti hai to qudrat bhi chahakti hai
nae patton ki aahaT se bhi shaKHen bhig jati hain
tere ehsas ki KHushbu hamesha taza rahti hai
teri rahmat ki barish se muraden bhig jati hain

agar safar meñ mire saath merā yaar chale
tavāf kartā huā mausam-e-bahār chale
lagā ke vaqt ko Thokar jo ḳhāksār chale
yaqīñ ke qāfile hamrāh be-shumār chale
navāznā hai to phir is tarah navāz mujhe
ki mere baa'd mirā zikr baar baar chale
ye jism kyā hai koī pairahan udhār kā hai
yahīñ sañbhāl ke pahnā yahīñ utaar chale
ye jugnuoñ se bharā āsmāñ jahāñ tak hai
vahāñ talak tirī nazroñ kā iqtidār chale
yahī to ek tamannā hai is musāfir kī
jo tum nahīñ to safar meñ tumhārā pyaar chale
agar safar mein mere sath mera yar chale
tawaf karta hua mausam-e-bahaar chale
laga ke waqt ko Thokar jo KHaksar chale
yaqin ke qafile hamrah be-shumar chale
nawazna hai to phir is tarah nawaz mujhe
ki mere ba'd mera zikr bar bar chale
ye jism kya hai koi pairahan udhaar ka hai
yahin sanbhaal ke pahna yahin utar chale
ye jugnuon se bhara aasman jahan tak hai
wahan talak teri nazron ka iqtidar chale
yahi to ek tamanna hai is musafir ki
jo tum nahin to safar mein tumhaara pyar chale

hamesha zindagī kī har kamī ko jiite rahte haiñ
jise ham jī nahīñ paa.e usī ko jiite rahte haiñ
hamāre dukh kī bārish ko koī dāman nahīñ miltā
hamārī aañkh ke bādal namī ko jiite rahte haiñ
kisī ke saath haiñ rasmeñ kisī ke saath haiñ qasmeñ
kisī ke saath jiinā hai kisī ko jiite rahte haiñ
hameñ ma.alūm hai ik din bharosa TuuT jā.egā
magar phir bhī sarāboñ meñ nadī ko jiite rahte haiñ
hamāre saath chaltī hai tumhāre pyaar kī ḳhushbū
lagā.ī thī jo tum ne us lagī ko jiite rahte haiñ
chahakte ghar mahakte khet aur vo gaañv kī galiyāñ
jinheñ ham chhoḌ aa.e un sabhī ko jiite rahte hai
ḳhudā ke nām-levā ham bhī haiñ tum bhī ho aur vo bhī
magar afsos sab apnī ḳhudī ko jiite rahte haiñ
hamesha zindagi ki har kami ko jite rahte hain
jise hum ji nahin pae usi ko jite rahte hain
hamare dukh ki barish ko koi daman nahin milta
hamari aankh ke baadal nami ko jite rahte hain
kisi ke sath hain rasmen kisi ke sath hain qasmen
kisi ke sath jina hai kisi ko jite rahte hain
hamein malum hai ek din bharosa TuT jaega
magar phir bhi sarabon mein nadi ko jite rahte hain
hamare sath chalti hai tumhaare pyar ki KHushbu
lagai thi jo tum ne us lagi ko jite rahte hain
chahakte ghar mahakte khet aur wo ganw ki galiyan
jinhen hum chhoD aae un sabhi ko jite rahte hai
KHuda ke nam-lewa hum bhi hain tum bhi ho aur wo bhi
magar afsos sab apni KHudi ko jite rahte hain

dhuup huī to āñchal ban kar kone kone chhā.ī ammāñ
saare ghar kā shor-sharāba sūnā-pan tanhā.ī ammāñ
saare rishte jeTh-dopahrī garm havā ātish añgāre
jharnā dariyā jhiil samundar bhīnī sī purvā.ī ammāñ
us ne ḳhud ko kho kar mujh meñ ek nayā ākār liyā hai
dhartī ambar aag havā jal jaisī hī sachchā.ī ammāñ
ghar meñ jhīne rishte maiñ ne lākhoñ baar udhaḌte dekhe
chupke chupke kar detī hai jaane kab turpāī ammāñ
bābū-jī guzre aapas meñ sab chīzeñ taqsīm huiiñ tab
maiñ ghar meñ sab se chhoTā thā mere hisse aa.ī ammāñ
dhup hui to aanchal ban kar kone kone chhai amman
sare ghar ka shor-sharaba suna-pan tanhai amman
sare rishte jeTh-dopahri garm hawa aatish angare
jharna dariya jhil samundar bhini si purwai amman
us ne KHud ko kho kar mujh mein ek naya aakar liya hai
dharti ambar aag hawa jal jaisi hi sachchai amman
ghar mein jhine rishte main ne lakhon bar udhaDte dekhe
chupke chupke kar deti hai jaane kab turpai amman
babu-ji guzre aapas mein sab chizen taqsim huin tab
main ghar mein sab se chhoTa tha mere hisse aai amman

nazar meñ ek bhī chehra nahīñ charāġhoñ kā
ġhubār hai mirī āñkhoñ meñ kin ujāloñ kā
chaTān hai tirā paikar to aañkh nam kyoñ hai
javāb DhūñDhtā rahtā huuñ in savāloñ kā
fazā meñ āñdhiyāñ is zor se chalī haiñ ki ab
parind bhuul ga.e rāsta uḌānoñ kā
hai aaj bhī mire pahlū meñ ik ajiib ḳhalish
ye iktisāb-e-karam hai tumhārī bāñhoñ kā
nazar mein ek bhi chehra nahin charaghon ka
ghubar hai meri aankhon mein kin ujalon ka
chaTan hai tera paikar to aankh nam kyon hai
jawab DhunDhta rahta hun in sawalon ka
faza mein aandhiyan is zor se chali hain ki ab
parind bhul gae rasta uDanon ka
hai aaj bhi mere pahlu mein ek ajib KHalish
ye iktisab-e-karam hai tumhaari banhon ka

basāratoñ ko rah-e-shauq meñ gañvā dekhā
tujhe na dekhā magar haañ ye hādisa dekhā
vajūd sauñp ke sab kuchh bachā liyā ham ne
na aañkh meñ koī aañsū na sāneha dekhā
kitāb-e-zīst bhī apnī nahīñ rahī ki yahāñ
har ik varaq pe nayā ek hāshiya dekhā
ḳhilāf-e-mauj samundar-shanās bah nikle
maiñ jis taraf gayā tūfān hī uThā dekhā
basaraton ko rah-e-shauq mein ganwa dekha
tujhe na dekha magar han ye hadisa dekha
wajud saunp ke sab kuchh bacha liya hum ne
na aankh mein koi aansu na saneha dekha
kitab-e-zist bhi apni nahin rahi ki yahan
har ek waraq pe naya ek hashiya dekha
KHilaf-e-mauj samundar-shanas bah nikle
main jis taraf gaya tufan hi uTha dekha

ashk umDeñ to unheñ palkoñ pe rokā jaa.e
kyoñ ye pindār-e-vafā sūrat-e-girya jaa.e
jab se dekhe haiñ tirī āñkhoñ ke sāgar ham ne
ik na.ī aarzū ubhrī hai ki Duubā jaa.e
maiñ samā.at meñ sameTe huuñ hazāroñ dushnām
zabt-e-ġham kā hai ye irshād na bolā jaa.e
ham ko is ḳhvāb-e-mohabbat se jagāyā kis ne
naqsh chehroñ pe adāvat kā na dekhā jaa.e
zaḳhm-ḳhurda na kahīñ uñgliyāñ vahshat ho jaa.eñ
barbat-e-dil ko kisī ke na yuuñ chheḌā jaa.e
dil hai maslūb-e-anā baam pe sūraj bhī nahīñ
kis tarah ghar ke añdheroñ ko ujālā jaa.e
paañv jab ḳhār-e-muġhīlāñ se haiñ chhalnī 'ābid'
kyoñ na phir ātish-e-namrūd meñ utrā jaa.e
ashk umDen to unhen palkon pe roka jae
kyon ye pindar-e-wafa surat-e-girya jae
jab se dekhe hain teri aankhon ke sagar hum ne
ek nai aarzu ubhri hai ki Duba jae
main samaat mein sameTe hun hazaron dushnam
zabt-e-gham ka hai ye irshad na bola jae
hum ko is KHwab-e-mohabbat se jagaya kis ne
naqsh chehron pe adawat ka na dekha jae
zaKHm-KHurda na kahin ungliyan wahshat ho jaen
barbat-e-dil ko kisi ke na yun chheDa jae
dil hai maslub-e-ana baam pe suraj bhi nahin
kis tarah ghar ke andheron ko ujala jae
panw jab KHar-e-mughilan se hain chhalni 'abid'
kyon na phir aatish-e-namrud mein utra jae

kaun thā jo dast-e-qātil ke liye tayyār thā
ek maiñ hī bazm-e-ahl-e-ḳhvāb meñ bedār thā
bhar liye haiñ tīrgī se ghar kī dīvāroñ ke ghaav
kyā nayā sūraj hamāre vāste āzād thā
ḳhushk nahroñ se sadā-e-tishnagī aatī rahī
aur samundar mauj-e-be-āvāz se sarshār thā
aa rahe the mausamoñ ke naam phūloñ ke payām
tum na the to mausam-e-gul bhī nigah meñ ḳhaar thā
de diyā ghar ke charāġhoñ ko havā kī god meñ
log kahte the ki ik saaya pas-e-dīvār thā
ab bhī yuuñ lagtā hai jaise har ḳhabar ho aaj kī
is liye barsoñ purānā mez par aḳhbār thā
kaun tha jo dast-e-qatil ke liye tayyar tha
ek main hi bazm-e-ahl-e-KHwab mein bedar tha
bhar liye hain tirgi se ghar ki diwaron ke ghaw
kya naya suraj hamare waste aazad tha
KHushk nahron se sada-e-tishnagi aati rahi
aur samundar mauj-e-be-awaz se sarshaar tha
aa rahe the mausamon ke nam phulon ke payam
tum na the to mausam-e-gul bhi nigah mein KHar tha
de diya ghar ke charaghon ko hawa ki god mein
log kahte the ki ek saya pas-e-diwar tha
ab bhi yun lagta hai jaise har KHabar ho aaj ki
is liye barson purana mez par aKHbar tha

ye kis ne ahd-e-farāmosh se sadā dī hai
abhī charāġh jalā.e hī the havā dī hai
ye virsa ham se na.ī nasl ko kabhī na mile
zabāñ hamāre buzurgoñ ne be-navā dī hai
ḳhirāj-e-ārzū-e-mausam-e-bahār hai ye
lahū lahū jo mire pairahan kī vaadī hai
koī bhī ghar se na nikle charāġh-e-dil le kar
amīr-e-shahr kī ye shahr meñ munādī hai
milī hai ye mah-o-anjum se dostī kī sazā
ki āftāb ne bīnā.ī tak jalā dī hai
kahāñ se kāTo.ge kal tum masarrateñ 'ābid'
ye fasl-e-ashk jo har aañkh meñ ugā dī hai
ye kis ne ahd-e-faramosh se sada di hai
abhi charagh jalae hi the hawa di hai
ye wirsa hum se nai nasl ko kabhi na mile
zaban hamare buzurgon ne be-nawa di hai
KHiraj-e-arzu-e-mausam-e-bahaar hai ye
lahu lahu jo mere pairahan ki wadi hai
koi bhi ghar se na nikle charagh-e-dil le kar
amir-e-shahr ki ye shahr mein munadi hai
mili hai ye mah-o-anjum se dosti ki saza
ki aaftab ne binai tak jala di hai
kahan se kaToge kal tum masarraten 'abid'
ye fasl-e-ashk jo har aankh mein uga di hai

dard kī aañch meñ jaltā hai ye ghar kyā kiije
ḳhvāb hotī hai tamanna kī sahar kyā kiije
ham bhī mānūs nahīñ dil ke añdheroñ se abhī
tā.er-e-shab bhī hai khole hue par kyā kiije
duur manzil hai kaḌī dhuup meñ karnā hai safar
kaT ga.e raah meñ jitne the shajar kyā kiije
vo ga.e vaqt kī mānind na lauTegā kabhī
ab luTā kar ye vafāoñ ke guhar kyā kiije
be-gavāhī ke bhañvar meñ hai mirī zaat ki ab
aañkh kī jhiil bhī hotī nahīñ tar kyā kiije
bārish-e-sang to be-vaj.h nahīñ hai 'ābid'
aa gayā mujh ko vafāoñ kā hunar kyā kiije
dard ki aanch mein jalta hai ye ghar kya kije
KHwab hoti hai tamanna ki sahar kya kije
hum bhi manus nahin dil ke andheron se abhi
taer-e-shab bhi hai khole hue par kya kije
dur manzil hai kaDi dhup mein karna hai safar
kaT gae rah mein jitne the shajar kya kije
wo gae waqt ki manind na lauTega kabhi
ab luTa kar ye wafaon ke guhar kya kije
be-gawahi ke bhanwar mein hai meri zat ki ab
aankh ki jhil bhi hoti nahin tar kya kije
barish-e-sang to be-wajh nahin hai 'abid'
aa gaya mujh ko wafaon ka hunar kya kije

gul sadāqat se mahakte hue tāsīr meñ rakh
sāneha dil pe jo guzre vahī tahrīr meñ rakh
tāq-e-zindāñ meñ charāġh-e-ġham-e-hastī na jalā
ātish-e-ishq-e-darūñ halqa-e-zanjīr meñ rakh
ḳhisht-e-be-faiz jo ārāsta guftār meñ hai
us ko buniyād banā kar kisī ta.amīr meñ rakh
zulmatoñ se kisī ghar kī nahīñ hotī pahchān
sang-o-gul hī nahīñ kuchh nuur bhī jāgīr meñ rakh
kab talak dosh pe ḳhvāboñ ke karegā parvāz
ham-nashīñ azm-e-safar vādī-e-tā'bīr meñ rakh
diid kī ziist se tā-marg talab aa pahuñchī
hīla-jū aur bahāne tū na tāḳhīr meñ rakh
sarvarī zor-e-takallum se na mil pā.egī
ham-nashīñ ijz-e-bayāñ ḳhūbī-e-taqrīr meñ rakh
gul sadaqat se mahakte hue tasir mein rakh
saneha dil pe jo guzre wahi tahrir mein rakh
taq-e-zindan mein charagh-e-gham-e-hasti na jala
aatish-e-ishq-e-darun halqa-e-zanjir mein rakh
KHisht-e-be-faiz jo aarasta guftar mein hai
us ko buniyaad bana kar kisi tamir mein rakh
zulmaton se kisi ghar ki nahin hoti pahchan
sang-o-gul hi nahin kuchh nur bhi jagir mein rakh
kab talak dosh pe KHwabon ke karega parwaz
ham-nashin azm-e-safar wadi-e-ta'bir mein rakh
did ki zist se ta-marg talab aa pahunchi
hila-ju aur bahane tu na taKHir mein rakh
sarwari zor-e-takallum se na mil paegi
ham-nashin ijz-e-bayan KHubi-e-taqrir mein rakh

pahlī sī dil ko ḳhvāhish-e-hijrat nahīñ rahī
kyā ai zamīñ hamārī zarūrat nahīñ rahī
āñgan meñ saarī raat barastī rahī ghaTā
dīvār ghar kī koī salāmat nahīñ rahī
yuñhī nahīñ irāda-e-pahlū-tahī ki ab
un se nibāh karne kī sūrat nahīñ rahī
patte haiñ ḳhushk phir bhī shajar se haiñ munsalik
kyā kījiye havā kī ināyat nahīñ rahī
dariyā meñ laakh maujeñ rahīñ sar-ba-kaf magar
kachche gharoñ ko ab koī vahshat nahīñ rahī
galiyoñ meñ phir se farsh-e-lahū bichh gayā tamām
insāñ meñ āj-kal ke sharāfat nahīñ rahī
pahli si dil ko KHwahish-e-hijrat nahin rahi
kya ai zamin hamari zarurat nahin rahi
aangan mein sari raat barasti rahi ghaTa
diwar ghar ki koi salamat nahin rahi
yunhi nahin irada-e-pahlu-tahi ki ab
un se nibah karne ki surat nahin rahi
patte hain KHushk phir bhi shajar se hain munsalik
kya kijiye hawa ki inayat nahin rahi
dariya mein lakh maujen rahin sar-ba-kaf magar
kachche gharon ko ab koi wahshat nahin rahi
galiyon mein phir se farsh-e-lahu bichh gaya tamam
insan mein aaj-kal ke sharafat nahin rahi

maiñ ajnabī rahā sab se magar sabhī meñ rahā
ye hausla bhī yahāñ par kisī kisī meñ rahā
qabā-e-azmat-e-insāñ milī faqīroñ ko
faqīh-e-shahr to kyā kyā na sarvarī meñ rahā
khiñchā hai zaḳhm-e-adāvat se dostī kā lahū
jise aziiz rakhā jaañ se dushmanī meñ rahā
charāġh rakh diye sūraj ke sāmne lā kar
magar vo farq na jaanā jo raushnī meñ rahā
zabān khultī to hotā qadam qadam maqtal
sukūt ḳhauf kī sūrat galī galī meñ rahā
main ajnabi raha sab se magar sabhi mein raha
ye hausla bhi yahan par kisi kisi mein raha
qaba-e-azmat-e-insan mili faqiron ko
faqih-e-shahr to kya kya na sarwari mein raha
khincha hai zaKHm-e-adawat se dosti ka lahu
jise aziz rakha jaan se dushmani mein raha
charagh rakh diye suraj ke samne la kar
magar wo farq na jaana jo raushni mein raha
zaban khulti to hota qadam qadam maqtal
sukut KHauf ki surat gali gali mein raha

shab kī āġhosh meñ jaagā huā ghar kis kā hai
us pe aaseb nahīñ hai to asar kis kā hai
aisā sailāb ki jangal ko bahā le jaa.e
aise sailāb meñ be-barg shajar kis kā hai
uñgliyoñ meñ utar aa.e haiñ basārat ke rumūz
tīrgī meñ rahe maḳhfī ye hunar kis kā hai
be-charāġhī hī rahī apne gharoñ kī mīrās
raushnī pūchhtī phirtī hai ki dar kis kā hai
vo musāfir to gayā chhoḌ ke yādeñ apnī
kis ko batlā.ūñ ki ye zād-e-safar kis kā hai
tum mirī raah se ho kar nahīñ guzre ho to phir
naqsh-e-pā ye taraf-e-rāhguzar kis kā hai
phir se mad.hosh-e-tamanna ke hue hosh-ba-jā
ham pe 'ābid' ye karam bār-e-digar kis kā hai
shab ki aaghosh mein jaga hua ghar kis ka hai
us pe aaseb nahin hai to asar kis ka hai
aisa sailab ki jangal ko baha le jae
aise sailab mein be-barg shajar kis ka hai
ungliyon mein utar aae hain basarat ke rumuz
tirgi mein rahe maKHfi ye hunar kis ka hai
be-charaghi hi rahi apne gharon ki miras
raushni puchhti phirti hai ki dar kis ka hai
wo musafir to gaya chhoD ke yaaden apni
kis ko batlaun ki ye zad-e-safar kis ka hai
tum meri rah se ho kar nahin guzre ho to phir
naqsh-e-pa ye taraf-e-rahguzar kis ka hai
phir se madhosh-e-tamanna ke hue hosh-ba-ja
hum pe 'abid' ye karam bar-e-digar kis ka hai

dil se mahrūmī-e-ehsās miTāne ke liye
gul khile haiñ mire zaḳhmoñ ko dukhāne ke liye
phir se āvāz ke dariyā meñ mire naam kī naav
bādbānoñ ko uThātī hai girāne ke liye
raat Dhaltī hai chalo DhūñD ke jugnū laa.eñ
vāda-e-anjum-o-mahtāb nibhāne ke liye
kuchh parinde mire āñgan meñ utar aa.e haiñ
bāl-o-par tez havāoñ se bachāne ke liye
sar se sūraj tirī chāhat kā Dhalā hai shāyad
mujh pe har sāya-e-dīvār girāne ke liye
apne jazboñ ko koī shakl na denā 'ābid'
varna sūrat ko bhī tarsoge dikhāne ke liye
dil se mahrumi-e-ehsas miTane ke liye
gul khile hain mere zaKHmon ko dukhane ke liye
phir se aawaz ke dariya mein mere nam ki naw
baadbanon ko uThati hai girane ke liye
raat Dhalti hai chalo DhunD ke jugnu laen
wada-e-anjum-o-mahtab nibhane ke liye
kuchh parinde mere aangan mein utar aae hain
baal-o-par tez hawaon se bachane ke liye
sar se suraj teri chahat ka Dhala hai shayad
mujh pe har saya-e-diwar girane ke liye
apne jazbon ko koi shakl na dena 'abid'
warna surat ko bhi tarsoge dikhane ke liye

ḳhuuñ mirā jis se huā hai ḳhanjar-e-ahbāb hai
ye haqīqat hai magar lagtā hai jaise ḳhvāb hai
is liye mujh sā numāyāñ ho gayā be-bāl-o-par
jis jagah maiñ huuñ vahāñ har aadmī surḳhāb hai
ham ne dekhā hai ki aksar Duub jaatā hai vahī
jo talāsh-e-gauhar-e-yaktā meñ zer-e-āb hai
ab kisī jañgal meñ jā rahiye ki apne shahr meñ
aadmī hī aadmī ke vāste nāyāb hai
zindagī apnī bil-āḳhir ho ga.ī us par tamām
jo kitāb-e-zindagī kā nā-mukammal baab hai
vo to ye kahiye shikasta ho chukā hai hausla
varna dil ab bhī kisī ke vasl ko betāb hai
KHun mera jis se hua hai KHanjar-e-ahbab hai
ye haqiqat hai magar lagta hai jaise KHwab hai
is liye mujh sa numayan ho gaya be-baal-o-par
jis jagah main hun wahan har aadmi surKHab hai
hum ne dekha hai ki aksar Dub jata hai wahi
jo talash-e-gauhar-e-yakta mein zer-e-ab hai
ab kisi jangal mein ja rahiye ki apne shahr mein
aadmi hi aadmi ke waste nayab hai
zindagi apni bil-aKHir ho gai us par tamam
jo kitab-e-zindagi ka na-mukammal bab hai
wo to ye kahiye shikasta ho chuka hai hausla
warna dil ab bhi kisi ke wasl ko betab hai

dhuup kā bojh bhalā maiñ ne uThāyā kab thā
maiñ to tanhā thā mirī zaat kā saayā kab thā
itne mānūs hue ġham se ki ab yaad nahīñ
vaqt ne dard kā ambār lagāyā kab thā
shaam utrī mire chehre pe to sochā maiñ ne
din mirī ziist ke āñgan meñ samāyā kab thā
dard baḌhtā hai to zaḳhmoñ se maiñ kartā huuñ savāl
sang maiñ ne kisī vahshī pe uThāyā kab thā
ab bhī hai sub.h mirī aañkh meñ zaḳhmī zaḳhmī
kaun kahtā hai ki maiñ shab kā satāyā kab thā
dhup ka bojh bhala main ne uThaya kab tha
main to tanha tha meri zat ka saya kab tha
itne manus hue gham se ki ab yaad nahin
waqt ne dard ka ambar lagaya kab tha
sham utri mere chehre pe to socha main ne
din meri zist ke aangan mein samaya kab tha
dard baDhta hai to zaKHmon se main karta hun sawal
sang main ne kisi wahshi pe uThaya kab tha
ab bhi hai subh meri aankh mein zaKHmi zaKHmi
kaun kahta hai ki main shab ka sataya kab tha

ye dāġh-e-hijr nahīñ miT sakā jabīñ kā lagā
zamīñ kahīñ kī hai paivand hai kahīñ kā lagā
milā hai dasht hameñ justujū meñ manzil kī
gumāñ thā paañv meñ aur aabla yaqīñ kā lagā
hamārā nām-o-nasab ham se pūchhne vaale
lahū na is tarah dāman pe āstīñ kā lagā
uThā ke dosh pe ḳheme nikal paḌe ham log
zarā na ḳhauf hameñ ajnabī zamīñ kā lagā
ye dagh-e-hijr nahin miT saka jabin ka laga
zamin kahin ki hai paiwand hai kahin ka laga
mila hai dasht hamein justuju mein manzil ki
guman tha panw mein aur aabla yaqin ka laga
hamara nam-o-nasab hum se puchhne wale
lahu na is tarah daman pe aastin ka laga
uTha ke dosh pe KHeme nikal paDe hum log
zara na KHauf hamein ajnabi zamin ka laga

ġham diyā hai to sivā hausla-e-ġham denā
ye to ik aag hai phir kyā ise shabnam denā
ab bhī soī huī rātoñ kī thakan baaqī hai
ḳhvāb denā hoñ zarūrī to zarā kam denā
vaqt se hī mujhe ummīd masīhā.ī kī thī
vaqt hī bhuul gayā zaḳhm ko marham denā
us ne ta.abīr ke sab bhed chhupā.e ham se
jis ne sīkhā hai hameñ ḳhvāb kā aalam denā
gham diya hai to siwa hausla-e-gham dena
ye to ek aag hai phir kya ise shabnam dena
ab bhi soi hui raaton ki thakan baqi hai
KHwab dena hon zaruri to zara kam dena
waqt se hi mujhe ummid masihai ki thi
waqt hi bhul gaya zaKHm ko marham dena
us ne tabir ke sab bhed chhupae hum se
jis ne sikha hai hamein KHwab ka aalam dena

shikve hameñ to jehd-e-mukarrar ke nahīñ haiñ
hijrat huī hai yuuñ ki kisī ghar ke nahīñ haiñ
kis jurm meñ ye pahlū-tahī ham se ravā hai
ai shīsha-e-gard ham koī patthar ke nahīñ haiñ
sar-basta-e-zanjīr kiyā ham ko jinhoñ ne
vo log usī ghar ke haiñ bāhar ke nahīñ haiñ
kis darja mukarram haiñ mire ashk na pūchho
vo daam mile haiñ ki jo gauhar ke nahīñ haiñ
vo dard sahā hai ki jo ġhairoñ kā nahīñ thā
vo zaḳhm lage haiñ ki jo ḳhanjar ke nahīñ haiñ
shikwe hamein to jehd-e-mukarrar ke nahin hain
hijrat hui hai yun ki kisi ghar ke nahin hain
kis jurm mein ye pahlu-tahi hum se rawa hai
ai shisha-e-gard hum koi patthar ke nahin hain
sar-basta-e-zanjir kiya hum ko jinhon ne
wo log usi ghar ke hain bahar ke nahin hain
kis darja mukarram hain mere ashk na puchho
wo dam mile hain ki jo gauhar ke nahin hain
wo dard saha hai ki jo ghairon ka nahin tha
wo zaKHm lage hain ki jo KHanjar ke nahin hain

ye dāġh-e-hijr nahīñ miT sakā jabīñ kā lagā
zamīñ kahīñ kī hai paivand hai kahīñ kā lagā
milā hai dasht hameñ justujū meñ manzil kī
gumāñ thā paañv meñ aur aabla yaqīñ kā lagā
hamārā nām-o-nasab ham se pūchhne vaale
lahū na is tarah dāman pe āstīñ kā lagā
uThā ke dosh pe ḳheme nikal paḌe ham log
zarā na ḳhauf hameñ ajnabī zamīñ kā lagā
ye dagh-e-hijr nahin miT saka jabin ka laga
zamin kahin ki hai paiwand hai kahin ka laga
mila hai dasht hamein justuju mein manzil ki
guman tha panw mein aur aabla yaqin ka laga
hamara nam-o-nasab hum se puchhne wale
lahu na is tarah daman pe aastin ka laga
uTha ke dosh pe KHeme nikal paDe hum log
zara na KHauf hamein ajnabi zamin ka laga

mohabbatoñ par dil-e-hazīñ ko nisār karnā
hai yuuñ ki jaise junūñ meñ ḳhud hī pe vaar karnā
ajab nahīñ vo bhī mere raste pe ḳhud ko Daale
vo jis ne sīkhā hai qāfiloñ ko ġhubār karnā
vo ek bārish kī muntazir be-shumār āñkheñ
vo ek tūfāñ kā bastiyoñ ko shumār karnā
mujhe to us ne tamām lamhe vahī diye haiñ
vahī jo ahl-e-junūñ ko hoñ iḳhtiyār karnā
shafaq utar kar tumhāre pallū se bañdh ga.ī hai
jo ho sake to sahar talak ye hisār karnā
aziyyatoñ kā ḳhamīr zaḳhm-e-nihāñ se uTThā
kabhī jo chāhā hai dil kā sahrā bahār karnā
mohabbaton par dil-e-hazin ko nisar karna
hai yun ki jaise junun mein KHud hi pe war karna
ajab nahin wo bhi mere raste pe KHud ko Dale
wo jis ne sikha hai qafilon ko ghubar karna
wo ek barish ki muntazir be-shumar aankhen
wo ek tufan ka bastiyon ko shumar karna
mujhe to us ne tamam lamhe wahi diye hain
wahi jo ahl-e-junun ko hon iKHtiyar karna
shafaq utar kar tumhaare pallu se bandh gai hai
jo ho sake to sahar talak ye hisar karna
aziyyaton ka KHamir zaKHm-e-nihan se uTTha
kabhi jo chaha hai dil ka sahra bahaar karna

yahī to ek shikāyat safar meñ rahtī hai
havā-e-gard musalsal nazar meñ rahtī hai
jazā-e-kāvish-e-ta.amīr ye milī hai hameñ
sadā-e-tesha sadā saath ghar meñ rahtī hai
hunar kisī meñ ho qismat hai us kī dar-badarī
ki āb-o-tāb-e-guhar kab guhar meñ rahtī hai
samā.atoñ kā payambar hī ban sake to sune
vo dāstāñ jo lab-e-chashm-e-tar meñ rahtī hai
har ek sub.h pe maqtal kā ho rahā hai gumāñ
na jaane kaun sī surḳhī ḳhabar meñ rahtī hai
yahi to ek shikayat safar mein rahti hai
hawa-e-gard musalsal nazar mein rahti hai
jaza-e-kawish-e-tamir ye mili hai hamein
sada-e-tesha sada sath ghar mein rahti hai
hunar kisi mein ho qismat hai us ki dar-badari
ki aab-o-tab-e-guhar kab guhar mein rahti hai
samaaton ka payambar hi ban sake to sune
wo dastan jo lab-e-chashm-e-tar mein rahti hai
har ek subh pe maqtal ka ho raha hai guman
na jaane kaun si surKHi KHabar mein rahti hai

ham ko jānāñ is nagrī meñ chalnā bhī dushvār huā
logoñ kā har sang-e-malāmat apne liye dīvār huā
dil ke sab dukhḌe dil meñ haiñ phir bhī unheñ ye shikva hai
chāk-garebāñ kyoñ phirte ho dāman kyoñ hai taar huā
sub.h se halkī halkī kasak thī mīThā mīThā dard sā thā
shaam kā pahlā taarā ubhrā zaḳhm-e-jigar bedār huā
ḳhud ko malāmat kyoñ karte ho apne aap se shikva kyā
jaan ke kab dhokā khāyā hai anjāne meñ pyaar huā
ham ko ḳhirad kī raah dikhāne vaale ye kyoñ bhuul ga.e
apne liye is rāh-e-junūñ meñ sahrā bhī gulzār huā
hum ko jaanan is nagri mein chalna bhi dushwar hua
logon ka har sang-e-malamat apne liye diwar hua
dil ke sab dukhDe dil mein hain phir bhi unhen ye shikwa hai
chaak-gareban kyon phirte ho daman kyon hai tar hua
subh se halki halki kasak thi miTha miTha dard sa tha
sham ka pahla tara ubhra zaKHm-e-jigar bedar hua
KHud ko malamat kyon karte ho apne aap se shikwa kya
jaan ke kab dhoka khaya hai anjaane mein pyar hua
hum ko KHirad ki rah dikhane wale ye kyon bhul gae
apne liye is rah-e-junun mein sahra bhi gulzar hua

yahī to ek shikāyat safar meñ rahtī hai
havā-e-gard musalsal nazar meñ rahtī hai
jazā-e-kāvish-e-ta.amīr ye milī hai hameñ
sadā-e-tesha sadā saath ghar meñ rahtī hai
hunar kisī meñ ho qismat hai us kī dar-badarī
ki āb-o-tāb-e-guhar kab guhar meñ rahtī hai
samā.atoñ kā payambar hī ban sake to sune
vo dāstāñ jo lab-e-chashm-e-tar meñ rahtī hai
har ek sub.h pe maqtal kā ho rahā hai gumāñ
na jaane kaun sī surḳhī ḳhabar meñ rahtī hai
yahi to ek shikayat safar mein rahti hai
hawa-e-gard musalsal nazar mein rahti hai
jaza-e-kawish-e-tamir ye mili hai hamein
sada-e-tesha sada sath ghar mein rahti hai
hunar kisi mein ho qismat hai us ki dar-badari
ki aab-o-tab-e-guhar kab guhar mein rahti hai
samaaton ka payambar hi ban sake to sune
wo dastan jo lab-e-chashm-e-tar mein rahti hai
har ek subh pe maqtal ka ho raha hai guman
na jaane kaun si surKHi KHabar mein rahti hai

fikr rakhte haiñ kahāñ zehn agar rakhte haiñ
dasht-e-be-āb meñ jo tuḳhm-e-hunar rakhte haiñ
har na.ī baat bhulā detī hai pahle kā ḳhayāl
vo to aḳhbār haiñ bas taaza ḳhabar rakhte haiñ
miT gayā rang-e-ta.alluq to ye chehre ke nuqūsh
ek ik ḳhatt-e-ta.assur meñ ḳhabar rakhte haiñ
aise logoñ kā milā ham ko zamāna jo log
kor-bīnā haiñ magar ham pe nazar rakhte haiñ
koī aahaT hai na dastak ki bichhaḌ jaa.e sukūt
jin ko dīvār mayassar ho vo dar rakhte haiñ
jab bhī aatī hai kisī samt se maqtal kī havā
dhyān aatā hai abhī dosh pe sar rakhte haiñ
fikr rakhte hain kahan zehn agar rakhte hain
dasht-e-be-ab mein jo tuKHm-e-hunar rakhte hain
har nai baat bhula deti hai pahle ka KHayal
wo to aKHbar hain bas taza KHabar rakhte hain
miT gaya rang-e-talluq to ye chehre ke nuqush
ek ek KHatt-e-tassur mein KHabar rakhte hain
aise logon ka mila hum ko zamana jo log
kor-bina hain magar hum pe nazar rakhte hain
koi aahaT hai na dastak ki bichhaD jae sukut
jin ko diwar mayassar ho wo dar rakhte hain
jab bhi aati hai kisi samt se maqtal ki hawa
dhyan aata hai abhi dosh pe sar rakhte hain

chāroñ taraf kuchh dīvāreñ sī rahtī haiñ aahoñ meñ lagī
merī miTTī tere ghar kī gahrī buniyādoñ meñ lagī
chup kī chādar oḌh to lī hai paañv chhupeñ sar khul chaa.e
mahrūmī kī dhuup na jaane kab se āvāzoñ meñ lagī
un se zulmat-e-dasht muqaddar aur siyāh na ho jaa.e
chhoḌ na detā chāñd kirneñ tum apne ḳhvāboñ meñ lagī
mujh se mere apne log bhī rahte haiñ begāne se
mere naam kī kaun sī tohmat un ke andāzoñ meñ lagī
is mausam meñ Daalī Daalī barf ke itne phuul khile
rañg-o-tapish se mahrūmī kī shāḳh mire jazboñ meñ lagī
chaaron taraf kuchh diwaren si rahti hain aahon mein lagi
meri miTTi tere ghar ki gahri buniyaadon mein lagi
chup ki chadar oDh to li hai panw chhupen sar khul chae
mahrumi ki dhup na jaane kab se aawazon mein lagi
un se zulmat-e-dasht muqaddar aur siyah na ho jae
chhoD na deta chand kirnen tum apne KHwabon mein lagi
mujh se mere apne log bhi rahte hain begane se
mere nam ki kaun si tohmat un ke andazon mein lagi
is mausam mein Dali Dali barf ke itne phul khile
rang-o-tapish se mahrumi ki shaKH mere jazbon mein lagi

abas hai shāḳh-e-qad-āvar pe āshiyāñ rakhnā
zamīñ ko raas kab aaya hai āsmāñ rakhnā
safar karo ki Thahar jaao ik azaab hai ye
qadam ko hijrat-o-manzil ke darmiyāñ rakhnā
kisī kā shor-e-fuġhāñ sun ke yaad aaya bahut
fasīl-e-ġham meñ mirā dard-e-be-zabāñ rakhnā
khulī fazā meñ to shabnam bhī baar lagtī hai
agar hai tarz-e-kuhan sar pe sā.ebāñ rakhnā
ye log apnī hī dīvār ke naqab-zan haiñ
kabhī na bhuul ke tum ghar kā pāsbāñ rakhnā
hai naav maujoñ kī zad meñ magar hameñ 'ābid'
na aaya bād-e-muḳhālif pe bādbāñ rakhnā
abas hai shaKH-e-qad-awar pe aashiyan rakhna
zamin ko ras kab aaya hai aasman rakhna
safar karo ki Thahar jao ek azab hai ye
qadam ko hijrat-o-manzil ke darmiyan rakhna
kisi ka shor-e-fughan sun ke yaad aaya bahut
fasil-e-gham mein mera dard-e-be-zaban rakhna
khuli faza mein to shabnam bhi bar lagti hai
agar hai tarz-e-kuhan sar pe saeban rakhna
ye log apni hi diwar ke naqab-zan hain
kabhi na bhul ke tum ghar ka pasban rakhna
hai naw maujon ki zad mein magar hamein 'abid'
na aaya baad-e-muKHalif pe baadban rakhna

kar chukā phuul maiñ jab saare jahāñ ke patthar
aa paḌe sar pe mire jaane kahāñ ke patthar
zarf-e-dil meñ namī-e-ashk-e-haqīqat na rahī
itne baḳhshe hameñ logoñ ne gumāñ ke patthar
pa-e-haq dar-pa.e-paikār koī miltā nahīñ
bañdh ga.e paañv se kyā vahshat-e-jāñ ke patthar
ḳhaak meñ mil ga.e sab phuul se logoñ ke vajūd
lag ga.e qabr pe bas nām-o-nishāñ ke patthar
kū-ba-kū ho ga.iiñ ta.amīr ibādat-gāheñ
jam.a karte hī rahe ham to makāñ ke patthar
zindagī ke liye gauhar vahī Thahre 'ābid'
log kahte haiñ jinheñ fikr-e-javāñ ke patthar
kar chuka phul main jab sare jahan ke patthar
aa paDe sar pe mere jaane kahan ke patthar
zarf-e-dil mein nami-e-ashk-e-haqiqat na rahi
itne baKHshe hamein logon ne guman ke patthar
pa-e-haq dar-pae-paikar koi milta nahin
bandh gae panw se kya wahshat-e-jaan ke patthar
KHak mein mil gae sab phul se logon ke wajud
lag gae qabr pe bas nam-o-nishan ke patthar
ku-ba-ku ho gain tamir ibaadat-gahen
jama karte hi rahe hum to makan ke patthar
zindagi ke liye gauhar wahi Thahre 'abid'
log kahte hain jinhen fikr-e-jawan ke patthar

ghar to luTtā hai magar ham ko miTāne vaale
kaun se des se lā.eñge zamāne vaale
dhuup baḳhshī hai to phir sāya-e-dīvār bhī de
log sūraj ko haiñ ma.abūd banāne vaale
dil ko āmāda-e-tajdīd-e-vafā kaise karūñ
ris rahe haiñ abhī nāsūr purāne vaale
yuuñ to milte haiñ har ik jism pe be-dāġh libās
uTh ga.e dil pe magar daaġh uThāne vaale
ghar meñ ghar kī koī sūrat to nikāleñ 'ābid'
aane vaale haiñ kabhī ke nahīñ aane vaale
ghar to luTta hai magar hum ko miTane wale
kaun se des se laenge zamane wale
dhup baKHshi hai to phir saya-e-diwar bhi de
log suraj ko hain mabud banane wale
dil ko aamada-e-tajdid-e-wafa kaise karun
ris rahe hain abhi nasur purane wale
yun to milte hain har ek jism pe be-dagh libas
uTh gae dil pe magar dagh uThane wale
ghar mein ghar ki koi surat to nikalen 'abid'
aane wale hain kabhi ke nahin aane wale

vo dil kī jhiil meñ utrā thā ek saa.at ko
ye umr ho ga.ī hai sahte is malāmat ko
kahīñ to sāya-e-dīvār-e-āgahī mil jaa.e
koī to aa.e kare ḳhatm is masāfat ko
tumhīñ se mil ke mirī dil se āshnā.ī ho
tumhāre baad hī jaanā hai is qayāmat ko
vo ek shaḳhs mujhe kar gayā sabhī se judā
taras rahā huuñ maiñ jis shaḳhs kī rifāqat ko
ajiib log haiñ is shahr ke ba-nām-e-vafā
havā.eñ dete haiñ har sho.ala-e-adāvat ko
javāz bhī to koī ho mirī tabāhī kā
chhupā rahe ho tabassum meñ kyoñ nadāmat ko
ga.e dinoñ kā manāte ho sog phir 'ābid'
hameñ yaqīñ hai na badloge apnī aadat ko
wo dil ki jhil mein utra tha ek saat ko
ye umr ho gai hai sahte is malamat ko
kahin to saya-e-diwar-e-agahi mil jae
koi to aae kare KHatm is masafat ko
tumhin se mil ke meri dil se aashnai ho
tumhaare baad hi jaana hai is qayamat ko
wo ek shaKHs mujhe kar gaya sabhi se juda
taras raha hun main jis shaKHs ki rifaqat ko
ajib log hain is shahr ke ba-nam-e-wafa
hawaen dete hain har shoala-e-adawat ko
jawaz bhi to koi ho meri tabahi ka
chhupa rahe ho tabassum mein kyon nadamat ko
gae dinon ka manate ho sog phir 'abid'
hamein yaqin hai na badloge apni aadat ko

vo jo apne the vahī ho ga.e harjā.ī bhī
baat peshānī pe likkhī huī pesh aa.ī bhī
dil to pahle hī thā mahsūr-e-ġham-e-tanhā.ī
us pe dharnā diye baiThī hai ye purvā.ī bhī
jis taraf ruḳh ho havā kā ye barastī hai vahīñ
abr kī tarh se hotī hai shanāsā.ī bhī
dil ko rahtī bhī hai ab mahfil-e-yārāñ kī talāsh
aur tabī.at hai ki us bazm meñ ghabrā.ī bhī
wo jo apne the wahi ho gae harjai bhi
baat peshani pe likkhi hui pesh aai bhi
dil to pahle hi tha mahsur-e-gham-e-tanhai
us pe dharna diye baiThi hai ye purwai bhi
jis taraf ruKH ho hawa ka ye barasti hai wahin
abr ki tarh se hoti hai shanasai bhi
dil ko rahti bhi hai ab mahfil-e-yaran ki talash
aur tabiat hai ki us bazm mein ghabrai bhi

kyā zamīñ kyā āsmāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
ham na hoñ to ye jahāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
dīda-o-dil kī rifāqat ke baġhair
fasl-e-gul ho yā ḳhizāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
pattharoñ meñ ham bhī patthar ho ga.e
ab ġham-e-sūd-o-ziyāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
kyā qayāmat hai ki apne des meñ
e'tibār-e-jism-o-jāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
kaise kaise sar-kashīda log the
jin kā ab nām-o-nishāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
ek ehsās-e-mohabbat ke sivā
hāsil-e-umr-e-ravāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
koī mauzū-e-suḳhan hī jab na ho
sirf andāz-e-bayāñ kuchh bhī nahīñ
kya zamin kya aasman kuchh bhi nahin
hum na hon to ye jahan kuchh bhi nahin
dida-o-dil ki rifaqat ke baghair
fasl-e-gul ho ya KHizan kuchh bhi nahin
pattharon mein hum bhi patthar ho gae
ab gham-e-sud-o-ziyan kuchh bhi nahin
kya qayamat hai ki apne des mein
e'tibar-e-jism-o-jaan kuchh bhi nahin
kaise kaise sar-kashida log the
jin ka ab nam-o-nishan kuchh bhi nahin
ek ehsas-e-mohabbat ke siwa
hasil-e-umr-e-rawan kuchh bhi nahin
koi mauzu-e-suKHan hi jab na ho
sirf andaz-e-bayan kuchh bhi nahin

ik to use har baat meñ had chāhiye merī
phir us pe mohabbat bhī ashad chāhiye merī
pahle use darkār thī shaam aur ye shāna
ab mujh ko bhulāne meñ madad chāhiye merī
bū aane lagī tujh se bhī duniyā kī mire yaar
kuchh roz mujhe sohbat-e-bad chāhiye merī
kahtī hai farishtoñ kī tarah Tokūñ na rokūñ
aur aadmī vaalī bhī sanad chāhiye merī
kyā din meñ zarūrī hai ki auroñ meñ raho tum
kyā raat meñ bas niyyat-e-bad chāhiye merī
ek to use har baat mein had chahiye meri
phir us pe mohabbat bhi ashad chahiye meri
pahle use darkar thi sham aur ye shana
ab mujh ko bhulane mein madad chahiye meri
bu aane lagi tujh se bhi duniya ki mere yar
kuchh roz mujhe sohbat-e-bad chahiye meri
kahti hai farishton ki tarah Tokun na rokun
aur aadmi wali bhi sanad chahiye meri
kya din mein zaruri hai ki auron mein raho tum
kya raat mein bas niyyat-e-bad chahiye meri

karūñgā ishq virāsat kā kuchh batā.ūñgā na.iiñ
maiñ ik ġharīb kī beTī ko āzmā.ūñgā na.iiñ
unheñ kaho ki bahut Dher shor-o-shar na kareñ
maiñ Dar gayā to ka.ī roz muskurā.ūñgā na.iiñ
tasallī dūñgā to mar jā.egī vo laḌkī hai
maiñ jaane dūñgā gale se use lagā.ūñgā na.iiñ
use ḳhabar bhī nahīñ hogī itnā chāhūñgā
use pata bhī nahīñ hogā maiñ batā.ūñgā na.iiñ
ye rāsta baḌī mushkil se tai kiyā maiñ ne
ye fāsla hai diloñ kā ise miTā.ūñgā na.iiñ
tirā mutālba hai terī yaad ke aañsū
maiñ ab ke royā to āñkhoñ ko bhī bachā.ūñgā na.iiñ
aur ab kī sālgirah par plan kyā hai tirā
aur ab kī baar to maiñ sāmne bhī ā.ūñgā na.iiñ
maiñ tujh se aañkh milā kar ġhazal sunā.ūñgā
maiñ ḳhud ko Dūbtā dekhūñgā aur bachā.ūñgā na.iiñ
karunga ishq wirasat ka kuchh bataunga nain
main ek gharib ki beTi ko aazmaunga nain
unhen kaho ki bahut Dher shor-o-shar na karen
main Dar gaya to kai roz muskuraunga nain
tasalli dunga to mar jaegi wo laDki hai
main jaane dunga gale se use lagaunga nain
use KHabar bhi nahin hogi itna chahunga
use pata bhi nahin hoga main bataunga nain
ye rasta baDi mushkil se tai kiya main ne
ye fasla hai dilon ka ise miTaunga nain
tera mutalba hai teri yaad ke aansu
main ab ke roya to aankhon ko bhi bachaunga nain
aur ab ki salgirah par plan kya hai tera
aur ab ki bar to main samne bhi aaunga nain
main tujh se aankh mila kar ghazal sunaunga
main KHud ko Dubta dekhunga aur bachaunga nain

vafā ke da.avoñ pe hañs rahā thā
mujhe nayā hijr ho gayā thā
bahut hī bad-shakl niklī duniyā
maiñ pahle parde pe dekhtā thā
use batātā thā merī bāteñ
ḳhudā mirī kaal sun rahā thā
samajh meñ kyā aatā merā lahja
kisī kī bātoñ meñ aa gayā thā
utaar pheñkī thī shaam sar se
abhī to paarā nahīñ chaḌhā thā
tum aaj tak ro rahe ho jo ġham
vo do dinoñ se ziyāda kā thā
ġharīb beva kā haath thāmā
madīne jaane kā rāsta thā
aur us kī haryānvī zabāñ thī
aur us ke hāthoñ meñ ik ghaḌā thā
ye jumla jo pahle kah diyā hai
ye vasl ke ain baad kā thā
wafa ke dawon pe hans raha tha
mujhe naya hijr ho gaya tha
bahut hi bad-shakl nikli duniya
main pahle parde pe dekhta tha
use batata tha meri baaten
KHuda meri kal sun raha tha
samajh mein kya aata mera lahja
kisi ki baaton mein aa gaya tha
utar phenki thi sham sar se
abhi to para nahin chaDha tha
tum aaj tak ro rahe ho jo gham
wo do dinon se ziyaada ka tha
gharib bewa ka hath thama
madine jaane ka rasta tha
aur us ki haryanwi zaban thi
aur us ke hathon mein ek ghaDa tha
ye jumla jo pahle kah diya hai
ye wasl ke ain baad ka tha

aisī vus.at ki chamakte haiñ sitāre dil meñ
us ko rahnā hī nahīñ aayā hamāre dil meñ
sab ne aa aa ke mirā zehnī tavāzun chheḌā
log jo jo bhī mohabbat se utāre dil meñ
tū ne kyā jurm kiyā hogā jo maiñ rahtā rahā
itnā arsa mire chandā tire pyāre dil meñ
terā ronā tire kuchh kaam nahīñ aa.egā dost
sabz battī pe nahīñ khulte ishāre dil meñ
us kī āñkhoñ se jo dekhe the unhī ḳhvāboñ ne
aaj kal aag lagā rakkhī hai saare dil meñ
koī do chaar na.e zaḳhm ki rash paḌ jaa.e
sirf ik Dar rahā kartā hai bechāre dil meñ
sachche dil vaalī mire hujre meñ rahtī hai huzūr
mīThe paanī kā kuaañ hai mire khāre dil meñ
merā allāh mire saath hai vo jāntī hai
us ne Darte hue chalvā.e haiñ aare dil meñ
aisi wusat ki chamakte hain sitare dil mein
us ko rahna hi nahin aaya hamare dil mein
sab ne aa aa ke mera zehni tawazun chheDa
log jo jo bhi mohabbat se utare dil mein
tu ne kya jurm kiya hoga jo main rahta raha
itna arsa mere chanda tere pyare dil mein
tera rona tere kuchh kaam nahin aaega dost
sabz batti pe nahin khulte ishaare dil mein
us ki aankhon se jo dekhe the unhi KHwabon ne
aaj kal aag laga rakkhi hai sare dil mein
koi do chaar nae zaKHm ki rash paD jae
sirf ek Dar raha karta hai bechaare dil mein
sachche dil wali mere hujre mein rahti hai huzur
miThe pani ka kuan hai mere khaare dil mein
mera allah mere sath hai wo jaanti hai
us ne Darte hue chalwae hain aare dil mein

ek daf.a vo mujhe dil meñ to aane detā
maiñ use shaam nahīñ detā zamāne detā
aap ke ġham pe bahut kaam kiyā hai maiñ ne
ab maiñ rotā huuñ to aañsū nahīñ aane detā
vo mujhe ek se pahle nahīñ sone detī
maiñ use ḳhvāb se jaldī nahīñ jaane detā
rab ke aage to tar-o-tāza gayā hotā maiñ
vaqt kuchh der mujhe Tek lagāne detā
sher kā rizq in āñkhoñ meñ hai lekin mire dost
dil mujhe hoñT se uupar nahīñ jaane detā
har hasīñ laḌkī ko taslīm kiyā kartā huuñ
koī misrā nahīñ maiñ girne girāne detā
ek dafa wo mujhe dil mein to aane deta
main use sham nahin deta zamane deta
aap ke gham pe bahut kaam kiya hai main ne
ab main rota hun to aansu nahin aane deta
wo mujhe ek se pahle nahin sone deti
main use KHwab se jaldi nahin jaane deta
rab ke aage to tar-o-taza gaya hota main
waqt kuchh der mujhe Tek lagane deta
sher ka rizq in aankhon mein hai lekin mere dost
dil mujhe honT se upar nahin jaane deta
har hasin laDki ko taslim kiya karta hun
koi misra nahin main girne girane deta

dūsrā ishq mirī jaan nahīñ kar saktā
ye tirā hāfiz-e-qur.ān nahīñ kar saktā
aisī hālat meñ tire ḳhvāb se lauTā hai ye jism
maiñ abhī vasl kā sāmān nahīñ kar saktā
dastaras meñ hai mirī kaif bhī kaifiyat bhī
zaḳhm bhar kar mujhe hairān nahīñ kar saktā
un pe ġhālib hai ka.ī chehroñ ke ishrāk kā diin
tū in āñkhoñ ko musalmān nahīñ kar saktā
pahlī qistoñ meñ tirī maut nahīñ ho saktī
apne theTar ko meñ vīrān nahīñ kar saktā
ye mirā āḳhirī patthar hai tirī yaad meñ dost
ab maiñ paanī ko pareshān nahīñ kar saktā
dusra ishq meri jaan nahin kar sakta
ye tera hafiz-e-quran nahin kar sakta
aisi haalat mein tere KHwab se lauTa hai ye jism
main abhi wasl ka saman nahin kar sakta
dastaras mein hai meri kaif bhi kaifiyat bhi
zaKHm bhar kar mujhe hairan nahin kar sakta
un pe ghaalib hai kai chehron ke ishrak ka din
tu in aankhon ko musalman nahin kar sakta
pahli qiston mein teri maut nahin ho sakti
apne theTar ko mein viran nahin kar sakta
ye mera aaKHiri patthar hai teri yaad mein dost
ab main pani ko pareshan nahin kar sakta

jab jab bhī dekhiye use ḳhūñ-bār sī lage
duniyā hamesha barsar-e-paikār sī lage
har har nafas pe rañg badaltī hai zindagī
ik phuul sī lage hai kabhī ḳhaar sī lage
chehra hai mere dost kā yā koī aa.ina
dekhūñ ulaT-palaT ke to bhī aarsī lage
aadat sī paḌ ga.ī hai use bolne kī tez
vo baat bhī kare hai to takrār sī lage
tum saath ho to ham bhī bayābāñ ko ghar kareñ
ye saḳht dhuup sāya-e-dīvār sī lage
har har qadam pe jaise ki biktā ho aadmī
bastī tamām misr ke bāzār sī lage
'ābid' tamām shahr pe aalam hai kaun sā
har ek shakl naqsh-ba-dīvār sī lage
jab jab bhi dekhiye use KHun-bar si lage
duniya hamesha barsar-e-paikar si lage
har har nafas pe rang badalti hai zindagi
ek phul si lage hai kabhi KHar si lage
chehra hai mere dost ka ya koi aaina
dekhun ulaT-palaT ke to bhi aarsi lage
aadat si paD gai hai use bolne ki tez
wo baat bhi kare hai to takrar si lage
tum sath ho to hum bhi bayaban ko ghar karen
ye saKHt dhup saya-e-diwar si lage
har har qadam pe jaise ki bikta ho aadmi
basti tamam misr ke bazar si lage
'abid' tamam shahr pe aalam hai kaun sa
har ek shakl naqsh-ba-diwar si lage

ye hai āb-e-ravāñ na Thahregā
umr kā kārvāñ na Thahregā
chhoḌ dī hai jagah sutūnoñ ne
sar pe ab sā.ebāñ na Thahregā
ret par hai asar havāoñ kā
koī nām-o-nishāñ na Thahregā
har qadam jo tumhārī samt uThā
sa.ī-e-rā.egāñ na Thahregā
marhala aa gayā tasādum kā
fāsla darmiyāñ na Thahregā
dil kā saudā hai kār-e-dil-dārāñ
farq-e-sūd-o-ziyāñ na Thahregā
kyoñ sunāte ho sab ko haal apnā
har koī rāzdāñ na Thahregā
chhoḌ degī zamīn mehvar ko
mustaqil āsmāñ na Thahregā
apnī āñkhoñ meñ aaj use bhar lo
der tak ye samāñ na Thahregā
juz terī mahfiloñ ke aur kahīñ
'ābid'-e-nā-tavāñ Thahre Thahregā
ye hai aab-e-rawan na Thahrega
umr ka karwan na Thahrega
chhoD di hai jagah sutunon ne
sar pe ab saeban na Thahrega
ret par hai asar hawaon ka
koi nam-o-nishan na Thahrega
har qadam jo tumhaari samt uTha
sai-e-raegan na Thahrega
marhala aa gaya tasadum ka
fasla darmiyan na Thahrega
dil ka sauda hai kar-e-dil-daran
farq-e-sud-o-ziyan na Thahrega
kyon sunate ho sab ko haal apna
har koi raazdan na Thahrega
chhoD degi zamin mehwar ko
mustaqil aasman na Thahrega
apni aankhon mein aaj use bhar lo
der tak ye saman na Thahrega
juz teri mahfilon ke aur kahin
'abid'-e-na-tawan Thahre Thahrega

ye mere shahr kā ik aur hādisa hogā
vo kal yahāñ mirā mehmān ban chukā hogā
talāsh meñ huuñ kisī kī maiñ kab se sargardāñ
usī tarah koī mujh ko bhī DhūñDhtā hogā
mirī tarah se koī chīḳhtā hai rāhoñ meñ
mirī tarah koī duniyā ko dekhtā hogā
lagā ke aa.egā chehra koī nayā shab meñ
vo jis ko baiTh ke din meñ tarāshtā hogā
shanāsā chehre bhī lagne lage haiñ begāne
ab apnā vaqt hī shāyad badal rahā hogā
udaas udaas sā khoyā huā sā rahtā hai
kuchh us se bhī koī kah kar badal gayā hogā
thakā thakā sā usī dar pe aa ke baiThā thā
na pūchhā hogā kisī ne to chal diyā hogā
jahāñ pahuñch ke qadam Dagmagā.e haiñ sab ke
usī maqām se ab apnā rāsta hogā
ye mere shahr ka ek aur hadisa hoga
wo kal yahan mera mehman ban chuka hoga
talash mein hun kisi ki main kab se sargardan
usi tarah koi mujh ko bhi DhunDhta hoga
meri tarah se koi chiKHta hai rahon mein
meri tarah koi duniya ko dekhta hoga
laga ke aaega chehra koi naya shab mein
wo jis ko baiTh ke din mein tarashta hoga
shanasa chehre bhi lagne lage hain begane
ab apna waqt hi shayad badal raha hoga
udas udas sa khoya hua sa rahta hai
kuchh us se bhi koi kah kar badal gaya hoga
thaka thaka sa usi dar pe aa ke baiTha tha
na puchha hoga kisi ne to chal diya hoga
jahan pahunch ke qadam Dagmagae hain sab ke
usi maqam se ab apna rasta hoga

kaisī kaisī raah meñ dīvāreñ karte haiñ haa.il log
phir bhī manzil pā lete haiñ ham jaise zinda dil log
vo dekho sāgar garjā tūfān uThā nayyā Duubī
aur tamāsha dekh rahe haiñ baiThe sāhil sāhil log
bazm sajā kar bheñT kiye haiñ hamdardī ke chand alfāz
merā dukhḌā baañT rahe haiñ mere ġham meñ shāmil log
bastī bastī ghuum rahe haiñ bhiiḌ bhare chaurāhoñ par
ujle ujle pahnāoñ meñ chehre badle qātil log
TuuT chaleñgī sab āshā.eñ tab hī jīvan raas aa.egā
kuchh din aur kaseñge ham par ta.ane mahfil mahfil log
kitnī ummīdoñ kī sham.eñ jalte hī bujh jaatī haiñ
ab bhī an-chāhe chhātī par dhar hī dete haiñ sil log
barf ke ā.īna-ḳhānoñ meñ sho.aloñ kā siñgār kareñge
aivānoñ meñ aish manā kar taḌpeñge patthar dil log
kaisi kaisi rah mein diwaren karte hain hail log
phir bhi manzil pa lete hain hum jaise zinda dil log
wo dekho sagar garja tufan uTha nayya Dubi
aur tamasha dekh rahe hain baiThe sahil sahil log
bazm saja kar bhenT kiye hain hamdardi ke chand alfaz
mera dukhDa banT rahe hain mere gham mein shamil log
basti basti ghum rahe hain bhiD bhare chaurahon par
ujle ujle pahnaon mein chehre badle qatil log
TuT chalengi sab aashaen tab hi jiwan ras aaega
kuchh din aur kasenge hum par tane mahfil mahfil log
kitni ummidon ki shamen jalte hi bujh jati hain
ab bhi an-chahe chhati par dhar hi dete hain sil log
barf ke aaina-KHanon mein shoalon ka singar karenge
aiwanon mein aish mana kar taDpenge patthar dil log

safar meñ aise ka.ī marhale bhī aate haiñ
har ek moḌ pe kuchh log chhūT jaate haiñ
ye jaan kar bhī ki patthar har ek haath meñ hai
jiyāle log haiñ shīshoñ ke ghar banāte haiñ
jo rahne vaale haiñ log un ko ghar nahīñ dete
jo rahne vaalā nahīñ us ke ghar banāte haiñ
jinheñ ye fikr nahīñ sar rahe rahe na rahe
vo sach hī kahte haiñ jab bolne pe aate haiñ
kabhī jo baat kahī thī tire ta.alluq se
ab us ke bhī ka.ī matlab nikāle jaate haiñ
safar mein aise kai marhale bhi aate hain
har ek moD pe kuchh log chhuT jate hain
ye jaan kar bhi ki patthar har ek hath mein hai
jiyale log hain shishon ke ghar banate hain
jo rahne wale hain log un ko ghar nahin dete
jo rahne wala nahin us ke ghar banate hain
jinhen ye fikr nahin sar rahe rahe na rahe
wo sach hi kahte hain jab bolne pe aate hain
kabhi jo baat kahi thi tere talluq se
ab us ke bhi kai matlab nikale jate hain

sharīk-e-ālam-e-kaif-o-surūr maiñ bhī thā
ki raat jashn meñ tere huzūr maiñ bhī thā
ajiib vaqt thā duniyā qarīb thī mere
ġhazab ye thā tire dāman se duur maiñ bhī thā
ġhamoñ ke ghere meñ jab raqs kar rahī thī hayāt
tamāsh-bīñ kī tarah be-shu.ūr maiñ bhī thā
na ruknā raah meñ shart-e-safar meñ shāmil thā
thakan se varna bahut chuur chuur maiñ bhī thā
utar rahā thā lahū kis balā kā āñkhoñ meñ
tire ḳhayāl meñ us dam zarūr maiñ bhī thā
guzarte vaqt ne pahre baiThā diye 'ābid'
ḳhatā.eñ un kī na thiiñ be-qusūr maiñ bhī thā
sharik-e-alam-e-kaif-o-surur main bhi tha
ki raat jashn mein tere huzur main bhi tha
ajib waqt tha duniya qarib thi mere
ghazab ye tha tere daman se dur main bhi tha
ghamon ke ghere mein jab raqs kar rahi thi hayat
tamash-bin ki tarah be-shuur main bhi tha
na rukna rah mein shart-e-safar mein shamil tha
thakan se warna bahut chur chur main bhi tha
utar raha tha lahu kis bala ka aankhon mein
tere KHayal mein us dam zarur main bhi tha
guzarte waqt ne pahre baiTha diye 'abid'
KHataen un ki na thin be-qusur main bhi tha

pardes meñ huuñ aur ghanī tīrgī to hai
par mutma.in huuñ raat tire shahr kī to hai
dhartī pe aa raheñgī abhī sab bulandiyāñ
chaTTān dhīre dhīre khisakne lagī to hai
is kā to ġham nahīñ ki muḳhālif sabhī hue
chubhtī huī sī baat bhī ham ne kahī to hai
phailā ke haath pair na so jaa.e chāñdnī
sāhil hai rut javān hai aur raat bhī to hai
kholo na khiḌkiyāñ ki saverā nahīñ huā
bujhte hue diye haiñ abhī raushnī to hai
tanhā.ī meñ ye kaun hai chauñkā gayā mujhe
vo aadmī nahīñ na sahī par koī to hai
pardes mein hun aur ghani tirgi to hai
par mutmain hun raat tere shahr ki to hai
dharti pe aa rahengi abhi sab bulandiyan
chaTTan dhire dhire khisakne lagi to hai
is ka to gham nahin ki muKHalif sabhi hue
chubhti hui si baat bhi hum ne kahi to hai
phaila ke hath pair na so jae chandni
sahil hai rut jawan hai aur raat bhi to hai
kholo na khiDkiyan ki sawera nahin hua
bujhte hue diye hain abhi raushni to hai
tanhai mein ye kaun hai chaunka gaya mujhe
wo aadmi nahin na sahi par koi to hai

maiñ apne jism meñ kuchh is tarah se bikhrā huuñ
ki ye bhī kah nahīñ saktā maiñ kaun huuñ kyā huuñ
unheñ ḳhushī hai isī baat se ki zinda huuñ
maiñ un kī daa.eñ hathelī kī ek rekhā huuñ
maiñ pī gayā huuñ ka.ī āñsuoñ ke sail-e-ravāñ
maiñ apne dil ko samundar banā.e baiThā huuñ
vo mere dost jo ek ek kar ke duur hue
maiñ un ko aaj bhī apne qarīb paatā huuñ
muhīt karne kī koshish fuzūl hai mujh ko
nadī kā chhor nahīñ huuñ maiñ bahtā dariyā huuñ
mujhī pe pheñke hai patthar jo koī aatā hai
ki jaise maiñ tirī khiḌkī kā koī shīsha huuñ
main apne jism mein kuchh is tarah se bikhra hun
ki ye bhi kah nahin sakta main kaun hun kya hun
unhen KHushi hai isi baat se ki zinda hun
main un ki daen hatheli ki ek rekha hun
main pi gaya hun kai aansuon ke sail-e-rawan
main apne dil ko samundar banae baiTha hun
wo mere dost jo ek ek kar ke dur hue
main un ko aaj bhi apne qarib pata hun
muhit karne ki koshish fuzul hai mujh ko
nadi ka chhor nahin hun main bahta dariya hun
mujhi pe phenke hai patthar jo koi aata hai
ki jaise main teri khiDki ka koi shisha hun

safar kā shauq na manzil kī justujū baaqī
musāfiroñ ke badan meñ nahīñ lahū baaqī
tamām raat havāoñ kā gasht jaarī thā
savere tak na rahā koī hū-ba-hū baaqī
sabhī tarah se ta.āruf to ho gayā un kā
rahī hai ab to mulāqāt rū-ba-rū baaqī
jo bhiiḌ bikhre to dekhūñ talab ye kaisī hai
dayār-e-ġhair meñ hai kis kī justujū baaqī
vahī nazāre vahī garmī-e-suḳhan hai magar
na hī vo baat na vo tarz-e-guftugū baaqī
zamāna mujh se judā ho gayā zamāna huā
rahā hai ab to bichhaḌne ko mujh se tū baaqī
usī lihāz kā 'ābid' malāl hai ham ko
rahā na aaj jo daurān-e-guftugū baaqī
safar ka shauq na manzil ki justuju baqi
musafiron ke badan mein nahin lahu baqi
tamam raat hawaon ka gasht jari tha
sawere tak na raha koi hu-ba-hu baqi
sabhi tarah se taaruf to ho gaya un ka
rahi hai ab to mulaqat ru-ba-ru baqi
jo bhiD bikhre to dekhun talab ye kaisi hai
dayar-e-ghair mein hai kis ki justuju baqi
wahi nazare wahi garmi-e-suKHan hai magar
na hi wo baat na wo tarz-e-guftugu baqi
zamana mujh se juda ho gaya zamana hua
raha hai ab to bichhaDne ko mujh se tu baqi
usi lihaz ka 'abid' malal hai hum ko
raha na aaj jo dauran-e-guftugu baqi

kār-nāma ai ġham-e-dil kuchh tirā ye kam nahīñ
bah ga.e āñkhoñ se dariyā aur āñkheñ nam nahīñ
saaf thā har lafz us kī be-badal taqrīr kā
phir lahū ne naqsh jo chhoḌe haiñ vo mub.ham nahīñ
har zamāne meñ nahīñ pahchānñā mushkil unheñ
sar qalam hote raheñge un ke lekin ġham nahīñ
karbalā hī ne kiye haiñ murtasim dil par nuqūsh
