varna is duniyā meñ ġham kī vārdāteñ kam nahīñ
dil hī dil vo bhīgī lakḌī kī tarah sulgā kiyā
us ke chehre se to lagtā thā ki koī ġham nahīñ
kaifiyat kaisī ajab is shahr kī yādoñ kī hai
garm hai ātish nahīñ aur sard hai shabnam nahīñ
ik alag tahzīb hai tanhā.iyoñ ke shahr kī
ek hī aalam hamesha aur koī mausam nahīñ
phir rahe haiñ log phir hāthoñ meñ sañg-reze liye
aur apne sar meñ saudā is ghaḌī kuchh kam nahīñ
ham se 'ābid' apne rahbar ko shikāyat ye rahī
aañkh mūñde un ke pīchhe chalne vaale ham nahīñ
kar-nama ai gham-e-dil kuchh tera ye kam nahin
bah gae aankhon se dariya aur aankhen nam nahin
saf tha har lafz us ki be-badal taqrir ka
phir lahu ne naqsh jo chhoDe hain wo mubham nahin
har zamane mein nahin pahchanna mushkil unhen
sar qalam hote rahenge un ke lekin gham nahin
karbala hi ne kiye hain murtasim dil par nuqush
warna is duniya mein gham ki wardaten kam nahin
dil hi dil wo bhigi lakDi ki tarah sulga kiya
us ke chehre se to lagta tha ki koi gham nahin
kaifiyat kaisi ajab is shahr ki yaadon ki hai
garm hai aatish nahin aur sard hai shabnam nahin
ek alag tahzib hai tanhaiyon ke shahr ki
ek hi aalam hamesha aur koi mausam nahin
phir rahe hain log phir hathon mein sang-reze liye
aur apne sar mein sauda is ghaDi kuchh kam nahin
hum se 'abid' apne rahbar ko shikayat ye rahi
aankh munde un ke pichhe chalne wale hum nahin

gītoñ kā shahr hai ki nagar soz-o-sāz kā
qalb-e-shikasta aur ye aalam gudāz kā
chāroñ taraf sajī haiñ dukāneñ ḳhulūs kī
chamkā hai kārobār har ik hīlā-sāz kā
vo chāhe ḳhvāb ho ki haqīqat magar kabhī
ehsāñ uThā.egā na libās-e-majāz kā
jis tarah chāhā jaa.e hai chāhā nahīñ abhī
andesha jaan khaa.e hai ifshā-e-rāz kā
bahrūpiyā hai koī phire hai nagar nagar
qātil kā ruup dhāre kabhī chārasāz kā
yuuñ hañste hañste dār-e-fanā se chalā hai vo
jaise safar nasīb ho arz-e-hijāz kā
'ābid' ġhamoñ kī dhuup meñ jalnā hai chaar din
bas qissa muḳhtasar hai ye umr-e-darāz kā
giton ka shahr hai ki nagar soz-o-saz ka
qalb-e-shikasta aur ye aalam gudaz ka
chaaron taraf saji hain dukanen KHulus ki
chamka hai karobar har ek hila-saz ka
wo chahe KHwab ho ki haqiqat magar kabhi
ehsan uThaega na libas-e-majaz ka
jis tarah chaha jae hai chaha nahin abhi
andesha jaan khae hai ifsha-e-raaz ka
bahrupiya hai koi phire hai nagar nagar
qatil ka rup dhaare kabhi chaarasaz ka
yun hanste hanste dar-e-fana se chala hai wo
jaise safar nasib ho arz-e-hijaz ka
'abid' ghamon ki dhup mein jalna hai chaar din
bas qissa muKHtasar hai ye umr-e-daraaz ka

hādsoñ se be-ḳhabar the log dhartī par tamām
āsmāñ kī nīlgūñ āñkhoñ meñ the manzar tamām
rafta rafta rasm-e-sañg-bārī jahāñ se uTh ga.ī
dhīre dhīre ho ga.e bastī ke sab patthar tamām
tishna-lab dhartī pe jab bahtā hai pyāsoñ kā lahū
muddatoñ maqtal meñ sar ḳham rahte haiñ ḳhanjar tamām
zindagī bikhrī huī hai is tarah fōtpath par
bastiyāñ ābād haiñ aur log haiñ be-ghar tamām
shāhrāheñ daf.atan sho.ale ugalne lag ga.iiñ
ghar kī jānib chal paḌā hai shahr ghabrā kar tamām
sub.h ke saare ujāle rāstoñ meñ kho ga.e
shab ke añdhiyāroñ meñ gum haiñ shaam ke manzar tamām
ab kahāñ vo log vo raunaq vo naġhme vo fazā
shahr kī galiyāñ haiñ suunī suune bām-o-dar tamām
hadson se be-KHabar the log dharti par tamam
aasman ki nilgun aankhon mein the manzar tamam
rafta rafta rasm-e-sang-bari jahan se uTh gai
dhire dhire ho gae basti ke sab patthar tamam
tishna-lab dharti pe jab bahta hai pyason ka lahu
muddaton maqtal mein sar KHam rahte hain KHanjar tamam
zindagi bikhri hui hai is tarah footpath par
bastiyan aabaad hain aur log hain be-ghar tamam
shahrahen dafatan shoale ugalne lag gain
ghar ki jaanib chal paDa hai shahr ghabra kar tamam
subh ke sare ujale raston mein kho gae
shab ke andhiyaron mein gum hain sham ke manzar tamam
ab kahan wo log wo raunaq wo naghme wo faza
shahr ki galiyan hain suni sune baam-o-dar tamam

gulāb rangoñ ko zā'frānī nahīñ karūñgā
maiñ aise paudoñ kī bāġhbānī nahīñ karūñgā
kisī kī ḳhātir ġhalat-bayānī nahīñ karūñgā
maiñ jhūTe logoñ kī tarjumānī nahīñ karūñgā
sunā hai ab vo ḳhilāf mere gavāhī degā
jo kah rahā thā ki bad-gumānī nahīñ karūñgā
sazā maiñ ḳhud ko kabhī na dūñgā tire kiye kī
jigar ko chhalnī lahū ko paanī nahīñ karūñgā
tumhāre ġham kā tumhārī yādoñ kā maiñ amiiñ huuñ
kahā thā tum se ki be-imānī nahīñ karūñgā
mu'āf tujh ko maiñ pahle bhī kar chukā huuñ lekin
dubāra tujh par ye mehrbānī nahīñ karūñgā
ye ġhair-mumkin hai phir bhī hākim banā to 'ādil'
sitam-rasīdoñ pe hukmrānī nahīñ karūñgā
gulab rangon ko za'frani nahin karunga
main aise paudon ki baghbani nahin karunga
kisi ki KHatir ghalat-bayani nahin karunga
main jhuTe logon ki tarjumani nahin karunga
suna hai ab wo KHilaf mere gawahi dega
jo kah raha tha ki bad-gumani nahin karunga
saza main KHud ko kabhi na dunga tere kiye ki
jigar ko chhalni lahu ko pani nahin karunga
tumhaare gham ka tumhaari yaadon ka main amin hun
kaha tha tum se ki be-imani nahin karunga
mu'af tujh ko main pahle bhi kar chuka hun lekin
dubara tujh par ye mehrbani nahin karunga
ye ghair-mumkin hai phir bhi hakim bana to 'adil'
sitam-rasidon pe hukmrani nahin karunga

apnī āñkhoñ se tabāhī ye nazāra dekhūñ
yā'nī tujh ko maiñ kisī aur kā hotā dekhūñ
merī dīvāngī is moḌ pe le aa.ī hai
har kisī chehre meñ bas ek hī chehra dekhūñ
ye jo tasvīr musavvir ne banā.ī varna
chāñd ko Thahre hue paanī meñ chaltā dekhūñ
tishnagī laakh sahī par ye nahīñ ho saktā
ḳhud ko lāchār banā.ūñ sū-e-dariyā dekhūñ
ye tirī zid ki taḌaptā huā dekhe mujh ko
merī ḳhvāhish ki hamesha tujhe hañstā dekhūñ
sāmne tujh ko biThā.ūñ tirā māthā chūmūñ
terī āñkheñ tirī zulfeñ tirā chehra dekhūñ
do qadam chal ke ye dil ne kahā 'ādil-rāhī'
āḳhirī baar palaT kar use jaatā dekhūñ
apni aankhon se tabahi ye nazara dekhun
ya'ni tujh ko main kisi aur ka hota dekhun
meri diwangi is moD pe le aai hai
har kisi chehre mein bas ek hi chehra dekhun
ye jo taswir musawwir ne banai warna
chand ko Thahre hue pani mein chalta dekhun
tishnagi lakh sahi par ye nahin ho sakta
KHud ko lachaar banaun su-e-dariya dekhun
ye teri zid ki taDapta hua dekhe mujh ko
meri KHwahish ki hamesha tujhe hansta dekhun
samne tujh ko biThaun tera matha chumun
teri aankhen teri zulfen tera chehra dekhun
do qadam chal ke ye dil ne kaha 'adil-rahi'
aaKHiri bar palaT kar use jata dekhun

us ne ye fāsla is vāste rakkhā hogā
paas aa kar mire baiThegā to charchā hogā
aaj phir us ne mujhe yaad kiyā hai shāyad
dil ne yūñhī to nahīñ shor machāyā hogā
dekhnā log mohabbat kī misāleñ deñge
naam aa.egā mirā zikr tumhārā hogā
dard bechainī taḌap ranj-o-alam tanhā.ī
ham ne sochā hī nahīñ itnā ḳhasāra hogā
jis ko din-rāt duāoñ meñ hai māñgā ham ne
vaqt aa.egā kisī din vo hamārā hogā
hijr is vāste manzūr kiyā hai maiñ ne
terā har zaḳhm mujhe dil se gavārā hogā
us kī bechainī batātī hai ki aadil 'rāhī'
bhūlā-bisrā hī koī yaad to aatā hogā
us ne ye fasla is waste rakkha hoga
pas aa kar mere baiThega to charcha hoga
aaj phir us ne mujhe yaad kiya hai shayad
dil ne yunhi to nahin shor machaya hoga
dekhna log mohabbat ki misalen denge
nam aaega mera zikr tumhaara hoga
dard bechaini taDap ranj-o-alam tanhai
hum ne socha hi nahin itna KHasara hoga
jis ko din-raat duaon mein hai manga hum ne
waqt aaega kisi din wo hamara hoga
hijr is waste manzur kiya hai main ne
tera har zaKHm mujhe dil se gawara hoga
us ki bechaini batati hai ki aadil 'rahi'
bhula-bisra hi koi yaad to aata hoga

use tum se mohabbat hai ġhalat-fahmī meñ mat rahnā
ye bas dil kī sharārat hai ġhalat-fahmī meñ mat rahnā
tumhī ko dekh kar vo muskurātā hai to hairat kyā
use hañsne kī aadat hai ġhalat-fahmī meñ mat rahnā
hue barbād to ab āh-o-zārī kar rahe ho tum
kahā bhī thā siyāsat hai ġhalat-fahmī meñ mat rahnā
maiñ tujh ko chāhtā huuñ baat ye sach hai magar phir bhī
mujhe terī zarūrat hai ġhalat-fahmī meñ mat rahnā hī
jhukī nazroñ se taknā aur ḳhamoshī se guzar jaanā
mohabbat kī rivāyat hai ġhalat-fahmī meñ mat rahnā
kiyā kartā huuñ 'rāhī' us kī tārīfeñ sabab ye hai
vo mujh se ḳhūbsūrat hai ġhalat-fahmī meñ mat rahnā
use tum se mohabbat hai ghalat-fahmi mein mat rahna
ye bas dil ki shararat hai ghalat-fahmi mein mat rahna
tumhi ko dekh kar wo muskuraata hai to hairat kya
use hansne ki aadat hai ghalat-fahmi mein mat rahna
hue barbaad to ab aah-o-zari kar rahe ho tum
kaha bhi tha siyasat hai ghalat-fahmi mein mat rahna
main tujh ko chahta hun baat ye sach hai magar phir bhi
mujhe teri zarurat hai ghalat-fahmi mein mat rahna hi
jhuki nazron se takna aur KHamoshi se guzar jaana
mohabbat ki riwayat hai ghalat-fahmi mein mat rahna
kiya karta hun 'rahi' us ki tarifen sabab ye hai
wo mujh se KHubsurat hai ghalat-fahmi mein mat rahna

kasak dil kī miTāne meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
kisī kā ġham bhulāne meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
kisī ko chaah kar apnā banānā Thiik hai lekin
mohabbat āzmāne meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
tumheñ paane kī ḳhvāhish meñ huā ehsās ye mujh ko
muqaddar āzmāne meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
jise minnat murādoñ se baḌī mushkil se paayā ho
use dil se bhulāne meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
ki jis dil kī zamīñ barsoñ se banjar ho to phir us par
na.ī chāhat ugāne meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
ġhazal paḌh kar to āsānī se mahfil luuT sakte ho
magar izzat kamāne meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
dil-e-muztar ko āḳhir kaun samjhā.egā ai 'rāhī'
sukūn-e-qalb paane meñ zarā sī der lagtī hai
kasak dil ki miTane mein zara si der lagti hai
kisi ka gham bhulane mein zara si der lagti hai
kisi ko chah kar apna banana Thik hai lekin
mohabbat aazmane mein zara si der lagti hai
tumhein pane ki KHwahish mein hua ehsas ye mujh ko
muqaddar aazmane mein zara si der lagti hai
jise minnat muradon se baDi mushkil se paya ho
use dil se bhulane mein zara si der lagti hai
ki jis dil ki zamin barson se banjar ho to phir us par
nai chahat ugane mein zara si der lagti hai
ghazal paDh kar to aasani se mahfil luT sakte ho
magar izzat kamane mein zara si der lagti hai
dil-e-muztar ko aaKHir kaun samjhaega ai 'rahi'
sukun-e-qalb pane mein zara si der lagti hai

gard jam jaa.e to shīsha nahīñ dekhā jaatā
ya.anī tasvīr ko dhuñdlā nahīñ dekhā jaatā
tishnagī aa tujhe dariyā ke havāle kar duuñ
tujh ko is haal meñ pyāsā nahīñ dekhā jaatā
tum mirā nām-o-nasab pūchh rahe ho sab se
ishq ho jaa.e to shajara nahīñ dekhā jaatā
lauT aane kī tasallī tirī jhūTī hī sahī
ab to muḌ-muḌ ke yuuñ rasta nahīñ dekhā jaatā
sher achchhe jo bure lagte haiñ duniyā ko mire
ho ġhazal meñ tirā charchā nahīñ dekhā jaatā
log milte haiñ bichhaḌte haiñ magar kyoñ mujh se
yuuñ tirā chhoḌ ke jaanā nahīñ dekhā jaatā
izz-o-tauqīr kā ye haal hasad meñ ham se
qad kisī kā bhī ho ūñchā nahīñ dekhā jaatā
gard jam jae to shisha nahin dekha jata
yani taswir ko dhundla nahin dekha jata
tishnagi aa tujhe dariya ke hawale kar dun
tujh ko is haal mein pyasa nahin dekha jata
tum mera nam-o-nasab puchh rahe ho sab se
ishq ho jae to shajara nahin dekha jata
lauT aane ki tasalli teri jhuTi hi sahi
ab to muD-muD ke yun rasta nahin dekha jata
sher achchhe jo bure lagte hain duniya ko mere
ho ghazal mein tera charcha nahin dekha jata
log milte hain bichhaDte hain magar kyon mujh se
yun tera chhoD ke jaana nahin dekha jata
izz-o-tauqir ka ye haal hasad mein hum se
qad kisi ka bhi ho uncha nahin dekha jata

hijr kā sog manānā kabhī dariyā ronā
yaad kar ke tujhe hañsnā kabhī ronā ronā
kyā batā.ūñ use kis baat pe hañste dekhā
kyā batā.ūñ mujhe kis baat pe aaya ronā
kaise bhūlūñgā vo bebāk adā.eñ us kī
us kī bāteñ to vo hañsnā vo lipaTnā ronā
baat auroñ kī nahīñ tū to mirā apnā thā
kaash tujh ko nazar aatā mire dil kā ronā
koī to baat use itnā rulātī hogī
achchhā lagtā hai kise TuuT ke tanhā ronā
tum to ḳhush the na mujhe chhoḌ ke jāte-jāte
vaqt-e-ruḳhsat tumheñ kis baat pe aaya ronā
muddatoñ baad ye ehsās huā hai 'rāhī'
muddatoñ baad phir aaya mujhe itnā ronā
hijr ka sog manana kabhi dariya rona
yaad kar ke tujhe hansna kabhi rona rona
kya bataun use kis baat pe hanste dekha
kya bataun mujhe kis baat pe aaya rona
kaise bhulunga wo bebak adaen us ki
us ki baaten to wo hansna wo lipaTna rona
baat auron ki nahin tu to mera apna tha
kash tujh ko nazar aata mere dil ka rona
koi to baat use itna rulati hogi
achchha lagta hai kise TuT ke tanha rona
tum to KHush the na mujhe chhoD ke jate-jate
waqt-e-ruKHsat tumhein kis baat pe aaya rona
muddaton baad ye ehsas hua hai 'rahi'
muddaton baad phir aaya mujhe itna rona

tujhe yaad kar ke bhulāne se pahle
maiñ royā bahut muskurāne se pahle
ki ro-ro ke sonā to hañs-hañs ke uThnā
ham aise na the dil lagāne se pahle
mire ḳhvāb rah jaa.eñ na phir adhūre
jabīñ chuum lenā jagāne se pahle
tum apnī tabāhī kā mātam to kar lo
mire haal pe muskurāne se pahle
bahut yaad aa.egī pāgal sī laḌkī
ye sochā nahīñ thā bhulāne se pahle
maiñ TuuTā maiñ bikhrā huā reza-reza
mirī jaañ tire ḳhat jalāne se pahle
tumheñ sirf ranj-o-alam hī mileñge
zarā soch lo dil lagāne se pahle
ġhazal pesh-e-ḳhidmat hai 'rāhī' kī sun lo
kahā us ne sab ko sunāne se pahle
tujhe yaad kar ke bhulane se pahle
main roya bahut muskurane se pahle
ki ro-ro ke sona to hans-hans ke uThna
hum aise na the dil lagane se pahle
mere KHwab rah jaen na phir adhure
jabin chum lena jagane se pahle
tum apni tabahi ka matam to kar lo
mere haal pe muskurane se pahle
bahut yaad aaegi pagal si laDki
ye socha nahin tha bhulane se pahle
main TuTa main bikhra hua reza-reza
meri jaan tere KHat jalane se pahle
tumhein sirf ranj-o-alam hi milenge
zara soch lo dil lagane se pahle
ghazal pesh-e-KHidmat hai 'rahi' ki sun lo
kaha us ne sab ko sunane se pahle

maiñ na kahtā thā mire yaar badal jaatā hai
vaqt kitnā bhī ho dushvār badal jaatā hai
maiñ ne bas dil kī sunī varna tire baare meñ
log kahte the ḳhabar-dār badal jaatā hai
hākim-e-vaqt yuuñ maġhrūr na ban hosh meñ aa
piir aatā hai to itvār badal jaatā hai
tujh pe kaise ho yaqīñ mujh ko ki ab tū yaksar
apnā kahtā to hai har baar badal jaatā hai
ye nazākat ye dikhāvā ye takabbur achchhā
yā'nī daulat se bhī me'yār badal jaatā hai
dekhne vaalo haqārat se na dekho mujh ko
bhuuk se jism kā ākār badal jaatā hai
kyā batā.ūñ ki mohabbat ke safar meñ 'rāhī'
ġham to rah jaatā hai ġham-ḳhvār badal jaatā hai
main na kahta tha mere yar badal jata hai
waqt kitna bhi ho dushwar badal jata hai
main ne bas dil ki suni warna tere bare mein
log kahte the KHabar-dar badal jata hai
hakim-e-waqt yun maghrur na ban hosh mein aa
pir aata hai to itwar badal jata hai
tujh pe kaise ho yaqin mujh ko ki ab tu yaksar
apna kahta to hai har bar badal jata hai
ye nazakat ye dikhawa ye takabbur achchha
ya'ni daulat se bhi me'yar badal jata hai
dekhne walo haqarat se na dekho mujh ko
bhuk se jism ka aakar badal jata hai
kya bataun ki mohabbat ke safar mein 'rahi'
gham to rah jata hai gham-KHwar badal jata hai

jise ham kah sakeñ apnā koī aisā nahīñ miltā
tire hamnām milte haiñ koī tujh sā nahīñ miltā
mohabbat ke safar meñ haiñ musāfir ham musāfir tum
hameñ manzil nahīñ miltī tumheñ rasta nahīñ miltā
kisī kī ruḳhsatī ke baad tanhā.ī ke aalam meñ
ġhamoñ kā saath hotā hai koī tanhā nahīñ miltā
samajh lenā koī maqsad hai us kī chāplūsī meñ
jhukā kar sar koī iḳhlās se itnā nahīñ miltā
jidhar dekho udhar sach bolne vaale hī milte haiñ
ta.ajjub hai koī is daur meñ jhūTā nahīñ miltā
talab hai raushnī kī to jalāo ḳhud diyā 'rāhī'
bujhāne tishnagī pyāse kī to dariyā nahīñ miltā
jise hum kah saken apna koi aisa nahin milta
tere hamnam milte hain koi tujh sa nahin milta
mohabbat ke safar mein hain musafir hum musafir tum
hamein manzil nahin milti tumhein rasta nahin milta
kisi ki ruKHsati ke baad tanhai ke aalam mein
ghamon ka sath hota hai koi tanha nahin milta
samajh lena koi maqsad hai us ki chaplusi mein
jhuka kar sar koi iKHlas se itna nahin milta
jidhar dekho udhar sach bolne wale hi milte hain
tajjub hai koi is daur mein jhuTa nahin milta
talab hai raushni ki to jalao KHud diya 'rahi'
bujhane tishnagi pyase ki to dariya nahin milta

hai asar is tarah dil par ishq kī tāsīr kā
āj-kal hai haal jaisā vādī-e-kashmīr kā
yuuñ to duniyā kā koī manzar mujhe bhāyā nahīñ
haañ magar shaidā huā huuñ maiñ tirī tasvīr kā
hai mirī duniyā meñ terī ahmiyat kuchh is tarah
martaba hai shā.erī meñ jis tarah se 'mīr' kā
yaad tum aaoge mujh ko merī jaañ ye jaan lo
zikr jab bhī aa.egā merī ġhazal meñ hiir kā
maiñ ne to bas ain likkhā thā lifāfe par magar
jaane kyā samjhā hai matlab us ne is tahrīr kā
tum se milnā aur phir mil kar bichhaḌ jaane kā ġham
faisla shāyad yahī hai kātib-e-taqdīr kā
sher maiñ ne bhī sunā.e ḳhuub 'rāhī' rāt-bhar
zikr chheḌā thā kisī ne bazm meñ jab 'mīr' kā
hai asar is tarah dil par ishq ki tasir ka
aaj-kal hai haal jaisa wadi-e-kashmir ka
yun to duniya ka koi manzar mujhe bhaya nahin
han magar shaida hua hun main teri taswir ka
hai meri duniya mein teri ahmiyat kuchh is tarah
martaba hai shaeri mein jis tarah se 'mir' ka
yaad tum aaoge mujh ko meri jaan ye jaan lo
zikr jab bhi aaega meri ghazal mein hir ka
main ne to bas ain likkha tha lifafe par magar
jaane kya samjha hai matlab us ne is tahrir ka
tum se milna aur phir mil kar bichhaD jaane ka gham
faisla shayad yahi hai katib-e-taqdir ka
sher main ne bhi sunae KHub 'rahi' raat-bhar
zikr chheDa tha kisi ne bazm mein jab 'mir' ka

tū ne hī har qadam pe diyā hausla mujhe
yārab nahīñ hai tere sivā aasrā mujhe
ik baar us ne kah to diyā dilrubā mujhe
taktā rahā maiñ aa.ine ko aa.ina mujhe
jin ke liye sanad thī mirī baat kal talak
dene lage haiñ aaj vahī mashvara mujhe
college meñ is liye bhī to jaatā rahā ki vo
ai kaash ik nazar hī sahī dekhtā mujhe
nārāz apne aap se huuñ maan yā na maan
tujh se shikāyateñ haiñ na koī gila mujhe
har aan har ḳhushī hai milī is ke bāvajūd
kyoñ lag rahī hai zindagī merī sazā mujhe
hāfiz mirā ḳhudā hai so kahnā fuzūl hai
apne sivā kisī kā nahīñ aasrā mujhe
is 'ain shiin qaaf meñ ik pal sukūñ nahīñ
detā hai jaise 'rāhī' koī bad-du'ā mujhe
tu ne hi har qadam pe diya hausla mujhe
yarab nahin hai tere siwa aasra mujhe
ek bar us ne kah to diya dilruba mujhe
takta raha main aaine ko aaina mujhe
jin ke liye sanad thi meri baat kal talak
dene lage hain aaj wahi mashwara mujhe
college mein is liye bhi to jata raha ki wo
ai kash ek nazar hi sahi dekhta mujhe
naraaz apne aap se hun man ya na man
tujh se shikayaten hain na koi gila mujhe
har aan har KHushi hai mili is ke bawajud
kyon lag rahi hai zindagi meri saza mujhe
hafiz mera KHuda hai so kahna fuzul hai
apne siwa kisi ka nahin aasra mujhe
is 'ain shin qaf mein ek pal sukun nahin
deta hai jaise 'rahi' koi bad-du'a mujhe

terī har baat pe tanqīd nahīñ kar saktā
haañ magar jhuuT kī tā.īd nahīñ kar saktā
tū agar jaan bhī māñge to ḳhushī se de duuñ
maiñ tire hukm kī tardīd nahīñ kar saktā
āḳhirī 'ishq kiyā maiñ ne magar pahlī baar
dūsrī baar ye tafrīd nahīñ kar saktā
maiñ ne dekhā hai badaltā huā lahja terā
is liye tujh se to ummīd nahīñ kar saktā
tū ne is haal meñ chhoḌā hai ki allāh allāh
'iid kā din hai magar 'iid nahīñ kar saktā
ye alag baat suḳhanvar huuñ maiñ 'ādil-rāhī'
dard itne haiñ ki tasvīr nahīñ kar saktā
teri har baat pe tanqid nahin kar sakta
han magar jhuT ki taid nahin kar sakta
tu agar jaan bhi mange to KHushi se de dun
main tere hukm ki tardid nahin kar sakta
aaKHiri 'ishq kiya main ne magar pahli bar
dusri bar ye tafrid nahin kar sakta
main ne dekha hai badalta hua lahja tera
is liye tujh se to ummid nahin kar sakta
tu ne is haal mein chhoDa hai ki allah allah
'id ka din hai magar 'id nahin kar sakta
ye alag baat suKHanwar hun main 'adil-rahi'
dard itne hain ki taswir nahin kar sakta

jin logoñ se merī yaarī hotī hai
un meñ koī baat to pyārī hotī
duniyā meñ ik shaḳhs hī pyārā lagtā hai
ham aisoñ meñ ye bīmārī hotī hai
jab bhī apne yāroñ se miltā huuñ maiñ
jaane kyoñ bas baat tumhārī hotī hai
sab ko dil kā raaz batānā Thiik nahīñ
duniyā-dārī duniyā-dārī hotī hai
jhuuT bahut āsān hai lekin ai 'rāhī'
sach kahne meñ kuchh dushvārī hotī hai
jin logon se meri yari hoti hai
un mein koi baat to pyari hoti
duniya mein ek shaKHs hi pyara lagta hai
hum aison mein ye bimari hoti hai
jab bhi apne yaron se milta hun main
jaane kyon bas baat tumhaari hoti hai
sab ko dil ka raaz batana Thik nahin
duniya-dari duniya-dari hoti hai
jhuT bahut aasan hai lekin ai 'rahi'
sach kahne mein kuchh dushwari hoti hai

vahāñ shāyad koī baiThā huā hai
abhī khiḌkī meñ ik jaltā diyā hai
mirā dil bhī ajab ḳhālī viyā hai
kisī kī yaad ne jis ko bharā hai
parinde shāḳh se lipTe hue haiñ
ye kaisā ḳhauf ḳhema-zan huā hai
mirī ḳhāmoshiyoñ kī jhiil meñ phir
kisī āvāz kā patthar girā hai
mohabbat kā muqaddar dekhte ho
havā ne kuchh to paanī par likhā hai
usī par khul rahe haiñ saare mausam
jo apne ghar se bāhar aa gayā hai
charāġho ab zarā apnī sunāo
havā kā kaam puurā ho chukā hai
mohabbat phir vahīñ le aa.ī 'ādil'
ye jañgal bār-hā dekhā huā hai
wahan shayad koi baiTha hua hai
abhi khiDki mein ek jalta diya hai
mera dil bhi ajab KHali wiya hai
kisi ki yaad ne jis ko bhara hai
parinde shaKH se lipTe hue hain
ye kaisa KHauf KHema-zan hua hai
meri KHamoshiyon ki jhil mein phir
kisi aawaz ka patthar gira hai
mohabbat ka muqaddar dekhte ho
hawa ne kuchh to pani par likha hai
usi par khul rahe hain sare mausam
jo apne ghar se bahar aa gaya hai
charagho ab zara apni sunao
hawa ka kaam pura ho chuka hai
mohabbat phir wahin le aai 'adil'
ye jangal bar-ha dekha hua hai

jo ashk ban ke hamārī palak pe baiThā thā
tumheñ bhī yaad hai ab tak vo ḳhvāb kis kā thā
hamesha pūchhtī rahtī hai rāstoñ kī havā
yūñhī ruke ho yahāñ yā kisī ne rokā thā
lagā huā hai abhī tak ye jaan ko khaTkā
ki us ne jaate hue kyuuñ palaT ke dekhā thā
ḳhabar kise hai kise pūchhiye batā.e kaun
purāne qasr meñ kyā sub.h-o-shām jaltā thā
vajūd hai ye kahīñ bah na jaa.e lahroñ meñ
girā girā ke palak aabjū ko rokā thā
fazā.eñ aisī to 'ādil' kabhī na mahkī thiiñ
havā ke haath pe ye kis kā naam likkhā thā
jo ashk ban ke hamari palak pe baiTha tha
tumhein bhi yaad hai ab tak wo KHwab kis ka tha
hamesha puchhti rahti hai raston ki hawa
yunhi ruke ho yahan ya kisi ne roka tha
laga hua hai abhi tak ye jaan ko khaTka
ki us ne jate hue kyun palaT ke dekha tha
KHabar kise hai kise puchhiye batae kaun
purane qasr mein kya subh-o-sham jalta tha
wajud hai ye kahin bah na jae lahron mein
gira gira ke palak aabju ko roka tha
fazaen aisi to 'adil' kabhi na mahki thin
hawa ke hath pe ye kis ka nam likkha tha

rāste sikhāte haiñ kis se kyā alag rakhnā
manzileñ alag rakhnā qāfila alag rakhnā
ba.ad ek muddat ke lauT kar vo aayā hai
aaj to kahānī se hādisa alag rakhnā
jis se ham ne sīkhā thā saath saath chalnā hai
ab vahī batātā hai naqsh-e-pā alag rakhnā
kūza-gar ne jaane kyuuñ aadmī banāyā hai
us ko sab khilaunoñ se tum zarā alag rakhnā
lauT kar to aa.e ho tajraboñ kī sūrat hai
par mirī kahānī se falsafa alag rakhnā
tum to ḳhuub vāqif ho ab tumhī batāo nā
kis meñ kyā milānā hai kis se kyā alag rakhnā
ḳhvāhishoñ kā ḳhamyāza ḳhvāb kyuuñ bhareñ 'ādil'
aaj merī āñkhoñ se rat-jagā alag rakhnā
raste sikhate hain kis se kya alag rakhna
manzilen alag rakhna qafila alag rakhna
baad ek muddat ke lauT kar wo aaya hai
aaj to kahani se hadisa alag rakhna
jis se hum ne sikha tha sath sath chalna hai
ab wahi batata hai naqsh-e-pa alag rakhna
kuza-gar ne jaane kyun aadmi banaya hai
us ko sab khilaunon se tum zara alag rakhna
lauT kar to aae ho tajrabon ki surat hai
par meri kahani se falsafa alag rakhna
tum to KHub waqif ho ab tumhi batao na
kis mein kya milana hai kis se kya alag rakhna
KHwahishon ka KHamyaza KHwab kyun bharen 'adil'
aaj meri aankhon se rat-jaga alag rakhna

paañv pattoñ pe dhīre se dhartā huā
vo guzar jā.egā yuuñ hī Dartā huā
bojh sūraj kā sar par uThāne ko hai
ek saaya nadī meñ utartā huā
shaam sāhil pe gum-sum sī baiThī huī
aur dariyā meñ sonā bikhartā huā
tere aane kī us ko ḳhabar kis ne dī
ek āshufta-sar hai sañvartā huā
dekhtā rah gayā apnī parchhā.iyāñ
vaqt guzrā hai kitnā Thahartā huā
panw patton pe dhire se dharta hua
wo guzar jaega yun hi Darta hua
bojh suraj ka sar par uThane ko hai
ek saya nadi mein utarta hua
sham sahil pe gum-sum si baiThi hui
aur dariya mein sona bikharta hua
tere aane ki us ko KHabar kis ne di
ek aashufta-sar hai sanwarta hua
dekhta rah gaya apni parchhaiyan
waqt guzra hai kitna Thaharta hua

din ke siine pe shaam kā patthar
ek patthar pe dūsrā patthar
ye sunā thā ki devtā hai vo
mere haq hī meñ kyuuñ huā patthar
dā.ere bante aur miTte the
jhiil meñ jab kabhī girā patthar
ab to ābād hai vahāñ bastī
ab kahāñ tere naam kā patthar
ho ga.e manziloñ ke sab raahī
de rahā hai kise sadā patthar
saare taare zamīñ pe gir jaate
zor se maiñ jo pheñktā patthar
naam ne kaam kar dikhāyā hai
sab ne dekhā hai tairtā patthar
tū use kyā uThā.egā 'ādil'
'mīr' tak se na uTh sakā patthar
din ke sine pe sham ka patthar
ek patthar pe dusra patthar
ye suna tha ki dewta hai wo
mere haq hi mein kyun hua patthar
daere bante aur miTte the
jhil mein jab kabhi gira patthar
ab to aabaad hai wahan basti
ab kahan tere nam ka patthar
ho gae manzilon ke sab rahi
de raha hai kise sada patthar
sare tare zamin pe gir jate
zor se main jo phenkta patthar
nam ne kaam kar dikhaya hai
sab ne dekha hai tairta patthar
tu use kya uThaega 'adil'
'mir' tak se na uTh saka patthar

safar ke ba.ad bhī mujh ko safar meñ rahnā hai
nazar se girnā bhī goyā ḳhabar meñ rahnā hai
abhī se os ko kirnoñ se pī rahe ho tum
tumheñ to ḳhvāb sā āñkhoñ ke ghar meñ rahnā hai
havā to aap kī qismat meñ honā likkhā thā
magar maiñ aag huuñ mujh ko shajar meñ rahnā hai
nikal ke ḳhud se jo ḳhud hī meñ Duub jaatā hai
maiñ vo safīna huuñ jis ko bhañvar meñ rahnā hai
tumhāre ba.ad koī rāsta nahīñ miltā
to tai huā ki udāsī ke ghar meñ rahnā hai
jalā ke kaun mujhe ab chale kisī kī taraf
bujhe diye ko to 'ādil' khañDar meñ rahnā hai
safar ke baad bhi mujh ko safar mein rahna hai
nazar se girna bhi goya KHabar mein rahna hai
abhi se os ko kirnon se pi rahe ho tum
tumhein to KHwab sa aankhon ke ghar mein rahna hai
hawa to aap ki qismat mein hona likkha tha
magar main aag hun mujh ko shajar mein rahna hai
nikal ke KHud se jo KHud hi mein Dub jata hai
main wo safina hun jis ko bhanwar mein rahna hai
tumhaare baad koi rasta nahin milta
to tai hua ki udasi ke ghar mein rahna hai
jala ke kaun mujhe ab chale kisi ki taraf
bujhe diye ko to 'adil' khanDar mein rahna hai

ek ik lamhe ko palkoñ pe sajātā huā ghar
raas aatā hai kise hijr manātā huā ghar
ḳhvāb ke ḳhadshe se ab niiñd uḌī jaatī hai
maiñ ne dekhā hai use chhoḌ ke jaatā huā ghar
gar zabāñ hotī to patthar hī batātā sab ko
kis qadar TuuTā hai vo ḳhud ko banātā huā ghar
us kā ab zikr na kar chhoḌ ke jaane vaale
tū ne dekhā hī kahāñ ashk bahātā huā ghar
ab use yaad kahūñ yaas kahūñ yā vahshat
mujh ko aatā hai nazar ḳhaak uḌātā huā ghar
thak gayā kyā mire tūlānī safar se 'ādil'
so gayā saath mire mujh ko sulātā huā ghar
ek ek lamhe ko palkon pe sajata hua ghar
ras aata hai kise hijr manata hua ghar
KHwab ke KHadshe se ab nind uDi jati hai
main ne dekha hai use chhoD ke jata hua ghar
gar zaban hoti to patthar hi batata sab ko
kis qadar TuTa hai wo KHud ko banata hua ghar
us ka ab zikr na kar chhoD ke jaane wale
tu ne dekha hi kahan ashk bahata hua ghar
ab use yaad kahun yas kahun ya wahshat
mujh ko aata hai nazar KHak uData hua ghar
thak gaya kya mere tulani safar se 'adil'
so gaya sath mere mujh ko sulata hua ghar

chāñd taare banā ke kāġhaz par
ḳhush hue ghar sajā ke kāġhaz par
bastiyāñ kyuuñ talāsh karte haiñ
log jañgal ugā ke kāġhaz par
jaane kyā ham se kah gayā mausam
ḳhushk pattā girā ke kāġhaz par
hañste hañste miTā diye us ne
shahr kitne basā ke kāġhaz par
ham ne chāhā ki ham bhī uḌ jaa.eñ
ek chiḌiyā uḌā ke kāġhaz par
log sāhil talāsh karte haiñ
ek dariyā bahā ke kāġhaz par
naav sūraj kī dhuup kā dariyā
tham ga.e kaise aa ke kāġhaz par
ḳhvāb bhī ḳhvāb ho ga.e 'ādil'
shakl-o-sūrat dikhā ke kāġhaz par
chand tare bana ke kaghaz par
KHush hue ghar saja ke kaghaz par
bastiyan kyun talash karte hain
log jangal uga ke kaghaz par
jaane kya hum se kah gaya mausam
KHushk patta gira ke kaghaz par
hanste hanste miTa diye us ne
shahr kitne basa ke kaghaz par
hum ne chaha ki hum bhi uD jaen
ek chiDiya uDa ke kaghaz par
log sahil talash karte hain
ek dariya baha ke kaghaz par
naw suraj ki dhup ka dariya
tham gae kaise aa ke kaghaz par
KHwab bhi KHwab ho gae 'adil'
shakl-o-surat dikha ke kaghaz par

mausam-e-gul meñ bhī gul nazr-e-ḳhizāñ haiñ saare
mutma.in koī nahīñ mahv-e-fuġhāñ haiñ saare
hosh-mandī se qadam aage baḌhāo logo
apnī jānib hī khiñche tīr-o-kamāñ haiñ saare
chahchahāne kī sadā aa.ī thī kal tak jin se
jaane kyoñ aaj vo ḳhāmosh makāñ haiñ saare
sirf dīvār kī ūñchā.ī nazar aatī hai
ai mire shahr mire log kahāñ haiñ saare
ab ḳhudā ḳhair kare qāfila vāloñ kī mire
kho.e kho.e hue manzil ke nishāñ haiñ saare
kitnā dhuñdlā diyā hālāt ne tum ko 'shauqī'
jin ko tum abr samajhte ho dhuāñ haiñ saare
mausam-e-gul mein bhi gul nazr-e-KHizan hain sare
mutmain koi nahin mahw-e-fughan hain sare
hosh-mandi se qadam aage baDhao logo
apni jaanib hi khinche tir-o-kaman hain sare
chahchahane ki sada aai thi kal tak jin se
jaane kyon aaj wo KHamosh makan hain sare
sirf diwar ki unchai nazar aati hai
ai mere shahr mere log kahan hain sare
ab KHuda KHair kare qafila walon ki mere
khoe khoe hue manzil ke nishan hain sare
kitna dhundla diya haalat ne tum ko 'shauqi'
jin ko tum abr samajhte ho dhuan hain sare

terī ummīd ke asbāb nazar aate nahīñ
kyoñ mujhe koī hasīñ ḳhvāb nazar aate nahīñ
itnā bhaTkā huuñ aziyyat ke bayābāñ meñ ki ab
koī bhī lamha-e-nāyāb nazar aate nahīñ
kis qadar dhuñdle haiñ mazlūm kī aahoñ se falak
mehr-o-anjum huuñ ki mahtāb nazar aate nahīñ
dast-bardār nahīñ rasm-e-ta.alluq se maiñ
phir bhalā kyoñ mujhe ahbāb nazar aate nahīñ
itnī duurī hai ab un se ki mujhe ai 'shauqī'
chain se haiñ ki vo betāb nazar aate nahīñ
teri ummid ke asbab nazar aate nahin
kyon mujhe koi hasin KHwab nazar aate nahin
itna bhaTka hun aziyyat ke bayaban mein ki ab
koi bhi lamha-e-nayab nazar aate nahin
kis qadar dhundle hain mazlum ki aahon se falak
mehr-o-anjum hun ki mahtab nazar aate nahin
dast-bardar nahin rasm-e-talluq se main
phir bhala kyon mujhe ahbab nazar aate nahin
itni duri hai ab un se ki mujhe ai 'shauqi'
chain se hain ki wo betab nazar aate nahin

ai ḳhudā hasrat-o-jazbāt ke maare hue log
ab kahāñ jaa.eñ ye hālāt ke maare hue log
terī duniyā kī kahānī bhī ajab hai maulā
dar-ba-dar rahte haiñ haq baat ke maare hue log
sub.h-e-nau ke liye zambīl-e-talab laa.e haiñ
dasht-e-vīrāñ meñ siyah raat ke maare hue log
tū bhī ārām zarā kar le ġhubār-e-manzil
abhī so.e haiñ musāfāt ke maare hue log
ho ke māyūs parī-ḳhāne se lauTe 'shauqī'
jaane kyoñ shoḳh ishārāt ke maare hue log
ai KHuda hasrat-o-jazbaat ke mare hue log
ab kahan jaen ye haalat ke mare hue log
teri duniya ki kahani bhi ajab hai maula
dar-ba-dar rahte hain haq baat ke mare hue log
subh-e-nau ke liye zambil-e-talab lae hain
dasht-e-viran mein siyah raat ke mare hue log
tu bhi aaram zara kar le ghubar-e-manzil
abhi soe hain musafat ke mare hue log
ho ke mayus pari-KHane se lauTe 'shauqi'
jaane kyon shoKH ishaaraat ke mare hue log

mas.ale aur bhī haiñ ishq ke āzār ke saath
sirf ik karb nahīñ umr kī raftār ke saath
haa.e mahrūmī-e-qismat ki tujhe pā na sake
ham har ik samt ga.e hasrat-e-dīdār ke saath
kaise maiñ aap kī tāzīm bajā lā.ūñgā
merī bantī hī nahīñ hāshiya-bardār ke saath
abhī ḳhush-rang hai tābānī mire āñgan kī
ranjisheñ hone lagīñ kyoñ dar-o-dīvār ke saath
dars dete haiñ bahut log payambar vaale
baiThtā koī nahīñ muflis-o-nādār ke saath
us ke hisse kā bhī ġham mujh ko atā kar de magar
an-ginat ḳhushiyāñ rahīñ maulā mire yaar ke saath
guftugū kā bhī salīqa nahīñ jin ko 'shauqī'
aaj phirte haiñ vahī mansab-o-dastār ke saath
masale aur bhi hain ishq ke aazar ke sath
sirf ek karb nahin umr ki raftar ke sath
hae mahrumi-e-qismat ki tujhe pa na sake
hum har ek samt gae hasrat-e-didar ke sath
kaise main aap ki tazim baja launga
meri banti hi nahin hashiya-bardar ke sath
abhi KHush-rang hai tabani mere aangan ki
ranjishen hone lagin kyon dar-o-diwar ke sath
dars dete hain bahut log payambar wale
baiThta koi nahin muflis-o-nadar ke sath
us ke hisse ka bhi gham mujh ko ata kar de magar
an-ginat KHushiyan rahin maula mere yar ke sath
guftugu ka bhi saliqa nahin jin ko 'shauqi'
aaj phirte hain wahi mansab-o-dastar ke sath

kaun sukh-chain se hai kis kī pazīrā.ī hai
terī duniyā meñ har ik moḌ pe rusvā.ī hai
jhiil sī āñkheñ tirī aur gulābī tire hoñT
merī chāhat ke hī sadqe meñ ye ra.anā.ī hai
maiñ jo chup-chāp sā baiThā huuñ tirī mahfil meñ
ye mirā shauq nahīñ zarbat-e-tanhā.ī hai
ghar meñ ghuT ghuT ke hī mar jaate haiñ bīmār ġharīb
ab shifā-ḳhāne meñ is auj pe mahñgā.ī hai
maiñ samundar to nahīñ adnā sā shā.ir huuñ magar
dariyā se baḌh ke mire sher meñ gahrā.ī hai
jaan kar bhī nahīñ pahchānte haiñ 'shauqī' log
terī bastī meñ ajab tarz-e-shanāsā.ī hai
kaun sukh-chain se hai kis ki pazirai hai
teri duniya mein har ek moD pe ruswai hai
jhil si aankhen teri aur gulabi tere honT
meri chahat ke hi sadqe mein ye ranai hai
main jo chup-chap sa baiTha hun teri mahfil mein
ye mera shauq nahin zarbat-e-tanhai hai
ghar mein ghuT ghuT ke hi mar jate hain bimar gharib
ab shifa-KHane mein is auj pe mahngai hai
main samundar to nahin adna sa shair hun magar
dariya se baDh ke mere sher mein gahrai hai
jaan kar bhi nahin pahchante hain 'shauqi' log
teri basti mein ajab tarz-e-shanasai hai

nasīb meñ hai judā.ī to ronā-dhonā kyā
hai saarī chiiz parā.ī to ronā-dhonā kyā
yahāñ to apne hī apnoñ ko maar dete haiñ
havā ne sham.a bujhā.ī to ronā-dhonā kyā
usī ne haath baḌhāyā thā dostī ke liye
usī ne baat baḌhā.ī to ronā-dhonā kyā
mire aziiz hī jab mere munharif nikle
huī ḳhilāf ḳhudā.ī to ronā-dhonā kyā
hazār saal ke jab būḌhe mar ga.e 'shauqī'
kamā.ī chiiz gañvā.ī to ronā-dhonā kyā
nasib mein hai judai to rona-dhona kya
hai sari chiz parai to rona-dhona kya
yahan to apne hi apnon ko mar dete hain
hawa ne shama bujhai to rona-dhona kya
usi ne hath baDhaya tha dosti ke liye
usi ne baat baDhai to rona-dhona kya
mere aziz hi jab mere munharif nikle
hui KHilaf KHudai to rona-dhona kya
hazar sal ke jab buDhe mar gae 'shauqi'
kamai chiz ganwai to rona-dhona kya

sard mausam hai bahut hijr kā āzār bhī hai
kyā kaheñ tujh se ye dil ġham meñ giraftār bhī hai
kaise kah duuñ kī tire baa'd mujhe chain paḌā
sub.h ġhamgīn mirī raat dil-āzār bhī hai
zindagī kahtī hai Thahro na baḌho aur baḌho
manzileñ duur haiñ aur rāsta dushvār bhī hai
na.ī ta.amīr kā saudā hai sar-o-dil meñ magar
sāmne sahn kī girtī huī dīvār bhī hai
merā maddāh mire fan se nahīñ shahr kā shahr
ḳhud kī pahchān meñ kirdār kā kirdār bhī hai
har kisī se nahīñ miltā huuñ maiñ jhuk kar 'shauqī'
darmiyāñ apne koī chiiz ye me.aar bhī hai
sard mausam hai bahut hijr ka aazar bhi hai
kya kahen tujh se ye dil gham mein giraftar bhi hai
kaise kah dun ki tere ba'd mujhe chain paDa
subh ghamgin meri raat dil-azar bhi hai
zindagi kahti hai Thahro na baDho aur baDho
manzilen dur hain aur rasta dushwar bhi hai
nai tamir ka sauda hai sar-o-dil mein magar
samne sahn ki girti hui diwar bhi hai
mera maddah mere fan se nahin shahr ka shahr
KHud ki pahchan mein kirdar ka kirdar bhi hai
har kisi se nahin milta hun main jhuk kar 'shauqi'
darmiyan apne koi chiz ye mear bhi hai

tanhā.ī kī āġhosh meñ thā sub.h se pahle
miltī rahī ulfat kī sazā sub.h se pahle
shāyad mire lafzoñ pe taras aa.e use ab
rote hue māñgī hai duā sub.h se pahle
saaya bhī mirā kho gayā tārīki-e-shab meñ
zulmat kā asar aisā rahā sub.h se pahle
jab raat meñ so jaatī hai ye saarī ḳhudā.ī
detā hai mujhe kaun sadā sub.h se pahle
shāyad ki muqaddar meñ na ho kal kā ye sūraj
ho jaa.e har ik qarz adā sub.h se pahle
'shauqī' tujhe mil jā.eñge shaiḳh aur barahman
is shahr ke maiḳhāne meñ aa sub.h se pahle
tanhai ki aaghosh mein tha subh se pahle
milti rahi ulfat ki saza subh se pahle
shayad mere lafzon pe taras aae use ab
rote hue mangi hai dua subh se pahle
saya bhi mera kho gaya tariki-e-shab mein
zulmat ka asar aisa raha subh se pahle
jab raat mein so jati hai ye sari KHudai
deta hai mujhe kaun sada subh se pahle
shayad ki muqaddar mein na ho kal ka ye suraj
ho jae har ek qarz ada subh se pahle
'shauqi' tujhe mil jaenge shaiKH aur barahman
is shahr ke maiKHane mein aa subh se pahle

Dūbte Dūbte sūraj ne ziyā.eñ diiñ haiñ
terī yādoñ ne bahut dil ko sadā.eñ diiñ haiñ
ye adālat kisī tahrīr kī muhtāj nahīñ
vaqt ne har kas-o-nā-kas ko sazā.eñ diiñ haiñ
zindagī tujh ko barahna nahīñ rakkhā hai kabhī
ham ne har dard ko lafzoñ kī qabā.eñ diiñ haiñ
sirf fayyāzī ke qisse na muarriḳh likhnā
bujhte sho.aloñ ko bhī to us ne havā.eñ diiñ haiñ
shā.erī yūñhī nahīñ puḳhta mirī ai 'shauqī'
mere ustād ne kuchh aisī duā.eñ diiñ haiñ
Dubte Dubte suraj ne ziyaen din hain
teri yaadon ne bahut dil ko sadaen din hain
ye adalat kisi tahrir ki muhtaj nahin
waqt ne har kas-o-na-kas ko sazaen din hain
zindagi tujh ko barahna nahin rakkha hai kabhi
hum ne har dard ko lafzon ki qabaen din hain
sirf fayyazi ke qisse na muarriKH likhna
bujhte shoalon ko bhi to us ne hawaen din hain
shaeri yunhi nahin puKHta meri ai 'shauqi'
mere ustad ne kuchh aisi duaen din hain

ai ḳhudā kaisā samāñ aayā hai
shahr meñ har sū dhuāñ chhāyā hai
luT ga.ī ḳhalq-e-ḳhudā kī hasrat
ahd-e-nau aisā ziyāñ laayā hai
hijr ke dasht meñ yaksar maiñ ne
ġham ke dariyā ko ravāñ paayā hai
sirf mujh ko nahīñ daulat kī talab
sab ko darkār yahāñ maayā hai
baḌī mushkil se jahāñ ko 'shauqī'
merā andāz-e-bayāñ bhāyā hai
ai KHuda kaisa saman aaya hai
shahr mein har su dhuan chhaya hai
luT gai KHalq-e-KHuda ki hasrat
ahd-e-nau aisa ziyan laya hai
hijr ke dasht mein yaksar main ne
gham ke dariya ko rawan paya hai
sirf mujh ko nahin daulat ki talab
sab ko darkar yahan maya hai
baDi mushkil se jahan ko 'shauqi'
mera andaz-e-bayan bhaya hai

yahī nahīñ ki faqat pyaar karne aa.e haiñ
ham ek umr kā tāvān bharne aa.e haiñ
vo ek rañg mukammal ho jis se terā vajūd
vo rañg ham tire ḳhāke meñ bharne aa.e haiñ
ThiThur na jaa.eñ ham is ijz kī bulandī par
ham apnī sat.h se nīche utarne aa.e haiñ
ye buuñd ḳhuun kī lauh-e-kitāb-e-ruḳh ke liye
ye til sar-e-lab-o-ruḳhsār dharne aa.e haiñ
lagā rahe haiñ abhī ḳheme ġham kī vaadī meñ
ham is pahāḌ se dāman ko bharne aa.e haiñ
tire laboñ ko milī hai shaguftagī gul kī
hamārī aañkh ke hisse meñ jharne aa.e haiñ
'nisār' band-e-qabā kholnā muhāl na thā
so ham jamāl-e-qabā band karne aa.e haiñ
yahi nahin ki faqat pyar karne aae hain
hum ek umr ka tawan bharne aae hain
wo ek rang mukammal ho jis se tera wajud
wo rang hum tere KHake mein bharne aae hain
ThiThur na jaen hum is ijz ki bulandi par
hum apni sath se niche utarne aae hain
ye bund KHun ki lauh-e-kitab-e-ruKH ke liye
ye til sar-e-lab-o-ruKHsar dharne aae hain
laga rahe hain abhi KHeme gham ki wadi mein
hum is pahaD se daman ko bharne aae hain
tere labon ko mili hai shaguftagi gul ki
hamari aankh ke hisse mein jharne aae hain
'nisar' band-e-qaba kholna muhaal na tha
so hum jamal-e-qaba band karne aae hain

jo ban-sañvar ke vo ik māh-rū nikaltā hai
to har zabān se bas allāh-hū nikaltā hai
halāl rizq kā matlab kisān se pūchho
pasīna ban ke badan se lahū nikaltā hai
zamīn aur muqaddar kī ek hai fitrat
ki jo bhī boyā vahī hū-ba-hū nikaltā hai
ye chāñd raat hī dīdār kā vasīla hai
ba-roz-e-īd hī vo ḳhūb-rū nikaltā hai
tire baġhair gulistāñ ko kyā huā 'ādil'
jo gul nikaltā hai be-rañg-o-bū nikaltā hai
jo ban-sanwar ke wo ek mah-ru nikalta hai
to har zaban se bas allah-hu nikalta hai
halal rizq ka matlab kisan se puchho
pasina ban ke badan se lahu nikalta hai
zamin aur muqaddar ki ek hai fitrat
ki jo bhi boya wahi hu-ba-hu nikalta hai
ye chand raat hi didar ka wasila hai
ba-roz-e-id hi wo KHub-ru nikalta hai
tere baghair gulistan ko kya hua 'adil'
jo gul nikalta hai be-rang-o-bu nikalta hai

'ishq meñ jānñā zarūrī hai
kyā nahīñ aur kyā zarūrī hai
kaam lījiye dimāġh se lekin
dil se bhī mashvara zarūrī hai
dār-e-zulmat meñ raushnī ke liye
nusḳha-e-kīmiyā zarūrī hai
chheḌ kar chhoḌ ne meñ ḳhatra hai
saañp ko mārnā zarūrī hai
rishta rakhiye masarratoñ se magar
ġham se bhī rābta zarūrī hai
ḳhāmushī achchhī chiiz hai lekin
vaqt par bolnā zarūrī hai
jo bhī patthar-sifat haiñ un se zarā
ā.īno fāsla zarūrī hai
aarzū hai agar gulāboñ kī
shāḳh-e-gul se vafā zarūrī hai
'ishq mein jaanna zaruri hai
kya nahin aur kya zaruri hai
kaam lijiye dimagh se lekin
dil se bhi mashwara zaruri hai
dar-e-zulmat mein raushni ke liye
nusKHa-e-kimiya zaruri hai
chheD kar chhoD ne mein KHatra hai
sanp ko marna zaruri hai
rishta rakhiye masarraton se magar
gham se bhi rabta zaruri hai
KHamushi achchhi chiz hai lekin
waqt par bolna zaruri hai
jo bhi patthar-sifat hain un se zara
aaino fasla zaruri hai
aarzu hai agar gulabon ki
shaKH-e-gul se wafa zaruri hai

vo tasavvur meñ to aatā hai chalā jaatā hai
dhaḌkaneñ dil kī baḌhātā hai chalā jaatā hai
hone lagtā hai mujhe jab bhī takabbur kā gumāñ
koī ā.īna dikhātā hai chalā jaatā hai
koī darvesh mujhe roz savālī ban kar
ḳhvāb-e-ġhaflat se jagātā hai chalā jaatā hai
kaun hai dost yahāñ kaun hamārā dushman
gardish-e-vaqt batātā hai chalā jaatā hai
merī turbat pe sar-e-shām du'āoñ kā charāġh
koī ashkoñ se jalātā hai chalā jaatā hai
baiTh jaatā huuñ rah-e-'ishq meñ thak kar to junūñ
manzil-e-shauq baḌhātā hai chalā jaatā hai
vaqt aatā hai dabe paañv hamesha 'ālam'
sab kī auqāt batātā hai chalā jaatā hai
wo tasawwur mein to aata hai chala jata hai
dhaDkanen dil ki baDhata hai chala jata hai
hone lagta hai mujhe jab bhi takabbur ka guman
koi aaina dikhata hai chala jata hai
koi darwesh mujhe roz sawali ban kar
KHwab-e-ghaflat se jagata hai chala jata hai
kaun hai dost yahan kaun hamara dushman
gardish-e-waqt batata hai chala jata hai
meri turbat pe sar-e-sham du'aon ka charagh
koi ashkon se jalata hai chala jata hai
baiTh jata hun rah-e-'ishq mein thak kar to junun
manzil-e-shauq baDhata hai chala jata hai
waqt aata hai dabe panw hamesha 'alam'
sab ki auqat batata hai chala jata hai

is se pahle mirī ḳhvāhish mujhe rusvā kar de
izzat-e-nafs ko ḳhāliq mire zinda kar de
mujh se duniyā kī ye hālat nahīñ dekhī jaatī
mere mālik mere ehsās ko andhā kar de
dekh achchhā nahīñ ahbāb kī ġhībat karnā
ye amal tujh ko kisī roz na tanhā kar de
aa na jaa.e kahīñ lahje meñ takabbur yā-rab
mere baḌhte hue qad ko zarā chhoTā kar de
shādmānī meñ tirī yaad nahīñ aatī hai
koī ġham mujh ko atā mere masīhā kar de
is se pahle meri KHwahish mujhe ruswa kar de
izzat-e-nafs ko KHaliq mere zinda kar de
mujh se duniya ki ye haalat nahin dekhi jati
mere malik mere ehsas ko andha kar de
dekh achchha nahin ahbab ki ghibat karna
ye amal tujh ko kisi roz na tanha kar de
aa na jae kahin lahje mein takabbur ya-rab
mere baDhte hue qad ko zara chhoTa kar de
shadmani mein teri yaad nahin aati hai
koi gham mujh ko ata mere masiha kar de

chāhtā jo bhī hai vo kah ke guzar jaatā hai
dil-e-hassās is ehsās se mar jaatā hai
zehn meñ baat buzurgoñ kī tabhī baiThtī hai
jab javānī kā nasha sar se utar jaatā hai
jab anā merī zarūrat kā galā ghoñTtī hai
rang ḳhud-dārī ke chehre kā utar jaatā hai
Dasne lagtī hai mirī ḳhāna-badoshī mujh ko
jab koī panchhī kabhī shaam ko ghar jaatā hai
jhūTī tārīf se hotī hai masarrat us ko
aa.ina koī dikhā de to biphar jaatā hai
jurm kartā hai koī aur yahāñ par aalam
aur ilzām kisī aur ke sar jaatā hai
chahta jo bhi hai wo kah ke guzar jata hai
dil-e-hassas is ehsas se mar jata hai
zehn mein baat buzurgon ki tabhi baiThti hai
jab jawani ka nasha sar se utar jata hai
jab ana meri zarurat ka gala ghonTti hai
rang KHud-dari ke chehre ka utar jata hai
Dasne lagti hai meri KHana-badoshi mujh ko
jab koi panchhi kabhi sham ko ghar jata hai
jhuTi tarif se hoti hai masarrat us ko
aaina koi dikha de to biphar jata hai
jurm karta hai koi aur yahan par aalam
aur ilzam kisi aur ke sar jata hai

haiñ uljhaneñ tamām mirī zindagī ke saath
insāf kar rahā huuñ magar shā'irī ke saath
ye aur baat hai maiñ ziyāda na mil sakūñ
miltā nahīñ kisī se magar be-dilī ke saath
kaam aa.ī tīrgī meñ charāġhoñ kī dostī
guzrī shab-e-hayāt mirī raushnī ke saath
bikhre hue vajūd ko apne sameT kar
ham jiinā chāhte haiñ baḌī sādgī ke saath
hai jis kā jaisā zarf vo vaisā kiyā kare
karte nahīñ haiñ ham to daġhā dostī ke saath
'ālam' amīr-e-shahr bhī kartā hai ehtirām
rahte haiñ itnī shaan se ham muflisī ke saath
hain uljhanen tamam meri zindagi ke sath
insaf kar raha hun magar sha'iri ke sath
ye aur baat hai main ziyaada na mil sakun
milta nahin kisi se magar be-dili ke sath
kaam aai tirgi mein charaghon ki dosti
guzri shab-e-hayat meri raushni ke sath
bikhre hue wajud ko apne sameT kar
hum jina chahte hain baDi sadgi ke sath
hai jis ka jaisa zarf wo waisa kiya kare
karte nahin hain hum to dagha dosti ke sath
'alam' amir-e-shahr bhi karta hai ehtiram
rahte hain itni shan se hum muflisi ke sath

kabhī shafaq to kabhī gul kabhī jināñ mahke
tumhāre naqsh-e-qadam bhī kahāñ kahāñ mahke
koī amīn-e-sadāqat idhar se guzrā hai
qadam qadam pe jo yuuñ rāh-e-imtihāñ mahke
ye kis ke naam kī ḳhushbū hai mere she'roñ meñ
nafas nafas hai mo'attar mashām-e-jāñ mahke
chaman-badosh vo aa.e mire tasavvur meñ
mire ḳhayāl-o-ma'ānī kā kul-jahāñ mahke
ye kis ne raḳht-e-safar bāñdhne kī Thānī hai
zamīn vajd meñ hai aur āsmāñ mahke
jinhoñ ne rāh-e-sadāqat meñ apnī jāneñ diiñ
paḌho jo dāstāñ un kī to dāstāñ mahke
kabhi shafaq to kabhi gul kabhi jinan mahke
tumhaare naqsh-e-qadam bhi kahan kahan mahke
koi amin-e-sadaqat idhar se guzra hai
qadam qadam pe jo yun rah-e-imtihan mahke
ye kis ke nam ki KHushbu hai mere she'ron mein
nafas nafas hai mo'attar masham-e-jaan mahke
chaman-badosh wo aae mere tasawwur mein
mere KHayal-o-ma'ani ka kul-jahan mahke
ye kis ne raKHt-e-safar bandhne ki Thani hai
zamin wajd mein hai aur aasman mahke
jinhon ne rah-e-sadaqat mein apni jaanen din
paDho jo dastan un ki to dastan mahke

rang īsār ke chehre kā nikhartā kaise
zaḳhm ahbāb na dete to sañvartā kaise
mirī qismat meñ bulandī kā safar likkhā thā
sāzish-e-vaqt se pastī meñ utartā kaise
hausla thā mirā mazbūt pahāḌoñ kī tarah
TuuT kar tinkoñ kī mānind bikhartā kaise
saaya thā hī nahīñ maalī kā chaman ke sar par
rang phūloñ kā yatīmī meñ nikhartā kaise
muddatoñ rahnā thā jis peḌ ke saa.e meñ mujhe
us kī shāḳhoñ ko batāo maiñ kutartā kaise
maiñ ne chāhā thā zarā der vo Thahre 'ālam'
vo to bahtā huā dariyā thā Thahartā kaise
rang isar ke chehre ka nikharta kaise
zaKHm ahbab na dete to sanwarta kaise
meri qismat mein bulandi ka safar likkha tha
sazish-e-waqt se pasti mein utarta kaise
hausla tha mera mazbut pahaDon ki tarah
TuT kar tinkon ki manind bikharta kaise
saya tha hi nahin mali ka chaman ke sar par
rang phulon ka yatimi mein nikharta kaise
muddaton rahna tha jis peD ke sae mein mujhe
us ki shaKHon ko batao main kutarta kaise
main ne chaha tha zara der wo Thahre 'alam'
wo to bahta hua dariya tha Thaharta kaise

maiñ samajh rahā thā ki vaqt ne tirā naam dil se miTā diyā
shab-e-ġham magar tirī yaad ne mujhe aaj phir se rulā diyā
na hai tīrgī se gila koī na hai raushnī kī talab mujhe
mirī hasratoñ ke charāġh ko tirī be-ruḳhī ne bujhā diyā
ye mire hī zarf kī baat thī na kisī se kuchh bhī kahā magar
tirī furqatoñ kā jo dard thā mire āñsuoñ ne batā diyā
mire ham-nashīñ mire ham-navā tujhe nazr kyā karūñ maiñ batā
mirā dil bhī merā nahīñ rahā tire 'ishq meñ hī luTā diyā
na masarratoñ se sukūn kī kabhī chand sāñseñ 'atā huiiñ
ġham-e-zindagī tirā shukriya mujhe tū ne jiinā sikhā diyā
kahūñ us ko achchhā yā maiñ burā nahīñ hotā mujh se ye faisla
kabhī dostī ne vafā kiyā kabhī dostī ne daġhā diyā
main samajh raha tha ki waqt ne tera nam dil se miTa diya
shab-e-gham magar teri yaad ne mujhe aaj phir se rula diya
na hai tirgi se gila koi na hai raushni ki talab mujhe
meri hasraton ke charagh ko teri be-ruKHi ne bujha diya
ye mere hi zarf ki baat thi na kisi se kuchh bhi kaha magar
teri furqaton ka jo dard tha mere aansuon ne bata diya
mere ham-nashin mere ham-nawa tujhe nazr kya karun main bata
mera dil bhi mera nahin raha tere 'ishq mein hi luTa diya
na masarraton se sukun ki kabhi chand sansen 'ata huin
gham-e-zindagi tera shukriya mujhe tu ne jina sikha diya
kahun us ko achchha ya main bura nahin hota mujh se ye faisla
kabhi dosti ne wafa kiya kabhi dosti ne dagha diya

ghar meñ ārām kā saaya nahīñ rahne detī
ab to tanhā.ī bhī tanhā nahīñ rahne detī
muflisī kitnī ḳhatarnāk hai tum kyā jaano
ye salāmat koī rishta nahīñ rahne detī
ye to achchhā huā sāñsoñ pe nahīñ bas us kā
varna duniyā mujhe zinda nahīñ rahne detī
chāhtī kyā hai ye āvāra-mizājī merī
ek markaz pe hamesha nahīñ rahne detī
kyā burī shai hai ye shohrat kī havas bhī 'ālam'
achchhe-achchhoñ ko bhī achchhā nahīñ rahne detī
ghar mein aaram ka saya nahin rahne deti
ab to tanhai bhi tanha nahin rahne deti
muflisi kitni KHatarnak hai tum kya jaano
ye salamat koi rishta nahin rahne deti
ye to achchha hua sanson pe nahin bas us ka
warna duniya mujhe zinda nahin rahne deti
chahti kya hai ye aawara-mizaji meri
ek markaz pe hamesha nahin rahne deti
kya buri shai hai ye shohrat ki hawas bhi 'alam'
achchhe-achchhon ko bhi achchha nahin rahne deti

naqsh-e-hastī miTā bhī detā hai
hādisa hausla bhī detā hai
sab vafādār to nahīñ hote
yaar koī daġhā bhī detā hai
vaqt kartā hai chashm-poshī bhī
haath meñ aa.ina bhī detā hai
aañkh meñ chubhtā hai ġhubār magar
qāfile kā pata bhī detā hai
aaj ke daur meñ huā sābit
khoTā sikka sadā bhī detā hai
naqsh-e-hasti miTa bhi deta hai
hadisa hausla bhi deta hai
sab wafadar to nahin hote
yar koi dagha bhi deta hai
waqt karta hai chashm-poshi bhi
hath mein aaina bhi deta hai
aankh mein chubhta hai ghubar magar
qafile ka pata bhi deta hai
aaj ke daur mein hua sabit
khoTa sikka sada bhi deta hai

ai añdhere raushnī kī zad meñ aanā chhoḌ de
āftāb-e-vaqt par unglī uThānā chhoḌ de
ḳhud-baḳhud mahfūz ho jā.egī terī aabrū
maġhribī tahzīb se ḳhud ko sajānā chhoḌ de
nasl-e-nau meñ haq-parastī kī sifat aa jā.egī
luqma-e-tar apne bachchoñ ko khilānā chhoḌ de
mauj-e-tūfāñ se nipaTnā ḳhuub aatā hai mujhe
merī kashtī ko bhañvar āñkheñ dikhānā chhoḌ de
qābiliyyat hai agar tujh meñ to kuchh ban kar batā
tanz kī talvār duniyā par chalānā chhoḌ de
ai amīr-e-shahr ghar meñ raushnī ke vāste
ḳhuun muflis kā charāġhoñ meñ jalānā chhoḌ de
bol kar aatā nahīñ insān par vaqt-e-zavāl
mere ḳhasta-hāl par tū muskurānā chhoḌ de
ai andhere raushni ki zad mein aana chhoD de
aaftab-e-waqt par ungli uThana chhoD de
KHud-baKHud mahfuz ho jaegi teri aabru
maghribi tahzib se KHud ko sajaana chhoD de
nasl-e-nau mein haq-parasti ki sifat aa jaegi
luqma-e-tar apne bachchon ko khilana chhoD de
mauj-e-tufan se nipaTna KHub aata hai mujhe
meri kashti ko bhanwar aankhen dikhana chhoD de
qabiliyyat hai agar tujh mein to kuchh ban kar bata
tanz ki talwar duniya par chalana chhoD de
ai amir-e-shahr ghar mein raushni ke waste
KHun muflis ka charaghon mein jalana chhoD de
bol kar aata nahin insan par waqt-e-zawal
mere KHasta-haal par tu muskurana chhoD de

aisā lagtā hai vo nādān samajhte haiñ mujhe
jo bhī tafrīh kā sāmān samajhte haiñ mujhe
ḳhairiyat bhī mirī mā'lūm nahīñ karte haiñ
is-qadar log pareshān samajhte haiñ mujhe
shahr se aao to aane kā sabab pūchhte haiñ
gaañv ke log bhī mehmān samajhte haiñ mujhe
is liye merī ḳhushāmad nahīñ kartā koī
sab manānā bahut āsān samajhte haiñ mujhe
maiñ huuñ fankār to fankār hī samjhā jaa.e
aap kyoñ hindū musalmān samajhte haiñ mujhe
maiñ ne har zaḳhm pe marham kī numā.ish kī hai
jaane kyoñ log namakdān samajhte haiñ mujhe
log kyā kahte haiñ parvāh nahīñ hai 'ālam'
itnā kaafī hai ki insān samajhte haiñ mujhe
aisa lagta hai wo nadan samajhte hain mujhe
jo bhi tafrih ka saman samajhte hain mujhe
KHairiyat bhi meri ma'lum nahin karte hain
is-qadar log pareshan samajhte hain mujhe
shahr se aao to aane ka sabab puchhte hain
ganw ke log bhi mehman samajhte hain mujhe
is liye meri KHushamad nahin karta koi
sab manana bahut aasan samajhte hain mujhe
main hun fankar to fankar hi samjha jae
aap kyon hindu musalman samajhte hain mujhe
main ne har zaKHm pe marham ki numaish ki hai
jaane kyon log namakdan samajhte hain mujhe
log kya kahte hain parwah nahin hai 'alam'
itna kafi hai ki insan samajhte hain mujhe

mere ḳhvāboñ ko nigalne kā irāda na kare
kah do sūraj se nikalne kā irāda na kare
us se baḌh kar koī muhtāj nahīñ ho saktā
gir ke jo shaḳhs sañbhalne kā irāda na kare
jo havāoñ ke mizājoñ se nahīñ hai vāqif
mere hamrāh vo chalne kā irāda na kare
guftugū zahr-bharī sun le jo insānoñ kī
saañp bhī zahr ugalne kā irāda na kare
apnī qismat meñ hai manzil to ḳhud aa jā.egī
ab junūñ raah badalne kā irāda na kare
niyyateñ saaf ghaTāoñ kī nahīñ haiñ 'ālam'
chāñd se kah do nikalne kā irāda na kare
mere KHwabon ko nigalne ka irada na kare
kah do suraj se nikalne ka irada na kare
us se baDh kar koi muhtaj nahin ho sakta
gir ke jo shaKHs sanbhalne ka irada na kare
jo hawaon ke mizajon se nahin hai waqif
mere hamrah wo chalne ka irada na kare
guftugu zahr-bhari sun le jo insanon ki
sanp bhi zahr ugalne ka irada na kare
apni qismat mein hai manzil to KHud aa jaegi
ab junun rah badalne ka irada na kare
niyyaten saf ghaTaon ki nahin hain 'alam'
chand se kah do nikalne ka irada na kare

tamām fitnoñ se ḳhud ko bachā liyā maiñ ne
munāfiqīn se pīchhā chhuḌā liyā maiñ ne
na jaane kis liye zahmat uThā rahe haiñ log
darāz qad bhī jab apnā ghaTā liyā maiñ ne
shanāḳht ho sake jis se fareb-kāroñ kī
janāb-e-vālā vo chashma lagā liyā maiñ ne
mirī anā pe zarā bhī kahīñ jo harf aayā
to āsmān ko sar par uThā liyā maiñ ne
tujhe maiñ tark karūñ kis tarah ġhazal-goī
tujhe to ziist kā hissa banā liyā maiñ ne
hue shikār jo ahbāb bad-gumānī ke
unheñ bhī husn-e-vafā se manā liyā maiñ ne
masarratoñ se bahut ghuT rahā thā dam 'ālam'
ġham-e-hayāt ko apnā banā liyā maiñ ne
tamam fitnon se KHud ko bacha liya main ne
munafiqin se pichha chhuDa liya main ne
na jaane kis liye zahmat uTha rahe hain log
daraaz qad bhi jab apna ghaTa liya main ne
shanaKHt ho sake jis se fareb-karon ki
janab-e-wala wo chashma laga liya main ne
meri ana pe zara bhi kahin jo harf aaya
to aasman ko sar par uTha liya main ne
tujhe main tark karun kis tarah ghazal-goi
tujhe to zist ka hissa bana liya main ne
hue shikar jo ahbab bad-gumani ke
unhen bhi husn-e-wafa se mana liya main ne
masarraton se bahut ghuT raha tha dam 'alam'
gham-e-hayat ko apna bana liya main ne

ḳhāna-e-dil ko sajāoge to yaad ā.uñgā
pyaar kī sham' jalāo.ge to yaad ā.ūñgā
bhīge manzar meñ mirā 'aks dikhā.ī degā
bārishoñ meñ jo nahāo.ge to yaad ā.ūñgā
hogī mahsūs tumheñ merī vafā kī ḳhushbū
tum koī ḳhushbū lagāoge to yaad ā.ūñgā
jab bhī aa.egā tumheñ sajne sañvarne kā ḳhayāl
paas ā.īne ke jāoge to yaad ā.ūñgā
ruuTh jaane pe koī jab na manā.egā tumheñ
aur tum sab ko manāoge to yaad ā.ūñgā
apnī tanhā.ī ko tum jab bhī sukūt-e-shab meñ
merī ġhazloñ ko sunāoge to yaad ā.ūñgā
bhūlne ke liye mujh ko mirī yādoñ ke nuqūsh
saf.ha-e-dil se miTāoge to yaad ā.ūñgā
KHana-e-dil ko sajaoge to yaad aaunga
pyar ki sham' jalaoge to yaad aaunga
bhige manzar mein mera 'aks dikhai dega
barishon mein jo nahaoge to yaad aaunga
hogi mahsus tumhein meri wafa ki KHushbu
tum koi KHushbu lagaoge to yaad aaunga
jab bhi aaega tumhein sajne sanwarne ka KHayal
pas aaine ke jaoge to yaad aaunga
ruTh jaane pe koi jab na manaega tumhein
aur tum sab ko manaoge to yaad aaunga
apni tanhai ko tum jab bhi sukut-e-shab mein
meri ghazlon ko sunaoge to yaad aaunga
bhulne ke liye mujh ko meri yaadon ke nuqush
safha-e-dil se miTaoge to yaad aaunga

jis kī ḳhātir saarā zamāna chhoḌ diyā
us ne merā phone uThānā chhoḌ diyā
saarī saarī raat satānā chhoḌ diyā
tum ne kyoñ ḳhvāboñ meñ aanā chhoḌ diyā
un kī ġhalat-fahmī ko kahāñ tak duur kareñ
rūThe huoñ ko ham ne manānā chhoḌ diyā
jab se haqīqat sāmne aa.ī ḳhvāboñ kī
tasvīroñ se dil bahlānā chhoḌ diyā
pūchh rahī haiñ aa kar maujeñ sāhil se
us ne kyoñ panghaT par aanā chhoḌ diyā
har din is ke pāgal-pan se tang aa kar
maiñ ne is dil ko samjhānā chhoḌ diyā
dost banā kar dhoka diyā jab se us ne
ham ne ziyāda dost banānā chhoḌ diyā
'ālam' jin se mil na sakā dil barsoñ se
ham ne un se haath milānā chhoḌ diyā
jis ki KHatir sara zamana chhoD diya
us ne mera phone uThana chhoD diya
sari sari raat satana chhoD diya
tum ne kyon KHwabon mein aana chhoD diya
un ki ghalat-fahmi ko kahan tak dur karen
ruThe huon ko hum ne manana chhoD diya
jab se haqiqat samne aai KHwabon ki
taswiron se dil bahlana chhoD diya
puchh rahi hain aa kar maujen sahil se
us ne kyon panghaT par aana chhoD diya
har din is ke pagal-pan se tang aa kar
main ne is dil ko samjhana chhoD diya
dost bana kar dhoka diya jab se us ne
hum ne ziyaada dost banana chhoD diya
'alam' jin se mil na saka dil barson se
hum ne un se hath milana chhoD diya

kyā batā.ūñ kisī ko hai kyā dostī
hai ġham-e-zindagī kī davā dostī
nā-tavāñ ḳhud ko mahsūs jab bhī kiyā
tū ne baḳhshā mujhe hausla dostī
dekh kar jis ko lagtī hai duniyā hasīñ
hai mohabbat kā vo aa.ina dostī
raushnī kā safar yā añdhere kā ho
har safar meñ rahī ham-navā dostī
lākhoñ ehsāñ haiñ tere mirī zaat par
haq tirā kis tarah ho adā dostī
jis se 'ālam' mahaktā hai merā vajūd
ḳhushbūoñ kī hai aisī fazā dostī
kya bataun kisi ko hai kya dosti
hai gham-e-zindagi ki dawa dosti
na-tawan KHud ko mahsus jab bhi kiya
tu ne baKHsha mujhe hausla dosti
dekh kar jis ko lagti hai duniya hasin
hai mohabbat ka wo aaina dosti
raushni ka safar ya andhere ka ho
har safar mein rahi ham-nawa dosti
lakhon ehsan hain tere meri zat par
haq tera kis tarah ho ada dosti
jis se 'alam' mahakta hai mera wajud
KHushbuon ki hai aisi faza dosti

mādar-e-hind kī 'azmat kā pata chaltā hai
husn-e-kashmīr se jannat kā pata chaltā hai
qatra-e-āb kī qīmat kā pata chaltā hai
dhuup meñ pyaas kī shiddat kā pata chaltā hai
jab bhī kāñdhoñ pe uThātā huuñ janāza koī
zindagī terī haqīqat kā pata chaltā hai
paañv ho jaate haiñ jab rāh-e-vafā meñ zaḳhmī
tab kahīñ 'ishq kī 'azmat kā pata chaltā hai
'ilm par apne bahut jab koī kartā hai ġhurūr
us ke andar kī jahālat kā pata chaltā hai
us kī tahqīq jab aatī hai ḳhalāoñ meñ nazar
'ilm insān kī tāqat kā pata chaltā hai
jab nahīñ miltī hameñ vaqt-e-zarūrat 'ālam'
tab kisī chiiz kī qīmat kā pata chaltā hai
madar-e-hind ki 'azmat ka pata chalta hai
husn-e-kashmir se jannat ka pata chalta hai
qatra-e-ab ki qimat ka pata chalta hai
dhup mein pyas ki shiddat ka pata chalta hai
jab bhi kandhon pe uThata hun janaza koi
zindagi teri haqiqat ka pata chalta hai
panw ho jate hain jab rah-e-wafa mein zaKHmi
tab kahin 'ishq ki 'azmat ka pata chalta hai
'ilm par apne bahut jab koi karta hai ghurur
us ke andar ki jahaalat ka pata chalta hai
us ki tahqiq jab aati hai KHalaon mein nazar
'ilm insan ki taqat ka pata chalta hai
jab nahin milti hamein waqt-e-zarurat 'alam'
tab kisi chiz ki qimat ka pata chalta hai

tire dimāġh se saarā futūr niklegā
mirī vafā kā natīja zarūr niklegā
na sar uThā ke chalo pattharoñ kī bastī meñ
lagegī Thes to saarā ġhurūr niklegā
tū hausle se añdhere kā sāmnā kariyo
isī añdhere ke pahlū se nuur niklegā
nizām-e-‘adl to mar'ūb mujrimoñ se hai
hameñ yaqīñ hai hamārā qusūr niklegā
haiñ chand roz kī mehmān uljhaneñ 'ālam'
tire sukūn kā sūraj zarūr niklegā
tere dimagh se sara futur niklega
meri wafa ka natija zarur niklega
na sar uTha ke chalo pattharon ki basti mein
lagegi Thes to sara ghurur niklega
tu hausle se andhere ka samna kariyo
isi andhere ke pahlu se nur niklega
nizam-e-‘adl to mar'ub mujrimon se hai
hamein yaqin hai hamara qusur niklega
hain chand roz ki mehman uljhanen 'alam'
tere sukun ka suraj zarur niklega

kyoñ ho mujh se ḳhafā kaho to sahī
kyā hai merī ḳhatā kaho to sahī
hañste hañste chhalak paḌīñ āñkheñ
kaun yaad aa gayā kaho to sahī
is qadar ham se barhamī kyoñ hai
kis ne kyā kah diyā kaho to sahī
shīsha-e-dil ko toḌ kar mere
aap ko kyā milā kaho to sahī
kis ne kis ko bhulā diyā āḳhir
kaun hai be-vafā kaho to sahī
jān-levā haiñ hijr ke lamhe
ab na hoñge judā kaho to sahī
kho.e kho.e se rahte ho 'ālam'
ye tumheñ kyā huā kaho to sahī
kyon ho mujh se KHafa kaho to sahi
kya hai meri KHata kaho to sahi
hanste hanste chhalak paDin aankhen
kaun yaad aa gaya kaho to sahi
is qadar hum se barhami kyon hai
kis ne kya kah diya kaho to sahi
shisha-e-dil ko toD kar mere
aap ko kya mila kaho to sahi
kis ne kis ko bhula diya aaKHir
kaun hai be-wafa kaho to sahi
jaan-lewa hain hijr ke lamhe
ab na honge juda kaho to sahi
khoe khoe se rahte ho 'alam'
ye tumhein kya hua kaho to sahi

dānista kabhī aisī himāqat nahīñ kartā
fankār huuñ tauhīn-e-mohabbat nahīñ kartā
kyā raas use aa.egī dastār-e-fazīlat
jo apne usūloñ kī hifāzat nahīñ kartā
is daur meñ ham us ko farishta hī kaheñge
fāqoñ meñ jo ġhairat kī tijārat nahīñ kartā
tūfān se laḌne kā agar shauq na hotā
maiñ ‘azmat-e-sāhil se baġhāvat nahīñ kartā
shāyad hai 'azīz us ko mirī muflisī 'ālam'
vo mere muqaddar kī marammat nahīñ kartā
danista kabhi aisi himaqat nahin karta
fankar hun tauhin-e-mohabbat nahin karta
kya ras use aaegi dastar-e-fazilat
jo apne usulon ki hifazat nahin karta
is daur mein hum us ko farishta hi kahenge
faqon mein jo ghairat ki tijarat nahin karta
tufan se laDne ka agar shauq na hota
main ‘azmat-e-sahil se baghawat nahin karta
shayad hai 'aziz us ko meri muflisi 'alam'
wo mere muqaddar ki marammat nahin karta

nuur paiham safar meñ rahtā hai
us kā chehrā nazar meñ rahtā hai
us se manzil kī azmateñ pūchho
jo musalsal safar meñ rahtā hai
pā-e-nāzuk sañbhāl kar rakhnā
dil tirī rah-guzar meñ rahtā hai
mujh meñ ḳhāmī talāshne vaale
'aib to har bashar meñ rahtā hai
ḳhairiyat pūchhī shukriya varna
kaun kis kī ḳhabar meñ rahtā hai
fā.eda kyā lahū jalāne se
jab añdherā hī ghar meñ rahtā hai
kyā karūñ le ke is havelī ko
merā maazī khañDar meñ rahtā hai
vo bulandī ko chhū nahīñ saktā
jo agar aur magar meñ rahtā hai
nur paiham safar mein rahta hai
us ka chehra nazar mein rahta hai
us se manzil ki azmaten puchho
jo musalsal safar mein rahta hai
pa-e-nazuk sanbhaal kar rakhna
dil teri rah-guzar mein rahta hai
mujh mein KHami talashne wale
'aib to har bashar mein rahta hai
KHairiyat puchhi shukriya warna
kaun kis ki KHabar mein rahta hai
faeda kya lahu jalane se
jab andhera hi ghar mein rahta hai
kya karun le ke is haweli ko
mera mazi khanDar mein rahta hai
wo bulandi ko chhu nahin sakta
jo agar aur magar mein rahta hai

kabhī ilm ne use maat dī kabhī āgahī ne harā diyā
jise tīrgī na harā sakī use raushnī ne harā diyā
kabhī ḳhushk un ke na lab hue rahī jin kī qatroñ se dostī
jo samundaroñ ke rafīq the unheñ tishnagī ne harā diyā
jinheñ bebasī na harā sakī unheñ phir na koī harā sakā
jo zarūratoñ ke ġhulām the unheñ har kisī ne harā diyā
hameñ sar-bulandī atā huī jahāñ jis mahāz pe DaT ga.e
mare roz jis kī talab meñ ham usī zindagī ne harā diyā
na hai ilm-o-fan kī talab tumheñ na taraqqiyoñ kā junūn hai
jo tumhārā tarz-e-hayāt hai tumheñ bas usī ne harā diyā
rah-e-ishq meñ jo fanā hue unheñ jāvedānī atā huī
jo asīr-e-husn-e-hayāt the unheñ be-hisī ne harā diyā
kabhi ilm ne use mat di kabhi aagahi ne hara diya
jise tirgi na hara saki use raushni ne hara diya
kabhi KHushk un ke na lab hue rahi jin ki qatron se dosti
jo samundaron ke rafiq the unhen tishnagi ne hara diya
jinhen bebasi na hara saki unhen phir na koi hara saka
jo zaruraton ke ghulam the unhen har kisi ne hara diya
hamein sar-bulandi ata hui jahan jis mahaz pe DaT gae
mare roz jis ki talab mein hum usi zindagi ne hara diya
na hai ilm-o-fan ki talab tumhein na taraqqiyon ka junun hai
jo tumhaara tarz-e-hayat hai tumhein bas usi ne hara diya
rah-e-ishq mein jo fana hue unhen jawedani ata hui
jo asir-e-husn-e-hayat the unhen be-hisi ne hara diya

dil kiyā dast-e-sitam-gar ke havāle ham ne
aa.ina kar diyā patthar ke havāle ham ne
dekhne ke liye maujoñ kī vasī.a-un-nazarī
tishnagī kī hai samundar ke havāle ham ne
dekh to shauq-e-shahādat kī tamanna zālim
kar diyā sar tire ḳhanjar ke havāle ham ne
harf-e-tadbīr kī tafsīr samajhne ke liye
na kiyā ḳhud ko muqaddar ke havāle ham ne
aur kyā duuñ maiñ sazā ḳhvāb-mahal ko aalam
zindagī kar to dī chhappar ke havāle ham ne
dil kiya dast-e-sitam-gar ke hawale hum ne
aaina kar diya patthar ke hawale hum ne
dekhne ke liye maujon ki wasia-un-nazari
tishnagi ki hai samundar ke hawale hum ne
dekh to shauq-e-shahadat ki tamanna zalim
kar diya sar tere KHanjar ke hawale hum ne
harf-e-tadbir ki tafsir samajhne ke liye
na kiya KHud ko muqaddar ke hawale hum ne
aur kya dun main saza KHwab-mahal ko aalam
zindagi kar to di chhappar ke hawale hum ne

hasīn ḳhvāb dikhāyā dikhā ke chhoḌ diyā
kisī ne apnā banāyā banā ke chhoḌ diyā
jo us kī yādoñ kā dīpak kabhī huā raushan
to āñsuoñ se bujhāyā bujhā ke chhoḌ diyā
kiyā na us ne mire dard ko kabhī mahsūs
hamesha dil ko dukhāyā dukhā ke chhoḌ diyā
batātā kaise maiñ hassās ke ma'ānī use
so aa.ine ko uThāyā uThā ke chhoḌ diyā
maiñ hausla na juTā paayā us ko chhūne kā
naqāb ruḳh se haTāyā haTā ke chhoḌ diyā
kahīñ na us kī burā.ī meñ ham hue shāmil
nazar se jis ko girāyā girā ke chhoḌ diyā
bahut salīqe se us ne kiyā nazar-andāz
qarīb apne biThāyā biThā ke chhoḌ diyā
na un se rakkhī kabhī raushnī kī ummīdeñ
diyoñ ko ham ne jalāyā jalā ke chhoḌ diyā
hasin KHwab dikhaya dikha ke chhoD diya
kisi ne apna banaya bana ke chhoD diya
jo us ki yaadon ka dipak kabhi hua raushan
to aansuon se bujhaya bujha ke chhoD diya
kiya na us ne mere dard ko kabhi mahsus
hamesha dil ko dukhaya dukha ke chhoD diya
batata kaise main hassas ke ma'ani use
so aaine ko uThaya uTha ke chhoD diya
main hausla na juTa paya us ko chhune ka
naqab ruKH se haTaya haTa ke chhoD diya
kahin na us ki burai mein hum hue shamil
nazar se jis ko giraya gira ke chhoD diya
bahut saliqe se us ne kiya nazar-andaz
qarib apne biThaya biTha ke chhoD diya
na un se rakkhi kabhi raushni ki ummiden
diyon ko hum ne jalaya jala ke chhoD diya

bevafā ab na mohabbat kī duhā.ī dūñgā
zindagī bhar maiñ tujhe zaḳhm-e-judā.ī dūñgā
jo mujhe jaisā samajhtā hai samajhne diije
apne baare meñ kahāñ tak maiñ safā.ī dūñgā
mere hisse meñ bhī aaya hai bulandī kā safar
āsmāñ vāloñ tumheñ maiñ bhī dikhā.ī dūñgā
baḳhsh degā vo mirī saarī ḳhatā.eñ fauran
us kī rahmat kī use itnī duhā.ī dūñgā
apne māñ-bāp ko kāñdhā bhī nahīñ de paayā
jo ye kahtā thā unheñ saarī kamā.ī dūñgā
maiñ safīrān-e-mohabbat kī sadā huuñ 'ālam'
mar bhī jā.ūñ to zamāne ko sunā.ī dūñgā
bewafa ab na mohabbat ki duhai dunga
zindagi bhar main tujhe zaKHm-e-judai dunga
jo mujhe jaisa samajhta hai samajhne dije
apne bare mein kahan tak main safai dunga
mere hisse mein bhi aaya hai bulandi ka safar
aasman walon tumhein main bhi dikhai dunga
baKHsh dega wo meri sari KHataen fauran
us ki rahmat ki use itni duhai dunga
apne man-bap ko kandha bhi nahin de paya
jo ye kahta tha unhen sari kamai dunga
main safiran-e-mohabbat ki sada hun 'alam'
mar bhi jaun to zamane ko sunai dunga

is liye to bujhā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
bujhne vaalā diyā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
jo bhī hai sab mirā muqaddar hai
zindagī se ḳhafā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
merī tā'zīm kyoñ kare duniyā
aadmī huuñ ḳhudā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
āñdhiy.oñ saañs chal rahī hai abhī
jal rahā huuñ bujhā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
bas zarā talḳhiyāñ mizāj meñ haiñ
dosto sar-phirā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
log jitnā burā batāte haiñ
yaar utnā burā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
mustarad kar de jis ko ye duniyā
vo ġhalat faisla nahīñ huuñ maiñ
mujh ko apnī talāsh hai 'ālam'
ḳhud se ab tak milā nahīñ huuñ maiñ
is liye to bujha nahin hun main
bujhne wala diya nahin hun main
jo bhi hai sab mera muqaddar hai
zindagi se KHafa nahin hun main
meri ta'zim kyon kare duniya
aadmi hun KHuda nahin hun main
aandhiyon sans chal rahi hai abhi
jal raha hun bujha nahin hun main
bas zara talKHiyan mizaj mein hain
dosto sar-phira nahin hun main
log jitna bura batate hain
yar utna bura nahin hun main
mustarad kar de jis ko ye duniya
wo ghalat faisla nahin hun main
mujh ko apni talash hai 'alam'
KHud se ab tak mila nahin hun main

mausam-e-vaqt badalnā hai badal jā.egā
azhdahā raat kā sūraj ko nigal jā.egā
shīsha-e-dil kī safā.ī pe tavajjoh diije
mausam-e-vaqt bahar-hāl badal jā.egā
bas vahī dosto is daur kā muusā hogā
raah paanī meñ banā kar jo nikal jā.egā
saath jo maañ kī du'ā.eñ haiñ to inshā-allāh
hādisa raah meñ aa.egā to Tal jā.egā
kyā ḳhabar thī ki zarā chain ke din aate hī
mere hamsā.e kā lahja hī badal jā.egā
log aa jā.eñge miTTī ke havāle kar ke
tere hamrāh faqat terā 'amal jā.egā
aañch īsār ke sho'loñ kī dikhāo 'ālam'
saḳht patthar bhī jo hogā to pighal jā.egā
mausam-e-waqt badalna hai badal jaega
azhdaha raat ka suraj ko nigal jaega
shisha-e-dil ki safai pe tawajjoh dije
mausam-e-waqt bahar-haal badal jaega
bas wahi dosto is daur ka musa hoga
rah pani mein bana kar jo nikal jaega
sath jo man ki du'aen hain to insha-allah
hadisa rah mein aaega to Tal jaega
kya KHabar thi ki zara chain ke din aate hi
mere hamsae ka lahja hi badal jaega
log aa jaenge miTTi ke hawale kar ke
tere hamrah faqat tera 'amal jaega
aanch isar ke sho'lon ki dikhao 'alam'
saKHt patthar bhi jo hoga to pighal jaega

bayāñ ġhairoñ se apnā ġham kareñ kyā
namak ko zaḳhm kā marham kareñ kyā
na.e mausam ke ḳhāke haiñ nazar meñ
guzashta fasl kā mātam kareñ kyā
utartā hī nahīñ hai us kā jaadū
batāo ḳhud pe paḌh kar dam kareñ kyā
use ham kis tarah dil se nikāleñ
ye dil suntā nahīñ to ham kareñ kyā
ham us kī be-ruḳhī kā zikr kar ke
use kuchh aur bhī barham kareñ kyā
hameñ jabran hī jiinā paḌ rahā hai
batā ai gardish-e-paiham kareñ kyā
ġhamoñ kī dhuup meñ jab jal chuke haiñ
ḳhushī kī chhāñv kā 'ālam' kareñ kyā
bayan ghairon se apna gham karen kya
namak ko zaKHm ka marham karen kya
nae mausam ke KHake hain nazar mein
guzashta fasl ka matam karen kya
utarta hi nahin hai us ka jadu
batao KHud pe paDh kar dam karen kya
use hum kis tarah dil se nikalen
ye dil sunta nahin to hum karen kya
hum us ki be-ruKHi ka zikr kar ke
use kuchh aur bhi barham karen kya
hamein jabran hi jina paD raha hai
bata ai gardish-e-paiham karen kya
ghamon ki dhup mein jab jal chuke hain
KHushi ki chhanw ka 'alam' karen kya

ishq merā hai agar raat kī raanī kī tarah
husn us kā bhī hai phūloñ kī javānī kī tarah
ai mirī jān-e-vafā terī vafāoñ kī qasam
tū mujhe yaad hai naanī kī kahānī kī tarah
kyā koī samjhe tire husn kī tahdārī ko
mujh pe khultī hai faqat misra-e-sānī kī tarah
kūcha-e-dil se guzartī haiñ jo terī yādeñ
ashk bahte haiñ mirī āñkhoñ se paanī kī tarah
chāhtā jab huuñ koī nazm kahūñ tere liye
maiñ ulajh jaatā huuñ alfāz-o-ma.ānī kī tarah
hai sivā kaun tire mujh ko jo taslīm kare
mere mahbūb mirī talḳh-bayānī kī tarah
na koī shor sharāba na koī halchal hai
zindagī lagtī hai Thahre hue paanī kī tarah
maiñ ne is dil kī tijorī meñ rakhā hai 'ālam'
us kī har chiiz ko anmol nishānī kī tarah
ishq mera hai agar raat ki rani ki tarah
husn us ka bhi hai phulon ki jawani ki tarah
ai meri jaan-e-wafa teri wafaon ki qasam
tu mujhe yaad hai nani ki kahani ki tarah
kya koi samjhe tere husn ki tahdari ko
mujh pe khulti hai faqat misra-e-sani ki tarah
kucha-e-dil se guzarti hain jo teri yaaden
ashk bahte hain meri aankhon se pani ki tarah
chahta jab hun koi nazm kahun tere liye
main ulajh jata hun alfaz-o-maani ki tarah
hai siwa kaun tere mujh ko jo taslim kare
mere mahbub meri talKH-bayani ki tarah
na koi shor sharaba na koi halchal hai
zindagi lagti hai Thahre hue pani ki tarah
main ne is dil ki tijori mein rakha hai 'alam'
us ki har chiz ko anmol nishani ki tarah

hameñ ḳhabar hai vo kyoñ ham se ab nahīñ miltā
yahāñ kisī se koī be-sabab nahīñ miltā
phir āftāb kahāñ apnī raushnī bāñTe
na.e charāġhoñ meñ husn-e-talab nahīñ miltā
batā rahī haiñ adīboñ ke ghar kī tahzībeñ
virāsatoñ meñ sabhī ko adab nahīñ miltā
maiñ jalne lagtā huuñ tanhā.iyoñ ke dozaḳh meñ
kabhī vo merī zarūrat pe jab nahīñ miltā
udaas mat ho jo hāsil na kar sakā us ko
kabhī kisī ko zamāne meñ sab nahīñ miltā
hai zaat aap kī taḳhlīq-e-do-jahāñ kā sabab
na milte aap hameñ ham ko rab nahīñ miltā
hamein KHabar hai wo kyon hum se ab nahin milta
yahan kisi se koi be-sabab nahin milta
phir aaftab kahan apni raushni banTe
nae charaghon mein husn-e-talab nahin milta
bata rahi hain adibon ke ghar ki tahziben
wirasaton mein sabhi ko adab nahin milta
main jalne lagta hun tanhaiyon ke dozaKH mein
kabhi wo meri zarurat pe jab nahin milta
udas mat ho jo hasil na kar saka us ko
kabhi kisi ko zamane mein sab nahin milta
hai zat aap ki taKHliq-e-do-jahan ka sabab
na milte aap hamein hum ko rab nahin milta

āñgan ke daraḳhtoñ ke liye kuchh bhī nahīñ hai
duniyā meñ buzurgoñ ke liye kuchh bhī nahīñ hai
haq chhīn ke letī hai yahāñ charb-zabānī
ḳhāmosh parindoñ ke liye kuchh bhī nahīñ hai
chaḌhte hue sūraj kī parastār hai duniyā
miTTī ke charāġhoñ ke liye kuchh bhī nahīñ hai
har ātish-e-namrūd ko gulzār banānā
ḳhāliq ke ḳhalīloñ ke liye kuchh bhī nahīñ hai
'ayyār qalam-kāroñ kī ḳhātir haiñ ḳhitābāt
ḳhud.dār adīboñ ke liye kuchh bhī nahīñ hai
mujrim ko 'adālat se dilā denā rihā.ī
'ālam' ye vakīloñ ke liye kuchh bhī nahīñ hai
aangan ke daraKHton ke liye kuchh bhi nahin hai
duniya mein buzurgon ke liye kuchh bhi nahin hai
haq chhin ke leti hai yahan charb-zabani
KHamosh parindon ke liye kuchh bhi nahin hai
chaDhte hue suraj ki parastar hai duniya
miTTi ke charaghon ke liye kuchh bhi nahin hai
har aatish-e-namrud ko gulzar banana
KHaliq ke KHalilon ke liye kuchh bhi nahin hai
'ayyar qalam-karon ki KHatir hain KHitabaat
KHuddar adibon ke liye kuchh bhi nahin hai
mujrim ko 'adalat se dila dena rihai
'alam' ye wakilon ke liye kuchh bhi nahin hai

chāñdnī raat hai maiñ huuñ mirī tanhā.ī hai
yaad aise meñ tirī dil meñ chalī aa.ī hai
vo daġhābāz hai zālim baḌā harjā.ī hai
phir bhī ye dil hai ki us kā hī tamannā.ī hai
vo mirī bazm-e-tasavvur meñ kuchh aise aa.e
jaise jannat mire āñgan meñ utar aa.ī hai
bāġh-e-firdaus hai sarqa tire husn-e-ruḳh kā
aur tafsīr-e-qayāmat tirī añgḌā.ī hai
na karūñ yaad maiñ tujh ko to ye dam ghuTtā hai
terī chāhat mujhe is moḌ pe le aa.ī hai
niiñd ojhal huī ḳhvāboñ kā safar ḳhatm huā
phir vahī maiñ vahī yādeñ vahī tanhā.ī hai
chandni raat hai main hun meri tanhai hai
yaad aise mein teri dil mein chali aai hai
wo daghabaz hai zalim baDa harjai hai
phir bhi ye dil hai ki us ka hi tamannai hai
wo meri bazm-e-tasawwur mein kuchh aise aae
jaise jannat mere aangan mein utar aai hai
bagh-e-firdaus hai sarqa tere husn-e-ruKH ka
aur tafsir-e-qayamat teri angDai hai
na karun yaad main tujh ko to ye dam ghuTta hai
teri chahat mujhe is moD pe le aai hai
nind ojhal hui KHwabon ka safar KHatm hua
phir wahi main wahi yaaden wahi tanhai hai

raakh maazī kī kuredoge to kyā pāoge
koī chingārī nikal aa.ī to jal jāoge
ek qatra bhī agar ho to bachā kar rakhnā
ḳhuun kā qaht paḌegā to kahāñ jāoge
ho lagī maġhribī tahzīb kī mehñdī jis meñ
kaise us haath se talvār uThā pāoge
jis se vābasta hai ajdād kī azmat kā bharam
us havelī ko jo bechoge to pachhtāoge
ahd-e-hāzir meñ vafāoñ kā natīja kyā hai
tum jo 'ālam' se miloge to samajh jāoge
rakh mazi ki kuredoge to kya paoge
koi chingari nikal aai to jal jaoge
ek qatra bhi agar ho to bacha kar rakhna
KHun ka qaht paDega to kahan jaoge
ho lagi maghribi tahzib ki mehndi jis mein
kaise us hath se talwar uTha paoge
jis se wabasta hai ajdad ki azmat ka bharam
us haweli ko jo bechoge to pachhtaoge
ahd-e-hazir mein wafaon ka natija kya hai
tum jo 'alam' se miloge to samajh jaoge

kahāñ tamām abhī karbalā kā manzar hai
hamāre saath na.e hausloñ kā lashkar hai
tujhe hai shauq bahut zarf nāpne kā magar
mire rafīq ye dariyā nahīñ samundar hai
is inqalāb ko duniyā meñ kaun rokegā
jo zalzale kī tarah mere dil ke andar hai
jo diip jaltā rahā raat bhar mirī ḳhātir
mire liye to vahī sūrajoñ se behtar hai
zamīn vaale use sirf dekh sakte haiñ
vo chāñd hai use chhūnā kahāñ mayassar hai
tire baġhair bhī dīvār-o-dar chamakte haiñ
tire baġhair bhī ghar kā diyā munavvar hai
kahan tamam abhi karbala ka manzar hai
hamare sath nae hauslon ka lashkar hai
tujhe hai shauq bahut zarf napne ka magar
mere rafiq ye dariya nahin samundar hai
is inqalab ko duniya mein kaun rokega
jo zalzale ki tarah mere dil ke andar hai
jo dip jalta raha raat bhar meri KHatir
mere liye to wahi surajon se behtar hai
zamin wale use sirf dekh sakte hain
wo chand hai use chhuna kahan mayassar hai
tere baghair bhi diwar-o-dar chamakte hain
tere baghair bhi ghar ka diya munawwar hai

jaane kyoñ mohabbat meñ dilkashī nahīñ miltī
dost roz milte haiñ dostī nahīñ miltī
zindagī agar chāho fāqa-mast ban jaao
roġhnī nivāloñ se zindagī nahīñ miltī
maslak-e-faqīrī meñ jo ḳhushī mayassar hai
taḳht-e-bādshāhī par vo ḳhushī nahīñ miltī
adh-khulī kalī shāyad bāġhbāñ ne phir toḌī
kyoñ guloñ ke chehroñ par tāzgī nahīñ miltī
un ko koī samjhā.e apnā jā.eza le leñ
jin ko apne sajdoñ meñ chāshnī nahīñ miltī
dil mirā añdhere meñ aaj bhī bhaTaktā hai
raushnī kī duniyā meñ raushnī nahīñ miltī
zard zard chehre haiñ ḳhauf-e-marg se 'ālam'
ab to koī bhī sūrat chāñd sī nahīñ miltī
jaane kyon mohabbat mein dilkashi nahin milti
dost roz milte hain dosti nahin milti
zindagi agar chaho faqa-mast ban jao
roghni niwalon se zindagi nahin milti
maslak-e-faqiri mein jo KHushi mayassar hai
taKHt-e-baadshahi par wo KHushi nahin milti
adh-khuli kali shayad baghban ne phir toDi
kyon gulon ke chehron par tazgi nahin milti
un ko koi samjhae apna jaeza le len
jin ko apne sajdon mein chashni nahin milti
dil mera andhere mein aaj bhi bhaTakta hai
raushni ki duniya mein raushni nahin milti
zard zard chehre hain KHauf-e-marg se 'alam'
ab to koi bhi surat chand si nahin milti

sharāfat chhīn letī hai sadāqat chhīn letī hai
qalam-kāroñ se ḳhuddārī zarūrat chhīn letī hai
riyā-kārī se bachiye ye bahut zahrīlī nāgin hai
ye nāgin zindagī bhar kī 'ibādat chhīn letī hai
zamāne meñ zarūrī hai bahut tā'līm kā honā
jahālat aadmī se ādmiyyat chhīn letī hai
bharī ho jeb to insāñ nashe meñ chuur rahtā hai
zarā sī tang-dastī sab nazākat chhīn letī hai
agar jannat kī chāhat hai to ḳhidmat shart hai maañ kī
agar maañ ruuTh jaatī hai to jannat chhīn letī hai
jahāñ tak ho sake 'ālam kisī se qarz mat lenā
miyāñ ye qarz-dārī ḳhair-o-barkat chhīn letī hai
sharafat chhin leti hai sadaqat chhin leti hai
qalam-karon se KHuddari zarurat chhin leti hai
riya-kari se bachiye ye bahut zahrili nagin hai
ye nagin zindagi bhar ki 'ibaadat chhin leti hai
zamane mein zaruri hai bahut ta'lim ka hona
jahaalat aadmi se aadmiyyat chhin leti hai
bhari ho jeb to insan nashe mein chur rahta hai
zara si tang-dasti sab nazakat chhin leti hai
agar jannat ki chahat hai to KHidmat shart hai man ki
agar man ruTh jati hai to jannat chhin leti hai
jahan tak ho sake 'alam kisi se qarz mat lena
miyan ye qarz-dari KHair-o-barkat chhin leti hai

kaise kah duuñ kahīñ e'lān nahīñ kartā hai
vo bhī ḳhāmoshī se ehsān nahīñ kartā hai
dil ko tahrīk-e-taraqqī to bahut miltī hai
hausla phir bhī ye nādān nahīñ kartā hai
aap ke naam se mansūb hue haiñ jab se
ab hameñ koī pareshān nahīñ kartā hai
kaam kartā hai bahut ġhair-zarūrī lekin
jo zarūrī hai vo insān nahīñ kartā hai
hai ye mumkin ho vahī shaḳhs munāfiq 'ālam'
jo bazāhir koī nuqsān nahīñ kartā hai
kaise kah dun kahin e'lan nahin karta hai
wo bhi KHamoshi se ehsan nahin karta hai
dil ko tahrik-e-taraqqi to bahut milti hai
hausla phir bhi ye nadan nahin karta hai
aap ke nam se mansub hue hain jab se
ab hamein koi pareshan nahin karta hai
kaam karta hai bahut ghair-zaruri lekin
jo zaruri hai wo insan nahin karta hai
hai ye mumkin ho wahi shaKHs munafiq 'alam'
jo bazahir koi nuqsan nahin karta hai

ye alag baat ki fursat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
ḳhud se mil kar hameñ rāhat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
ham to karnā bhī nahīñ chāhte dil kā saudā
aur munāsib hameñ qīmat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
'ishq vo jurm hai is jurm ko karne vaalo
is ke mujrim ko zamānat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
dauḌte bhī nahīñ shohrat ke ham aage pīchhe
aur āsānī se shohrat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
har jagah log mohazzab bhī nahīñ hote haiñ
har jagah dosto 'izzat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
ham ne maanā ki bure aap nahīñ haiñ lekin
aap meñ koī sharāfat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
aish beTe kī kamā.ī se bahū kartī hai
maañ ko ab duudh kī ujrat bhī nahīñ miltī hai
har kisī se nahīñ rakhtā huuñ maiñ rishta 'ālam'
har kisī se ye tabī'at bhī nahīñ miltī hai
ye alag baat ki fursat bhi nahin milti hai
KHud se mil kar hamein rahat bhi nahin milti hai
hum to karna bhi nahin chahte dil ka sauda
aur munasib hamein qimat bhi nahin milti hai
'ishq wo jurm hai is jurm ko karne walo
is ke mujrim ko zamanat bhi nahin milti hai
dauDte bhi nahin shohrat ke hum aage pichhe
aur aasani se shohrat bhi nahin milti hai
har jagah log mohazzab bhi nahin hote hain
har jagah dosto 'izzat bhi nahin milti hai
hum ne mana ki bure aap nahin hain lekin
aap mein koi sharafat bhi nahin milti hai
aish beTe ki kamai se bahu karti hai
man ko ab dudh ki ujrat bhi nahin milti hai
har kisi se nahin rakhta hun main rishta 'alam'
har kisi se ye tabi'at bhi nahin milti hai

ḳhuddāriyoñ kī had se nikalnā paḌā mujhe
māhaul kī chitāoñ meñ jalnā paḌā mujhe
vo maslahat thī kyā thī mujhe kuchh nahīñ pata
apnā har ik usuul badalnā paḌā mujhe
sochā thā maiñ rahūñgā hamesha 'urūj par
sūraj kī tarh shaam ko Dhalnā paḌā mujhe
maañ ke hasīn chāñd se chehre ko dekh kar
bachpan kī yaad aa.ī machalnā paḌā mujhe
bujhtā jo maiñ to miTtā nishāñ ḳhāndān kā
