maiñ āḳhirī charāġh thā jalnā paḌā mujhe
paanā kaThin hai zevar-e-kirdār dosto
chāñdī kī tarh aag meñ galnā paḌā mujhe
yūñhī kahāñ mile haiñ ye do-chār phuul bhī
'ālam' hazār kāñToñ pe chalnā paḌā mujhe
KHuddariyon ki had se nikalna paDa mujhe
mahaul ki chitaon mein jalna paDa mujhe
wo maslahat thi kya thi mujhe kuchh nahin pata
apna har ek usul badalna paDa mujhe
socha tha main rahunga hamesha 'uruj par
suraj ki tarh sham ko Dhalna paDa mujhe
man ke hasin chand se chehre ko dekh kar
bachpan ki yaad aai machalna paDa mujhe
bujhta jo main to miTta nishan KHandan ka
main aaKHiri charagh tha jalna paDa mujhe
pana kaThin hai zewar-e-kirdar dosto
chandi ki tarh aag mein galna paDa mujhe
yunhi kahan mile hain ye do-chaar phul bhi
'alam' hazar kanTon pe chalna paDa mujhe

jis tarah bachche buzurgoñ ke charan chūmte haiñ
ham mohabbat se mohabbat kā badan chūmte haiñ
muñh lagāte nahīñ bāzār ke phūloñ ko kabhī
ham faqat apne gulāboñ ke dahan chūmte haiñ
maiñ ne hālāt pe rakkhī hai ġhazal kī buniyād
is liye log mirā rang-e-suḳhan chūmte haiñ
muñh pe mal lete haiñ ham ḳhāk-e-madīna kī tarah
maañ ke qadmoñ kī tarah ḳhāk-e-vatan chūmte haiñ
zindagī meñ to unheñ bojh samajhte haiñ magar
log marne pe buzurgoñ kā kafan chūmte haiñ
aur baḌh jaatā hai manzil pe pahuñchne kā surūr
aable jab mire pairoñ kī thakan chūmte haiñ
jis tarah bachche buzurgon ke charan chumte hain
hum mohabbat se mohabbat ka badan chumte hain
munh lagate nahin bazar ke phulon ko kabhi
hum faqat apne gulabon ke dahan chumte hain
main ne haalat pe rakkhi hai ghazal ki buniyaad
is liye log mera rang-e-suKHan chumte hain
munh pe mal lete hain hum KHak-e-madina ki tarah
man ke qadmon ki tarah KHak-e-watan chumte hain
zindagi mein to unhen bojh samajhte hain magar
log marne pe buzurgon ka kafan chumte hain
aur baDh jata hai manzil pe pahunchne ka surur
aable jab mere pairon ki thakan chumte hain

zamāne par 'ayāñ merā hunar hone nahīñ detā
na jaane kyoñ mujhe vo mo'tabar hone nahīñ detā
vo zālim apnī yādoñ se sadā ābād rakhtā hai
mire TuuTe hue dil ko khañDar hone nahīñ detā
ḳhudā ke fazl se paa.ī hai vo ehsās kī daulat
kisī bhī baat ko maiñ darguzar hone nahīñ detā
hamesha is adā se vo mirī imdād kartā hai
zarā bhī merī ġhairat ko ḳhabar hone nahīñ detā
koī mausam koī rut ho tasavvur us ke chehre kā
kisī jalve ko mahbūb-e-nazar hone nahīñ detā
tū mujh se us kī yādoñ kā asāsa chhīn le yārab
ye merī ḳhvāhishoñ ko muḳhtasar hone nahīñ detā
zamane par 'ayan mera hunar hone nahin deta
na jaane kyon mujhe wo mo'tabar hone nahin deta
wo zalim apni yaadon se sada aabaad rakhta hai
mere TuTe hue dil ko khanDar hone nahin deta
KHuda ke fazl se pai hai wo ehsas ki daulat
kisi bhi baat ko main darguzar hone nahin deta
hamesha is ada se wo meri imdad karta hai
zara bhi meri ghairat ko KHabar hone nahin deta
koi mausam koi rut ho tasawwur us ke chehre ka
kisi jalwe ko mahbub-e-nazar hone nahin deta
tu mujh se us ki yaadon ka asasa chhin le yarab
ye meri KHwahishon ko muKHtasar hone nahin deta

farsh-e-maḳhmal pe kabhī niiñd na aa.ī mujh ko
itnī raas aa.ī mire ghar kī chaTā.ī mujh ko
baat sāhil kī jo hotī to sañbhal bhī jaatā
us ne mañjdhār meñ auqāt batā.ī mujh ko
azm par mere musallat hai junūñ manzil kā
kaise rokegī mirī ābla-pā.ī mujh ko
jis ne jis tarah se chāhā mujhe badnām kiyā
raas aa.ī nahīñ duniyā kī bhalā.ī mujh ko
zulmat-e-shab meñ maiñ tanhā hī laḌūñgā 'ālam'
in charāġhoñ ne agar aañkh dikhā.ī mujh ko
farsh-e-maKHmal pe kabhi nind na aai mujh ko
itni ras aai mere ghar ki chaTai mujh ko
baat sahil ki jo hoti to sanbhal bhi jata
us ne manjdhaar mein auqat batai mujh ko
azm par mere musallat hai junun manzil ka
kaise rokegi meri aabla-pai mujh ko
jis ne jis tarah se chaha mujhe badnam kiya
ras aai nahin duniya ki bhalai mujh ko
zulmat-e-shab mein main tanha hi laDunga 'alam'
in charaghon ne agar aankh dikhai mujh ko

vo tohmateñ na lagātā to aur kyā kartā
mire hunar na chhupātā to aur kyā kartā
khaḌī thiiñ har-sū mazālim kī āñdhiyāñ phir maiñ
charāġh-e-haq na jalātā to aur kyā kartā
ġharībī saath mirā de rahī thī bachpan se
na us kā saath nibhātā to aur kyā kartā
maiñ chhāle maañ kī hathelī pe dekhtā kaise
kamāne shahr na aatā to aur kyā kartā
tamām bastī pareshāñ thī raushnī ke liye
maiñ apnā ghar na jalātā to aur kyā kartā
samajh rahā thā farishta vo ḳhud ko ai 'ālam'
maiñ aa.ina na dikhātā to aur kyā kartā
wo tohmaten na lagata to aur kya karta
mere hunar na chhupata to aur kya karta
khaDi thin har-su mazalim ki aandhiyan phir main
charagh-e-haq na jalata to aur kya karta
gharibi sath mera de rahi thi bachpan se
na us ka sath nibhata to aur kya karta
main chhaale man ki hatheli pe dekhta kaise
kamane shahr na aata to aur kya karta
tamam basti pareshan thi raushni ke liye
main apna ghar na jalata to aur kya karta
samajh raha tha farishta wo KHud ko ai 'alam'
main aaina na dikhata to aur kya karta

sachchā.ī kabhī apnī safā.ī nahīñ detī
mahsūs to hotī hai dikhā.ī nahīñ detī
mazlūmoñ kī fariyād pe larzāñ hai falak tak
aur ahl-e-siyāsat ko sunā.ī nahīñ detī
yuuñ zulm-o-tashaddud ke añdhere haiñ ki tauba
jiine kī koī raah dikhā.ī nahīñ detī
hañs hañs ke sitam fāqoñ ke sah letī hai lekin
ḳhud.dār ġharībī to duhā.ī nahīñ detī
dil sāgar-e-afkār meñ Duubā ho to 'ālam'
kānoñ ko maza naġhma-sarā.ī nahīñ detī
sachchai kabhi apni safai nahin deti
mahsus to hoti hai dikhai nahin deti
mazlumon ki fariyaad pe larzan hai falak tak
aur ahl-e-siyasat ko sunai nahin deti
yun zulm-o-tashaddud ke andhere hain ki tauba
jine ki koi rah dikhai nahin deti
hans hans ke sitam faqon ke sah leti hai lekin
KHuddar gharibi to duhai nahin deti
dil sagar-e-afkar mein Duba ho to 'alam'
kanon ko maza naghma-sarai nahin deti

chāhtā jo bhī hai vo kah ke guzar jaatā hai
dil-e-hassās is ehsās se mar jaatā hai
zehn meñ baat buzurgoñ kī tabhī baiThtī hai
jab javānī kā nasha sar se utar jaatā hai
jab anā merī zarūrat kā galā ghoñTtī hai
rang ḳhud-dārī ke chehre kā nikhar jaatā hai
Dasne lagtī hai mirī ḳhāna-badoshī mujh ko
jab koī panchhī kabhī shaam ko ghar jaatā hai
jhūTī tārīf se hotī hai masarrat us ko
aa.ina koī dikhā de to biphar jaatā hai
jurm kartā hai koī aur yahāñ par 'ālam'
aur ilzām kisī aur ke sar jaatā hai
chahta jo bhi hai wo kah ke guzar jata hai
dil-e-hassas is ehsas se mar jata hai
zehn mein baat buzurgon ki tabhi baiThti hai
jab jawani ka nasha sar se utar jata hai
jab ana meri zarurat ka gala ghonTti hai
rang KHud-dari ke chehre ka nikhar jata hai
Dasne lagti hai meri KHana-badoshi mujh ko
jab koi panchhi kabhi sham ko ghar jata hai
jhuTi tarif se hoti hai masarrat us ko
aaina koi dikha de to biphar jata hai
jurm karta hai koi aur yahan par 'alam'
aur ilzam kisi aur ke sar jata hai

kisī ke zehn meñ kyā hai nazar nahīñ aatā
mizāj paḌhne kā sab ko hunar nahīñ aatā
har ek shaḳhs musāfir hai aisī manzil kā
jahāñ se koī kabhī lauT kar nahīñ aatā
hazāroñ fan pe yahāñ dastaras hai logoñ ko
hameñ salīqe se koī hunar nahīñ aatā
zabān-o-dil kī tahārat kā jā.eza le leñ
jinheñ hai shikva du'ā meñ asar nahīñ aatā
jise samajhte haiñ āsān ham bahut 'ālam'
hameñ samajh meñ vahī 'umr-bhar nahīñ aatā
kisi ke zehn mein kya hai nazar nahin aata
mizaj paDhne ka sab ko hunar nahin aata
har ek shaKHs musafir hai aisi manzil ka
jahan se koi kabhi lauT kar nahin aata
hazaron fan pe yahan dastaras hai logon ko
hamein saliqe se koi hunar nahin aata
zaban-o-dil ki tahaarat ka jaeza le len
jinhen hai shikwa du'a mein asar nahin aata
jise samajhte hain aasan hum bahut 'alam'
hamein samajh mein wahi 'umr-bhar nahin aata

kyā ḳhabar tujh ko o dāman ko chhuḌāne vaale
aur bhī haiñ mujhe siine se lagāne vaale
nāpte kaise mire zarf kī gahrā.ī ko
Dubkiyāñ ḳhitta-e-sāhil meñ lagāne vaale
ai havāo na kahīñ haath jalā lo tum bhī
bujh ga.e mere charāġhoñ ko bujhāne vaale
jism mar saktā hai āvāz nahīñ martī hai
yaad rakkheñ mirī āvāz dabāne vaale
ḳhud ko kaise kisī manzil ke havāle kartā
muntazir the mirī aamad ke zamāne vaale
baap kī qabr pe miTTī bhī nahīñ Dālte haiñ
phuul netāoñ kī qabroñ pe chaḌhāne vaale
kya KHabar tujh ko o daman ko chhuDane wale
aur bhi hain mujhe sine se lagane wale
napte kaise mere zarf ki gahrai ko
Dubkiyan KHitta-e-sahil mein lagane wale
ai hawao na kahin hath jala lo tum bhi
bujh gae mere charaghon ko bujhane wale
jism mar sakta hai aawaz nahin marti hai
yaad rakkhen meri aawaz dabane wale
KHud ko kaise kisi manzil ke hawale karta
muntazir the meri aamad ke zamane wale
bap ki qabr pe miTTi bhi nahin Dalte hain
phul netaon ki qabron pe chaDhane wale

apnī ḳhudī ko tum sar-e-bāzār bech kar
zinda ho kaise daulat-e-kirdār bech kar
yārab ye kyā 'azāb hai nasl-e-jadīd par
kartī hai aish purkhoñ kī dastār bech kar
hāsil kī us ke beTe ne kursī mudīr kī
itnā paḌhāyā baap ne aḳhbār bech kar
us bad-nasīb baap kī majbūriyāñ na pūchh
ḳhushiyāñ ḳharīdtā hai jo ghar-bār bech kar
mahñgī bahut paḌī mujhe sūraj kī dostī
pachhtā rahā huuñ sāya-e-dīvār bech kar
jin ko shu’ūr-e-bandagī kartā hai rab 'atā
jangal ḳharīd lete haiñ ghar-bār bech kar
'ālam' isī tarah se jo ham muntashir rahe
khā jā.eñge vatan ko ye ġhaddār bech kar
apni KHudi ko tum sar-e-bazar bech kar
zinda ho kaise daulat-e-kirdar bech kar
yarab ye kya 'azab hai nasl-e-jadid par
karti hai aish purkhon ki dastar bech kar
hasil ki us ke beTe ne kursi mudir ki
itna paDhaya bap ne aKHbar bech kar
us bad-nasib bap ki majburiyan na puchh
KHushiyan KHaridta hai jo ghar-bar bech kar
mahngi bahut paDi mujhe suraj ki dosti
pachhta raha hun saya-e-diwar bech kar
jin ko shu’ur-e-bandagi karta hai rab 'ata
jangal KHarid lete hain ghar-bar bech kar
'alam' isi tarah se jo hum muntashir rahe
kha jaenge watan ko ye ghaddar bech kar

adab ko itnā girā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
suḳhan kī 'azmat ghaTā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
diyoñ kā nām-o-nishāñ miTā kar tum un kā ḳhūn-e-jigar milā kar
charāġh apnā jalā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
hamesha jis ne samāj meñ kī tumhāre 'aiboñ kī parda-poshī
usī pe tohmat lagā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
hai ghar meñ jis se ḳhudā kī rahmat hai jis ke qadmoñ ke nīche jannat
usī ko zahmat batā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
jinhoñ ne tum ko janam diyā hai paḌhā likhā kar baḌā kiyā hai
unheñ hī āñkheñ dikhā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
hai jin se shāḳh-e-vafā mahaktī hai jin ke ḳhuuñ meñ vatan-parastī
unheñ fasādī batā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
mohabbatoñ ke gulāb tum par hamesha ham ne kiye nichhāvar
hamīñ pe nashtar chalā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
masarratoñ ke diye jalā kar zarūratoñ kā galā dabā kar
ġhamoñ ko 'ālam' chhupā rahe ho koī sunegā to kyā kahegā
adab ko itna gira rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
suKHan ki 'azmat ghaTa rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
diyon ka nam-o-nishan miTa kar tum un ka KHun-e-jigar mila kar
charagh apna jala rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
hamesha jis ne samaj mein ki tumhaare 'aibon ki parda-poshi
usi pe tohmat laga rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
hai ghar mein jis se KHuda ki rahmat hai jis ke qadmon ke niche jannat
usi ko zahmat bata rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
jinhon ne tum ko janam diya hai paDha likha kar baDa kiya hai
unhen hi aankhen dikha rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
hai jin se shaKH-e-wafa mahakti hai jin ke KHun mein watan-parasti
unhen fasadi bata rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
mohabbaton ke gulab tum par hamesha hum ne kiye nichhawar
hamin pe nashtar chala rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega
masarraton ke diye jala kar zaruraton ka gala daba kar
ghamon ko 'alam' chhupa rahe ho koi sunega to kya kahega

kabhī dāstān-e-hastī ye tamām tak na pahuñche
na fanā se āshnā ho to davām tak na pahuñche
tū pilā mujhe nazar se ki ye jaam tak na pahuñche
kahīñ bāda-e-mohabbat sar-e-ām tak na pahuñche
tū sitam kī qaiñchiyoñ se par-e-ārzū jo kaaTe
koī tā.ir-e-taḳhayyul tire baam tak na pahuñche
mirā vaqt-e-vāpsī hai tū na aa mire sirhāne
ki jafā kī koī tohmat tire naam tak na pahuñche
jo sanam-kade meñ jalva tirā dekh le barahman
tirā naam chhoḌ kar vo kabhī raam tak na pahuñche
tirī ek yaad rangīñ mirī ziist kā sahārā
jo vo sub.h ko na aa.e to ye shaam tak na pahuñche
mirā āḳhirī thā sajda ki nafas ne saath chhoḌā
tire dar pe sar jhukāyā to qiyām tak na pahuñche
mirā kārvān-e-hastī mire sabr hī ne luuTā
kabhī aah bhī jo khīñchī tire naam tak na pahoñche
ġham-e-ishq gar na ho to na ho dil asīr-e-gesū
ki na ho jo daana taa.ir kabhī daam tak na pahuñche
maiñ jhukā huuñ bandagī ko to vo ruḳh phirā rahe haiñ
ki salām rafta rafta ye payām tak na pahuñche
jo naqāb-e-ruḳh ulaT kar kabhī sāmne bhī aaya
jo chaḌhā.e tevaroñ ko ki salām tak na pahuñche
jo pilā de muskurā kar tū jhukī jhukī nazar se
koī haath mai-kade meñ kabhī jaam tak na pahuñche
kabhi dastan-e-hasti ye tamam tak na pahunche
na fana se aashna ho to dawam tak na pahunche
tu pila mujhe nazar se ki ye jam tak na pahunche
kahin baada-e-mohabbat sar-e-am tak na pahunche
tu sitam ki qainchiyon se par-e-arzu jo kaTe
koi tair-e-taKHayyul tere baam tak na pahunche
mera waqt-e-wapsi hai tu na aa mere sirhane
ki jafa ki koi tohmat tere nam tak na pahunche
jo sanam-kade mein jalwa tera dekh le barahman
tera nam chhoD kar wo kabhi ram tak na pahunche
teri ek yaad rangin meri zist ka sahaara
jo wo subh ko na aae to ye sham tak na pahunche
mera aaKHiri tha sajda ki nafas ne sath chhoDa
tere dar pe sar jhukaya to qiyam tak na pahunche
mera karwan-e-hasti mere sabr hi ne luTa
kabhi aah bhi jo khinchi tere nam tak na pahonche
gham-e-ishq gar na ho to na ho dil asir-e-gesu
ki na ho jo dana tair kabhi dam tak na pahunche
main jhuka hun bandagi ko to wo ruKH phira rahe hain
ki salam rafta rafta ye payam tak na pahunche
jo naqab-e-ruKH ulaT kar kabhi samne bhi aaya
jo chaDhae tewaron ko ki salam tak na pahunche
jo pila de muskura kar tu jhuki jhuki nazar se
koi hath mai-kade mein kabhi jam tak na pahunche

nahīñ mujh ko hasrat mā-sivā pas ab us kī yaad se kaam hai
na vo ab shabāb ke valvale na ḳhayāl-e-shīsha-o-jām hai
maiñ tire hī naam pe huuñ fidā tirī yaad kā mujhe aasrā
tire sang-e-dar pe mirī qazā mirī zindagī kā payām hai
kabhī aah kī kabhī ġhash hue kabhī dil ko thaam ke ro diye
tire hijr meñ hameñ roz-o-shab yahī mashġhala yahī kaam hai
jo nikal paḌe mire ashk-e-ġham sar-e-bazm aap ḳhafā na hoñ
jo ubal ke mil ga.ī ḳhaak meñ vo sharāb fāzil-e-jām hai
ye na pūchho kitnī hai dāstāñ nahīñ sunñā chāhte so raho
kahūñ kaise apnī zabāñ se maiñ ki fasāna merā tamām hai
jo guzar gayā koī rāh-rau mirī qabr par to ye kah uThā
ye kisī javān kī qabr hai ki udaas jo sar-e-shām hai
huiiñ chaar āñkheñ bhī gar kabhī to nigāh sharm se pher lī
ye ajab tarah kī hai dostī na salām hai na kalām hai
vo jo ik hai 'ālī'-e-ḳhasta-tan vo asīr-e-zulf-e-habīb hai
jahāñ dekhiye yahī tazkira yahī zikr sā sar-e-ām he
nahin mujh ko hasrat ma-siwa pas ab us ki yaad se kaam hai
na wo ab shabab ke walwale na KHayal-e-shisha-o-jam hai
main tere hi nam pe hun fida teri yaad ka mujhe aasra
tere sang-e-dar pe meri qaza meri zindagi ka payam hai
kabhi aah ki kabhi ghash hue kabhi dil ko tham ke ro diye
tere hijr mein hamein roz-o-shab yahi mashghala yahi kaam hai
jo nikal paDe mere ashk-e-gham sar-e-bazm aap KHafa na hon
jo ubal ke mil gai KHak mein wo sharab fazil-e-jam hai
ye na puchho kitni hai dastan nahin sunna chahte so raho
kahun kaise apni zaban se main ki fasana mera tamam hai
jo guzar gaya koi rah-rau meri qabr par to ye kah uTha
ye kisi jawan ki qabr hai ki udas jo sar-e-sham hai
huin chaar aankhen bhi gar kabhi to nigah sharm se pher li
ye ajab tarah ki hai dosti na salam hai na kalam hai
wo jo ek hai 'ali'-e-KHasta-tan wo asir-e-zulf-e-habib hai
jahan dekhiye yahi tazkira yahi zikr sa sar-e-am he

zindagī ik dard-o-ġham kā saaz hai
maut jis kī āḳhirī āvāz hai
vaañ to ā.īna hai mashq-e-nāz hai
muntashir yaañ zindagī kā saaz hai
dil hamārā dard se ḳhālī na kar
ye hamārī zindagī kā raaz hai
aaj phir barseñge naġhme bazm meñ
aaj phir hāthoñ pe us ke saaz hai
har nishāna dil pe lagtā hai mire
kaun kohna-mashq tīr-andāz hai
sun rahā huuñ dil se naġhmoñ kī sadā
dost se miltī huī āvāz hai
naġhma-bāz ik zindagī kā saaz hai
dahr kā har zarra ham-āvāz hai
jal rahā hai jism kā ḳhākī qafas
tā.ir-e-jāñ mā.il-e-parvāz hai
ḳhatm kar 'ālī' fasāna ḳhatm kar
sunñe vaalā mahv-e-ḳhvāb-e-nāz hai
zindagi ek dard-o-gham ka saz hai
maut jis ki aaKHiri aawaz hai
wan to aaina hai mashq-e-naz hai
muntashir yan zindagi ka saz hai
dil hamara dard se KHali na kar
ye hamari zindagi ka raaz hai
aaj phir barsenge naghme bazm mein
aaj phir hathon pe us ke saz hai
har nishana dil pe lagta hai mere
kaun kohna-mashq tir-andaz hai
sun raha hun dil se naghmon ki sada
dost se milti hui aawaz hai
naghma-baz ek zindagi ka saz hai
dahr ka har zarra ham-awaz hai
jal raha hai jism ka KHaki qafas
tair-e-jaan mail-e-parwaz hai
KHatm kar 'ali' fasana KHatm kar
sunne wala mahw-e-KHwab-e-naz hai

bahār aa.ī hai aalam meñ ajab vahshat kā sāmāñ hai
bayābāñ meñ kabhī ghar hai kabhī ghar meñ bayābāñ hai
mirī pābandiyāñ hī jab mirī āzādiyāñ Thahrīñ
to gulshan ho ki sahrā sab mirī nazroñ meñ zindāñ hai
har ik sarmast-e-irfāñ hai magar hai farq bas itnā
kahīñ dariyā meñ qatra hai kahīñ qatre meñ tūfāñ hai
chaman meñ phuul haiñ phūloñ pe kuchh bikhre hue tinke
mirā ujḌā nasheman bhī gulistāñ-dar-gulistāñ hai
samajh meñ kuchh nahīñ aatā duā kis chiiz kī māñgūñ
kabhī jiine kī ḳhvāhish hai kabhī marne kā armāñ hai
kahāñ kā qissa hai āḳhir ye dil meñ kyā samā.ī hai
palaT jaao palaT jaao idhar gor-e-ġharībāñ hai
na chhoḌā farq kuchh vahshat ne mere jeb-o-dāmāñ meñ
garebāñ hai jo dāman hai jo dāman hai garebāñ hai
rukī hai lab pe jaañ aakar pe ab to maut bhī 'ālī'
ajab kuchh kashmakash meñ hai na mushkil hai na āsāñ hai
bahaar aai hai aalam mein ajab wahshat ka saman hai
bayaban mein kabhi ghar hai kabhi ghar mein bayaban hai
meri pabandiyan hi jab meri aazadiyan Thahrin
to gulshan ho ki sahra sab meri nazron mein zindan hai
har ek sarmast-e-irfan hai magar hai farq bas itna
kahin dariya mein qatra hai kahin qatre mein tufan hai
chaman mein phul hain phulon pe kuchh bikhre hue tinke
mera ujDa nasheman bhi gulistan-dar-gulistan hai
samajh mein kuchh nahin aata dua kis chiz ki mangun
kabhi jine ki KHwahish hai kabhi marne ka arman hai
kahan ka qissa hai aaKHir ye dil mein kya samai hai
palaT jao palaT jao idhar gor-e-ghariban hai
na chhoDa farq kuchh wahshat ne mere jeb-o-daman mein
gareban hai jo daman hai jo daman hai gareban hai
ruki hai lab pe jaan aakar pe ab to maut bhi 'ali'
ajab kuchh kashmakash mein hai na mushkil hai na aasan hai

hujūm-e-ġham-e-jāvedāñ ho rahā hai
mire sabr kā imtihāñ ho rahā hai
fasāna tire ishq kā kah rahā huuñ
zamāna mirā ham-zabāñ ho rahā hai
bas ik mere hī āshiyāñ kī ḳhalish se
jise dekhiye bāġhbāñ ho rahā hai
na Duube kahīñ ārzūoñ kī kashtī
mirā bahr-e-ġham phir ravāñ ho rahā hai
zarā bāġhbāñ ho gayā hai jo ġhāfil
har ik phuul ik āshiyāñ ho rahā hai
tirī raah meñ kārvāñ zindagī kā
ġhubār-e-pas-e-kārvāñ ho rahā hai
nasheman ke tinkoñ se phūTe haiñ ġhunche
mirā āshiyāñ gulsitāñ ho rahā hai
hujum-e-gham-e-jawedan ho raha hai
mere sabr ka imtihan ho raha hai
fasana tere ishq ka kah raha hun
zamana mera ham-zaban ho raha hai
bas ek mere hi aashiyan ki KHalish se
jise dekhiye baghban ho raha hai
na Dube kahin aarzuon ki kashti
mera bahr-e-gham phir rawan ho raha hai
zara baghban ho gaya hai jo ghafil
har ek phul ek aashiyan ho raha hai
teri rah mein karwan zindagi ka
ghubar-e-pas-e-karwan ho raha hai
nasheman ke tinkon se phuTe hain ghunche
mera aashiyan gulsitan ho raha hai

mil ga.ī dard kī davā dil ko
rakhe allāh mere qātil ko
ishq ne daaġh vo diyā dil ko
aa ga.ī sharm māh-e-kāmil ko
kaT chukī thī rag-e-hayāt mirī
rahm kab aaya mere qātil ko
maanā rahzan hai rāhbar merā
kyā kahūñ maiñ charāġh-e-manzil ko
kis kī kashtī lagī kināre se
zalzala aa rahā hai sāhil ko
sub.h ko par tarāshe jā.eñge
koī kar de ḳhabar anādil ko
dāġh-e-dil merā dekhne vaale
sham.a kahte haiñ māh-e-kāmil ko
maanā zālim haiñ bevafā haiñ phuul
shikva zebā nahīñ anādil ko
yūñhī dekhā nahīñ ma.āl-e-ishq
zahmateñ dī haiñ dast-e-qātil ko
maiñ chalā gard-e-kārvāñ ke saath
kah do merā salām manzil ko
maanā aajiz haiñ jaañ se parvāne
chāhiye kyā charāġh-e-mahfil ko
maut ne shaam se sulāyā mujhe
niiñd shab bhar na aa.ī qātil ko
Duub kar pā liyā sukūn-e-hayāt
pahoñche sāhil pe kho ke sāhil ko
un pe ik roz paḌ ga.ī thī nazar
umr bhar jhelnā paḌā dil ko
ġham meñ phūloñ ke bārhā 'ālī'
dekhā rote hue anādil ko
mil gai dard ki dawa dil ko
rakhe allah mere qatil ko
ishq ne dagh wo diya dil ko
aa gai sharm mah-e-kaamil ko
kaT chuki thi rag-e-hayat meri
rahm kab aaya mere qatil ko
mana rahzan hai rahbar mera
kya kahun main charagh-e-manzil ko
kis ki kashti lagi kinare se
zalzala aa raha hai sahil ko
subh ko par tarashe jaenge
koi kar de KHabar anadil ko
dagh-e-dil mera dekhne wale
shama kahte hain mah-e-kaamil ko
mana zalim hain bewafa hain phul
shikwa zeba nahin anadil ko
yunhi dekha nahin maal-e-ishq
zahmaten di hain dast-e-qatil ko
main chala gard-e-karwan ke sath
kah do mera salam manzil ko
mana aajiz hain jaan se parwane
chahiye kya charagh-e-mahfil ko
maut ne sham se sulaya mujhe
nind shab bhar na aai qatil ko
Dub kar pa liya sukun-e-hayat
pahonche sahil pe kho ke sahil ko
un pe ek roz paD gai thi nazar
umr bhar jhelna paDa dil ko
gham mein phulon ke barha 'ali'
dekha rote hue anadil ko

nazar dekhte haiñ jigar dekhte haiñ
tujhe har taraf jalva-gar dekhte haiñ
vo hañs kar adā se jidhar dekhte haiñ
zamāne ko zer-o-zabar dekhte haiñ
yahī haiñ jo ḳhud-bīniyāñ to tumhīñ ko
lagegī tumhārī nazar dekhte haiñ
rahī jab na paañv uThāne kī tāqat
khule aaj zindāñ ke dar dekhte haiñ
kahīñ aa bhī o sub.h-e-ummīd-e-ālam
tirī raah murġh-e-sahar dekhte haiñ
palaT kar vo aa.e haiñ mayyat se merī
yahī ḳhvāb ham raat bhar dekhte haiñ
jo mumkin nahīñ tere dar tak rasā.ī
to baiThe tirī rahguzar dekhte haiñ
kahīñ baaġh meñ gar bhaḌakte haiñ sho'le
to ghabrā ke ham bāl-o-par dekhte haiñ
chamakte haiñ jab āsmāñ par sitāre
to ham apne dāġh-e-jigar dekhte haiñ
nazar dekhte hain jigar dekhte hain
tujhe har taraf jalwa-gar dekhte hain
wo hans kar ada se jidhar dekhte hain
zamane ko zer-o-zabar dekhte hain
yahi hain jo KHud-biniyan to tumhin ko
lagegi tumhaari nazar dekhte hain
rahi jab na panw uThane ki taqat
khule aaj zindan ke dar dekhte hain
kahin aa bhi o subh-e-ummid-e-alam
teri rah murgh-e-sahar dekhte hain
palaT kar wo aae hain mayyat se meri
yahi KHwab hum raat bhar dekhte hain
jo mumkin nahin tere dar tak rasai
to baiThe teri rahguzar dekhte hain
kahin bagh mein gar bhaDakte hain sho'le
to ghabra ke hum baal-o-par dekhte hain
chamakte hain jab aasman par sitare
to hum apne dagh-e-jigar dekhte hain

tujh ko dekhe ik zamāna ho gayā
zahr ab to āb-o-dāna ho gayā
ishq jiine kā bahāna ho gayā
daam thā qismat se daana ho gayā
muskurā kar tū ravāna ho gayā
merī vahshat kā bahāna ho gayā
sair karke tū chaman se kyā chalā
dil bhī pahlū se ravāna ho gayā
ek din ro.e the terī yaad meñ
thā ye qissa jo fasāna ho gayā
dī jilā aisī tasavvur ne tire
dil mirā ā.īna-ḳhāna ho gayā
pūchhte ho haal kyā 'ālī' kā ab
mar gayā vo to zamāna ho gayā
tujh ko dekhe ek zamana ho gaya
zahr ab to aab-o-dana ho gaya
ishq jine ka bahana ho gaya
dam tha qismat se dana ho gaya
muskura kar tu rawana ho gaya
meri wahshat ka bahana ho gaya
sair karke tu chaman se kya chala
dil bhi pahlu se rawana ho gaya
ek din roe the teri yaad mein
tha ye qissa jo fasana ho gaya
di jila aisi tasawwur ne tere
dil mera aaina-KHana ho gaya
puchhte ho haal kya 'ali' ka ab
mar gaya wo to zamana ho gaya

lagā ke dil kabhī aañsū bhī ham bahā na sake
lagī jo aag jigar meñ use bujhā na sake
kiyā za.iif tire qasd-e-justujū ne hameñ
ki tā-lahad bhī ham apne qadam se jā na sake
vo aaj bazm meñ tevar chaḌhā.e aa.e haiñ
ki hāl-e-dil koī apnā unheñ sunā na sake
azal se naam pe mere faroġh likkhā thā
vo mujh ko laakh miTāyā kiye miTā na sake
sulā ke qabr meñ dete ho thapkiyāñ sāhib
ki mujh ko shor-e-qayāmat bhī ab jagā na sake
hamārā daulat-e-duniyā ne sar buland kiyā
ki dar pe dost ke sajde ko sar jhukā na sake
hamāre dil meñ likhī thī magar tirī ulfat
ki ham jamāl-e-jahāñ se fareb khā na sake
burā ho rang-e-ruḳh-e-nā-murād kā 'ālī'
kisī kā raaz kaleje meñ ham chhupā na sake
laga ke dil kabhi aansu bhi hum baha na sake
lagi jo aag jigar mein use bujha na sake
kiya zaif tere qasd-e-justuju ne hamein
ki ta-lahad bhi hum apne qadam se ja na sake
wo aaj bazm mein tewar chaDhae aae hain
ki haal-e-dil koi apna unhen suna na sake
azal se nam pe mere farogh likkha tha
wo mujh ko lakh miTaya kiye miTa na sake
sula ke qabr mein dete ho thapkiyan sahib
ki mujh ko shor-e-qayamat bhi ab jaga na sake
hamara daulat-e-duniya ne sar buland kiya
ki dar pe dost ke sajde ko sar jhuka na sake
hamare dil mein likhi thi magar teri ulfat
ki hum jamal-e-jahan se fareb kha na sake
bura ho rang-e-ruKH-e-na-murad ka 'ali'
kisi ka raaz kaleje mein hum chhupa na sake

ye qarz to merā hai chukā.egā koī aur
dukh mujh ko hai aur niir bahā.egā koī aur
kyā phir yūñhī dī jā.egī ujrat pe gavāhī
kyā terī sazā ab ke bhī pā.egā koī aur
anjām ko pahuñchūñgā maiñ anjām se pahle
ḳhud merī kahānī bhī sunā.egā koī aur
tab hogī ḳhabar kitnī hai raftār-e-taġhayyur
jab shaam Dhale lauT ke aa.egā koī aur
ummīd-e-sahar bhī to virāsat meñ hai shāmil
shāyad ki diyā ab ke jalā.egā koī aur
kab bār-e-tabassum mire hoñToñ se uThegā
ye bojh bhī lagtā hai uThā.egā koī aur
is baar huuñ dushman kī rasā.ī se bahut duur
is baar magar zaḳhm lagā.egā koī aur
shāmil pas-e-parda bhī haiñ is khel meñ kuchh log
bolegā koī hoñT hilā.egā koī aur
ye qarz to mera hai chukaega koi aur
dukh mujh ko hai aur nir bahaega koi aur
kya phir yunhi di jaegi ujrat pe gawahi
kya teri saza ab ke bhi paega koi aur
anjam ko pahunchunga main anjam se pahle
KHud meri kahani bhi sunaega koi aur
tab hogi KHabar kitni hai raftar-e-taghayyur
jab sham Dhale lauT ke aaega koi aur
ummid-e-sahar bhi to wirasat mein hai shamil
shayad ki diya ab ke jalaega koi aur
kab bar-e-tabassum mere honTon se uThega
ye bojh bhi lagta hai uThaega koi aur
is bar hun dushman ki rasai se bahut dur
is bar magar zaKHm lagaega koi aur
shamil pas-e-parda bhi hain is khel mein kuchh log
bolega koi honT hilaega koi aur

vo mere haal pe royā bhī muskurāyā bhī
ajiib shaḳhs hai apnā bhī hai parāyā bhī
ye intizār sahar kā thā yā tumhārā thā
diyā jalāyā bhī maiñ ne diyā bujhāyā bhī
maiñ chāhtā huuñ Thahar jaa.e chashm-e-dariyā meñ
laraztā aks tumhārā bhī merā saayā bhī
bahut mahīn thā parda laraztī āñkhoñ kā
mujhe dikhāyā bhī tū ne mujhe chhupāyā bhī
bayāz bhar bhī ga.ī aur phir bhī saada hai
tumhāre naam ko likkhā bhī aur miTāyā bhī
wo mere haal pe roya bhi muskuraya bhi
ajib shaKHs hai apna bhi hai paraya bhi
ye intizar sahar ka tha ya tumhaara tha
diya jalaya bhi main ne diya bujhaya bhi
main chahta hun Thahar jae chashm-e-dariya mein
larazta aks tumhaara bhi mera saya bhi
bahut mahin tha parda larazti aankhon ka
mujhe dikhaya bhi tu ne mujhe chhupaya bhi
bayaz bhar bhi gai aur phir bhi sada hai
tumhaare nam ko likkha bhi aur miTaya bhi

ye aur baat ki rañg-e-bahār kam hogā
na.ī rutoñ meñ daraḳhtoñ kā baar kam hogā
ta.alluqāt meñ aa.ī hai bas ye tabdīlī
mileñge ab bhī magar intizār kam hogā
maiñ sochtā rahā kal raat baiTh kar tanhā
ki is hujūm meñ merā shumār kam hogā
palaT to aa.egā shāyad kabhī yahī mausam
tire baġhair magar ḳhush-gavār kam hogā
bahut tavīl hai 'ānas' ye zindagī kā safar
bas ek shaḳhs pe dār-o-madār kam hogā
ye aur baat ki rang-e-bahaar kam hoga
nai ruton mein daraKHton ka bar kam hoga
talluqat mein aai hai bas ye tabdili
milenge ab bhi magar intizar kam hoga
main sochta raha kal raat baiTh kar tanha
ki is hujum mein mera shumar kam hoga
palaT to aaega shayad kabhi yahi mausam
tere baghair magar KHush-gawar kam hoga
bahut tawil hai 'anas' ye zindagi ka safar
bas ek shaKHs pe dar-o-madar kam hoga

bāhar bhī ab andar jaisā sannāTā hai
dariyā ke us paar bhī gahrā sannāTā hai
shor thame to shāyad sadiyāñ biit chukī haiñ
ab tak lekin sahmā sahmā sannāTā hai
kis se bolūñ ye to ik sahrā hai jahāñ par
maiñ huuñ yā phir gūñgā bahrā sannāTā hai
jaise ik tūfān se pahle kī ḳhāmoshī
aaj mirī bastī meñ aisā sannāTā hai
na.ī sahar kī chaap na jaane kab ubhregī
chāroñ jānib raat kā gahrā sannāTā hai
soch rahe ho socho lekin bol na paḌnā
dekh rahe ho shahr meñ kitnā sannāTā hai
mahv-e-ḳhvāb haiñ saarī dekhne vaalī āñkheñ
jāgne vaalā bas ik andhā sannāTā hai
Darnā hai to an-jānī āvāz se Darnā
ye to 'ānis' dekhā-bhālā sannāTā hai
bahar bhi ab andar jaisa sannaTa hai
dariya ke us par bhi gahra sannaTa hai
shor thame to shayad sadiyan bit chuki hain
ab tak lekin sahma sahma sannaTa hai
kis se bolun ye to ek sahra hai jahan par
main hun ya phir gunga bahra sannaTa hai
jaise ek tufan se pahle ki KHamoshi
aaj meri basti mein aisa sannaTa hai
nai sahar ki chap na jaane kab ubhregi
chaaron jaanib raat ka gahra sannaTa hai
soch rahe ho socho lekin bol na paDna
dekh rahe ho shahr mein kitna sannaTa hai
mahw-e-KHwab hain sari dekhne wali aankhen
jagne wala bas ek andha sannaTa hai
Darna hai to an-jaani aawaz se Darna
ye to 'anis' dekha-bhaala sannaTa hai

ajab talāsh-e-musalsal kā iḳhtitām huā
husūl-e-rizq huā bhī to zer-e-dām huā
thā intizār manāeñge mil ke dīvālī
na tum hī lauT ke aa.e na vaqt-e-shām huā
har ek shahr kā me.aar muḳhtalif dekhā
kahīñ pe sar kahīñ pagḌī kā ehtirām huā
zarā sī umr adāvat kī lambī fehristeñ
ajiib qarz virāsat meñ mere naam huā
na thī zamīn meñ vus.at mirī nazar jaisī
badan thakā bhī nahīñ aur safar tamām huā
ham apne saath liye phir rahe haiñ pachhtāvā
ḳhayāl lauT ke jaane kā gaam gaam huā
ajab talash-e-musalsal ka iKHtitam hua
husul-e-rizq hua bhi to zer-e-dam hua
tha intizar manaenge mil ke diwali
na tum hi lauT ke aae na waqt-e-sham hua
har ek shahr ka mear muKHtalif dekha
kahin pe sar kahin pagDi ka ehtiram hua
zara si umr adawat ki lambi fehristen
ajib qarz wirasat mein mere nam hua
na thi zamin mein wusat meri nazar jaisi
badan thaka bhi nahin aur safar tamam hua
hum apne sath liye phir rahe hain pachhtawa
KHayal lauT ke jaane ka gam gam hua

kitne hī peḌ ḳhauf-e-ḳhizāñ se ujaḌ ga.e
kuchh barg-e-sabz vaqt se pahle hī jhaḌ ga.e
kuchh āñdhiyāñ bhī apnī muāvin safar meñ thiiñ
thak kar paḌāv Daalā to ḳheme ukhaḌ ga.e
ab ke mirī shikast meñ un kā bhī haath hai
vo tiir jo kamān ke panje meñ gaḌ ga.e
suljhī thiiñ gutthiyāñ mirī dānist meñ magar
hāsil ye hai ki zaḳhmoñ ke Tāñke ukhaḌ ga.e
nirvān kyā bas ab to amaañ kī talāsh hai
tahzīb phailne lagī jañgal sukaḌ ga.e
is band ghar meñ kaise kahūñ kyā tilism hai
khole the jitne qufl vo hoñToñ pe paḌ ga.e
be-saltanat huī haiñ ka.ī ūñchī gardaneñ
bāhar saroñ ke dast-e-tasallut se dhaḌ ga.e
kitne hi peD KHauf-e-KHizan se ujaD gae
kuchh barg-e-sabz waqt se pahle hi jhaD gae
kuchh aandhiyan bhi apni muawin safar mein thin
thak kar paDaw Dala to KHeme ukhaD gae
ab ke meri shikast mein un ka bhi hath hai
wo tir jo kaman ke panje mein gaD gae
suljhi thin gutthiyan meri danist mein magar
hasil ye hai ki zaKHmon ke Tanke ukhaD gae
nirwan kya bas ab to aman ki talash hai
tahzib phailne lagi jangal sukaD gae
is band ghar mein kaise kahun kya tilism hai
khole the jitne qufl wo honTon pe paD gae
be-saltanat hui hain kai unchi gardanen
bahar saron ke dast-e-tasallut se dhaD gae

ik karb-e-musalsal kī sazā deñ to kise deñ
maqtal meñ haiñ jiine kī duā deñ to kise deñ
patthar haiñ sabhī log kareñ baat to kis se
is shahr-e-ḳhamoshāñ meñ sadā deñ to kise deñ
hai kaun ki jo ḳhud ko hī jaltā huā dekhe
sab haath haiñ kāġhaz ke diyā deñ to kise deñ
sab log savālī haiñ sabhī jism barahna
aur paas hai bas ek ridā deñ to kise deñ
jab haath hī kaT jaa.eñ to thāmegā bhalā kaun
ye soch rahe haiñ ki asā deñ to kise deñ
bāzār meñ ḳhushbū ke ḳharīdār kahāñ haiñ
ye phuul haiñ be-rañg batā deñ to kise deñ
chup rahne kī har shaḳhs qasam khaa.e hue hai
ham zahr bharā jaam bhalā deñ to kise deñ
ek karb-e-musalsal ki saza den to kise den
maqtal mein hain jine ki dua den to kise den
patthar hain sabhi log karen baat to kis se
is shahr-e-KHamoshan mein sada den to kise den
hai kaun ki jo KHud ko hi jalta hua dekhe
sab hath hain kaghaz ke diya den to kise den
sab log sawali hain sabhi jism barahna
aur pas hai bas ek rida den to kise den
jab hath hi kaT jaen to thamega bhala kaun
ye soch rahe hain ki asa den to kise den
bazar mein KHushbu ke KHaridar kahan hain
ye phul hain be-rang bata den to kise den
chup rahne ki har shaKHs qasam khae hue hai
hum zahr bhara jam bhala den to kise den

patthar haiñ sabhī log kareñ baat to kis se
is shahr-e-ḳhamoshāñ meñ sadā deñ to kise deñ
hai kaun ki jo ḳhud ko hī jaltā huā dekhe
sab haath haiñ kāġhaz ke diyā deñ to kise deñ
sab log savālī haiñ sabhī jism barahna
aur paas hai bas ek ridā deñ to kise deñ
jab haath hī kaT jaa.eñ to thāmegā bhalā kaun
ye soch rahe haiñ ki asā deñ to kise deñ
patthar hain sabhi log karen baat to kis se
is shahr-e-KHamoshan mein sada den to kise den
hai kaun ki jo KHud ko hi jalta hua dekhe
sab hath hain kaghaz ke diya den to kise den
sab log sawali hain sabhi jism barahna
aur pas hai bas ek rida den to kise den
jab hath hi kaT jaen to thamega bhala kaun
ye soch rahe hain ki asa den to kise den

vo kuchh gahrī soch meñ aise Duub gayā hai
baiThe baiThe nadī kināre Duub gayā hai
aaj kī raat na jaane kitnī lambī hogī
aaj kā sūraj shaam se pahle Duub gayā hai
vo jo pyāsā lagtā thā sailāb-zada thā
paanī paanī kahte kahte Duub gayā hai
mere apne andar ek bhañvar thā jis meñ
merā sab kuchh saath hī mere Duub gayā hai
shor to yuuñ uTThā thā jaise ik tūfāñ ho
sannāTe meñ jaane kaise Duub gayā hai
āḳhirī ḳhvāhish puurī kar ke jiinā kaisā
'ānas' bhī sāhil tak aa ke Duub gayā hai
wo kuchh gahri soch mein aise Dub gaya hai
baiThe baiThe nadi kinare Dub gaya hai
aaj ki raat na jaane kitni lambi hogi
aaj ka suraj sham se pahle Dub gaya hai
wo jo pyasa lagta tha sailab-zada tha
pani pani kahte kahte Dub gaya hai
mere apne andar ek bhanwar tha jis mein
mera sab kuchh sath hi mere Dub gaya hai
shor to yun uTTha tha jaise ek tufan ho
sannaTe mein jaane kaise Dub gaya hai
aaKHiri KHwahish puri kar ke jina kaisa
'anas' bhi sahil tak aa ke Dub gaya hai

ho jā.egī jab tum se shanāsā.ī zarā aur
baḌh jā.egī shāyad mirī tanhā.ī zarā aur
kyuuñ khul ga.e logoñ pe mirī zaat ke asrār
ai kaash ki hotī mirī gahrā.ī zarā aur
phir haath pe zaḳhmoñ ke nishāñ gin na sakoge
ye uljhī huī Dor jo suljhā.ī zarā aur
tardīd to kar saktā thā phailegī magar baat
is taur bhī hogī tirī rusvā.ī zarā aur
kyuuñ tark-e-ta.alluq bhī kiyā lauT bhī āyā?
achchhā thā ki hotā jo vo harjā.ī zarā aur
hai diip tirī yaad kā raushan abhī dil meñ
ye ḳhauf hai lekin jo havā aa.ī zarā aur
laḌnā vahīñ dushman se jahāñ gher sako tum
jītoge tabhī hogī jo paspā.ī zarā aur
baḌh jā.eñge kuchh aur lahū bechne vaale
ho jaa.e agar shahr meñ mahñgā.ī zarā aur
ik Dūbtī dhaḌkan kī sadā log na sun leñ
kuchh der ko bajne do ye shahnā.ī zarā aur
ho jaegi jab tum se shanasai zara aur
baDh jaegi shayad meri tanhai zara aur
kyun khul gae logon pe meri zat ke asrar
ai kash ki hoti meri gahrai zara aur
phir hath pe zaKHmon ke nishan gin na sakoge
ye uljhi hui Dor jo suljhai zara aur
tardid to kar sakta tha phailegi magar baat
is taur bhi hogi teri ruswai zara aur
kyun tark-e-talluq bhi kiya lauT bhi aaya?
achchha tha ki hota jo wo harjai zara aur
hai dip teri yaad ka raushan abhi dil mein
ye KHauf hai lekin jo hawa aai zara aur
laDna wahin dushman se jahan gher sako tum
jitoge tabhi hogi jo paspai zara aur
baDh jaenge kuchh aur lahu bechne wale
ho jae agar shahr mein mahngai zara aur
ek Dubti dhaDkan ki sada log na sun len
kuchh der ko bajne do ye shahnai zara aur

jīvan ko dukh dukh ko aag aur aag ko paanī kahte
bachche lekin so.e hue the kis se kahānī kahte
sach kahne kā hausla tum ne chhīn liyā hai varna
shahr meñ phailī vīrānī ko sab vīrānī kahte
vaqt guzartā jaatā aur ye zaḳhm hare rahte to
baḌī hifāzat se rakkhī hai terī nishānī kahte
vo to shāyad donoñ kā dukh ik jaisā thā varna
ham bhī patthar mārte tujh ko aur dīvānī kahte
tabdīlī sachchā.ī hai is ko mānte lekin kaise
ā.īne ko dekh ke ik tasvīr purānī kahte
terā lahja apnāyā ab dil meñ hasrat sī hai
apnī koī baat kabhī to apnī zabānī kahte
chup rah kar iz.hār kiyā hai kah sakte to 'ānas'
ek alāhida tarz-e-suḳhan kā tujh ko baanī kahte
jiwan ko dukh dukh ko aag aur aag ko pani kahte
bachche lekin soe hue the kis se kahani kahte
sach kahne ka hausla tum ne chhin liya hai warna
shahr mein phaili virani ko sab virani kahte
waqt guzarta jata aur ye zaKHm hare rahte to
baDi hifazat se rakkhi hai teri nishani kahte
wo to shayad donon ka dukh ek jaisa tha warna
hum bhi patthar marte tujh ko aur diwani kahte
tabdili sachchai hai is ko mante lekin kaise
aaine ko dekh ke ek taswir purani kahte
tera lahja apnaya ab dil mein hasrat si hai
apni koi baat kabhi to apni zabani kahte
chup rah kar izhaar kiya hai kah sakte to 'anas'
ek alahida tarz-e-suKHan ka tujh ko bani kahte

milan kī saa.at ko is tarah se amar kiyā hai
tumhārī yādoñ ke saath tanhā safar kiyā hai
sunā hai us rut ko dekh kar tum bhī ro paḌe the
sunā hai bārish ne pattharoñ par asar kiyā hai
salīb kā baar bhī uThāo tamām jīvan
ye lab-kushā.ī kā jurm tum ne agar kiyā hai
tumheñ ḳhabar thī haqīqateñ talḳh haiñ jabhī to!
tumhārī āñkhoñ ne ḳhvāb ko mo'atabar kiyā hai
ghuTan baḌhī hai to phir usī ko sadā.eñ dī haiñ
ki jis havā ne har ik shajar be-samar kiyā hai
hai tere andar basī huī ek aur duniyā
magar kabhī tū ne itnā lambā safar kiyā hai
mire hī dam se to raunaqeñ tere shahr meñ thiiñ
mire hī qadmoñ ne dasht ko rah-guzar kiyā hai
tujhe ḳhabar kyā mire laboñ kī ḳhamoshiyoñ ne!
tire fasāne ko kis qadar muḳhtasar kiyā hai
bahut sī āñkhoñ meñ tīrgī ghar banā chukī hai
bahut sī āñkhoñ ne intizār-e-sahar kiyā hai
milan ki saat ko is tarah se amar kiya hai
tumhaari yaadon ke sath tanha safar kiya hai
suna hai us rut ko dekh kar tum bhi ro paDe the
suna hai barish ne pattharon par asar kiya hai
salib ka bar bhi uThao tamam jiwan
ye lab-kushai ka jurm tum ne agar kiya hai
tumhein KHabar thi haqiqaten talKH hain jabhi to!
tumhaari aankhon ne KHwab ko mo'atabar kiya hai
ghuTan baDhi hai to phir usi ko sadaen di hain
ki jis hawa ne har ek shajar be-samar kiya hai
hai tere andar basi hui ek aur duniya
magar kabhi tu ne itna lamba safar kiya hai
mere hi dam se to raunaqen tere shahr mein thin
mere hi qadmon ne dasht ko rah-guzar kiya hai
tujhe KHabar kya mere labon ki KHamoshiyon ne!
tere fasane ko kis qadar muKHtasar kiya hai
bahut si aankhon mein tirgi ghar bana chuki hai
bahut si aankhon ne intizar-e-sahar kiya hai
